# astro-ph.HE [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Prospects for Improving the Theoretical Uncertainty for Tests of General Relativity with the EHT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30753)
*Lia Medeiros,George N. Wong,Feryal Ozel*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过大样本高分辨率模拟图像，系统标定了黑洞图像中亮环尺寸与分析黑洞阴影尺寸之间的关系，量化了理论不确定性来源，并提出了通过更高频观测、几何约束、天体物理约束及长时间观测来降低不确定性的具体途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 校准黑洞图像中的亮环（bright ring）尺寸与分析黑洞阴影（black hole shadow）尺寸之间的关系，对于利用事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope, EHT）图像进行黑洞质量测量以及广义相对论（general relativity）检验至关重要。

Method: 采用多种吸积流（accretion-flow）建模方法生成的大规模高分辨率模拟图像数据集，覆盖宽泛的系统参数与初始条件范围，对亮环与阴影之间的校准关系进行系统标定与不确定性分析。

Result: 理论不确定性可通过以下方式显著降低：(i) 在345 GHz频率观测；(ii) 应用几何图像约束（如PRIMO图像重建算法中的环宽推断）；(iii) 引入天体物理约束（如M87黑洞自旋轴与长波射电喷流对齐或反平行）；(iv) 假设吸积流为磁捕获（magnetically arrested）场位形。此外，后续多年观测数据的积累将进一步降低不确定性，而驻留时间滤波（dwell-time filtering）被识别为有前景的精度提升途径。

Conclusion: 亮环-阴影校准关系的理论不确定性可以通过更高频观测、更先进的图像重建技术、天体物理约束以及长时间监测来有效降低，其中驻留时间滤波有望成为提升校准精度的重要方法。

Abstract: We characterize the relationship between the size of the bright ring observed in simulated black hole images and the size of the analytic black hole shadow. Calibrating this relationship is crucial for mass measurements and, when independent mass measurements are available, for tests of general relativity using Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) images. We perform this calibration using a large set of high-resolution simulated images generated with different accretion-flow modeling approaches and spanning a wide range of system parameters and initial conditions. We show that the theoretical uncertainty in this relationship can be reduced significantly through future observations, improved imaging techniques, and the application of astrophysical or model-based constraints. In particular, the uncertainty decreases compared to existing measurements when (i) observing at 345 GHz, (ii) applying geometric image constraints, such as the ring width inference from the PRIMO image reconstruction algorithm, (iii) incorporating astrophysical constraints such as the black hole spin axis in M87 being aligned (or anti-aligned) with the large-scale jet observed at longer radio wavelengths, and (iv) assuming that the accretion flow can be described by a magnetically arrested field configuration. Finally, we quantify how the uncertainty is expected to decrease as additional observations are obtained in subsequent years and identify dwell-time filtering, i.e., evaluating the persistence of a geometric measurement over time, as a promising avenue for improving the precision of the calibration.

</details>


### [2] [Magnetar Formation from Accretion Induced Collapse of White Dwarfs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30839)
*Luís Felipe Longo Micchi,Patrick Chi-Kit Cheong,David Radice*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究采用广义相对论中微子磁流体力学（MHD）模拟，系统分析了快速旋转磁化白矮星通过吸积致坍缩（AIC）形成的后坍缩演化，揭示了原初磁星（proto-magnetar）的旋转、磁场和热结构，以及不稳定性驱动的磁能释放和爆发活动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在刻画快速旋转、磁化白矮星发生吸积致坍缩（accretion-induced collapse, AIC）后遗迹的演化特征，特别是其旋转、磁场和热结构，以及不稳定性发展和能量含量的变化。

Method: 采用保形平直近似下的广义相对论中微子磁流体力学（general-relativistic neutrino MHD）代码 Gmunu，针对旋转磁化白矮星的坍缩过程进行了九组轴对称模拟，追踪从坍缩、反弹至反弹后约1秒的演化过程。

Result: 坍缩产生快速旋转的原初磁星及其周围的持续吸积盘；遗迹质量与自转频率范围分别为1.15–1.45 M⊙和2.9–4.9 kHz，初始磁场越强，自转越慢；反弹后约10毫秒内发生整体振荡，驱动引力波发射和极向磁场能量调制；归一化磁能演化呈近似普适行为；遗迹内部在反弹后1秒内仍保持强磁场（≳10¹³ G）与高温（≳20 MeV）；磁场拓扑呈现表面极向场~10¹² G与环向场~10¹⁴ G的结构；当磁能超过旋转能（~10⁵² erg）时，核心失稳，引发磁通量爆发性释放、物质抛射和耀斑活动。

Conclusion: AIC遗迹中磁能与旋转能的相对大小决定了核心不稳定性与磁爆发活动的触发条件，系统表现出普适性的磁能演化规律及丰富的多信使（multimessenger）辐射特征。

Abstract: We aim to characterize the post-collapse evolution of accretion-induced collapse (AIC) remnants of rapidly rotating, magnetized white dwarfs, focusing on their rotational, magnetic, and thermal structure, as well as the development of instabilities and their energy content. We perform nine axis-symmetric general-relativistic neutrino magnetohydrodynamic (MHD) simulations of collapsing, rapidly rotating, magnetized white dwarfs. The simulations follow the system from collapse through bounce and up to $\sim$1 s post-bounce. The simulations are performed by the conformally flat general relativistic neutrino MHD code \texttt{Gmunu}. The collapse produces a rapidly rotating proto-magnetar surrounded by a persistent accretion disk lasting at least $\sim 1$ s after bounce. The remnant mass and spin span 1.15--1.45 $M_{\odot}$ and 2.9--4.9 kHz, respectively, with stronger initial magnetic fields generally leading to lower rotation rates. During the first $\sim 10$ ms, the proto-magnetar exhibits global oscillations that drive both gravitational-wave emission and coherent modulation of the poloidal magnetic field energy. The magnetic energy evolution, normalized to its bounce value, follows an approximately universal behavior across all models. The remnant interior remains strongly magnetized ($\gtrsim 10^{13}$ G) and hot ($\gtrsim 20$ MeV) up to 1 s after bounce, with maxima of both quantities co-located in the inner $\sim 10$ km. The magnetic field topology shows surface poloidal fields of ${\sim}10^{12}$ G and toroidal fields of ${\sim}10^{14}$ G, with strong toroidal components extending into the equatorial region. When the magnetic energy exceeds the rotational energy ($\sim 10^{52}$ erg), the remnant core becomes unstable, leading to episodic magnetic flux expulsion, mass ejection, and flare-like activity in which magnetic energy is released and thermalized in the surrounding material.

</details>


### [3] [Multipolar Magnetic-Field Inference for PSR J0740+6620 with Neural-Network-Accelerated NICER Pulse-Profile Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30886)
*Farhana Taiyebah,Constantinos Kalapotharakos,Greg Olmschenk,Wendy F. Wallace,Soumi De,Abu Bucker Siddik,Diane Oyen,Thibault Lechien,Zorawar Wadiasingh*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究利用 NICER 的 32 能段辐射曲线数据，结合神经网络代理（neural-network surrogate）和并行马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo），对毫秒脉冲星 PSR J0740+6620 的多极表面磁场结构进行了统计推断。模型采用偏移偶极子加轴对称四极子（offset dipole plus axisymmetric quadrupole）的真空静磁场描述发射足点，在11维磁场参数空间中进行后验采样，发现多极参数化存在严重简并，磁场方位角得到一定约束，而纬度、范围和形态约束较弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高质量毫秒脉冲星 PSR J0740+6620 的磁场拓扑结构对理解其辐射机制至关重要。已有研究基于几何热点（geometric hotspots）简化假设，但未充分探索磁场的多极特征；本研究旨在利用高维磁场参数化，结合神经网络加速推断，填补这一空白。

Method: 基于 Olmschenk et al. (2025) 的神经网络代理框架，将发射区建模为偏移偶极子加轴对称四极子静磁场的开放场线足点（open-field-line footpoints）。固定质量、半径、观测者倾角和热点温度比为 Dittmann et al. (2024) 的最大似然值，探索11维磁场参数空间。使用卷积神经网络（convolutional neural network）代理在 $5.12\times10^7$ 个合成辐射曲线上训练，并在4000个CPU核心上并行进行集成马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（ensemble MCMC）计算，将似然评估加速约400倍。对两种校准温度权重（Tw=1.31 和 Tw=1.41）分别进行独立推断。

Result: 两种温度权重下的后验分布、后验预测光变曲线和最大似然值非常相似，表明对该选择不敏感。偏移模型能再现观测的双峰光变曲线，但后验呈现宽而多模态分布，反映了背景主导的数据特征与多极参数化的简并性。热点密度图显示脉冲相位约束了发射的大致方位角位置，而纬度、表面范围和形态的约束较弱。零偏移模型在所选磁场基底下不被支持。

Conclusion: 神经网络加速的磁场推断方法成功扩展至 PSR J0740+6620，表明当前数据对多极磁场参数的约束能力有限。未来工作应发展能谱依赖、力自由（force-free）以及X射线/伽马射线联合分析扩展。

Abstract: We investigate the multipolar surface magnetic-field structure of the high-mass millisecond pulsar PSR J0740+6620 using the 32-bin bolometric NICER pulse profile of Dittmann et al. (2024). Building on the neural-network surrogate framework of Olmschenk et al. (2025), we model the emitting regions as open-field-line footpoints of an offset dipole plus axisymmetric quadrupole static vacuum field, rather than as prescribed geometric hotspots. We fix the stellar mass, radius, observer inclination, and hotspot temperature ratio to the Dittmann et al. (2024) maximum-likelihood values and explore the resulting 11-dimensional magnetic-field space. To make this feasible, we train convolutional neural-network surrogates on $5.12\times10^7$ synthetic bolometric light curves and use them in a parallel ensemble Markov Chain Monte Carlo calculation on 4000 CPU cores, accelerating likelihood evaluations by a factor of $\gtrsim 400$. We perform independent inferences for two calibrated temperature-weight prescriptions, Tw=1.31 and Tw=1.41, encoding the relative bolometric weight associated with the hotspot temperature difference. The posteriors, posterior-predictive light curves, and maximum-likelihood values are very similar, indicating weak sensitivity to this choice. The offset model reproduces the observed double-peaked profile and yields broad, multimodal posteriors, reflecting both the background-dominated data and degeneracies of the multipolar parameterization. The hotspot-density map shows that pulse phases constrain the approximate azimuthal placement of the emission, while latitude, surface extent, and morphology remain weakly constrained. A restricted zero offset run is disfavored within the adopted field basis. This work extends neural-network-accelerated magnetic-field inference to PSR J0740+6620 and motivates future energy-dependent, force-free, and joint X-ray/$γ$-ray extensions.

</details>


### [4] [The location of the upper edge of the pair-instability supernovae black hole mass gap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31757)
*Jeremy Sakstein,Djuna Croon*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究通过一系列恒星演化模拟，量化了核反应率、混合过程及星风等输入参数对超新星对不稳定性（PISN）黑洞质量间隙上边缘位置的影响，发现12C(α,γ)16O反应率是最主要的不确定来源，可使上边缘偏移约30 M⊙，并指出上边缘虽存在显著理论不确定性，但作为探测对不稳定性的直接探针具有重要价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波观测开始探测超新星对不稳定性（pair-instability supernova, PISN）黑洞质量间隙的上边缘，这一边界是恒星演化的关键理论预言。然而，该边界对恒星演化输入参数（如核反应率、混合过程及星风）的不确定性敏感程度尚不明确，亟需系统量化。

Method: 采用一系列恒星演化模拟，系统变化核反应率（包括12C(α,γ)16O、triple-α、16O+16O反应等）、混合过程及星风等输入参数，量化各参数对PISN黑洞质量间隙上边缘位置的影响程度。

Result: 12C(α,γ)16O反应率是主导不确定来源，使上边缘偏移ΔM~30 M⊙；triple-α反应率产生约25 M⊙的偏移；16O+16O反应使上边缘偏移约15 M⊙，但下边缘不变，因此可改变质量间隙的宽度。其他过程影响在≲10 M⊙水平。上边缘对时空分辨率变化稳健，表明当前模拟已可靠分辨。

Conclusion: PISN质量间隙上边缘存在显著的理论不确定性，主要由核反应率引起。与下边缘相比，上边缘受天体物理污染影响较小，可作为探测控制对不稳定性（pair instability）的核过程（nuclear processes）的直接探针，对引力波数据中高质量黑洞的识别与解释具有重要启示。

Abstract: Gravitational wave observations are beginning to probe the upper edge of the pair-instability supernova (PISN) black hole mass gap, a key prediction of stellar evolution. In this work, we quantify the sensitivity of this boundary to uncertainties in stellar evolution using a suite of simulations that vary inputs including nuclear reaction rates, mixing processes, and stellar winds. We find that the $^{12}{\rm C}(α,γ)^{16}{\rm O}$ reaction rate is the dominant source of uncertainty, shifting the upper edge by $ΔM\sim30\,{\rm M}_\odot$, with the triple-$α$ rate producing a comparable shift of $\sim25\,{\rm M}_\odot$. Notably, $^{16}{\rm O}+^{16}{\rm O}$ reactions shift the upper edge by $\sim15\,{\rm M}_\odot$ while leaving the lower edge unchanged, implying they can widen or narrow the mass gap. Other processes affect the location at the $\lesssim10\,{\rm M}_\odot$ level. In contrast to the lower edge, we find that the upper edge is robust to variations in spatial and temporal resolution, indicating that it is reliably resolved in current simulations. Our results demonstrate that the upper edge carries substantial theoretical uncertainty and, while comparatively less affected by astrophysical contamination than the lower edge, provides a direct probe of the nuclear processes governing pair instability. We discuss the implications for interpreting high-mass black hole detections in gravitational wave data.

</details>

### [5] [The On-Sky Performance of the LSST Camera CCD Array](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31806)
*Sean Patrick MacBride,Aaron Roodman,Stuart Marshall,Yousuke Utsumi,Kevin Fanning,John Banovetz,Theo Schutt,Alexander Broughton,Shuang Liang,Andrew P. Rasmussen,Pierre Antilogus,John Gregg Thayer,Homer Neal,Anthony S. Johnson,Pierre Astier,Seth W. Digel,Andrew Bradshaw,Johan Bregeon,James Chiang,Céline Combet,Guillaume Dargaud,Johnny H. Esteves,Marcelle Soares-Santos,Thibault Guillemin,Claire Juramy-Gilles,Craig S. Lage,Myriam Migliore,Daniel Polin,J. Anthony Tyson,Renee Nichols,Steven M. Ritz,Eli S. Rykoff,Adrian Shestakov,Adam Snyder,Max Turri,Duncan Wood,Travis Lange,Martin Nordby,Hannah Mary Margaret Pollek,Shawn Osier,Boyd Bowdish,Diane Hascall,Margaux Lopez,Scott P. Newbry,Juan Carlos Lazarte,Vincent Lee,Michael Silva,Dave Kiehl,Andrew Hau,Tom Nieland,Nico Linton,David Shelley,Yongqiang,Qiu,Mark Freytag,Stephen Cisneros,Chris Mendez,Stephen A. Tether,Alan M. Eisner,Dmitry Onoprienko,Owen Saxton,Kevin A. Reil,Vincent J. Riot,Justin Wolfe,Scott E. Winters,Brian J. Bauman,William Wahl,Paul O'Connor,Françoise Virieux,Alexandre Boucaud,Camille Parisel,Éric Aubourg,Eric Lagorio,Pierre Karst,Aurélien Marini,Didier Laporte,Francis Vezzu,Guillaume Daubard,Patrick Breugnon,Tim W. Bond,Eric Charles,Richard Dubois,Steven M. Kahn,Andrés A. Plazas Malagón,Rafe H. Schindler,Joanne Bogart,Hye Yun Park,Aurélien Barrau,Christopher Z. Waters,Merlin Fisher-Levine,Antoine Bernard,Mile Kusulja*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文描述了LSST相机CCD（电荷耦合器件）从2024年5月接收至运行首年的在轨性能，涵盖受电气短路与数模转换器故障影响的CCD修复、读出时序优化、焦平面主动清除安全机制的实施，以及首年运行期间观测到的传感器特征与整体性能表现。结果表明该相机能够执行覆盖整个南天的宽场、快速、深场光学成像巡天任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LSST相机焦平面包含189个科学CCD，是人类迄今建造的最大焦平面系统，作为Rubin天文台2026年启动的时域巡天（Legacy Survey of Space and Time）核心仪器，其CCD性能直接决定巡天质量与科学产出。

Method: 从CCD接收到在轨运行期间进行系统功能性测试，包括修复电气短路与数模转换器（analog-digital converter）故障、根据巡天策略变化调整读出时序（readout timing）优化，以及通过CCD主动清除机制（active clearing mechanism）增强焦平面安全保障。

Result: 成功恢复了受故障影响的多个CCD功能；实现了读出时序的动态优化；部署了主动清除机制以提升焦平面安全性；在首年运行中观测到了特定的传感器特征（sensor features）。

Conclusion: LSST相机CCD截至目前的运行表现证明其具备在Rubin天文台执行覆盖全天南半球天空的宽场、快速、深场光学成像巡天的能力。

Abstract: The focal plane of the LSST Camera contains 189 individual science CCDs, arranged into 21 raft tower modules, along with 4 wavefront and 8 guider CCDs located in 4 additional corner RTMs. Altogether, the LSST Camera CCDs compose the largest focal plane ever constructed. The LSST Camera is the primary instrument of Rubin Observatory, which will begin the Legacy Survey of Space and Time in 2026. In this paper, we describe the on-sky performance of the LSST Camera CCDs, from receipt at NSF/DOE Vera C. Rubin Observatory in May 2024 to on-sky observations during the first year of operations. We discuss the process to establish functionality of several CCDs which were affected by an electrical short and faulty analog-digital converter, optimizations of readout timing in response to changes in the survey strategy, and implementation of enhanced focal plane safety measures through an active clearing mechanism on the CCDs. Finally, we discuss sensor features observed on-sky, and global performance during the first year of operations. The operations to date of the LSST Camera CCDs have demonstrated the capability of performing a wide, fast, and deep optical imaging survey of the entire southern sky at the Rubin Observatory.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.SR'></div>

# astro-ph.SR [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Parameterizing the Standing Accretion Shock Instability for Inference with Galactic Supernova Neutrino Signals at IceCube](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30756)
*Dwaipayan Mukherjee,Mohamed Rameez,Basudeb Dasgupta*

Main category: astro-ph.SR

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对核塌缩超新星中驻留激波不稳定性（SASI）的参量化模型，利用中微子观测数据（特别是IceCube）实现对SASI参数的高精度统计推断，频率重建精度达亚百分比级别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核塌缩超新星模拟揭示了流体动力学不稳定时期——驻留激波不稳定性（standing accretion shock instability, SASI），该期间恒星物质发生准周期振荡。中微子携带了这一时期的信息，但缺乏有效的参数化方法来系统提取这些信息并实现统计推断。

Method: 提出一种SASI调制的参量化（parametrization）方案，用以描述其宽泛特征。通过分析中微子事件率数据，结合统计推断（statistical inference）方法，从观测数据中重建SASI参数。

Result: 以银河系超新星（Galactic supernovae）为基准示例，IceCube能够识别不稳定时期并重建其参数：SASI频率精度达亚百分比（sub-percent）水平，峰值时间精度达百分比（percent）水平，振幅和持续时间精度在百分之几到百分之十的水平。

Conclusion: 所提出的参量化方法有效支持从高统计量中微子事件率数据中推断SASI参数，IceCube具备精确识别和重建超新星不稳定时期特征的能力。

Abstract: Simulations of core-collapse supernovae have revealed an epoch of hydrodynamic instability in which the matter of the collapsing star undergoes quasi-periodic oscillations, known as the standing accretion shock instability (SASI). Neutrinos produced in the core of the star travel through this oscillating matter, and information about this epoch is encoded in their high-statistics event rate observable at neutrino observatories. We propose a parametrization of the SASI-modulation to study its broad features, enabling statistical inference of SASI parameters. For the benchmark Galactic supernovae considered, we show that IceCube can identify this epoch of instability and reconstruct its parameters with precision at the sub-percent level for the SASI frequency, percent level for the peak time, and a few to ten percent level for the amplitude and duration.

</details>

### [7] [Controllable Thouless Pumping Switching Dynamics of Gap Solitons Mediated by Finite Bogoliubov Excitations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31006)
*Tao Jiang,Jie Liu,Li-Chen Zhao*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 本文研究了非线性间隙孤子（gap solitons）的Thouless泵浦动力学（Thouless pumping dynamics），发现通过调制非线性参数和改变周期势相对相位的斜坡速率（ramping rate），可以诱导有限Bogoliubov激发，进而实现陈数切换（Chern number switching）。该机制为操控间隙孤子的拓扑泵浦输运提供了可行策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非线性间隙孤子（gap solitons）在Thouless泵浦过程中的动力学行为，并尝试通过调节非线性参数和周期势相对相位的斜坡速率（ramping rate）来实现拓扑陈数切换（Chern number switching）。

Method: 通过调制非线性参数和改变周期势之间相对相位的斜坡速率（ramping rate），研究近绝热斜坡（near-adiabatic ramping）条件下间隙孤子的泵浦动力学；分析孤子化学势（soliton chemical potential）与Bloch拓扑能带之间的对应关系。

Result: 近绝热斜坡条件下，间隙孤子会经历非线性不稳定性（nonlinear instabilities），并伴随有限Bogoliubov激发（finite Bogoliubov excitations）。这种有限激发导致孤子粒子损失（particle loss），进而引发孤子传播方向反转，标志着陈数切换（Chern number switching）的发生。

Conclusion: 有限Bogoliubov激发介导的孤子泵浦操控策略是可行的，对拓扑量子输运（topological quantum transport）和量子计算（quantum computing）应用具有潜在意义。

Abstract: We investigate the Thouless pumping dynamics of nonlinear gap solitons and attempt to realize topological Chern number switching by modulating nonlinear parameters and varying the ramping rate of the relative phase between periodic potentials. We find that gap solitons can undergo nonlinear instabilities accompanied by finite Bogoliubov excitations under near-adiabatic ramping. Such finite Bogoliubov excitations induce the particle loss of the solitons, leading to reversed propagation directions that signals the occurrence of Chern number switching with analyzing the correspondence between soliton chemical potential and Bloch topological energy band. Our findings offer a feasible strategy for manipulating the Thouless pump dynamics of gap solitons mediated by finite Bogoliubov excitations, with implications for topological quantum transport and quantum computing applications.

### [8] [Unresolved-Sideband Optomechanics with Hexagonal Boron Nitride: Induced Transparency, Gain, and Frequency Combs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31212)
*Francesco Fogliano,Thibaud Ruelle,David Jaeger,Martino Poggio*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文实验研究了非分辨边带极限（unresolved-sideband regime）下的光机诱导透明（OMIT），使用光纤法布里-珀罗微腔与悬浮六方氮化硼（hBN）鼓膜谐振器耦合的系统，观测到从透明谷到增益特征的转变，并生成了光机频率梳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光机诱导透明（OMIT）通常在分辨边带极限（resolved-sideband regime）下建模与研究，但许多紧凑微腔平台工作在非分辨边带极限（unresolved-sideband limit, κ ≫ Ωₘ），该领域的实验研究尚不充分。

Method: 采用可调谐光纤法布里-珀罗微腔（fiber-based Fabry-Perot microcavity）与悬浮六方氮化硼（hBN）鼓膜谐振器耦合，构建膜片-腔中间（membrane-in-the-middle）几何结构；通过测量OMIT光谱随泵浦功率和腔失谐的变化，并利用完整线性化光机械响应进行定量拟合。

Result: 系统实现了大单光子耦合率（g₀/2π ∼ 180 kHz），观测到从透明谷到增益特征（gain feature）的转变；标准旋波近似（rotating-wave approximation）在该极限下失效，而非线性驱动生成了光机械频率梳（optomechanical frequency combs）。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了hBN光纤腔作为非分辨边带光力学、非线性动力学及混合器件集成的多功能架构。

Abstract: Optomechanically induced transparency (OMIT) is usually modeled and studied in the resolved-sideband regime, but many compact microcavity platforms operate in the unresolved-sideband limit $(κ\gg Ω_m)$. Here we investigate OMIT in this regime using a tunable fiber-based Fabry-Perot microcavity coupled to a suspended hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) drum resonator in a membrane-in-the-middle geometry. The system achieves a large single-photon coupling rate of $g_0/2π\sim 180$ kHz and exhibits strong radiation-pressure backaction. By measuring OMIT spectra as a function of pump power and cavity detuning, we observe a crossover from a transparency-like dip to a gain feature in the reflected response. These maps are quantitatively reproduced by the full linearized optomechanical response, demonstrating the breakdown of the standard rotating-wave approximation used in the resolved-sideband limit. Finally, we drive the system into a nonlinear regime to generate optomechanical frequency combs. These results establish hBN fiber-cavities as a versatile architecture for unresolved-sideband optomechanics, nonlinear dynamics, and hybrid device integration.

Conclusion: 该工作为基于简单活性材料的中红外等离激元调制器和混频器（mixer）提供了可行的实现路径，有助于推动8–12 μm大气窗口内的自由空间光通信应用。

Abstract: We present a free-space plasmonic modulator based on a single heavily-doped semiconductor layer. We investigate its ability to modulate both the linear and nonlinear response at mid-infrared frequencies slightly below the plasma frequency of the semiconductor. We demonstrate electric control of the linear transmittance and reflectance, and of the efficiency of third-harmonic generation with a field-effect gate structure. We discuss further performance optimization of the device in terms of modulation speed and depth towards a fast modulator with very simple active material requirements. Our results establish a viable route toward practical plasmonic modulators and mixers operating in the mid-infrared atmospheric window available for free-space communications at wavelengths between 8 and 12 um.

### [10] [Stationary covariance spectra of discrete-time non-normal random recurrent dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31944)
*Jacob A. Zavatone-Veth*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文利用自由概率（free-probability）方法，为具有随机非正态高斯权重的离散时间动力学系统，形式化推导了稳态协方差谱（stationary covariance spectrum）矩母函数的封闭泛函方程，并分析了临界区域的尾特征值行为；而在连续时间情形下，该方法导致无穷维的Schwinger-Dyson方程而非封闭标量方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主成分分析（PCA）广泛用于刻画循环神经网络（recurrent neural networks）动力学结构，但对于随机非正态（non-normal）动力学的稳态协方差谱（stationary covariance spectrum）仍缺乏完整理解。

Method: 采用自由概率（free-probability）方法，形式推导离散时间动力学中随机非正态高斯权重下稳态协方差谱矩母函数的封闭泛函方程；对连续时间情形应用相同方法。

Result: 离散时间情形下得到了矩母函数的封闭泛函方程，可分析临界区域尾特征值（tail eigenvalues）行为；连续时间情形则得到无穷维Schwinger-Dyson方程层级，而非封闭标量方程。

Conclusion: 这些结果对于将非正态动力学模型与神经数据进行比较具有参考意义，但连续时间情形下自由概率方法无法直接得到封闭解。

Abstract: Principal component analysis is widely used to characterize structure in the dynamics of recurrent neural networks. For stationary noise-driven dynamics, the distribution of variance among the principal components is determined by the spectrum of the stationary covariance matrix. While the spectral properties of this matrix are well-understood for linear networks with normal synaptic weight matrices, our understanding of the stationary covariance spectrum for random non-normal dynamics remains incomplete. In this note, we use a free-probability approach to formally derive a closed functional equation for the moment generating function of the limiting stationary covariance spectrum of discrete-time dynamics with random non-normal Gaussian weights. This characterization allows us to analyze the behavior of tail eigenvalues in the critical regime. In contrast, applying the same approach to the analogous continuous-time dynamics leads to an infinite hierarchy of Schwinger-Dyson equations, rather than a closed scalar equation. We conclude with some comments regarding the relevance of these results to comparisons of models of non-normal dynamics to neural data.

### [11] [Ollivier-Ricci Curvature for Causal Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04910)
*Joe Barton,Samuël Borza,Jona Röhrig*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文借助洛伦兹最优输运（Lorentzian optimal transport），为因果集（causal sets）引入了一种新的 Ollivier–Ricci 曲率概念，并通过数值实验在闵可夫斯基、德西特和反德西特空间中恢复了预期的常曲率特征，证明该构造能从序关系数据中捕捉类时 Ricci 曲率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在因果集这一离散时空离散化框架中，缺乏一种能够从序关系（order-theoretic data）内在定义 Ricci 曲率的方法。本文旨在通过洛伦兹最优输运工具，为因果集建立一种类时 Ricci 曲率的 mesoscopic 定义。

Method: 利用洛伦兹最优输运和新的洛伦兹渐近公式（该公式可从临近因果钻石（causal diamonds）上概率测度之间的输运距离恢复类时 Ricci 曲率），将上述连续公式离散化，沿最大链（maximal chains）定义基于因果钻石上概率测度的介观 Ricci 曲率。研究了包括 idle 型和 Lin–Lu–Yau 型曲率在内的多种变体，并通过高密度泊松喷洒（Poisson sprinkling）数值实验对闵可夫斯基、de Sitter 和 anti-de Sitter 空间进行验证。

Result: 证明了局部到全局的传播结果（local-to-global propagation results）以及类时 Bonnet–Myers 定理；对一系列显式因果集进行了曲率计算；高密度泊松喷洒数值实验成功恢复了闵可夫斯基、de Sitter 和 anti-de Sitter 空间预期的常曲率特征。

Conclusion: 该构造能够从因果集的纯序关系数据中捕捉类时 Ricci 曲率，为因果集几何的曲率研究提供了新的理论工具和数值验证。

Abstract: We introduce a novel notion of Ollivier--Ricci curvature for causal sets using Lorentzian optimal transport. The construction is motivated by a new Lorentzian asymptotic formula of independent interest, which recovers timelike Ricci curvature, up to higher-order terms, from the transport distance between probability measures on nearby causal diamonds. Passing to the discrete setting, this leads to a mesoscopic notion of Ricci curvature defined along maximal chains and built from probability measures on causal diamonds. We study several variants, including idle and Lin--Lu--Yau type curvatures, prove local-to-global propagation results and timelike Bonnet--Myers theorems, and compute the curvature for a range of explicit causal sets. We design high-density Poisson sprinkling numerical experiments recovering the expected constant-curvature signatures of Minkowski, de Sitter, and anti-de Sitter space. These results provide evidence that the construction captures timelike Ricci curvature from order-theoretic data.

</details>


### [12] [Four-dimensional electrostatic system with harmonic (anti-)self-dual Weyl tensor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30878)
*Robson Lousa*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了作为带有宇宙学常数的静态爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦时空空间因子的四维静电系统。在电场与时间延迟函数梯度处处共线的假设下，证明了Weyl张量的(反)自对偶分量的调和性对底层几何施加了强刚性，导致流形局部共形平坦并具有局部翘曲积结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究带有宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）的静态爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦（Einstein–Maxwell）时空中，由空间因子导出的四维静电系统（electrostatic system）的几何约束条件，特别是Weyl张量分量调和性对底层几何结构的刚性影响。

Method: 假设电场与时间延迟函数（lapse function）梯度处处共线，通过分析Weyl张量（Weyl tensor）的(反)自对偶（(anti-)self-dual）分量的调和性（harmonicity），推导其对几何性质的约束条件，包括Ricci张量的本征向量关系和水平集的几何特性。

Result: 证明时间延迟函数的梯度是Ricci张量（Ricci tensor）的本征向量（eigenvector），且其正则水平集（regular level sets）为全脐（totally umbilic）且具有常平均曲率（constant mean curvature）的子流形。进一步得出该流形是局部共形平坦（locally conformally flat）的，并允许一维基和三维常曲率纤维的局部翘曲积（warped product）结构。

Conclusion: 在给定电场与时间延迟函数梯度共线的条件下，Weyl张量的(反)自对偶分量的调和性对底层几何施加了强刚性约束，将系统严格限定为局部共形平坦的翘曲积几何结构。

Abstract: We investigate four-dimensional electrostatic systems arising as spatial factors of static Einstein--Maxwell spacetimes with cosmological constant. Assuming that the electric field is everywhere collinear with the gradient of the lapse function, we prove that the harmonicity of one of the (anti-)self-dual components of the Weyl tensor imposes strong rigidity on the underlying geometry. More precisely, we show that the gradient of the lapse function is an eigenvector of the Ricci tensor and that the regular level sets of the lapse function are totally umbilic with constant mean curvature. As a consequence, the manifold is locally conformally flat and admits a local warped product structure with one-dimensional base and three-dimensional fiber of constant curvature.

### [13] [Eigenstate Transitions, Duality, and Anomalous Diffusion in a Quasiperiodic Qi-Wu-Zhang Chern Insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31604)
*Tengming Lou,Haiyang Wang,Haijiao Ji,Haiwen Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究磁性Qi-Wu-Zhang Chern绝缘体模型，发现当准周期调制增强时，系统可经历从扩展相到临界相的转变，并在特定参数范围内保持临界态（无局域化），通过平均逆参与率（IPR）的有限尺寸标度、幺正变换和Lyapunov指数分析解释了这一相图，揭示了磁性Chern绝缘体是实现稳健临界性与反常量子输运的自然平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准周期系统通常在准周期调制增强时经历扩展态、临界态与局域态之间的过渡。本文旨在探索是否存在一种系统能够在整个能谱范围内避免局域化，并揭示其背后的物理机制。

Method: 将二维磁性Qi-Wu-Zhang Chern绝缘体模型在无理磁通下约化为一维自旋子准周期链，通过调节跃迁振幅t_x 控制矩阵在位调制；采用平均逆参与率的有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling of average inverse participation ratio）定量刻画临界态，并利用对偶变换（dual transformation）将t_x与t_y互换，结合Lyapunov指数（Lyapunov exponent）分析解释相图，最后通过波包动力学（wave-packet dynamics）区分弹道输运、反常扩散与局域化等不同输运行为。

Result: 当|m+2|>t_y时，增大t_x产生常规的扩展-临界-局域化序列，临界线位于t_x=t_y；当|m+2|≤t_y时，系统在t_x=|m+2|处从扩展相转变为临界相，并在更强的准周期调制下保持临界态，不发生局域化。在该持久临界区（persistent critical regime）内，平均逆参与率标度行为为 {\overline{\mathrm{IPR}}}\sim q^{-α}，其中0<α<1。

Conclusion: 本文证明磁性Chern绝缘体模型能够实现一种无局域化的全谱过渡，并识别出该体系作为研究稳健临界性与反常量子输运的自然平台。结果为准周期系统中临界相的鲁棒性及反常量子动力学提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Quasiperiodic systems usually interpolate between extended, critical, and localized states as the quasiperiodic modulation is increased. Here we show that the magnetic Qi-Wu-Zhang Chern-insulator model realizes a distinct full-spectrum transition in which localization is avoided. For an irrational magnetic flux, the two-dimensional model reduces to a spinor quasiperiodic chain with a matrix onsite modulation controlled by the hopping amplitude $t_x$. When $|m+2|>t_y$, increasing $t_x$ produces the conventional extended-critical-localized sequence with a critical line at $t_x=t_y$. In contrast, when $|m+2|\le t_y$, the system changes from an extended phase to a critical phase at $t_x=|m+2|$ and remains critical even for stronger quasiperiodic modulation. Finite-size scaling of the average inverse participation ratio gives $\overline{\mathrm{IPR}}\sim q^{-α}$ with $0<α<1$ throughout this persistent critical regime. A dual transformation exchanging $t_x$ and $t_y$, together with a Lyapunov-exponent analysis, explains the phase diagram. Wave-packet dynamics further distinguish ballistic, anomalous-diffusive, and localized regimes. These results identify magnetic Chern-insulator systems as a natural platform for robust criticality and anomalous quantum transport.

</details>


### [14] [Activated dynamics in the quantum random field Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31663)
*Ivan Balog,Lovro Šaravanja,Andrei A. Fedorenko*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文利用非微扰泛函重整化群（NP-FRG）研究了量子随机场伊辛模型（quantum random-field Ising model）的临界动力学，揭示了零温下经典随机场伊辛模型的固定点如何通过激活动力学（activated dynamics）控制量子弛豫行为，并建立了弛豫时间对数标度与静态临界指数及动力学核指数σ之间的定量关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子随机场伊辛模型中的动力学临界行为尚未被充分理解，特别是零温下动力学核的流动存在有限尺度发散和表观局域化（apparent localization）问题，亟需一种非微扰的理论框架来正确描述其临界动力学。

Method: 采用非微扰泛函重整化群（NP-FRG）方法，计算了动力学核$F_k(ω)$在完整松原频率（Matsubara frequency）依赖下的重整化群流，并选用与运行尺度（running scale）适配的调节子（regulator）以避免发散。

Result: 零温下动力学呈现激活形式，弛豫时间满足$\ln τ \sim ξ^Ψ$，其中指数$Ψ$由静态随机场伊辛模型（RFIM）的临界指数和动力学核指数$σ$共同决定。有限温度下则交叉到经典热激活标度行为。

Conclusion: 该结果定量实现了先前对量子随机场模型提出的启发式激活场景（heuristic activation scenario），并为分析其他具有类似局域化奇异性倾向的无序量子系统（disordered quantum systems）的动力学建立了框架。

Abstract: We study the critical dynamics of the quantum random-field Ising model using the nonperturbative functional renormalization group (NP-FRG). The static critical behavior is found to be controlled by the zero-temperature fixed point of the classical random-field Ising model, where both thermal and quantum fluctuations are dangerously irrelevant. Considering a family of quantum dynamical universality classes defined by a bare dynamical kernel $F_Λ(ω)\sim |ω|^σ$, we show how this fluctuationless fixed point nevertheless controls the quantum dynamics by computing the full Matsubara-frequency dependence of the running dynamical kernel $F_k(ω)$. This is essential at zero temperature: a naive treatment of the dynamical kernel flow leads to a divergence at a finite length scale, resulting in apparent localization. In contrast, keeping the full frequency dependence of the dynamical kernel and choosing a regulator adapted to its running scale yields a controlled flow. The resulting dynamics is of activated form, with a relaxation time given by $\ln τ\sim ξ^Ψ$. The exponent $Ψ$ is determined by the static RFIM fixed-point exponents and by $σ$. At finite temperature, the flow crosses over to the classical thermally activated scaling of the random-field Ising model. These results provide a quantitative field-theoretic realization of the heuristic activation scenario proposed earlier for the quantum random-field model and establish a framework for analyzing the dynamics of other disordered quantum systems that may exhibit similar tentative localization-like singularities.

</details>

### [15] [Search for physics beyond the standard model in four and three top quark production events using proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30862)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文基于CMS探测器在LHC上收集的13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据（积分亮度138 fb⁻¹），通过四顶夸克和三顶夸克产生事件寻找超出标准模型的新物理。在标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）框架下约束了六个Wilson系数，排除了质量在400 GeV到1.6 TeV之间的窄宽度顶夸克亲和（topphilic）重共振态，并提取了包含C宇称偶（CP-even）和奇（CP-odd）贡献的顶夸克Yukawa耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超出标准模型（standard model）的新物理搜索是当前高能物理的核心问题之一。顶夸克（top quark）由于质量最大，与希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）的耦合最强，是探测新物理的敏感探针。多顶夸克产生过程（如四顶夸克和三顶夸克产生）为约束顶夸克相关的新相互作用提供了独特窗口。

Method: 利用CMS探测器记录的13 TeV质子-质子（proton-proton）对撞数据，积分亮度为138 fb⁻¹。选取含有两个同号轻子、三个或四个轻子（电子或缪子）的事例。在标准模型有效场论（Standard Model Effective Field Theory, SMEFT）框架下，对修改第三代夸克间或顶夸克与希格斯玻色子相互作用的六个Wilson系数进行约束。此外，还搜索了窄宽度顶夸克亲和重共振态（topphilic heavy resonances），并提取了包含CP-偶和CP-奇贡献的顶夸克Yukawa耦合（top quark Yukawa coupling）。

Result: 给出了六个SMEFT Wilson系数的约束结果。排除了自旋和颜色状态不同的窄宽度顶夸克亲和重共振态，排除质量范围在400 GeV到1.6 TeV之间。提取了顶夸克Yukawa耦合，同时考虑了CP-偶和CP-奇两种贡献。

Conclusion: 该研究利用多顶夸克产生过程对超出标准模型的新物理给出了有效场论框架下的全面约束，包括Wilson系数、重共振态排除以及顶夸克Yukawa耦合的提取。结果对理解顶夸克与希格斯玻色子的相互作用以及寻找第三代夸克相关的新物理具有重要意义。

Abstract: A search for physics beyond the standard model using four and three top quark production events is reported. The analyzed proton-proton collision data were recorded at 13 TeV with the CMS detector at the CERN LHC in 2016$-$2018 and correspond to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. Events with two same-sign, three, or four leptons (electrons and/or muons) are selected. Constraints on six Wilson coefficients that modify interactions between four third-generation quarks or between top quarks and the Higgs boson in the standard model effective field theory framework are derived. The data are further used to exclude narrow topphilic heavy resonances in the mass ranges between 400 GeV and 1.6 TeV depending on their spin and color states. Finally, the top quark Yukawa coupling is extracted, considering both $CP$-even and $CP$-odd contributions.

</details>


### [16] [Measurement of $J/ψ$-jet correlations in $pp$ and Pb+Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\text{NN}}}=5.02$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31375)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文利用ATLAS探测器在5.02 TeV的Pb+Pb和质子-质子（pp）碰撞中测量J/ψ介子的产额，通过区分孤立与非孤立J/ψ（基于反kt喷注（anti-kt jet）匹配），以及直接（prompt）与非直接（non-prompt）产生，系统研究了粲偶素（charmonium）产生与喷注活动（jet activity）的关联，为粲偶素产生机制及其在夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）中的介质抑制提供了新约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重离子碰撞中粲偶素（charmonia，c\bar{c}夸克束缚态）的产额因与夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）相互作用而显著压低，理解该压低机制需详细认识粲偶素产生过程，而量化粲偶素产生与喷注活动（jet activity）的关联是约束产生机制的关键。

Method: 在双缪子（dimuon）衰变道测量J/ψ介子产生，区分孤立（isolated）与非孤立（non-isolated）J/ψ以及直接（prompt）与非直接（non-prompt）产生；非孤立J/ψ通过匹配J/ψ候选者到反kt喷注（anti-kt jets，R=0.2，pT>20 GeV）定义，并扣除J/ψ信号以量化伴随喷注活动。

Result: 报道了Pb+Pb中的J/ψ产额、pp中的截面以及核修正因子（nuclear modification factor），覆盖非孤立、孤立和 inclusive J/ψ，最高至pT=60 GeV；同时给出了孤立分数（isolated fractions）和非直接分数（non-prompt fractions）。观察到强J/ψ压低持续至最高测量pT，且非孤立、孤立与 inclusive J/ψ之间存在差异。

Conclusion: 这些结果为粲偶素产生机制及其在介质中的抑制提供了新的实验约束。

Abstract: Yields of charmonia, bound states of $c\bar{c}$ quarks, are observed to be strongly suppressed in heavy-ion collisions relative to proton-proton collisions as a result of their interaction with the quark-gluon plasma produced in such collisions. Understanding the mechanisms responsible for this suppression requires a detailed understanding of charmonium production. To constrain the production mechanisms, it is essential to quantify how charmonium production correlates with jet activity. Measurements of $J/ψ$ production in the dimuon decay channel are presented for inclusive $J/ψ$ mesons and for $J/ψ$ mesons that are either isolated or not isolated from jets, separately for prompt and non-prompt production. Non-isolated $J/ψ$ mesons are defined by matching $J/ψ$ candidates to anti-$k_t$ jets with $R=0.2$ and $p_\mathrm{T}>20$ GeV, reconstructed without signal from the $J/ψ$ meson, allowing the quantification of jet activity accompanying $J/ψ$ production. The analysis uses Pb+Pb and $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\text{NN}}}=5.02$ TeV recorded by the ATLAS experiment at the LHC, corresponding to integrated luminosities of 1.82 nb$^{-1}$ and 0.26 fb$^{-1}$, respectively. The $J/ψ$ yields in Pb+Pb, cross sections in $pp$, and nuclear modification factors are presented for non-isolated, isolated, and inclusive $J/ψ$ up to $p_\mathrm{T}=60$ GeV. Isolated fractions and non-prompt fractions are reported in both $pp$ and Pb+Pb collisions. Strong $J/ψ$ suppression is observed to persist up to the highest measured $p_\mathrm{T}$ values, with differences observed between non-isolated, isolated, and inclusive $J/ψ$. These results provide new constraints on charmonium production mechanisms and their in-medium suppression.

</details>

### [17] [Explaining Machine Learning and Memorization with Statistical Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31110)
*Robin Theriault*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本论文旨在利用统计力学（statistical mechanics）的数学工具，从理论上理解人工神经网络（NN）与机器学习（ML），重点关注对抗性攻击（adversarial attacks）和隐式低维学习（implicitly low-dimensional learning），并通过研究密集联想记忆（DAM）和受限玻尔兹曼机（RBM）这两类模型来探讨学习与记忆的不同程度。 


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人工神经网络与机器学习算法在理论上缺乏深入理解，这阻碍了其潜力的充分挖掘和弱点的克服：例如，训练中权重的低维子空间（low-dimensional subspace）学习结构未被有效利用，且训练好的网络易受对抗性攻击（adversarial attacks）干扰，其理论基础尚不清晰。

Method: 采用统计力学（statistical mechanics）中的数学工具，分析两类模型——密集联想记忆（dense associative memory, DAM）与受限玻尔兹曼机（restricted Boltzmann machine, RBM）——在不同程度的学习与记忆下拟合数据的方式，并探究这些模型不同版本之间的联系以提升分析效率。

Result: 论文通过统计力学工具揭示了DAM与RBM两类模型在拟合数据时学习与记忆的不同程度，并建立了不同版本模型之间的有用联系，从而使得理论分析更为高效。

Conclusion: 本论文增进了对神经网络与机器学习在对抗性攻击和隐式低维学习方面的理论理解，证明了统计力学方法在揭示模型内部机制方面的有效性。

Abstract: Artificial neural networks (NNs) and machine learning (ML) algorithms are poorly understood from a theoretical perspective, which makes it difficult to fully realize their potential and overcome their weaknesses. For instance, ML algorithms train NN weights by moving them along a low-dimensional subspace of their allowed values, but this implicitly low-dimensional learning structure is not properly exploited to improve training because its nature is not well understood. Moreover, trained NNs are easily confused by pervasive adversarial attacks whose theoretical underpinnings are still unclear. This thesis aims to improve our theoretical understanding of NNs and ML, with a particular focus on adversarial attacks and implicitly low-dimensional learning. For this purpose, we use mathematical tools from statistical mechanics to study different types of NNs and ways in which they can fit the data. In particular, we study two classes of models that fit the data with various degrees of learning and memorization: dense associative memory (DAM) and restricted Boltzmann machines (RBM). In the process, we investigate connections between different versions of these models that are useful to make analytical investigations more efficient.

</details>

### [18] [Invasion with size-dependent dispersion range](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31942)
*Ulysse Marquis*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 本文通过引入种群规模依赖性扩散（size-dependent dispersal）扩展了经典聚并菌落模型（coalescing colony model），推导出广义动力学方程并绘制生长相图，发现主菌落呈现线性扩张、幂律增长、指数增长和有限时间爆炸四种不同标度行为。物理模型模拟表明该理论能正确预测周长标度，但无法预测体积标度，且在高扩散指数下预测的卫星种群比例与模拟结果存在显著偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典聚并菌落模型假设扩散距离与入侵种群规模无关，然而在生物入侵、转移性肿瘤生长和城市扩张等实际场景中，种群规模可能直接调控扩散能力。本研究旨在放松这一假设，考察种群规模依赖性扩散如何从根本上改变入侵动力学。

Method: 作者将扩散距离设为与主菌落线性尺寸 r 的幂律关系 r^μ（0 ≤ μ ≤ 1），推导出该扩展模型的广义动力学方程，并采用前置序贡献（leading order contribution）方法绘制生长相图。同时构建空间显式物理模型进行数值模拟，与理论预测进行比较。

Result: 主菌落随 μ 取值呈现线性扩张、幂律生长、指数增长和有限时间爆炸四种标度行为。理论能正确预测菌落周长的标度，但无法预测体积的标度，后者偏差源于主菌落形态的有效圆对称性破缺（effective breakdown of circular symmetry）。聚并菌落模型预测种群占比在 μ<1 时呈幂律衰减至 0，在 μ=1 时维持宏观卫星种群；物理模型模拟则在 μ>μ^*≈0.7 时发现理论未能捕获的持续卫星种群。

Conclusion: 种群规模与扩散距离的耦合从根本上改变了入侵动力学的标度行为。聚并菌落框架在高扩散指数下丢失了形态对称性和卫星种群的关键细节，这一发现对生物入侵、转移性肿瘤和城市扩张等跨尺度复杂系统具重要启示。

Abstract: The coalescing colony model provides a minimal framework for biological invasions with long-range dispersion. In its standard formulation, the dispersion range is assumed independent of the size of the invading population. Here, we relax this assumption and consider size-dependent dispersal: a main colony of linear size $r$ emits secondary colonies at distance $r^μ$, with $0 \leq μ\leq 1$. We derive the generalized dynamical equations for this extended model and map out the growth phase diagram for the leading order contribution. Depending on $μ$, the main colony exhibits distinct regimes: linear expansion, power-law growth, exponential regime and finite-time blow-up. We confront these theoretical predictions with a spatially explicit physical model. While the coalescing colony approach correctly captures the scaling of the perimeter, it fails to predict the scaling of the volume. We trace this discrepancy to an effective breakdown of circular symmetry in the morphology of the main colony. Finally, we quantify temporal evolution of the population fraction residing outside of the main colony. The coalescing colony model predicts its decay to~$0$ like a power-law when~$μ<1$, and a macroscopic amount of the population remains in the secondary colonies at~$μ=1$. Simulations of the physical model reveal a persistent satellite population not captured by the theory at~$μ>μ^*\approx 0.7$. Broadly, our findings highlight how coupling dispersal range to population size fundamentally alters invasion dynamics, with implications for biological invasions, metastatic growth, and urban expansion.

</details>

### [19] [Galaxy Power Spectrum at Two-Loop Order: Implications for Weak Lensing Surveys and New Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30713)
*Mikhail M. Ivanov*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在微扰论有效场论（EFT）框架下计算了宇宙学星系功率谱（galaxy power spectrum）至双圈阶（two-loop order），推导了五阶偏倚算符及重正化条件，与N体模拟达到千分之一精度吻合，并将质量涨落振幅σ₈的误差棒较单圈模型压缩约40%，有望显著提升Euclid、LSST等巡天数据分析的统计精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有宇宙学大尺度结构（large-scale structure）分析多停留在一圈阶（one-loop order），但更高阶修正对充分利用下一代巡天数据（如Euclid、LSST、Roman）中更高波数（k）区间的信息、实现更精确的宇宙学参数约束至关重要，同时也能探测超出标准模型的新物理（如超轻轴子暗物质）。

Method: 在有效场论（EFT）框架下，利用宇宙学微扰论（cosmological perturbation theory）计算至双圈阶的星系功率谱；推导五阶偏倚算符（galaxy bias operators）并给出双圈重正化条件；采用与CLASS-PT代码一致的重正化方案；使用时间切片微扰论（time-sliced perturbation theory）实现红外重求和（IR resummation）；识别冗余算符以确定独立的EFT参数。

Result: 双圈星系功率谱需要每类星系样本额外引入21个EFT参数；与PT Challenge N体模拟在z=0.61的对比显示，在k≤0.85 h Mpc⁻¹范围内一致性达到千分之一（per mille）量级；在保守先验下，双圈模型对σ₈的测量无偏且误差棒比线性理论模型窄三倍，较单圈模型改善约40%。

Conclusion: 双圈EFT分析能够显著提升星系成团性与星系-透镜两点关联函数（2×2 pt）的统计约束力，对Euclid、LSST、Roman等巡天项目具有重要应用前景；同时可在波数0.4–0.8 h Mpc⁻¹区间探测修改物质功率谱形状的新物理，例如质量mₐ∼10⁻²⁴ eV的超轻轴子暗物质子组分。

Abstract: We compute the galaxy power spectrum at two-loop order in cosmological perturbation theory (effective field theory, EFT). We derive galaxy bias operators through the fifth order and obtain two-loop renormalization conditions for the their bias coefficients. We compute the two-loop integrals using a renormalization scheme consistent with the CLASS-PT code, allowing for an easy interface of our new computations with standard tools used in the one-loop galaxy power spectrum and bispectrum analyses. We also derive the relevant higher-derivative and stochastic contributions, and implement IR resummation using time-sliced perturbation theory. Having identified the redundant operators, we find that the two-loop galaxy power spectrum requires 21 additional EFT parameters per galaxy sample. We compare our computation with the galaxy-galaxy and galaxy-matter power spectra from the PT Challenge N-body simulation at $z=0.61$ and find a per mille-level agreement up to $k=0.85~h$Mpc$^{-1}$. We show that even with conservative priors on all EFT parameters, the two-loop model produces an unbiased measurement of the mass fluctuation amplitude $σ_8$ with three times narrower error-bars than the linear theory model. The improvement over the one-loop model is $\simeq 40\%$. This suggests significant gains in the two-loop EFT analyses of galaxy clustering and galaxy--lensing two-point functions ($2\times2$ pt) from CMB lensing maps and imaging surveys like Euclid, LSST, and Roman. In addition, our two-loop computation offers a probe of new physics scenarios that modify the shape of the matter power spectrum at wavenumbers $(0.4-0.8)~h$Mpc$^{-1}$ such as the presence of ultra-light axion dark matter sub-components with masses $m_a\sim 10^{-24}$ eV.

</details>


### [20] [Numerical polology: towards next-generation model-building for cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30785)
*Will Barker,Will Handley,Michael Hobson,Anthony Lasenby,Carlo Marzo,Alessandro Santoni,Leonardo Torcellini*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种数值极学（polology）框架，用于自动发现具有一致相互作用的鬼场自由（ghost-free）微扰理论模型，并通过采样耦合空间生成理论模型先验，在高达三阶的张量场论中测试该方法，随后展示了该框架在黑洞超辐射、动力学暗能量和引力波观测三个方向上的约束流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗扇区（dark sector）不必局限于简单的场内容；许多紫外（ultraviolet）完备理论暗示了比标量-张量或暗光子模型远为丰富的物理图像，因此需要一种系统性的方法来自动发现并筛选具有一致相互作用的理论模型。

Method: 该方法基于极学（polology），即对传播子极点（propagator poles）的研究——这些极点对应任意理论中的粒子态。研究团队构建了一个数值框架，通过对耦合空间（coupling space）进行采样来产生理论模型先验（theoretical model priors），从而发现微扰（perturbative）且无鬼场（ghost-free）的模型。该方法在高达三阶的张量场论（tensor field theories）上进行了测试。

Result: 该框架成功在高达三阶的张量场论上得到验证，并展示了其在三个观测约束流程中的应用：黑洞超辐射（black hole superradiance）案例M33 X-7、动力学暗能量（dynamical dark energy）结合DESI DR2、Pantheon和SH0ES数据、以及引力波（gravitational waves）数据集GWTC-3。

Conclusion: 该数值极学框架提供了一种系统性的方法来探索暗扇区的丰富理论可能性，能够自动生成无鬼场且具有一致相互作用的模型先验，并可对接多种观测数据的约束管道，从而弥合紫外完备理论与低能观测之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: The dark sector need not be restricted to simple field content. Indeed, simple bosonic configurations, such as scalar-tensor or dark photon models, contrast with the much richer picture painted by many ultraviolet scenarios. Polology is the study of propagator poles, which correspond to particle states in any given theory. We outline a numerical polology framework for discovering perturbative, ghost-free models with consistent interactions, which produces theoretical model priors by sampling the coupling space. The method is tested on tensor field theories of up to rank three. Subsequent observational constraint pipelines are illustrated for black hole superradiance (M33 X-7), dynamical dark energy (DESI DR2, Pantheon and SH0ES) and gravitational waves (GWTC-3).

</details>


### [21] [Galaxy bias renormalization: Two-loop Power Spectrum, One-loop Trispectrum and Bispectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31280)
*Thomas Bakx,Mathias Garny,Henrique Rubira,Zvonimir Vlah*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在实空间中对五阶重整化星系偏袒（fifth-order renormalized galaxy bias）在单圈和双圈层次上给出了完整处理，包括次领头阶的梯度修正，并提供了双圈功率谱、单圈双谱和三谱的完整计算，以及联合建模的完全重整化框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有星系偏袒模型在高阶统计量（如双谱、三谱）和更高圈层次上缺乏完整的重整化处理，尤其是梯度修正和随机重整化效应尚未被系统纳入。

Method: 采用算符乘积展开（operator product expansion）处理两个、三个或四个算符在重合点处的随机重整化，在梯度领头阶引入随机抵消项；通过求解重整化群方程（renormalization group equations）处理高阶梯度偏袒系数的尺度依赖；所有圈积分的紫外发散均被相应的抵消项吸收。

Result: 验证了所有圈积分的紫外极限被抵消项完全吸收；求解重整化群方程后发现高阶梯度偏袒系数具有显著的尺度依赖（scale-dependence）；由于重整化方案在算符层次显式进行，结果可自然推广到更高N点函数、更高圈序和场级分析。

Conclusion: 本文构建了一个完整的实空间五阶重整化偏袒框架，实现了双圈功率谱及单圈双谱、三谱的联合建模，并表明该框架具有向更高阶统计量和场级分析的可扩展性。

Abstract: We present a complete treatment of fifth-order renormalized galaxy bias at the one- and two-loop level in real space, including gradient corrections to deterministic bias operators at next-to-leading order. We then provide a complete computation of the two-loop power spectrum as well as the one-loop bispectrum and trispectrum of biased tracers, and demonstrate how to jointly model these statistics in a fully renormalized framework. These statistics also require stochastic renormalization of products of two, three or four operators at coincidence, which we include at leading order in gradients by means of an operator product expansion. We verify that all UV limits of loop integrals are absorbed by the counterterms we consider. Upon solving the resulting renormalization group equations, we find a pronounced scale-dependence of higher-gradient bias coefficients. Since our renormalization prescription is performed manifestly at the operator level, our results can also easily be extended to higher $N$-point functions, higher loop orders and field-level analyses.

</details>


### [22] [Cosmological Viability of Exponential Infrared $f(T)$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31324)
*Mahmoud Hashim,Eleonora Di Valentino,Jackson Levi Said,Waleed El Hanafy*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用当前宇宙学观测数据检验指数型红外f(T)遥平行引力（exponential infrared f(T) teleparallel gravity）的宇宙学可行性。该理论通过扭转修正实现晚期宇宙加速膨胀，不增加六参数空间，但两个解分支中仅有模型I可部分缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension），而模型II因背景与扰动观测的联合约束被决定性排除，表明扰动观测量（perturbation observables）对遥平行引力提供了超出背景膨胀历史的严格互补检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验指数型红外f(T)遥平行引力作为ΛCDM替代模型的宇宙学可行性，特别关注其能否缓解当前的宇宙学张力（如哈勃张力），并揭示背景与扰动观测对这类修正引力模型的联合约束能力。

Method: 使用Planck、ACT和SPT的宇宙微波背景（CMB）观测数据，结合DESI重子声学振荡（BAO）数据和Pantheon+ Ia型超新星数据，对两个解分支（模型I与模型II）进行参数约束与统计分析。

Result: 模型I在缓解哈勃张力方面优于ΛCDM，但被联合数据集在统计上不偏好；模型II被决定性排除。模型II的失败源于背景约束（晚期距离测量）与扰动约束之间的相互作用，导致参数Ω_m h²、A_s、n_s、τ_reio发生关联偏移，从而恶化对CMB阻尼尾部的拟合，并使光学深度推至非物理值。

Conclusion: 扰动观测量对遥平行引力提供了超出背景膨胀历史的严格且互补的检验；仅基于背景扩张史的理论可能被扰动数据决定性排除。

Abstract: We investigate the cosmological viability of exponential infrared $f(T)$ teleparallel gravity using current cosmological observations. This framework realizes late-time cosmic acceleration through torsional modifications of gravity without enlarging the six-parameter cosmological parameter space of spatially flat $Λ$CDM, and admits two distinct solution branches: a phantom-like model (Model I) and a model featuring a negative-to-positive transition in the effective torsional dark-energy density (Model II). We constrain both branches using CMB observations from Planck, ACT, and SPT together with DESI BAO and Pantheon+ Type Ia supernovae. We find that the principal branch (Model I) alleviates the Hubble tension relative to $Λ$CDM, but remains statistically disfavoured by the combined dataset. The secondary branch (Model II) is decisively ruled out. We show that the failure of Model II originates from the interplay between background and perturbation constraints: once late-time distance measurements constrain the expansion history, the model becomes overconstrained, forcing correlated shifts in $Ω_{\rm m}h^2$, $A_s$, $n_s$, and $τ_{\rm reio}$, degrading the fit to the CMB damping tail and driving the optical depth to unphysical values. Our results demonstrate that perturbation observables provide stringent and complementary tests of teleparallel gravity beyond the background expansion history.

</details>


### [23] [Running into tension: primordial black holes from ultra-slow-roll inflation, spectral running, and the Hubble tension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31362)
*Miguel A. Sabogal,Antonio J. Iovino,Sunny Vagnozzi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究早期暗能量（EDE）等前复合新物理如何改变CMB数据推断的谱运行指数α_s，进而影响单场超慢滚（USR）暴胀原初黑洞（PBH）模型的可行性。结果显示，EDE会提高α_s的推断值，加剧与USR模型预测的负α_s之间的张力，表明哈勃常数张力与PBH模型面临的问题相互关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单场超慢滚（ultra-slow-roll, USR）暴胀模型预测负的谱运行（spectral running）α_s<0，但与ACT等CMB数据提示的正运行存在冲突。由于CMB推断的暴胀参数对前复合膨胀史（pre-recombination expansion history）敏感，而后者正是哈勃张力（Hubble tension）所涉及新物理的作用区域，因此有必要研究这类新物理如何影响α_s约束。

Method: 以轴子类早期暗能量（axion-like early dark energy, EDE）作为前复合新物理的基准模型，结合Planck、ACT、South Pole Telescope的CMB数据以及DESI DR2的重子声学振荡（Baryon Acoustic Oscillation）数据，对α_s及其运行之运行β_s进行联合约束，并与ΛCDM模型的结果进行对比。

Result: 对于大多数数据集组合，从ΛCDM切换到EDE会使推断的α_s增大。物理机制是：在固定声学角尺度θ_s后，EDE会增大扩散-声学角尺度比θ_d/θ_s，而α_s的正向偏移通过增强小尺度功率来补偿这种额外的阻尼效应。

Conclusion: 哈勃张力所指向的新物理会进一步加剧USR PBH模型面临的挑战。更广泛而言，在哈勃张力和前复合膨胀史问题得到解决之前，基于CMB推断的暴胀参数（如n_s和α_s）进行暴胀模型选择可能是草率的。

Abstract: Single-field ultra-slow-roll (USR) inflation is among the most studied mechanisms for primordial black hole (PBH) formation. These models predict a negative spectral running ($α_s<0$), whose magnitude increases with the PBH mass. This is in tension with recent hints for positive running from Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) data. However, inflationary parameters inferred from CMB data are sensitive to the assumed pre-recombination expansion history, which is precisely where new physics motivated by the Hubble tension should operate. Focusing on axion-like early dark energy (EDE) as a benchmark, we investigate the effect of such pre-recombination new physics on $α_s$, and hence on the viability of USR PBH models, in light of state-of-the-art CMB data from Planck, ACT, and the South Pole Telescope, together with Baryon Acoustic Oscillation data from DESI DR2. Our analysis therefore provides an updated set of constraints on $α_s$ and the running of the running $β_s$. For most dataset combinations, moving from $Λ$CDM to EDE increases the inferred $α_s$: once the acoustic angular scale $θ_s$ is fixed, EDE increases the diffusion-to-acoustic angular scale ratio $θ_d/θ_s$, and the shift in $α_s$ compensates this extra damping by increasing small-scale power. In this sense, tension calls for tension: taking the Hubble tension seriously as an indication for new physics strengthens the challenges faced by USR PBH models. More broadly, our analysis stresses that inflationary model selection using CMB-inferred inflationary parameters such as $n_s$ and $α_s$ may be premature, especially until the Hubble tension, and more generally the pre-recombination expansion history, is understood.

</details>


### [24] [Ultralight dark matter mixed with primordial black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31629)
*Xing-Yu Yang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了超轻暗物质（ULDM）与原始黑洞（PBHs）混合晕的动力学，将连续PBH贡献与离散散粒噪声贡献分离，发现连续效应对孤子区的修正可达百分之几十，而离散散粒噪声在银河时标上动力学上可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗物质候选者质量跨度极大，从超轻玻色子场到大质量致密天体，本文旨在连接这两种极端情形，研究ULDM与PBHs混合系统的物理效应。

Method: 将混合ULDM-PBH晕中的PBH贡献分离为连续贡献与离散散粒噪声贡献：前者进入平均化的薛定谔-泊松（Schrödinger-Poisson）背景，后者作为微扰处理，诱导ULDM本征模跃迁和孤子加热。

Result: 对于基准混合晕（ULDM粒子质量10^{-22}eV，维里质量约10^{10}M_☉，PBH占比1%），连续PBH分量对背景密度、引力势及低能ULDM本征值修正不足1%，但在相干孤子区产生约20%的径向模参与度变化；恒星质量PBH的离散散粒噪声导致的ULDM模跃迁极慢，最快低能多重态跃迁时标达约10^9 Gyr。

Conclusion: 在该参数区间内，连续PBH贡献是主导效应，而离散PBH散粒噪声在银河时标上动力学上可忽略不计。

Abstract: Dark matter candidates span many orders of magnitude in mass, from ultralight bosonic fields to massive compact objects. In this work, we connect these two extremes by investigating ultralight dark matter (ULDM) mixed with primordial black holes (PBHs). We study mixed ULDM-PBH halos by separating the continuum PBH contribution from the shot-noise fluctuation generated by discrete PBHs. The continuum contribution enters the averaged Schrödinger-Poisson background, while the discreteness contribution is treated as a perturbation that induces ULDM eigenmode transitions and soliton heating. The two contributions have distinct parametric dependencies: continuum effects scale with PBH fraction, whereas discreteness-driven transition rates scale with the product of PBH fraction and individual PBH mass in the perturbative regime. For a fiducial mixed halo with ULDM particle mass $10^{-22}\,\mathrm{eV}$, virial mass of order $10^{10}\,M_{\odot}$, and PBH fraction $1\%$, the continuum PBH component modifies the background density, gravitational potential, and low-lying ULDM eigenvalues only at the sub-percent level. Nevertheless, this percent-level continuum PBH contribution produces a tens-of-percent response in the coherent soliton region, changing the radial mode participation by about $20\%$. For stellar-mass PBHs, the discrete shot-noise fluctuation induces extremely slow ULDM mode transitions, with the fastest low-lying multiplet transition having a timescale of order $10^9\,\mathrm{Gyr}$ for solar-mass PBHs. In this regime, the leading PBH effect is the continuum contribution, while discrete PBH shot noise is dynamically negligible on galactic timescales.

### [25] [Athermality of generalized Gibbs ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30762)
*Riccardo Senese,Bruno Bertini,Katja Klobas,Pasquale Calabrese*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究利用量子资源理论中的“非热性（athermality）”概念，定量刻画了可积量子系统在非平衡演化后形成的广义吉布斯系综（GGE）与普通吉布斯系综（GE）之间的差异，发现当后猝灭哈密顿量处于基态临界时，非热性会出现异常小值且在临界点处具有奇异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管广义吉布斯系综（generalized Gibbs ensemble, GGE）已被广泛研究，但对其与普通吉布斯系综（Gibbs ensemble, GE）在定量上究竟有多大差异仍缺乏刻画。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 在量子资源理论（quantum resource theory）框架下，将非热性（athermality）定义为给定态与最近热态之间的相对熵（relative entropy）。基于此定义，计算了多个典型可积模型（包括自由XY自旋链、相互作用的Lieb-Liniger模型、XXZ自旋链和谐振子链）中量子猝灭（quantum quench）后的非热性。

Result: 发现当后猝灭哈密顿量（post-quench Hamiltonian）的基态处于临界（critical）时，非热性通常变得异常小，尽管所探测的物理状态处于有限能量密度；同时证明非热性在临界点处会系统性地产生奇异性（singularity），该奇异性源自GGE的熵。

Conclusion: 非热性可作为定量比较GGE与GE差异的有效工具；在临界条件下，GGE与GE的偏离显著减小，且该行为具有奇异性特征，为理解可积系统的热化机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: Integrable quantum systems evolving from non-equilibrium initial states do not thermalize to conventional Gibbs ensembles (GE). Instead, at long times they relax to generalized Gibbs ensembles (GGEs), which incorporate the full set of local and quasi-local conserved quantities. While GGEs have been extensively studied in the literature, a quantitative characterization of how different they are from ordinary GEs is still lacking. In this work, we address this question by employing the concept of athermality, which we define within quantum resource theory as the relative entropy between a given state and the closest thermal state. We compute the athermality for several quantum quenches in paradigmatic integrable models, including the free XY spin chain, the interacting Lieb-Liniger model, the XXZ spin chain, and the harmonic chain. We find that often the athermality becomes anomalously small when the post-quench Hamiltonian is critical in its ground state, despite probing physics at a finite energy density. We also prove that it systematically develops a singularity at criticality, which is inherited from the entropy of the GGE.

</details>


### [26] [Quantitative description of cognitive fatigue in repetitive monotonous tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31234)
*Shahar Hod*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用时间依赖的西西弗斯随机爬升模型（Sisyphus random climb model）对重复单调任务中出现的警惕性下降（vigilance decrement）现象进行定量描述，推导出成功概率函数 $S(t;\mathcal{N})$，并证明单次操作成功概率 $s(t)$ 的逆幂律行为 $s(t)\sim t^{-1/\mathcal{N}}$ 是区分所有工人都能最终完成任务与部分工人永远无法成功完成任务的关键边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有实证研究表明，从事重复单调任务的工人会因认知疲劳（cognitive fatigue）导致随任务时间增长的表现能力逐渐下降，即警惕性下降现象。然而，该现象缺乏定量的理论描述，本文旨在通过数学模型填补这一空白。

Method: 采用时间依赖的西西弗斯随机爬升模型，利用解析技术推导出成功概率函数 $S(t;\mathcal{N})$，该函数表示工人在 $t$ 次或更少重复操作内，连续完成 $\mathcal{N}$ 次无错误成功操作的概率。模型引入随时间变化的单次操作失败概率 $1-s(t)$，以刻画工人因疲劳导致的性能衰退。

Result: 证明了单次操作成功概率 $s(t)$ 的逆幂律行为 $s(t)\sim t^{-1/\mathcal{N}}$ 构成了一个临界边界：当 $s(t)$ 的衰减快于该边界时，成功函数 $S[t;s(t),\mathcal{N}]$ 渐近趋近于 1（所有工人最终都能完成任务）；反之，成功函数渐近趋近于某个小于 1 的值，部分疲劳工人将永远无法成功完成任务。

Conclusion: 西西弗斯随机爬升模型能够定量描述警惕性下降现象，并揭示了单次操作成功概率的衰减律如何决定工人群体的最终任务完成情况，为理解认知疲劳对重复单调任务绩效的影响提供了理论框架。

Abstract: There is strong qualitative empirical evidence in the scientific literature that, due to cognitive fatigue, workers performing repetitive and monotonous tasks are characterized by a gradual deterioration in their performance abilities as the time-on-task increases, a phenomenon known as the vigilance decrement. Using a time-dependent Sisyphus random climb model, we provide a quantitative description of this intriguing phenomenon. In particular, we use analytical techniques in order to determine the success probability function $S(t;{\cal N})$ of Sisyphus workers, the time-dependent fraction of workers who succeed, after making $t$ repetitive operations or less, to complete their task by making ${\cal N}$ successful operations in a row without a single fault in between. It is explicitly shown that the functional behavior of the increasing-in-time one-operation tumble probability $1-s(t)$ of exhausted Sisyphus workers may have a dramatic effect on the probability of the workers to achieve their ultimate goal in repetitive monotonous processes. In particular, we prove that the Sisyphus random climb model with the inverse power law functional behavior $s(t)\sim t^{-1/{\cal N}}$ of the one-operation success probability marks the boundary between Sisyphus workers whose success functions $S[t;s(t),{\cal N}]$ approach $1$ asymptotically in time (implying that all the workers eventually complete their task) and Sisyphus workers whose success functions approach an asymptotic value which is less than $1$, in which case some of the exhausted Sisyphus workers never complete their task successfully.

</details>


### [27] [Self-propulsion of a polaron with an oscillating coupling to its quantum bath](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31555)
*Jacopo Romano,Andrea Gambassi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种浸入量子气体中的杂质（极化子），其与周围介质的耦合随时间周期性调制且符号交替变化。通过积分掉浴自由度，推导出有效的速度依赖阻力，发现高于临界调制频率时低速下阻力系数变负，引发自推进。经典极限下表征了转变随频率和化学势的变化，并计算了量子修正，发现转变依然稳健但可被精确测量抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受主动量子物质（active quantum matter）研究的驱动，探索量子气体中杂质（即极化子（polaron））在耦合强度随时间周期性交替调制下的动力学行为。

Method: 通过积分掉浴自由度（bath degrees of freedom），推导出作用在杂质上的有效速度依赖阻力（velocity-dependent drag force）；在经典极限下分析转变特征，并计算领头阶量子修正。

Result: 高于临界调制频率时，低速下的阻力系数（drag coefficient）变为负值，表明系统进入自推进（self-propulsion）态；该转变在量子修正下依然稳健，但可被足够精确的杂质位置测量所抑制。

Conclusion: 从主动量子物质的角度，揭示了极化子系统中耦合调制的非平衡效应可诱导自推进行为，且量子观测对非平衡相变有抑制作用。

Abstract: Motivated by the quest for active quantum matter, we investigate the dynamics of an impurity immersed in a quantum gas -- a polaron -- whose coupling to the surrounding medium is periodically modulated in time, alternating in sign. By integrating out the bath degrees of freedom, we derive an effective velocity-dependent drag force acting on the impurity. Above a critical modulation frequency, the corresponding drag coefficient becomes negative at low velocities, signaling the onset of self-propulsion. In the classical limit, we characterize this transition as a function of the modulation frequency and the bath chemical potential. We then compute the leading-order quantum corrections to the impurity dynamics and show that, while the transition remains robust, it can be suppressed by sufficiently precise measurements of the impurity position.

</details>


### [28] [Exactly solvable non-unitary conformal interfaces in unitary CFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32035)
*Qicheng Tang,Zixia Wei,Xueda Wen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文在格点（lattice）上直接构造了一类非幺正（non-unitary）且同时满足精确共形（conformal）与精确可解（exactly solvable）的界面（interface），建立了其对应的边界与界面共形场论（CFT）描述，揭示了非幺正边界态的双正交基结构、复数有效中心荷（effective central charge）以及对全球量子淬火（global quantum quench）的非幺正推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有共形场论中的边界与界面大多局限于幺正（unitary）情形，而物理中许多耗散、非平衡或开放系统需要非幺正框架。该工作旨在格点-连续对应框架下，通过解析延拓（analytic continuation）已知幺正共形界面的散射数据，系统构造非幺正共形界面并建立其CFT描述。

Method: 通过对已知精确幺正共形界面的散射数据进行解析延拓，构造出由SL(2, ℂ)参数化的非幺正界面族；利用精确格点-连续对应推导折叠图像（folded picture）中的共形边界态（conformal boundary states）；引入双正交基（biorthogonal basis）定义闭弦通道（closed-string channel）中的Hilbert空间，分别指定入射和出射边界态；通过格点解析与数值计算以及展开图像（unfolded picture）中的界面CFT分析验证有效中心荷的行为。

Result: 得到了一个由SL(2, ℂ)参数化的非紧凑（non-compact）非幺正共形界面族，该族打破概率流守恒。非幺正边界的CFT构造要求入射与出射边界态由一对对偶双正交基独立指定，从而导出了非幺正推广的Cardy条件（Cardy's condition）。非幺正界面展现出由复数有效中心荷主导的对数纠缠标度（logarithmic entanglement scaling）；对于SU(1,1)子类，有效中心荷保持实数但随透射系数增大会无界增长。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了非幺正共形边界与界面的严格格点-连续对应框架，提出了非幺正边界CFT的一致构造方案（包括双正交基要求和推广的Cardy条件）。揭示了非幺正界面中复数有效中心荷及其对数纠缠标度行为，并将非幺正边界条件推广到全球量子淬火问题中，建立了其有效温度与边界条件改变算符（boundary-condition-changing operator）共形维数之间的关系。

Abstract: We construct directly on the lattice a class of non-unitary interfaces that are both exactly conformal and exactly solvable, and establish their corresponding boundary and interface conformal field theory (CFT) descriptions. The construction is obtained by analytically continuing the scattering data of known exact unitary conformal interfaces on the lattice, yielding an $SL(2,\mathbb C)$-parametrized family, which is non-compact and breaks probability-current conservation. Exploiting the exact lattice-continuum correspondence, we derive the conformal boundary states in the folded picture. We show that a proper definition of the Hilbert space in the closed-string channel requires the incoming and outgoing boundary states to be specified independently by boundary data associated with a pair of dual biorthogonal bases, in close analogy with the right and left eigenvectors of a non-Hermitian Hamiltonian. This requirement determines a consistent CFT construction of non-unitary boundaries and interfaces, and leads to a non-unitary generalization of the conventional Cardy's condition for unitary boundary CFT. Beyond their formal construction, these non-unitary interfaces are shown to exhibit logarithmic entanglement scaling governed by an effective central charge that is generally complex. For the $SU(1,1)$ subclass, the effective central charge remains real but grows without bound as the transmission coefficient increases. This result is demonstrated through analytical and numerical lattice calculations, as well as an interface CFT analysis in the unfolded picture. Finally, we present a general CFT analysis of a class of global quantum quenches whose initial states are prepared with non-unitary boundaries. We relate their effective temperature to the conformal dimension of the boundary-condition-changing operators associated with non-unitary boundary conditions.

</details>


### [29] [Effects of confinement in a Brownian gas with simultaneous stochastic resetting and dynamically emergent correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31634)
*Gabriele de Mauro,Satya N. Majumdar,Gregory Schehr*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了在外部势阱中同时受随机重置（stochastic resetting）到原点的 $N$ 个非相互作用布朗粒子系统，发现共同重置会诱导出强烈的动态涌现关联（dynamically emergent correlations, DEC），并系统分析了势阱形态（从谐振势到盒约束）如何影响非平衡稳态的密度、关联函数、极值统计（extreme value statistics, EVS）和间隙统计，揭示了三种普适类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非相互作用粒子在共同随机重置作用下如何产生动态涌现关联，以及外部约束（confinement）形态对这些关联和系统非平衡稳态性质的影响，尤其是不同势阱类型（谐振势与盒约束）是否会导致定性差异。

Method: 采用势阱形式 $V(x)=κ|x|^α$（$α\geq0$），重点解析地处理两种可解情形：谐振势（harmonic confinement, HC, $α=2$）和盒约束（box confinement, BC, $α\to\infty$）。推导稳态联合分布、密度、关联函数、极值统计和间隙统计的精确解，并借助模拟和标度论证（scaling arguments）推广到一般 $α$。

Result: 在 HC 和 BC 中密度行为相似，但归一化相关系数（normalized correlation coefficient）截然不同：BC 中呈非单调并超过无约束极限，因硬壁抑制了去关联轨迹；HC 中则单调增加趋于无约束极限。对一般 $α$，当 $0<α<α_c=1+\sqrt{5}$ 时行为单调，$α>α_c$ 时非单调。极值方面，HC 中最大值 $M_1=O(\sqrt{\ln N})$，极限分布具有有界支撑和由两长度尺度比控制的形状转变；BC 中最大值距边界 $O(1/N)$，但波动呈具有对数修正的宽幂律尾。相邻粒子间隙（gap）在 BC 中典型值更小但反常波动更强。最终识别出三种普适类：$0\leqα\leq1$、$1<α<\infty$ 和奇异极限 $α\to\infty$。

Conclusion: 非相互作用布朗粒子在共同重置下可产生强涌现关联，且关联性质对外部势阱形态高度敏感：约束的刚性问题（软势 vs. 硬壁）决定了关联函数是单调还是非单调，并深刻影响极值统计和间隙统计的定性与定量行为。系统呈现出跨越 $α$ 参数的三种普适类结构。

Abstract: We study $N$ non-interacting Brownian particles in an external potential under simultaneous stochastic resetting to the origin. Although they do not interact directly, common resets generate strong dynamically emergent correlations (DEC). We analyze how confinement modifies these correlations and the nonequilibrium stationary state for $V(x)=κ|x|^α$, $α\geq0$, focusing mainly on two analytically tractable cases: harmonic confinement (HC), $α=2$, and box confinement (BC), $α\to\infty$. In both cases the stationary state is controlled by the competition between confinement and resetting lengths. We derive exact results for the stationary joint distribution, density, correlations, extreme value statistics (EVS), and gap statistics. While the density behaves similarly in HC and BC, the normalized correlation coefficient differs sharply. In BC it is non-monotonic and overshoots the unconfined value, as hard walls suppress decorrelating trajectories. In HC it instead increases monotonically toward the unconfined limit. For general $α$, the behavior is monotonic for $0<α<α_c=1+\sqrt{5}$ and non-monotonic for $α>α_c$. The difference between HC and BC is also visible in edge observables. In HC, the maximum scales as $M_1=O(\sqrt{\ln N})$ and has a limiting distribution with bounded support and a shape transition controlled by the ratio of the two length scales. In BC, the maximum is at distance $O(1/N)$ from the boundary, as in equilibrium, but its fluctuations have a broad power-law tail with logarithmic corrections. The first gap shows a similar contrast: BC gives a smaller typical gap but stronger anomalous fluctuations than HC. Finally, we extend the EVS analysis to general $α$ and identify, via simulations and scaling arguments, three universality classes: $0\leqα\leq1$, $1<α<\infty$, and the singular limit $α\to\infty$.

</details>


### [30] [Non-Maxwellian Velocity Statistics in Supercooled Liquids and Their Possible Relation to Super-Arrhenius Viscosity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31985)
*Giorgi Tsereteli,Zohar Nussinov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟证明，过冷液体（supercooled liquids）可表现出持久的非麦克斯韦速度分布（non-Maxwellian velocity distributions），这种偏离与超阿伦尼乌斯缓慢弛豫（super-Arrhenius relaxation）相关。研究引入了一种不强制麦克斯韦分布的新型随机恒温器（stochastic thermostats），发现由此产生的非麦克斯韦速度分布的过剩峰度（excess kurtosis）$κ\lesssim0.3$可显著抑制结晶。温度涨落的无量纲宽度 $\overline{A}$ 与 $κ$ 满足 $κ\simeq3\overline{A}^{2}$，且从45种玻璃形成体的黏度数据和比热特征中提取的 $\overline{A}$ 近乎恒定（均值0.08，标准差0.03），与模拟结果一致。这连接了慢弛豫、输运和热力学测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典平衡统计力学（equilibrium statistical mechanics）认为，固定质量粒子的速度分布由温度唯一决定为麦克斯韦分布（Maxwellian distribution），无论相互作用、密度或结构如何。然而，过冷玻璃形成液体（supercooled glass forming liquids）实现的是长寿命亚稳态（metastable states），可能规避平衡结晶，从而打破麦克斯韦统计的假设前提。本文旨在检验这些亚稳态是否确实表现出非麦克斯韦速度分布，并探索其与慢弛豫、输运及热力学测量之间的潜在联系。

Method: 基于一个一般性理论结果——长寿命亚稳态可在强度量（intensive variables）上呈现有限宽度的分布，从而温度分布导致非麦克斯韦速度统计——数值模拟采用新型随机恒温器（stochastic thermostats），这类恒温器产生稳态（stationary states）但不强制麦克斯韦速度分布。通过模拟获得长寿命亚稳态，并分析其速度分布的过剩峰度（excess kurtosis）$κ$。此外，将温度涨落的无量纲宽度 $\overline{A}$（满足 $κ\simeq3\overline{A}^{2}$）与45种玻璃形成体的黏度数据和比热特征进行对比。

Result: 模拟结果显示，长寿命亚稳态的速度分布相对于麦克斯韦分布具有过剩峰度 $0<κ\lesssim0.3$，且随着 $κ$ 增大，结晶受到强烈抑制。从45种玻璃形成体的黏度数据和比热特征中提取的 $\overline{A}$ 几乎恒定，均值为0.08，标准差为0.03，与模拟中观察到的 $κ$ 值一致。

Conclusion: 长时非麦克斯韦速度统计可能将慢弛豫（slow relaxation）、输运（transport）和热力学测量（thermodynamic measurements）联系起来。独立于所检验的理论，本文引入的随机恒温器为分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟提供了一条获得非麦克斯韦速度统计的新途径。

Abstract: For particles of fixed mass, classical equilibrium statistical mechanics dictates a Maxwellian velocity distribution determined solely by the temperature, regardless of the interactions, density, or structure. Supercooled glass forming liquids realize long lived metastable states that evade equilibrium crystallization and may thus violate assumptions underlying Maxwellian statistics. We numerically demonstrate that supercooled liquids can exhibit persistent non-Maxwellian velocity distributions with deviations connected to their exceptionally slow super-Arrhenius relaxation. Our work is motivated by a general result establishing that long lived metastable states may exhibit finite width distributions of intensive variables. A distribution of temperatures implies non-Maxwellian velocity statistics. We test this prediction by introducing stochastic thermostats that generate stationary states while, unlike conventional thermostats, not imposing Maxwellian velocity distributions. Simulations with these thermostats yield long lived states that have, by comparison to Maxwellian velocity distributions, an excess kurtosis $0<κ\lesssim0.3$. Crystallization is strongly impeded with increasing $κ$. In a minimal description, temperature fluctuations are characterized by a dimensionless width $\overline{A}$ with $κ\simeq3\overline{A}^{2}$. The nearly constant $\overline{A}$ (of an average value $0.08$ and standard deviation $0.03$) found in viscosity data collapse across $45$ glass formers and in specific heat signatures is consistent with kurtosis found in our simulations. Long time non-Maxwellian velocity statistics may thus link slow relaxation, transport, and thermodynamic measurements. Independent of the tested theory, the stochastic thermostats that we introduce offer a molecular dynamics route to non-Maxwellian velocity statistics.

### [31] [Exploring the entropic asymmetry on logical stochastic resonance with energetically equivalent intrinsic outputs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31989)
*Vipul Rai,Moupriya Das*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了双阱势阱（double-well potential）中宽度不对称性（width asymmetry）或熵不对称性（entropic asymmetry）对逻辑随机共振（logical stochastic resonance, LSR）的影响。结果表明，增加宽度不对称性能持续提升逻辑输出的成功概率P(logic)，并且与能量偏置结合时，可在显著降低能量成本的前提下实现可靠逻辑门操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有逻辑随机共振研究主要关注双阱势阱的能量不对称性（energetic asymmetry），即两阱深度不等，而势阱宽度不对称性（即熵不对称性）的作用尚未被探索。本文旨在系统研究宽度不对称性对OR与AND逻辑门操作的影响。

Method: 通过布朗动力学（Brownian dynamics）在双阱势阱中模拟受输入信号驱动的逻辑操作，系统改变势阱的宽度不对称性，并结合能量偏置（energetic bias），定量分析逻辑输出成功概率P(logic)的变化。

Result: 增加宽度不对称性持续提升最优P(logic)；宽度不对称性与能量偏置结合可在显著降低能量成本的情况下实现可靠逻辑门操作；所需能量偏置随宽度不对称性增大而逐渐减小。

Conclusion: 宽度不对称性作为一种几何效应（geometric effect），在不改变两逻辑输出态能量等价性的前提下，有效提升逻辑随机共振性能，并为构建低能耗可靠逻辑门提供了新途径。

Abstract: Small-scale systems are inherently subject to environmental noise that can be harnessed constructively to realize reliable logic operations -- a phenomenon known as logical stochastic resonance (LSR), where a bistable system produces correct logical outputs within an optimal window of noise intensity. The Brownian dynamics governed by appropriate inputs inside a double-well potential, modeling the bistable system, mimic the logic operations. The two wells of this potential represent two distinct logical output states 0 and 1. Asymmetry in this potential is known to be essential for improving logical reliability. However, prior studies have focused on energetic asymmetry, characterized by unequal depths of the two wells of the potential. This left the role of the width asymmetry in the potential, unexplored. This latter class of asymmetry emerges due to the dissimilar widths of the two wells of the potential. It can be classified as the entropic asymmetry between the two logical output states. Here, we systematically investigate the effect of width or the entropic asymmetry in the system on the logical response for OR and AND gate operations. Unlike energetic asymmetry, width asymmetry preserves the energetic equivalence of the two intrinsic logical output states, making it a geometric effect. We find that increasing width asymmetry consistently improves the optimal P(logic), the quantifier measuring the successful logical outcome. Moreover, when it is combined with an energetic bias, it produces reliable logic gate operation at a significantly reduced energetic cost compared to the symmetric case. The requirement of this energy bias also diminishes gradually with the increasing degree of width asymmetry in the potential.

### [32] [Multifractal Scaling in Hi-C Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31997)
*Seong-Gyu Yang,Lucas Hedström,Jan Smrek,Ludvig Lizana*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文证明Hi-C图谱（Hi-C maps）中的多分形标度（multifractal scaling）源自接触概率的幂律形式 $P(s)$，并解析推导了质量指数 $\tau(q)$ 的表达式，揭示了该多分形行为是染色质组织（chromatin organization）的普适特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究发现Hi-C图谱和显微成像数据呈现多分形标度（multifractal scaling），但其起源尚不明确，已有工作仅通过假设性模型进行描述，缺乏直接的物理解释。

Method: 从具有单一指数 $\gamma$ 的接触概率 $P(s)$ 出发，解析推导质量指数 $\tau(q)$，该指数描述了接触密度（contact density）的 $q$ 阶矩随粗粒化盒尺寸 $l$ 的标度行为；同时将分析推广至双指数 $P(s)$ 情形。

Result: $\tau(q)$ 在大 $q$ 处的斜率为：当 $\gamma<1$ 时为 $2-\gamma$，当 $\gamma\geq 1$ 时为 $1$；该行为对噪声鲁棒，且在不同物种间一致，具有普适性。双指数 $P(s)$ 情形下多分形行为呈现盒尺寸 $l$ 依赖性。

Conclusion: 该研究为Hi-C图谱中的多分形标度提供了物理解释，建立了多分形性与聚合物接触统计（polymer contact statistics）之间的直接联系，将 $\tau(q)$ 的大 $q$ 斜率映射到已知的聚合物接触指数（polymer contact exponent）。

Abstract: The three-dimensional organization of the genome exhibits rich, scale-dependent structure, as revealed by both chromosome contact maps (e.g., Hi-C maps) and chromatin density measured by microscopy. Recent studies have reported multifractal scaling in these data. Yet, the origin of this scaling behavior remains unclear: existing efforts describe it through postulated models. Here, we show that the multifractal structure of Hi-C maps is a direct consequence of the power-law contact probability $P(s)$, which is itself an empirical observable measured from Hi-C maps. Starting from $P(s)$ with a single exponent $γ$, we analytically derive the mass exponent $τ(q)$, which characterizes how the $q$-th moment of contact density scales with box size $l$ used to coarse-grain the genomic coordinate. This multifractal behavior reflects the geometric competition between intra- and inter-segment contacts. We find that the slope of $τ(q)$ at large $q$ is given by $2 -γ$ when $γ<1$, and by $1$ when $γ\geq 1$. We further show that this behavior is robust to noise and consistent across diverse organisms, indicating that it is a universal feature of chromatin organization. We extend our analysis into double-exponent $P(s)$, and show the $l$ dependence in multifractal behavior. Taken together, these results provide a physical explanation for multifractal scaling and establish a direct link between the multifractality in Hi-C maps and polymer contact statistics, with the large-$q$ slope of $τ(q)$ mapping onto a known polymer contact exponent.

</details>

### [33] [The Dynamics of Quantum Gravity: the Missing Piece in the Spacetime Emergentist Account](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31559)
*Álvaro Mozota Frauca*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出，量子引力（quantum gravity）中“时空涌现（spacetime emergence）”的分析是不完整的，因为现有讨论忽视了这些理论的动力学具有不同于标准量子理论的“量子”特性；作者认为时空功能主义（spacetime functionalism）无法解决这一困境，当前量子引力进路未能提供从真正量子非时空实体到时空的成功还原实例，因而弱化了时空涌现论者的立场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力暗示时空可能不是基础的，研究者试图论证时空可以从非时空实体中“涌现（emerge）”。然而，现有分析（如功能主义）忽略了这些理论中动力学本身的“量子”特性与标准量子理论存在差异，因此需要重新审视涌现方案是否成立。

Method: 采用概念分析与批判论证的方法，剖析现有“时空涌现”论证（特别是时空功能主义）的逻辑缺陷，重点考察量子引力理论中动力学与运动学（kinematics）的区分，以及其量子性（quantumness）对涌现主张带来的挑战。

Result: 作者论证：(1) 当前一些量子引力进路似乎未能提供有意义（meaningful）的理论；(2) 时空功能主义对此困境无帮助；(3) 时空涌现论者的立场被削弱，因为他们缺乏任何将时空成功还原为真正量子非时空实体（truly quantum non-spatiotemporal stuff）的成功实例。

Conclusion: 时空涌现论面临根本性困难：不仅需要解释理论中运动学与经典（classical）方面如何满足时空角色，还必须处理动力学与量子方面的诠释问题。由于缺乏成功的还原案例，时空涌现论和量子引力理论目前均未达到可信的理论地位。

Abstract: Quantum gravity suggests that spacetime may not be fundamental, and it has been argued that we can understand a theory without a fundamental spacetime if we are able to claim that spacetime `emerges' from some non-spatiotemporal entities. In this sense, strategies like functionalism have been deployed to claim that this emergence is possible and plausible, both in principle and in practice for current approaches to quantum gravity. In this article I argue that this analysis is incomplete, as it tends to overlook the way the dynamics of these theories is `quantum' in a way that differs from standard quantum theory. The challenge for the emergentist (and for the quantum gravity theorist) is to give an interpretation not only to the kinematical and classical aspects of these theories, but to the dynamical and quantum ones, and to show how the spacetime roles can be fulfilled, if possible at all. Therefore, I argue that some current approaches to quantum gravity seem to fail to provide meaningful theories, that spacetime functionalism is of no help, and that the position of the spacetime emergentists is weakened, as they lack any example of a successful reduction of spacetime to some truly quantum non-spatiotemporal stuff.

</details>
