### [34] [Atomic-Scale Characterization of Oxide Interfaces and Superlattices Using Scanning Transmission Electron Microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30859)
*Steven R. Spurgeon,Renae Gannon*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文综述了扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）在氧化物界面与超晶格研究中的核心作用，涵盖成像、衍射及能谱分析技术，探讨了界面电导、电荷屏蔽效应、界面工程及原子尺度化学映射等关键现象，并介绍了新兴的等离子体制备技术与人工智能引导的显微方法，强调了STEM与其他技术及理论计算结合对发展功能氧化物预测模型的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氧化物界面与超晶格中的结构-性能关系复杂，需要高分辨率表征技术来揭示其物理机制。STEM结合电子能量损失谱（EELS）和能量色散X射线谱（EDS）提供了无与伦比的分析能力，但目前缺乏对这些技术在关键现象研究中应用的系统梳理。

Method: 采用扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）成像和衍射技术，耦合电子能量损失谱（EELS）与能量色散X射线谱（EDS）两种光谱学方法，进行高分辨率结构-性能关系分析。此外，还讨论了新兴的等离子体制备技术与人工智能（AI）引导的原位和非原位显微方法。

Result: 研究揭示了氧化物超晶格中的界面电导行为、磁电异质结构中的电荷屏蔽效应、铁氧化物中的界面工程以及控制原子尺度化学映射的复杂物理机制。等离子体制备技术与AI引导方法展示了在显微学中的应用潜力。

Conclusion: STEM表征提供的独特见解可与其他实验技术和理论计算整合，有助于开发更具预测性的功能氧化物行为模型，从而推动对氧化物界面及相关材料系统的深入理解。

Abstract: Scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM) is a cornerstone of our understanding of oxide interfaces and superlattices. No other technique provides the same level of insight into structure, chemistry, composition, and dynamics across as wide a variety of material systems. STEM imaging and diffraction, coupled with electron energy loss (EELS) and energy-dispersive X-ray (EDS) spectroscopies, offer unparalleled, high-resolution analysis of structure--property relationships. In this chapter we highlight investigations into key phenomena, including interfacial conductivity in oxide superlattices, charge screening effects in magnetoelectric heterostructures, interface engineering in iron oxides, and the complex physics governing atomic-scale chemical mapping. We also discuss emerging plasma preparation techniques and artificial intelligence-guided approaches to both ex situ and in situ microscopy. These studies illustrate how unique insights from STEM characterization can be integrated with other techniques and theory calculations to develop more predictive models for the behavior of functional oxides.

### [35] [Adaptive fine-tuning of foundation models for crystal structure prediction: Discovery of high-pressure phases in the CaFeNi system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30870)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体结构预测（crystal structure prediction, CSP）是化学与材料科学的关键挑战，但进化CSP因依赖反复的从头计算（ab initio）弛豫和能量排序而计算昂贵。尽管机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials, MLIPs）可加速CSP，但其应用受限于需要大规模训练集以及难以选择应由密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）标记的候选结构。

Method: 引入一种自洽的、基础模型辅助的CSP工作流，将进化搜索与自适应数据选择和微调相结合。从预训练的MLIP出发，算法在迭代过程中自适应地选取紧凑、具代表性且物理相关的结构子集用于DFT标记，从而减少冗余计算并改进系统特定的势函数。

Result: 将该方法应用于化学复杂的Ca-Fe-Ni三元体系。工作流复现了已知的低压凸包（convex hull），并实现了高效的高压探索。预测了一种此前未报道的化合物Ca₆FeNi，该化合物在100 GPa以上变得热力学稳定。

Conclusion: 基于基础模型且数据高效的CSP能在保持精度的同时大幅降低计算成本，并能够在复杂多组分体系中实现新材料发现。

Abstract: The prediction of crystal structures is a key challenge in chemistry and materials science, but evolutionary crystal structure prediction (CSP) remains computationally expensive because it relies on repeated \textit{ab initio} relaxations and energy ranking. Machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) can accelerate CSP, yet their use is limited by the need for large training sets and by the difficulty of choosing which candidate structures should be labeled by density functional theory (DFT). Here we introduce a self-consistent, foundation-model-assisted CSP workflow that combines evolutionary search with adaptive data selection and fine-tuning. Starting from a pretrained MLIP, the algorithm rapidly explores configuration space while iteratively selecting compact, representative, and physically relevant subsets of structures for DFT labeling, thereby reducing redundant calculations and improving a system-specific potential. We apply the method to the chemically complex Ca--Fe--Ni ternary system. The workflow reproduces the known low-pressure convex hull and enables efficient high-pressure exploration. It predicts a previously unreported compound, Ca$_6$FeNi, which becomes thermodynamically stable above 100~GPa. These results show that foundation-model-based, data-efficient CSP can greatly reduce computational cost while preserving accuracy and enabling the discovery of new materials in complex multicomponent systems.

Method: 基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算三元凸包，从每个原子的内能（internal energy per atom）角度验证多型体相对于所有竞争相La-O-W化合物的稳定性。

Abstract: Structure and chemical composition of non-stoichiometric $\mathrm{(N \times H)}$-polytypes, $\mathrm{N} \in \{3,\,4,\,5,\,6,\,7\}$, belonging to the family of La2WO6-related tungstates, are presented and the basic rules behind their construction are formulated. The polytypes are validated from the point of view of the internal energy per atom against all the competing La-O-W compounds by means of the ternary convex hull computed by DFT. According to DFT, the ground state of the La2WO6 family surprisingly turned out to be the as-yet hypothetical tungstate La2WO6.oP36, isostructural with the known compound Gd2WO6, closely related to the basic building H-block of the polytypes. One more candidate for an experimentally accessible low-energy structure, La2WO6.mC72, derived from the already observed Sm2MoO6, has been identified to lie only $ΔE \approx 5\:\mathrm{meV/at.} \cong 60\:\mathrm{K}$ above the convex envelope.

### [38] [Role of polarity in the growth of cubic GaN within silicon inverted pyramids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30924)
*David Lister,Melissa Radford,Sara Fortin,Bilal Janjua,Mohsen Asad,Karen Kavanagh,Simon Watkins*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过有机金属气相外延（OMVPE）在硅倒金字塔模板上选择性生长立方相GaN（c-GaN），发现极性（polarity）在四重对称几何结构中显著影响c-GaN生长，导致对称性由四重降为二重，并观察到两种极性反转边界结构，其中一种为未见报道的未掺杂六方相GaN（h-GaN）基面反转畴界。研究指出，在微LED等小型器件中必须防止此类极性反转界面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 立方相GaN（c-GaN）因其缺乏自发内极化（spontaneous internal polarization），适用于基于微LED的短距离通信，有望比传统六方相GaN（h-GaN）实现更高速度。尽管c-GaN为亚稳相，已有在硅V形或U形槽中生长的成熟方法，但将其扩展至楔形或倒金字塔等小尺寸器件时，倒金字塔模板中GaN生长的报道有限且结果矛盾，因此需要系统研究。

Method: 在硅倒金字塔模板上，采用有机金属气相外延（organometallic vapor phase epitaxy, OMVPE）进行GaN的选择性区域生长（selective area growth），并通过截面透射电子显微镜（cross-sectional TEM）对样品进行分析。

Result: 极性是理解四重对称几何中c-GaN生长的关键因素，与长槽中生长情况不同。四重对称模板中的c-GaN因极性作用对称性降为二重。在典型生长条件下（底层h-GaN极性均匀），两个h-GaN到c-GaN的晶界（grain boundary）存在极性反转（polarity inversion）。观测到两种不同的反转边界结构，其中一种为先前未报道的未掺杂h-GaN基面反转畴界（inversion domain boundary）。

Conclusion: 对于微LED等小型器件，必须防止极性反转界面的形成，可通过抑制模板两个面上h-GaN的生长或局部控制h-GaN极性来实现。

Abstract: A lack of spontaneous internal polarization makes cubic GaN (c-GaN) a well-suited material for emerging micro-LED-based short-range communication, where c-GaN promises increased speed over conventional hexagonal GaN (h-GaN). Although c-GaN is metastable, there are well-established methods for growing it in Si V- or U-grooves; the logical step is to truncate these grooves to wedges or inverted pyramids for small devices. There are limited reports of GaN grown in inverted pyramid templates, and the results are contradictory. To study this process, we perform selective area growth of GaN using organometallic vapor phase epitaxy (OMVPE) on Si inverted pyramidal templates and analyze our samples by cross-sectional TEM. We find that polarity is critical to understanding the growth of c-GaN in this four-fold geometry, in contrast to the growth in long grooves. This effect fits within the broader set of challenges of polar-on-nonpolar heteroepitaxy; the c-GaN inside the four-fold symmetric template has its symmetry reduced by polarity to be two-fold. In typical growth conditions -- where the underlying h-GaN polarity is uniform -- we find this implies that two h-GaN to c-GaN grain boundaries will have a polarity inversion. We observe two different structures at these inverting boundaries, including a previously unreported inversion domain boundary along the basal plane of the undoped h-GaN. These findings show that for small devices -- such as micro-LEDs -- the polarity-inverting interfaces must be prevented, for example by suppressing the growth of h-GaN on two facets of the template or by locally controlling the h-GaN polarity.

### [39] [Prebiotic Chemistry Assemblies of L-Cysteine on Defect-Free Pyrite Terraces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30929)

Result: 获得了两种不同的超分子相：一种为致密且高度有序的超分子网络，另一种为排列较疏松、不稳定的超分子网络。揭示了三聚体（trimer）基的分子间相互作用是这些图案形成的根源。L-Cys自组装可在无缺陷FeS₂平台上形成，关键在于基底电子结构与分子间相互作用的协同效应，而无须主导性缺陷参与。

Conclusion: 黄铁矿（pyrite）的自催化活性可能在原始条件下触发了这类非静态自组装结构的表面聚合过程，从而支持了Wächtershäuser关于生命起源的假说。

Abstract: Wächtershäuser's theory proposes iron-sulfur minerals as key platforms for molecular synthesis and supramolecular organization in prebiotic environments. However, defects have been traditionally considered at the center of such assemblies, thereby underestimating the contributions of regular and pristine interfaces. Here, we combine scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy (STM/STS) with density functional theory (DFT) to investigate the fundamental prebiotic chemistry system of L-Cysteine (L-Cys) on defectless FeS$_2$(100) terraces. To do so, we first achieved atomically ordered, defect-free terraces that act as support of two distinct supramolecular phases of L-Cys: one compact, highly ordered supramolecular network and another less packed, labile supramolecular network. We unveil trimer-based intermolecular interactions to be at the origin of these pattern formations. These results demonstrate that L-Cys self-assemblies can be hosted on flawless FeS$_2$ terraces due to the cooperative interplay between substrate electronic structure and intermolecular interactions, without the participation of dominant defects. Therefore, the autocatalytic activity of pyrite could have triggered the on-surface polymerization process of these non-static self-assembled structures under primordial conditions, thereby endorsing Wächtershäuser's postulates on the origin of life.

### [40] [Computed materials proposals depart from the structural memory of experimental discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30967)
*Dan Nguyen,Karen Cao,Brian Chu,Nick Lemoff,Paul Kienzle,William Ratcliff*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究将167,500个无机晶体结构数据库（ICSD）条目嵌入连续结构相似性空间，划分图社区（graph communities）并进行时间回放。发现实验发现呈现强结构记忆：82.9%的新化学式进入已有社区，新建社区比例从1930年代的40.2%降至2010年代的2.6%。将GNoME、MatterGen等计算数据集投射到冻结历史地图后，顺序为：留出ICSD > MatterGen > {GNoME ~ MP-theoretical} > JARVIS > Alexandria。结构偏离实验盆地并非生成式AI特有，而是计算集的普遍现象。结合结构邻近性与简化化学式先例，定义了历史可合成性先验（historical synthesizability prior）用于筛选计算材料。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将167,500个ICSD条目嵌入连续结构相似性空间，划分图社区，并进行时间回放分析。将GNoME、MatterGen-public、Materials Project、JARVIS-DFT和Alexandria-PBE等计算数据集投射到冻结的历史结构地图上，进行排序比较。

Result: 实验发现显示强结构记忆：82.9%的新化学式进入已有社区，新社区形成率从1930年代的40.2%降至2010年代的2.6%。社区具有化学意义，识别出铜氧化物（cuprates）、巨磁阻锰氧化物（colossal-magnetoresistance manganites）、MAX相（MAX phases）和锂离子电池阴极（Li-ion battery cathodes）等九大教科书级领域复兴。投射排序为：留出ICSD > MatterGen > {GNoME ~ MP-theoretical} > JARVIS > Alexandria。结构偏离实验盆地是计算集的普遍现象。

Conclusion: 结合结构邻近性（structural proximity）与简化化学式先例（reduced-formula precedent），可定义历史可合成性先验，用于对计算材料进行分类筛选（triaging computed materials）。该方法为生成式AI和高通量计算产出的海量候选结构提供了基于实验历史的校准参照。

Abstract: Generative AI and high-throughput DFT pipelines propose millions of inorganic crystal structures, but lack a calibrated reference frame against experimentally realized chemistry. Here we embed 167,500 Inorganic Crystal Structure Database entries in a continuous structural-similarity space, partition it into graph communities, and replay them in time. Experimental discovery shows strong structural memory: 82.9% of new formulas enter pre-existing communities; new-community formation falls from 40.2% (1930s) to 2.6% (2010s). The communities are chemically meaningful, positively identifying nine textbook field-defining renaissances, including cuprates, colossal-magnetoresistance manganites, MAX phases, and Li-ion battery cathodes. Projecting GNoME, MatterGen-public, Materials Project, JARVIS-DFT, and Alexandria-PBE into frozen historical maps yields a cutoff-robust ordering: held-out ICSD > MatterGen > {GNoME ~ MP-theoretical} > JARVIS > Alexandria. Structural departure from experimental basins is not specific to generative AI but general across the tested computed sets. Combining structural proximity with reduced-formula precedent defines a historical synthesizability prior for triaging computed materials.

Conclusion: 该发现重新定义了GSST的原子结构，弥合了其光学性质方面的理论-实验差距，并将局域化学有序性（local chemical ordering）确立为高性能光子学材料的关键设计原则。

Abstract: Ge2Sb2SexTe5-x (GSST) alloys represent an emerging class of phase-change materials for integrated photonics. However, the microscopic origins underlying their superior performance compared to the parent compound Ge2Sb2Te5 remain elusive. By using atomic simulations, this work elucidates that the thermal stability and low optical loss of GSST are fundamentally governed by the formation of an in-layer compound-like structure with SeTe2 or Se2Te stoichiometry depending on the Se content, contrasting to the previously believed pure-element-layered model where Se and Te atoms occupy separate layers inside GSST. The newly identified compound-layered structures maintaining stability at temperature above 370 K, yield an enlarged bandgap, weakened antibonding character, and more importantly, a moderate refractive index as well as decreased extinction coefficient which align better with the experiment compared to the previously believed model. The present findings not only help bridge the long-standing theory-experiment gap regarding the optical properties of GSST by redefining its atomic structure, but also establish local chemical ordering as a critical materials design principle for high-performance photonics.

</details>


### [42] [High-Mobility and High-Reliability Top-Gate Oxide Semiconductor Transistors by Oxygen Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31217)

Result: 富氧工艺结合无氧退火可有效抑制氧空位（oxygen vacancies）及其与氢的相互作用，同时减少富氧缺陷（如氧二聚体，O-O bonds）的形成，从而实现了兼具高迁移率、陡峭亚阈值摆幅（subthreshold slope）以及高温下高PBTI可靠性的顶栅富铟（In-rich）氧化物半导体晶体管。

Conclusion: 对富氧缺陷的理解为克服氧化物半导体晶体管中迁移率与稳定性之间的权衡（mobility-stability trade-off）提供了新的视角。富氧工艺与无氧退火的组合策略是实现高性能、高可靠氧化物半导体晶体管的有效途径。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the role of oxygen (O) on the performance of top-gate (TG) atomic-layer-deposited (ALD) oxide semiconductor transistors. The results reveal distinct defect characteristics and positive bias temperature instability (PBTI) degradation mechanisms between oxygen-rich (O-rich) and oxygen-deficient (O-poor) devices. It is found that an O-rich device fabrication process followed by O-free annealing can effectively achieve TG indium-rich (In-rich) oxide semiconductor transistors with high mobility, high reliability and high stability in hydrogen environment because O-rich process can suppress oxygen vacancies and their interaction with hydrogen, while O-free annealing plays a critical role in minimizing the formation of O-rich defects such as oxygen dimers (O-O bonds). Consequently, TG In-rich transistors with high mobility, steep subthreshold slope, and high PBTI reliability at high temperature are demonstrated. The understanding of O-rich defects provides a new insight to overcome the mobility-stability trade-off.

### [43] [Symmetry-Enforced Ferroelectric Switching of Two-Dimensional Altermagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31241)
*Jiangyu Zhao,Yibo Liu,Guoli Wu,Xinru Li,Ying Dai,Baibiao Huang,Yandong Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过铁电（ferroelectric）层工程实现二维交错磁体（altermagnet）非易失性、确定性切换的普适方法，并在In2Se3/MnPTe3/In2Se3三层异质结中通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）验证了该机制，发现铁电极化反转可精确翻转交错磁自旋劈裂模式，从而产生可电学区分的反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交错磁性（altermagnetism）虽具有强动量依赖的自旋劈裂（momentum-dependent spin splitting）且净磁化强度为零，但两个等价自旋劈裂态之间的非易失性、确定性切换仍未解决，这成为该领域发展的根本瓶颈。

Method: 提出一种普适的层工程（layer-engineering）范式：将常规反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）单层夹在两个相同铁电（ferroelectric）层之间，利用面外极化（out-of-plane polarization）打破空间对称性以诱导稳健的交错磁劈裂；全局联合宇称-时间对称性（combined parity-time symmetry）确保铁电极化反转精确翻转自旋劈裂图案。采用第一性原理计算对In2Se3/MnPTe3/In2Se3三层结构进行严格验证。

Result: 计算结果表明，铁电驱动的自旋劈裂反转可确定性地翻转反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）信号，为电学区分两个交错磁态提供了明确的输运指纹。

Conclusion: 该机制不受限于单相本征材料的严格对称性要求，建立了一个适用于电学可寻址交错磁自旋电子学（electrically addressable altermagnetic spintronics）的通用物理框架。

Abstract: Altermagnetism features strong momentum-dependent spin splitting despite zero net magnetization, offering a transformative platform for next-generation spintronics. However, the nonvolatile and deterministic switching between its two equivalent spin-splitting states remains a fundamental bottleneck. Here, we propose a universal layer-engineering paradigm to achieve symmetry-enforced ferroelectric switching of two-dimensional altermagnetism. By sandwiching a conventional antiferromagnetic monolayer between two identical ferroelectric layers, the out-of-plane polarization cleanly breaks the spatial symmetry to induce robust altermagnetic splitting. Crucially, the global combined parity-time symmetry dictates that reversing the ferroelectric polarization exactly inverts the altermagnetic spin-splitting pattern. We rigorously validate this mechanism in the In2Se3/MnPTe3/In2Se3 trilayer using first-principles calculations. As a direct consequence, the ferroelectrically driven spin-splitting reversal deterministically flips the anomalous Hall effect signal, providing an unambiguous transport fingerprint to electrically distinguish the two altermagnetic states. Unconstrained by the stringent symmetry requirements of intrinsic single-phase materials, our findings establish a versatile physical framework for electrically addressable altermagnetic spintronics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 框架由两部分组成：动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte Carlo, KMC）用于评估给定掺杂剂构型的离子电导率；因子分解机-二次优化退火（factorization machine with quadratic-optimization annealing, FMQA）作为一种基于伊辛机（Ising machine）的黑箱优化算法，从小规模构型-电导率数据集中迭代学习代理模型（surrogate model）并提出预期可最大化电导率的构型。为应对大规模KMC模拟单元中的组合爆炸，采用分区配置空间实现并行优化。

Conclusion: 该框架结合实验后，能够从实测电导率反推微观结构，为理解潜在的输运机制提供洞见。

Abstract: Maximizing ionic conductivity remains a fundamental challenge in the atomistic design of solid electrolytes. To this end, we present a framework that combines kinetic Monte Carlo (KMC) and factorization machine with quadratic-optimization annealing (FMQA), an Ising-machine-based black-box optimization algorithm for large-scale combinatorial optimization. KMC evaluates the ionic conductivity for a given dopant configuration, whereas FMQA iteratively learns a surrogate model from a small configuration-conductivity dataset and proposes configurations expected to maximize conductivity. To address the severe combinatorial explosion in large KMC simulation cells, we partition the configuration space for parallel optimization. As a proof of concept, we apply this KMC-FMQA framework to bulk 8 mol % yttria-stabilized zirconia, identifying a dopant configuration with an order-of-magnitude higher conductivity than that of random configurations and the experimentally reported conductivity. Combined with experiments, this framework will enable the determination of microscopic structures from measured conductivity, providing insight into the underlying transport mechanisms.

### [45] [Three-phonon mixing as a source of light-induced chirality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31356)
*Y . Zhu,A. Vanderhaegen,Z. Zeng,M. Först,M. Fechner,C. Putzke,P. J. W. Moll,D. Prabhakaran,P. Radaelli,A. Cavalleri*

TL;DR: 本文通过硼磷酸盐（BPO₄）的中红外光泵实验，揭示了非共振激发下一种三模耦合（three-mode mixing）机制对光致手性（photo-induced chirality）的贡献，为透明材料中非线性声子线形（nonlinear phononic lineshapes）提供了定量基础，并拓展了晶格操控（lattice control）的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中远红外光脉冲已被广泛用于驱动固体集体模式以超快操控材料功能性质，然而远离共振激发时相关的非线性声子动力学路径尚不明确，需要定量理解。

Method: 以硼磷酸盐（BPO₄）为模型体系，利用中红外激发在原本非手性的晶体中诱导手性，通过改变泵浦脉冲频率（pump frequency），系统对比共振与非共振条件下的光致手性响应。

Result: 共振激发下的光致手性可由双声子混合（two-phonon mixing）导致的声子整流（phonon rectification）解释；当泵浦脉冲偏离共振（detuned from resonance）时，三模耦合（three-mode mixing）机制变得重要，而其他脉冲拉曼项（impulsive Raman terms）的贡献可忽略。

Conclusion: 这些结果为透明材料中非线性声子线形提供了定量基础，并为通过晶格控制实现材料功能超快调控开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Mid- and far-infrared optical pulses have found wide applicability in experiments in which collective modes of solids are driven nonlinearly, as a means to manipulate functional properties of materials on ultrafast time scales. In the illustrative case of boron phosphate (BPO$_4$), mid-infrared excitation has been used to induce chirality in an otherwise achiral crystal. The pump frequency dependence of photo-induced chirality reveals that, while on-resonance excitation is understood in terms of the well-documented phonon rectification from two-phonon mixing, additional pathways become relevant when the pump pulse is detuned from resonance. We find that a three-mode mixing mechanism becomes important in this case, whereas the contributions from other impulsive Raman terms are negligible. The results reported here provide a quantitative foundation for nonlinear phononic lineshapes in transparent materials, and open up new opportunities for lattice control.

Abstract: Ultrafast optical on-off switching of magnetic order promises near-petahertz information processing. Here, we present a high-throughput first-principles screening of the MC3D database of experimentally known inorganic crystals, identifying nearly 440 non-magnetic semiconductors that develop spin polarization under photoexcitation with linearly polarized pulses via a light-induced exchange-driven instability. We determine how the crystal field environment and band-edge orbital character govern the magnitude and the type of magnetic order of the photoinduced state and we unveil systematic chemical and periodic trends that provide intuitive guidance for materials selection. Our results argue that on-off switching of magnetization with linearly polarized femtosecond pulses is a widespread occurrence in non-magnetic semiconductors, opening novel avenues for experimental verification and application.

Conclusion: 观测到的反聚束现象可以通过先前已建立的俄歇猝灭路径来解释，从而证实了高功率下的俄歇猝灭机制，但对CsPb(Cl₁₋ₓBrₓ)₃:Yb³⁺中此前描述的量子剪裁提出了质疑。

Many groups have reproduced absolute photoluminescence quantum yields over 100%, but others have struggled to obtain such high values. Here, we test the quantum-cutting capabilities of CsPbCl3:Yb3+ nanocrystals and bulk material using photon-correlation analysis. A quantum-cutting material is expected to exhibit photon bunching, but our experiments on CsPbCl3:Yb3+ show no such behavior. In fact, we observe the opposite -- anti-bunching -- under focused-excitation conditions. This observation can be explained with the previously established Auger-quenching pathway in CsPbCl3:Yb3+. Conclusion: 侧链工程（side-chain engineering）可作为在金属有机框架（metal-organic framework, MOF）中编程宏观热力学响应的实用途径。

Abstract: Achieving continuous control over macroscopic thermal expansion remains a fundamental challenge in solid-state physics. Using classical and path-integral molecular dynamics alongside lattice dynamics at near-\emph{ab initio} accuracy, we report an entropy-driven thermal-expansion crossover from positive (PTE) to negative thermal expansion (NTE) in alkoxy-functionalized MOF-5, an archetypal metal-organic framework (MOF). We demonstrate that this non-linear response is continuously tunable via the alkoxy side-chain length, quantified by the number of carbon atoms $n$ grafted onto the archetypal cubic MOF-5 framework: systems with short chains ($n \le 2$) exhibit monotonic NTE, whereas longer chains ($n \ge 3$) trigger a pronounced PTE-to-NTE crossover. At low temperatures, thermal activation of longer side chains opens additional conformational states and generates steric pressure inside the pore, driving positive expansion through a gain in side-chain conformational entropy. Conversely, at elevated temperatures, the side chains enhance transverse linker fluctuations and strengthen the string-tension mechanism associated with low-frequency framework modes, causing structural contraction favored by framework vibrational entropy. Finally, by varying the concentration of side-chain-functionalized linkers, the thermal expansion coefficient can be continuously regulated to realize negative, near-zero, and positive thermal expansion within selected temperature windows. These results establish side-chain engineering as a practical route for programming macroscopic thermodynamic responses in MOFs.

</details>


### [50] [Tuning topological phase and Dirac point position via Pb and Sb substitution in Mn$_{1-x}$Pb$_{x}$(Bi$_{1-y}$Sb$_{y}$)$_{2}$Te$_{4}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31525)
*T. P. Makarova,D. A. Estyunin,V. A. Golyashov,K. A. Kokh,O. E. Tereshchenko,A. S. Frolov,S. Ideta,Y. Kumar,K. Shimada,A. M. Shikin*

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了Mn$_{1-x}$Pb$_{x}$(Bi$_{1-y}$Sb$_{y}$)$_{2}$Te$_{4}$晶体在宽浓度范围内的性质，发现体带隙仅由Pb浓度决定，在Pb含量40-50%时发生拓扑相变（topological phase transition）；狄拉克点（Dirac point）位置由Pb/Sb比值而非绝对Sb含量决定；磁性质主要受Mn亚晶格被Pb稀释的影响，对Sb不敏感。同时替代Mn和Bi可实现拓扑相与费米能级（Fermi level）位置的独立调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator）材料中，实现拓扑相与电子结构的独立调控是当前研究的核心问题之一。本研究旨在通过多元素同时替代的策略，探索Mn$_{1-x}$Pb$_{x}$(Bi$_{1-y}$Sb$_{y}$)$_{2}$Te$_{4}$体系中各组分对带隙、狄拉克点位置和磁性质的独立影响机制。

Method: 对Mn$_{1-x}$Pb$_{x}$(Bi$_{1-y}$Sb$_{y}$)$_{2}$Te$_{4}$晶体在x = 10-60%、y = 5-60%的宽浓度范围内进行系统实验研究，通过改变Pb和Sb的替代比例，分别测量体带隙（bulk band gap）、狄拉克点位置和磁性质，分析各组分与这些物理量之间的关联。

Result: 体带隙大小仅由Pb浓度决定，在Pb含量40-50%时带隙闭合，对应拓扑相变；狄拉克点位置由Pb/Sb比值而非Sb绝对含量决定；磁性质依赖于Mn亚晶格被Pb的稀释程度，对Sb含量不敏感。

Conclusion: 通过同时替代Mn和Bi，可以在Mn$_{1-x}$Pb$_{x}$(Bi$_{1-y}$Sb$_{y}$)$_{2}$Te$_{4}$体系中实现拓扑相与费米能级位置的独立控制，为拓扑绝缘体材料的多参数调控提供了新思路。

Abstract: This study presents a systematic investigation of Mn$_{1-x}$Pb$_{x}$(Bi$_{1-y}$Sb$_{y}$)$_{2}$Te$_{4}$ crystals over a wide range of concentrations (x = 10-60%, y = 5-60%). It was found that the value of the bulk band gap is determined exclusively by the Pb concentration and it closes at Pb 40-50 %, which corresponds to a topological phase transition. The position of the Dirac point is determined by the Pb/Sb ratio, rather than the absolute Sb content. The magnetic properties depend on the dilution of the Mn sublattice by Pb and are weakly sensitive to Sb. We show that the simultaneous substitution of Mn and Bi allows independent control of the topological phase and the position of the Fermi level.

### [51] [Geometrically necessary boundaries accommodate the residual elastic strain in cold-rolled Fe-3%Si](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31538)
*Aditya Shukla,Nikolas Mavrikakis,Can Yildirim*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用暗场X射线显微术（DFXM）同时三维映射了50%冷轧Fe-3%Si合金晶粒内的取向差与残余弹性应变场，发现几何必要边界（GNBs）是长程残余弹性应变的主要承载与分布者，而附带位错边界（IDB）结构在GNB限定的子域内发展并携带相近的应变水平，为铁素体钢回复与再结晶建模提供了直接的实验输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在晶内尺度上，变形金属中塑性变形容纳结构与残余弹性应变场之间的关系尚不清晰，主要原因在于缺乏能够同时、三维、体敏地获取位错边界尺度上两种场的实验技术。

Method: 采用暗场X射线显微术（dark-field X-ray microscopy, DFXM），对50%冷轧Fe-3%Si合金的一个晶粒进行三维映射，同时获取晶内取向差（misorientation）和残余弹性应变（residual elastic strain），并非破坏性地解析几何必要边界（GNBs）与附带位错边界（IDB）胞结构。

Result: 弹性应变场与塑性变形亚结构的关联分析表明：GNBs是长程残余弹性应变的主要承载者和分布者，将晶粒体积分隔为具有不同平均d-spacing的子域；IDBs和位错胞相关的塑性取向差则在GNB限定的子域内发展，并携带较为相近的弹性应变值。

Conclusion: 这支持了一种机制图像：在变形状态下，GNBs容纳了几乎所有长程残余弹性应变，而塑性滑移延伸至GNB内部，组织成应变水平相近的IDB胞结构。所量化的三维取向差与应变梯度为铁素体钢（如电工钢）的回复与再结晶建模提供了直接的实验输入。

Abstract: The relationship between plastic deformation accommodation structures and residual elastic strain fields in deformed metals is poorly understood at the intragranular scale, largely because no experimental technique has provided simultaneous, three-dimensional, bulk-sensitive access to both fields at the length scale of dislocation boundaries. Here we use dark-field X-ray microscopy (DFXM) to map intragranular misorientation and residual elastic strain simultaneously in three dimensions within a grain of 50% cold-rolled Fe 3%Si alloy. We resolve geometrically necessary boundaries (GNBs) and incidental dislocation boundary (IDB) cell structures in the bulk non-destructively. Correlating the elastic strain field with the segmented plastically deformed substructure reveals that GNBs act as the primary carriers and distributors of long range residual elastic strain. GNBs separate subdomains of distinct mean d-spacing, across the grain volume. The plastic misorientation associated with IDBs and dislocation cells develops within GNB-delimited subdomains that carry comparatively similar values of elastic strain. This supports a mechanistic picture in which GNBs accommodate nearly all the long-range residual elastic strain in the deformed state, while plastic slip propagates into GNB interiors to organize into IDB cells with similar strain levels. The three-dimensional misorientation and strain gradients quantified here provide direct experimental input for recovery and recrystallization modelling in ferritic steels, such as electrical steels.

### [52] [Growth optimization of shallow Ge quantum wells grown by molecular beam epitaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31540)
*J. T. Dong,J. P. Thompson,R. Card,K. Sardashti,C. J. K. Richardson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 系统优化了MBE生长条件，利用厚缓冲层（buffer layer）消除特定缺陷，并确定了最佳生长温度。对样品进行了低温迁移率测量与迁移率建模分析。

Result: 在22纳米深的Ge量子阱中，于2K温度下获得了105,000 cm²/Vs的空穴迁移率（hole mobility）峰值，这是目前浅层MBE生长样品中的最高值。迁移率建模表明，生长温度优化带来的迁移率提升主要归因于界面粗糙度散射（interface roughness scattering）的降低。

Conclusion: 通过生长条件优化，MBE生长的Ge量子阱性能得到显著提升；进一步改善迁移率有望通过改进表面钝化（surface passivation）实现。

Abstract: Shallow strained Ge quantum wells have gained recent attention for realizing scalable, high-performance hybrid superconductor/semiconductor-based qubits. Epitaxial superconducting contacts can improve the quality and consistency of the superconductor/semiconductor interface. The growth of Ge quantum wells by molecular beam epitaxy is then motivating due to the relative ease of integration with epitaxial superconductor growth. However, the performance of Ge quantum wells grown by molecular beam epitaxy (MBE) has been limited. To improve the properties of MBE-grown Ge quantum wells, the growth conditions were systematically optimized. Thick buffer layers are utilized to eliminate certain defects, and an optimal growth temperature is found. A peak hole mobility of 105,000 cm\textsuperscript{2}/Vs at 2 K is obtained in a 22-nm deep Ge quantum well, demonstrating that the Ge quantum wells grown in this study represent the highest mobilities for shallow MBE-grown samples. Mobility modeling indicates that the increase in mobility due to growth temperature optimization are likely due to a reduction in interface roughness scattering, and further improvements in mobility are expected through improved surface passivation.

### [53] [Spin-related transport in a polycrystalline NiCo2O4 film: Drastic current-induced change in resistivity-temperature characteristics via spin injection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31563)
*Shiho Sugiyama,Masaaki Tanaka,Ryosho Nakane*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过测量多晶NiCo2O4薄膜在不同电流和温度下的电阻率-温度（ρ-T）特性，发现随电流增大，ρ-T曲线从半导体型转变为金属型，并建立了包含自旋排列空间依赖性的自旋相关输运模型，揭示了晶界附近缺陷区域的居里温度增强和自旋注入效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于NiCo2O4（NCO）理论上具有半金属性（half-metallicity），研究其在硅基高性能自旋输运器件（spin-transport devices）中的应用潜力。

Method: 系统测量在MgAl2O4/Si(001)衬底上生长的多晶NCO薄膜的电阻率-温度（ρ-T）依赖关系，变化面内电流（100 nA至1 mA）和温度（4至290 K），并结合电流-电压和磁电阻测量。

Result: 随电流增大，ρ-T曲线从半导体型（dρ/dT<0）经非单调型转变为金属型（dρ/dT>0）。100 nA下呈现多晶缺陷NCO特征，1 mA下则呈现外延少缺陷NCO特征。这种电流诱导演化反映了晶界附近缺陷区域居里温度（Curie temperature）的增强以及自旋排列（spin alignment）的增强。

Conclusion: 提出了一个扩展传统跳跃导电模型的自旋相关输运模型，该模型包含自旋排列对温度和电流的依赖性及其在多晶NCO中的空间分布。分析表明从晶粒体到晶界的自旋注入增强了晶界的自旋排列和双交换相互作用（double-exchange interactions），从而促进导电。该模型得到电流-电压和磁电阻特征的进一步支持。

Abstract: We have studied spin-related transport in a polycrystalline NiCo2O4 (NCO) film on a MgAl2O4/Si(001) substrate, motivated by potential applications of the theoretical half-metallicity of NCO to Si-based high-performance spin-transport devices. Our approach is to systematically measure and analyze the temperature dependence of the film's resistivity ($ρ-T$) with various in-plane currents (100 nA$-$1 mA) and temperatures (4$-$290 K). With increasing current, the $ρ-T$ curve changes drastically from semiconducting ($dρ/dT<0$) to non-monotonic and eventually toward metallic ($dρ/dT>0$). A distinctive feature is that the single NCO film exhibits a $ρ-T$ characteristic of polycrystalline defective NCO at 100 nA, whereas it exhibits a $ρ-T$ characteristic of epitaxial less-defective NCO over a wide temperature range at 1 mA. This current-induced evolution of $ρ-T$ reflects the enhancement of the Curie temperature of defective regions near grain boundaries, accompanied by enhanced spin alignment there. We proposed a spin-related transport model that extends conventional hopping conduction models by incorporating the temperature- and current-dependent degree of spin alignment, as well as its spatial dependence inherent to polycrystalline NCO. This model comprehensively explains the interplay between the spin-alignment profile and transport mechanism. The analysis reveals that spin injection from grain bodies to grain boundaries enhances the spin alignment there and strengthens double-exchange interactions, facilitating conduction. This phenomenon strongly depends on both temperature and current. Our findings provide evidence of spin-polarized electrons inside the grain bodies, highlighting the potential of our polycrystalline NCO film as an efficient spin source. The present model is further supported by current$-$voltage and magnetoresistance features.

Conclusion: 非晶态In-Zn-O薄膜，特别是Zn/(In+Zn)比约为0.12且呈现适度缺氧（intermediate oxygen deficiency）的成分，可作为有效且透明的导电铜扩散阻挡层，适用于光伏电池应用。

Abstract: In light of the increasing supply chain concerns regarding silver for solar cell metallization, the replacement of the silver contacts by copper is desirable. As copper diffuses readily in silicon, deposition of an additional diffusion barrier to protect the respective absorber material stacks is required. We investigate multifunctional layers of transparent conductive oxides (TCOs) from the In-Zn-O system to serve as front electrode and Cu diffusion barrier coating, focusing on purely amorphous layers without grain boundaries to impede copper diffusion. We employ a 2D combinatorial approach to simultaneously screen the Zn/(In+Zn) ratio and the oxygen content in a single materials library deposited by magnetron sputtering without intentional substrate heating. Cu diffusion barrier performance was evaluated by depositing Cu on top of intentionally ultrathin In-Zn-O libraries of 7 nm on silicon wafers and annealing them at temperatures of 200-450°C. Both the formation of copper silicides, as well as the silicon photoluminescence signal were monitored. The first was detected only after the crystallization of the In-Zn-O films and required annealing temperatures of 450°C and above. Even for extended dwell times of 20 h at a relevant process temperature of 200°C, we find no evidence of Cu ingress for most of our fabricated In-Zn-O compositions, whereas Si/Cu stacks without In-Zn-O barriers showed a reduction of their photo-luminescence intensity already after less than 1 h. These results suggest thin amorphous In-Zn-O films with an optimal Zn/(In+Zn) ratio of ~0.12 and intermediate oxygen deficiency as effective transparent conductive Cu diffusion barriers for solar cell applications.

### [56] [A technical report on the surface-energy and morphology-based screening for electrode/electrolyte interface compatibility in SOFC/ReSOC materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31828)
*Guido Violano,Luciano Afferrante*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于表面特性的方法论，通过接触角测量（水与甘油）和共聚焦形貌分析，构建电极-电解质配对的兼容性矩阵，作为固体氧化物电池（solid oxide cells）早期预电化学筛选工具，以优先评估界面兼容性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过水和甘油的接触角测量，采用Owens-Wendt-Rabel-Kaelble方法确定总表面自由能、色散分量和极性分量；利用共聚焦形貌（confocal topography）提取ISO 25178粗糙度参数，包括平均粗糙度、峰谷高度、谷深、偏度、峰度和表面斜率；结合能量亲和力与形态适配性构建兼容性矩阵，重点分析电解质表面。

Result: 具有最佳兼容性的界面并非表面自由能（surface free energy）最高的组合，而是那些兼具高黏附功（adhesion work）、低界面能（interfacial energy）以及适合连续电极沉积的基底形貌的组合。

Conclusion: 该表面方法可作为合理的预电化学筛选工具，用于优先排序电极-电解质组合，后续通过电化学阻抗谱（electrochemical impedance spectroscopy）、面积比电阻、接触电阻、微观结构分析和耐久性测试进行验证；虽不能替代电化学表征，但为连接表面化学、形貌与界面形成提供了物理基础。

Abstract: The performance and durability of solid oxide fuel cells and reversible solid oxide cells are strongly affected by the electrode-electrolyte interface, where charge transfer, ionic transport, adhesion, morphology and thermomechanical stability interact. Early-stage compatibility screening is usually based on electrochemical or compositional criteria, whereas surface-related descriptors are rarely included in a unified framework. This work proposes a surface-based methodology to assess the expected compatibility of candidate electrode-electrolyte pairings. Contact-angle measurements with water and glycerol are used to determine total, dispersive and polar surface free energy components through the Owens-Wendt-Rabel-Kaelble method. Confocal topography is used to extract ISO 25178 roughness parameters, including average roughness, peak-to-valley height, valley depth, skewness, kurtosis and surface slope. A compatibility matrix is constructed by combining energetic affinity and morphological suitability, with emphasis on the electrolyte surface, since the electrode is deposited directly onto the electrolyte substrate. The results indicate that the most promising interfaces are not necessarily those with the highest surface free energy, but those combining high adhesion work, low interfacial energy and a substrate morphology suitable for continuous electrode deposition. The proposed approach provides a rational pre-electrochemical screening tool to prioritize electrode-electrolyte combinations for subsequent validation by electrochemical impedance spectroscopy, area specific resistance, electrical contact resistance, microstructural analysis and durability testing. Although it does not replace electrochemical characterization, it offers a physically grounded way to connect surface chemistry, topography and interface formation in solid oxide cell materials.

</details>


### [57] [Giant perpendicular Edelstein polarization in 2D compensated magnets via bichromatic Floquet driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31867)
*Mohsen Yarmohammadi,Daegeun Jo,Marco Berritta,Libor Šmejkal,James K. Freericks,Peter M. Oppeneer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文证明，通过结合 Rashba 自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）与双色 Floquet 驱动（bichromatic Floquet driving），可以在二维交变磁体（altermagnets）及更广泛的反常自旋极化磁体中激活巨大的垂直埃德斯坦极化（perpendicular Edelstein polarizations, PEPs），而单色驱动无法实现这一效果。该机制由系统磁宇称（magnetic parity）和第二束激光谐波（harmonics）决定的普适选择定则（universal selection rules）所支配，为垂直磁写入（perpendicular memory writing）提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为，在具有高阶谐波（如d波交变磁体）的反常磁体中，自旋-群对称性（spin-group symmetries）严格禁止非相对论性埃德斯坦极化（nonrelativistic Edelstein polarization）响应。因此，寻找能够突破这一对称性限制并在此类材料中实现有效自旋-电荷转换的物理机制，是本研究的主要驱动力。

Method: 将 Rashba 自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）与双色 Floquet 驱动相结合，具体包括双线性（bilinear）、双圆偏振（bicircular）和圆-线偏振（circular-linear）等双频率驱动构型。双频率驱动通过动态打破二重旋转对称性（two-fold rotational symmetry），在材料中引入无杂散场的面内类塞曼场（in-plane Zeeman-like field）。

Result: 双色 Floquet 驱动在二维交变磁体及更广泛的反常自旋极化磁体中激活了巨大的垂直埃德斯坦极化（PEPs），响应强度达 0.5–1.5 μ_B，且以轨道磁矩（orbital contribution）为主导。该巨大响应的产生受控于普适选择定则，该定则与系统的磁宇称以及第二束激光的谐波直接相关。

Conclusion: 所发现的巨大垂直埃德斯坦极化为实现垂直磁写入提供了强有力的物理机制，拓展了交变磁体在自旋电子学（spintronics）中的应用前景。

Abstract: While unconventional $p$-wave magnets can generate nonrelativistic Edelstein polarizations, spin-group symmetries strictly forbid these responses in unconventional magnets with higher-order harmonics, such as $d$-wave altermagnets. Here, we demonstrate that combining Rashba spin-orbit coupling with bichromatic Floquet driving activates giant perpendicular Edelstein polarizations (PEPs) across 2D altermagnets and broader classes of unconventional spin-polarized magnets -- a feat monochromatic driving cannot achieve. By dynamically breaking two-fold rotational symmetry, the two-frequency drive (including bilinear, bicircular, and circular-linear configurations) induces a stray-field-free in-plane Zeeman-like field that generates orbitally dominated PEPs (0.5--1.5 $μ_{\rm B}$). This massive response is governed by universal selection rules tied to the system's magnetic parity and the second beam's harmonics. These emergent PEPs provide a powerful mechanism for perpendicular memory writing.

</details>


### [58] [Proximity-Induced Skyrmion Stabilization at the Cu2OSeO3/Bi2Se3 Interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31896)
*Sina Mehboodi,Victor Ukleev,Chen Luo,Radu-Marius Abrudan,Jie Xiao,Ronny Golnak,Florin Radu,Matthias Kronseder,Christian H. Back,Aisha Aqeel*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过宽频铁磁共振谱与共振弹性X射线散射实验，研究了拓扑绝缘体Bi2Se3与手性磁绝缘体Cu2OSeO3界面处邻近诱导的磁相互作用。结果表明，界面处存在两种共存的手性自旋纹理（skyrmion）相，且界面态比体态具有更宽的磁场稳定区间，验证了界面工程可有效增强拓扑磁异质结构中手性自旋纹理的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索拓扑绝缘体与手性磁绝缘体界面处邻近诱导的磁相互作用，特别是低温斯格明子（skyrmion）相的稳定性增强机制，为拓扑磁异质结（topological-magnetic heterostructures）中非共线自旋纹理的调控提供界面工程途径。

Method: 采用宽频铁磁共振（broadband ferromagnetic resonance）谱学技术，并结合场循环（field cycling）方法分辨斯格明子共振分支；进一步使用共振弹性X射线散射（resonant elastic x-ray scattering）测量验证界面相的磁场范围。

Result: 在Cu2OSeO3/Bi2Se3异质结中观察到额外共振模式，并分辨出两个逆时针斯格明子共振分支（间隔约238 MHz），对应体斯格明子晶格（bulk skyrmion lattice）与界面斯格明子相（interfacial skyrmion phase）共存。界面斯格明子相在磁场中具有比体相更宽的温度-磁场稳定区间。

Conclusion: 邻近诱导的交换耦合（proximity-induced exchange coupling）与界面Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction）增强是界面斯格明子相稳定性的关键机制。界面工程可有效拓展斯格明子相与倾斜锥形相（tilted conical phase）的稳定区间，为拓扑磁异质结构中的自旋纹理调控提供新策略。

Abstract: We investigate proximity-induced magnetic interactions at the interface between the topological insulator Bi2Se3 and the chiral magnetic insulator Cu2OSeO3, with particular focus on the low temperature skyrmion phase. Broadband ferromagnetic resonance spectroscopy reveals enhanced stability of noncollinear spin textures in the Cu2OSeO3/Bi2Se3 heterostructure compared with bare Cu2OSeO3. In addition to an extra resonance mode in the tilted conical phase that is absent in bare Cu2OSeO3, field cycling resolves two counterclockwise skyrmion resonance branches separated by approximately 238 MHz, consistent with the coexistence of a bulk skyrmion lattice and an interfacial skyrmion phase stabilized by proximity-induced exchange coupling and enhanced interfacial Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions. The finite frequency separation indicates that the two skyrmion phases occupy distinct magnetic energy landscapes while retaining similar resonance character. Resonant elastic x-ray scattering measurements further confirm that the interfacial skyrmion phase spans a broader magnetic-field range than the bulk phase, demonstrating enhanced stability and ordering of topological spin textures at the interface. These findings establish interface engineering as a promising route for extending the stability regime of skyrmion and tilted-conical phases in topological-magnetic heterostructures.

</details>


### [59] [What enables GaOx as hole transport layer for a 16 percent 1.0 eV CuInSe2 Bottom Cells with VOC above 550 mV?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31923)
*Francesco Lodola,Zhuangyi Zhou,Boaz Koren,Saeed Bayat,Alessandro Magon,Yucheng Hu,Adrian-Marie Philippe,Michele Melchiorre,Hasan Arif Yetkin,Gunnar Kusch,Nathalie Valle,Rachel A. Oliver,Susanne Siebentritt*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高效非外延光伏技术中，仅黄铜矿（chalcopyrite）材料可实现低至1.00 eV的带隙可调性，适合叠层应用。GaOx虽被证明是有效的空穴传输层（hole transport layer），但在含铟透明背接触的双面太阳能电池中会形成有害层。因此需要探究使GaOx层具备导电性的具体条件。

Method: 采用共蒸发低带隙吸收层过程中通过离子交换（ion exchange）形成的GaOx空穴传输层。系统研究了额外Cu、Na以及溅射氧化层过程中的氧流量对GaOx导电性的影响。

Result: 发现无需额外Cu、无需Na、氧流量也无系统性影响。GaOx层部分结晶（partly crystalline）。优化的钝化空穴传输层使CuInSe2底电池活性区效率超过16%，并实现了552 meV的认证开路电压记录。

Conclusion: 在特定条件下形成的GaOx层可具备导电性，从而作为有效的钝化空穴传输层，使基于CuInSe2的低带隙底电池在不依赖Ag或重碱金属的情况下实现高效性能。

Abstract: Among the highly efficient photovoltaic technologies, that do not rely on epitaxy, only chalcopyrites have a bandgap tunable down to 1.00 eV, the ideal for tandem applications. This is obtained with a pure CuInSe2 absorber without Ga. GaOx has been shown to be an efficient hole transport layer that prevents recombination at the metallic back contact. On the other hand, GaOx has proven detrimental, when it forms on In containing transparent back contacts in bifacial solar cells. Here, we investigate the conditions that make the GaOx layer conductive. We employ a GaOx hole transport layer that is formed through ion exchange during co-evaporation of the low band gap absorber layer. We find that no additional Cu is needed, and that Na is not necessary for a conductive GaOx. Nor did we find a systematic influence of oxygen flow during the sputtering process of the oxide layer. The GaOx layer is partly crystalline. The optimized passivating hole transport layer enables a CuInSe2 bottom solar cell, without any addition of Ag or heavy alkalis, with an active area efficiency above 16% and a record-certified open-circuit voltage VOC of 552meV

### [60] [Magnetic Bloch Oscillations in Odd-Wave Magnets and the Nonlinear Edelstein Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30732)
*Jonas Habel,Johannes Knolle*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出在奇宇称磁体（odd-wave magnets）中，磁化强度可呈现类似布洛赫振荡（Bloch oscillations）的阻尼振荡行为（称为“磁布洛赫振荡”），并最终弛豫至稳态埃德尔斯坦值（Edelstein value）；该效应通过一维p波磁体的最小模型和二维推广得到解析与数值验证，且可通过太赫兹亚周期光谱中的高次谐波产生进行实验检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究主要关注电荷输运中的布洛赫振荡现象，但电荷载流子同时具有自旋自由度，因此自然产生一个开放问题：磁学可观测量中是否也能出现布洛赫振荡。本文旨在探讨这一问题。

Method: 采用解析与数值方法，构建一维p波磁体的最小模型（minimal one-dimensional model of a p-wave magnet）作为出发点，并将结果推广至二维情形。通过弛豫动力学分析，刻画磁化强度从瞬态振荡到稳态埃德尔斯坦值的演化过程。

Result: 奇宇称磁体的磁化强度在弛豫至稳态埃德尔斯坦值之前，可经历磁布洛赫振荡；此外，埃德尔斯坦磁化强度（Edelstein magnetization）对外加电场呈普遍的非线性依赖关系。该效应可通过太赫兹亚周期光波谱学（THz sub-cycle lightwave spectroscopy）中的高次谐波产生进行实验检测。

Conclusion: 磁布洛赫振荡为非常规磁体中自旋-电荷耦合（spin-charge coupling）提供了一种本质上的非平衡态特征信号，拓展了布洛赫振荡现象从电荷到磁学自由度的适用范围，并为实验检测提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Bloch oscillations (BOs) are a quantum phenomenon in which electrons subjected to an electric field in a periodic potential exhibit an oscillating current without a net drift. In real conductors, scattering reduces the coherence required for BOs driving the system toward a steady state with a DC current. While previous studies have focused on charge transport, charge carriers also possess spin, raising the question of whether BOs can emerge in magnetic observables. Here, we show that the magnetization of odd-wave magnets can undergo BOs before relaxing to the steady-state Edelstein value, a phenomenon we term $\textit{magnetic}$ BOs. Using analytical and numerical methods, we demonstrate this effect in a minimal one-dimensional model of a p-wave magnet and generalize it to two dimensions. Our analysis further reveals that the Edelstein magnetization is generically nonlinear in the applied electric field. Finally, we argue that magnetic BOs can be detected in materials through higher-harmonic generation in THz sub-cycle lightwave spectroscopy. Magnetic BOs provide a genuine non-equilibrium signature of spin-charge coupling in unconventional magnets.

</details>


### [61] [The competition between low-temperature kinks and magnons at the vicinity of the deconfinement transition point in 1D easy-axis XXZ ferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31000)
*P. N. Bibikov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究一维易轴XXZ铁磁体中退禁闭相变点附近的有序相与量子超临界低温区，提出由不同低能激发主导的物理解释：两个有序相由磁子（magnons）主导，量子超临界区则由扭结（kinks）主导，并以伊辛模型（Ising model）为例进行详细处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解一维易轴XXZ铁磁体在退禁闭相变点附近的有序相与量子超临界（quantum supercritical）低温区的物理本质，并建立其与主导低能激发类型之间的对应关系。

Method: 通过分析退禁闭相变点附近有序相与量子超临界区的低能激发谱（low-energy excitations），确定各区域的主导激发类型：磁子（magnons）对应有序相，扭结（kinks）对应量子超临界区，并对伊辛模型（Ising model）进行详细处理。

Result: 发现两个有序相均由磁子激发主导，而量子超临界低温区则由扭结激发主导。

Conclusion: 一维易轴XXZ铁磁体的退禁闭相变点附近，有序相与量子超临界区分别由不同类型低能激发（磁子与扭结）主导，该解释框架可推广至伊辛模型的详细分析。

Abstract: Studying the ordered phases and quantum supercritical low-temperature regime at the vicinity of the deconfinement transition point in 1D easy-axis XXZ ferromagnet, we suggest their interpretations according to the corresponding dominant lowest-energy excitations. We show, that the two ordered phases are governed by magnons, while the quantum supercritical regime is governed by kinks. Within this framework the Ising model is treated in detail.

### [62] [Investigation of the $J_1$-$J_2$ Heisenberg model on the triangular lattice: A study with projected entangled-pair states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31021)
*Litao Ma,Wei-Lin Tu,Didier Poilblanc,Ji-Yao Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本工作采用无限投影纠缠对态（infinite PEPS）系统研究三角晶格阻挫 $J_1$-$J_2$ 海森堡模型，发现 $120^\circ$ Néel 态在 $J_2/J_1\approx 0.08$ 处直接转变为量子自旋液体（QSL），并通过对称性分析指出该 QSL 相最有可能是无能隙的 U(1) Dirac 自旋液体，而非 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 拓扑有序相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三角晶格上阻挫 $J_1$-$J_2$ 海森堡模型中的量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid, QSL）相的性质仍然是悬而未决且活跃争论的问题，亟需更精确的数值研究以澄清其基态性质。

Method: 采用无限投影纠缠对态（infinite projected entangled-pair state, PEPS）方法，在不同对称性约束下系统研究该模型；构建了完全对称的 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 共振价键（Resonating Valence Bond, RVB）态，并进一步扩展至更大键维度（bond dimension, $D$）的 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 对称 PEPS（最高 $D=7$）。

Result: 发现 $120^\circ$ Néel 态在 $J_2/J_1\approx 0.08$ 处直接转变为 QSL，磁有序坍缩；通过幺正旋转或自发自旋长程序，条纹反铁磁相也可被无限 PEPS 精确描述。在波函数优化中，自旋子（spinon）凝聚且拓扑涡旋激发（vison）被禁闭，排除了 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 拓扑有序，强有力地表明 QSL 相是无能隙的（gapless）。

Conclusion: 三角晶格 $J_1$-$J_2$ 海森堡模型中的 QSL 相最自然地与 U(1) Dirac 自旋液体（U(1) Dirac spin liquid）图像一致，而非 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 拓扑有序相。

Abstract: The nature of the quantum spin liquid (QSL) phase in the frustrated $J_1$-$J_2$ Heisenberg model on the triangular lattice remains an open and actively debated problem. In this work, we employ the infinite projected entangled-pair state (PEPS) to systematically investigate the model under different symmetry constraints. Our simulations reveal a direct transition from the $120^\circ$ Néel state to a putative QSL at $J_2/J_1\approx 0.08$, signaled by the collapse of magnetic order. We further show that, through either an appropriate unitary rotation or spontaneous spin long-range order, the stripe antiferromagnetic phase can also be accurately captured within the infinite PEPS framework. A central focus of our study is the role played by the PEPS symmetry in approximating the QSL ground-state sandwiched between the two magnetic phases. We first found that a fully-symmetric topological $\mathbb{Z}_2$ Resonating Valence Bond state, which can be written as a simple PEPS with bond dimension $D=3$, exhibits a reasonably good variational energy. Motivated by this finding, we have further constructed generic $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric PEPS of larger bond dimension (up to $D=7$). We found that, under wavefunction optimization, spinons condense and, simultaneously, topological vison excitations get confined, hence precluding $\mathbb{Z}_2$ topological order. This strongly indicates the gapless (or critical) nature of the QSL phase, which is most naturally consistent with a U(1) Dirac spin liquid scenario.

### [63] [Nonlinear topological laser based on multipole insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31067)
*Zi-Yuan Li,Zi-Xiang Hu,Qi Li*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了二维Benalcazar-Bernevig-Hughes (BBH)模型中的高阶拓扑绝缘体（HOTI），通过将激光模式限制在拓扑角态或边缘态，证明了长时间演化后的稳定光激发主要由模型哈密顿量的拓扑性质决定；引入多个诊断比率（如角态衰减比τ₁、边角比τ₂和角间转移比χ）来量化拓扑特征，并揭示了拓扑相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维高阶拓扑绝缘体（higher-order topological insulators, HOTIs）具有独特的边缘态和角态，为开发高阶拓扑激光器提供了理想平台；然而，如何从系统的动力学演化中有效提取拓扑特征并实现可控的激光激发仍是一个关键问题。

Method: 采用Benalcazar-Bernevig-Hughes (BBH)模型作为研究对象，该模型具有量子化的四极矩和拓扑保护的角态与边缘态；通过控制增益将激光模式限制在选定的拓扑角态或边缘态，并引入角态衰减比τ₁、边角比τ₂和角间转移比χ等诊断比率来表征拓扑特征。

Result: 长时间演化后的稳定光激发主要由模型哈密顿量的拓扑性质决定；τ₁和τ₂随跳跃参数γ/λ的突变直接揭示了拓扑相变；通过调节晶格位点奇偶性可灵活调控角态的局域位置；角态与边缘态之间的双稳态难以实现。

Conclusion: 所提出的诊断比率提供了一套从系统动力学演化中提取拓扑特征的综合工具集，为高阶拓扑激光器的设计和工作机制提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Two-dimensional higher-order topological insulators (HOTIs), characterized by distinctive one-dimensional edge states and zero-dimensional corner states, provide an ideal platform for developing higher-order topological lasers. In this work, we systematically investigate the two-dimensional Benalcazar-Bernevig-Hughes (BBH) model, which hosts quantized quadrupole moments and topologically protected corner and edge states. By confining the lasing mode to selected topological corner or edge states under controlled gain, we demonstrate that the stable light excitation achieved after long-time evolution is predominantly determined by the topological properties of the model Hamiltonian. To characterize the system's topological features, we introduce several diagnostic ratios: the corner decay ratio $τ_{1}$ and edge-to-corner ratio $τ_{2}$ quantify the localization degree and spatial extent of corner states, respectively, while the inter-corner transfer ratio $χ$ measures the intensity transfer efficiency mediated by coherent edge-state dynamics. The abrupt changes in $τ_{1}$ and $τ_{2}$ as functions of the hopping parameter $γ/λ$ directly reveal topological phase transitions, providing a comprehensive toolkit for extracting topological signatures from the system's dynamical evolution. Additionally, modulating the lattice site parity enables flexible tuning of corner state localization positions, offering insights for device engineering. Our calculations reveal that achieving bistability between corner states and edge states is relatively challenging.

</details>


### [64] [Phonon-induced pseudogap phase in TiSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31298)
*Sotirios Fragkos,Nina Girotto Erhardt,Evgenia Symeonidou,Hibiki Orio,Dominique Descamps,Stéphane Petit,Polychronis Tsipas,Kai Rossnagel,Jakub Schusser,Athanasios Dimoulas,Samuel Beaulieu,Dino Novko*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用时间分辨极紫外光电子能谱和第一性原理电子-声子计算，对三种1T相过渡金属二硫族化合物（TMDCs）在室温下的正常态电子结构进行了激发态能带映射。研究发现，强电子-声子诱导的热涨落对正常相电子结构有深远影响：在中等耦合体系中（HfTe₂、ZrTe₂）仅导致谱展宽和能带重整化，而在强耦合体系（TiSe₂）中则观测到软声子诱导的动量依赖谱权重抑制（赝能隙）。该工作确立了TiSe₂的正常相为声子诱导的赝能隙相，受强电荷密度波（CDW）涨落主导，完善了其相图并推广至其他强电子-声子耦合TMDCs。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用时间分辨角分辨极紫外光电子能谱（time- and angle-resolved extreme ultraviolet photoemission spectroscopy）和第一性原理电子-声子计算（ab initio electron-phonon calculations），对三种典型的1T相TMDCs（TiSe₂、HfTe₂、ZrTe₂）在室温下进行激发态能带映射（excited state band mapping）。

Result: 在中等电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）体系（HfTe₂、ZrTe₂）中，热涨落仅导致小的谱展宽（spectral broadening）和能带重整化（band renormalization）；在强耦合体系（TiSe₂）中，观测到软声子诱导（soft-phonon-induced）、动量依赖的谱权重抑制（momentum-dependent suppression of spectral weight），即赝能隙（pseudogaps），其延伸至费米能级以上约1 eV。

Conclusion: TiSe₂的正常相被确立为声子诱导的赝能隙相（phonon-induced pseudogap phase），受强CDW涨落主导，从而揭示了TiSe₂相图中此前缺失的方面，并对其他处于强电子-声子耦合区域的TMDCs具有更广泛的启示意义。

Abstract: To comprehend quantum ordered states, such as charge density waves (CDW), in layered transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDCs), it is essential to uncover their underlying normal states. Here, we use time- and angle-resolved extreme ultraviolet photoemission spectroscopy and ab initio electron-phonon calculations to perform excited state band mapping of three prototypical 1T TMDCs, i.e., TiSe$_2$, HfTe$_2$, and ZrTe$_2$, at room temperature. The results reveal the profound impact of strong electron-phonon-induced thermal fluctuations on the normal-phase electronic structure. Specifically, in the moderate electron-phonon coupling regime, as in HfTe$_2$ and ZrTe$_2$, thermal fluctuations only lead to small spectral broadening and band renormalization. In the strongly coupled case, exemplified by TiSe$_2$, we observe soft-phonon-induced, momentum-dependent suppression of spectral weight, i.e., pseudogaps - extending up to 1 eV above the Fermi level. Our work establishes the normal phase of TiSe$_2$ as a phonon-induced pseudogap phase governed by strong CDW fluctuations, thereby uncovering previously missing aspects of the TiSe$_2$ phase diagram, with broader implications for other TMDCs in the strong electron-phonon coupling regime.

### [65] [Ultrafast Fluence-Reversal Fingerprint of Fragile Kondo Hybridization in CePt$_2$In$_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31361)
*Xin-Yi Tian,Qi-Yi Wu,Chen Zhang,Hao Liu,Yang Luo,Bo Chen,Ying Zhou,Zhong-Tuo Fu,Jin-Dong Bai,Chun-Hui Lyu,Zi-Jie Xu,Hai-Long Deng,Hai-Yun Liu,Jun He,Yu-Xia Duan,Jian-Qiao Meng*

TL;DR: 本文利用飞秒泵浦-探测反射率技术研究弱杂化近藤晶格化合物CePt₂In₇，发现其准粒子弛豫行为随温度和泵浦通量呈现非单调反转，揭示Kondo杂化能隙是一个可动态重构的脆弱多体态，而非刚性电子结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用飞秒泵浦-探测反射率（femtosecond pump-probe reflectivity）对弱杂化近藤晶格化合物CePt₂In₇进行测量，结合拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）识别相干光学声子作为内禀晶格温度计，提取无声子贡献的电子振幅A_elec以分析非线性电子响应。

Result: 在低通量下，低于T*≈40K出现慢速准粒子弛豫通道，符合Rothwarf-Taylor瓶颈（Rothwarf-Taylor bottleneck）响应，低能重组能标2Δ≈7.4meV。电子振幅A_elec呈现通量反转特征：从杂化交叉区（hybridization-crossover regime）的弱线性行为，转变为Rothwarf-Taylor瓶颈抑制，最终在最低温下出现反常高通量增强。

Conclusion: 该反转现象无法用刚性固定能隙的瓶颈模型解释，而是揭示了光致重分布（photoinduced redistribution）的脆弱Kondo杂化电子响应的超快光学特征，支持Kondo杂化能隙为可动态重构的脆弱多体态。

Abstract: The emergence of heavy quasiparticles in a Kondo lattice is usually viewed as the formation of a low-energy hybridization gap. Whether this gap represents a rigid electronic structure or a fragile many-body state that can be dynamically reconfigured remains a central question for heavy-fermion systems near magnetic order, quantum criticality, and unconventional superconductivity. Here we use femtosecond pump-probe reflectivity to interrogate this problem in the weakly hybridized Kondo-lattice compound CePt$_2$In$_7$. At low fluence, a slow quasiparticle relaxation channel emerges below $T^* \sim$ 40 K and follows a Rothwarf-Taylor bottleneck response with a low-energy recombination scale 2$Δ\approx$ 7.4 meV. Coherent optical phonons, independently identified by Raman spectroscopy, act as an internal lattice thermometer and rule out large quasi-equilibrium lattice heating as the origin of the nonlinear electronic response. The phonon-free electronic amplitude $A_{\rm elec}$ reveals a fluence-reversal fingerprint: with cooling from the hybridization-crossover regime, the response evolves from weak-linear behavior to Rothwarf-Taylor-like bottleneck suppression and finally to anomalous high-fluence enhancement at the lowest temperatures. This reversal cannot be accounted for by a rigid fixed-gap bottleneck alone and instead identifies an ultrafast optical signature of photoinduced redistribution of a fragile Kondo-hybridized electronic response.

### [66] [The exceptional origin of the strange metal and the LFL-HFL transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31810)
*Eoin Quinn*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于超共形代数（superconformal algebra）D(2,1;α) 的代数框架来描述强关联电子的奇异金属（strange metal）态。该代数可通过两种不同的缩并（contraction）分别得到朗道-费米液体（LFL）和哈伯德-费米液体（HFL）的代数结构，二者之间的竞争产生了奇异金属态。论文推导了一个无参数的预测公式，并刻画了低温下的相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异金属态是强关联电子系统中一个长期未解的难题，其行为偏离传统的朗道-费米液体（Landau-Fermi liquid, LFL）理论。现有理论缺乏统一的代数框架来描述奇异金属、LFL 以及可能存在的其他金属态之间的内在关联。

Method: 采用例外超共形代数 D(2,1;α) 作为出发点，通过对其共形部分进行两种不同的缩并（contraction），分别得到对应于 LFL 的规范费米子（canonical fermions）代数，以及对应于哈伯德-费米液体（Hubbard-Fermi liquid, HFL）的哈伯德算子（Hubbard operators）代数。将奇异金属态建模为一个 (0+1) 维超共形浴（superconformal bath），并分析其热力学性质。

Result: 推导出一个无参数预测公式：4π²γ⁻¹ = χₛ⁻¹ + χc⁻¹，将索末菲系数（Sommerfeld coefficient）γ 与静态自旋磁化率（spin susceptibility）χₛ 和电荷磁化率（charge susceptibility）χc 联系起来。发现低温下 LFL-HFL 转变是不连续的，并据此绘制了相图。

Conclusion: 该代数框架为理解奇异金属态提供了一种统一的结构性视角，并得出了可实验检验的定量预测。作者还将该框架与微观晶格模型及关联绝缘体（correlated insulators）的唯象学建立了联系，表明其具有更广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: We propose an algebraic framework for the strange metal regime of strongly correlated electrons. We show that the exceptional superconformal algebra $D(2,1;α)$ admits two distinct contractions of its conformal sector: one to a pair of canonical fermions, the underlying degrees of freedom of the Landau-Fermi liquid (LFL), and one to the algebra of Hubbard operators, which characterise a distinct metallic regime, the Hubbard-Fermi liquid (HFL). We argue that competition between these two metallic states drives the emergence of the strange metal as a $0+1$D superconformal bath. We analyse the resulting thermodynamics, and obtain a parameter-free prediction, $4π^2γ^{-1} =χ_s^{-1} + χ_c^{-1}$, relating the Sommerfeld coefficient to the static spin and charge susceptibilities. We further show that the LFL-HFL transition is discontinuous at low temperature, owing to a degeneracy at the emergence of the HFL, and map out the resulting phase diagram. We connect the framework to microscopic lattice models and to the phenomenology of correlated insulators.

</details>


### [67] [Design Principles for Quasi-Isotropic Exchange in Rare-Earth Quantum Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31558)
*Kotaro Shimizu,Esteban Agustin Ghioldi,Filip Ronning,Cristian D. Batista*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过微扰理论揭示了Ce³⁺和Yb³⁺基绝缘体中超交换相互作用的微观起源，指出各向同性交换主要来自基态Kramers二重态内的虚拟跃迁，而各向异性相互作用则主要源于激发多重态过程，据此提出了准各向同性交换的轨道设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀土量子材料（rare-earth quantum materials）能产生量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquids）和拓扑磁结构等涌现现象，但强自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）导致了强各向异性交换相互作用，使得实现准各向同性海森堡磁性（Heisenberg magnetism）变得困难，因此需要理解其超交换（superexchange）的微观起源。

Method: 采用多轨道哈伯德模型（multiorbital Hubbard model）的简并微扰论（degenerate perturbation theory），分析具有边共享八面体几何结构（edge-sharing octahedral geometry）的Ce³⁺和Yb³⁺基绝缘体中的超交换机制。

Result: 各向同性交换主要源于基态Kramers二重态（Kramers doublet）内的虚拟跃迁，而各向异性相互作用主要来自涉及激发多重态（excited multiplets）的过程。当基态二重态相对于垂直于超交换平面（由稀土离子和配体离子组成）的量子化轴具有强最大角动量（maximal-angular-momentum）特征时，准各向同性交换被促进。该机制在理想和畸变几何结构中均得到验证，并与实验研究的Yb基绝缘体广泛一致。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个实用的理论框架，用于在稀土量子材料中工程设计准各向同性相互作用（quasi-isotropic interactions）。

Abstract: Rare-earth quantum materials provide a promising platform for emergent phenomena ranging from quantum spin liquids with long-range entanglement to topological magnetic textures. However, the strong spin-orbit coupling that stabilizes their low-energy pseudospin degrees of freedom also tends to generate strongly anisotropic exchange interactions, complicating the realization of quasi-isotropic Heisenberg magnetism. Here we investigate the microscopic origin of superexchange in $\mathrm{Ce}^{3+}$- and $\mathrm{Yb}^{3+}$-based insulators with edge-sharing octahedral geometry. Using degenerate perturbation theory for a multiorbital Hubbard model, we show that isotropic exchange originates predominantly from virtual hopping within the ground-state Kramers doublet, whereas anisotropic interactions arise primarily from processes involving excited multiplets. This leads to a simple orbital design principle: quasi-isotropic exchange is promoted when the ground-state doublet has a strong maximal-angular-momentum character with respect to the quantization axis perpendicular to the superexchange plane spanned by rare-earth and ligand ions. We demonstrate this mechanism for both ideal and distorted geometries and show that it is broadly consistent with experimentally studied Yb-based insulators. Our results establish a practical framework for engineering quasi-isotropic interactions in rare-earth quantum materials.

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文首次通过非极化非弹性中子散射测量的动态磁结构因子 $S_{\rm M}(Q, E)$ 的傅里叶变换，得到了动态磁对分布函数 $D_{\rm M}(r, E)$，并利用简单磁模型和代表性磁体（如 FeTiO$_3$ 和 YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_6$）研究了实空间局域磁动力学行为，揭示了包括声学-光学磁振子模式转变在内的能量依赖特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过非极化非弹性中子散射（nonpolarized inelastic neutron scattering）测量动态磁结构因子 $S_{\rm M}(Q, E)$，再经傅里叶变换（Fourier transform）得到动态磁对分布函数 $D_{\rm M}(r, E)$。针对简单磁模型在低能极限下推导出 $D_{\rm M}(r, E)$ 的解析方程，并将理论结果与数值模拟进行比较。

Result: 成功推导了低能极限下简单磁模型的 $D_{\rm M}(r, E)$ 方程，并通过比较理论方程与模拟结果，展示了实空间局域磁振子（magnon）模式的能量依赖特征，包括从声学（acoustic）到光学（optical）磁振子模式的转变。分析揭示了即使在非周期条件下，纳米尺度实空间中每个自旋对关联在特定能量下伴随符号变化的局域磁振子模式。

Conclusion: 本文提出的动态磁对分布函数方法为研究局域磁动力学（local magnetic dynamics）提供了独特的分析工具，特别适用于非周期体系中的实空间磁激发表征。

Abstract: The dynamic magnetic pair-density function (DymPDF) $D_{\rm M}(r, E)$ is obtained via the Fourier transform of the dynamic magnetic structure factor, $S_{\rm M}(Q, E)$, which is measured using nonpolarized inelastic neutron scattering. While there is a long history of magnetic excitation studies with $S_{\rm M}(Q, E)$, there are no reports on $D_{\rm M}(r, E)$. In this study, we examine simple magnet models and representative magnet examples, such as FeTiO$_{3}$ and YBa$_{2}$Cu$_{3}$O$_{6}$, to investigate the real-space dynamics of $D_{\rm M}(r, E)$. We derive the $D_{\rm M}(r, E)$ equations for simple magnet models in a low energy limit. By comparing these equations to the simulations, we demonstrate the characteristic energy dependence of real-space local magnon modes, including the transition of the magnon mode from acoustic to optical. Our novel analysis reveals the local magnon modes accompanied by a sign change in each spin-pair correlation at a given energy in nanoscale real space even under non-periodic conditions. This method is unique for studying local magnetic dynamics.

### [69] [Vector alignment in matrix Lie groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30868)
*Congzhou M Sha*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出并扩展了一种李代数方法（Lie algebra method），用于从含噪声的成对观测数据中恢复任意经典矩阵李群（classical matrix Lie groups）的群元素（group element），并通过牛顿型修正（Newton-style correction）改进了噪声情况下的最优性，同时在 Lean 4 中给出了形式化证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 两个观测者（observer）对同一物理系统存在规范差异（gauge difference），该差异可表示为作用在其共同向量表示（vector representation）上的群元素（group element）。从有限且含噪声的成对观测中恢复该群元素，在理论和实验中均有实际意义。

Method: 方法包含四个精确步骤：伪逆（pseudoinverse）、矩阵对数（matrix logarithm）、向李代数（Lie algebra）的投影、矩阵指数（matrix exponential）。投影是唯一依赖具体群的步骤，当投影像位于李代数 $\mathfrak{g}$ 且残差正交于 $\mathfrak{g}$ 时，该投影产生唯一的最小二乘最优元素。针对噪声数据，进一步引入牛顿型修正以改善最优性。

Result: 导出了经典矩阵李群（包括 $GL(n)$, $SL(n)$, $SO(n)$, $U(n)$, $SO(p,q)$, $Sp(n)$, $Spin(n)$, $SE(n)$ 实域和复域形式）的显式投影公式。无噪声情况下步骤精确；修正方法在无噪声时与原方法一致，在含噪声时性能介于无修正李代数方法和朴素最小二乘优化之间。所有投影、最优性及修正恒等式均在 Lean 4.31.0（含 Mathlib 4.31.0）中形式化证明，数值实验在 Julia 中完成基准测试。

Conclusion: 该方法从 $SO(3)$ 和 Lorentz 群 $SO(3,1)_+$ 推广到所有经典矩阵李群，且形式化证明了投影算子的最优性。修正步骤弥补了李代数方法在噪声情形下仅对领先阶（leading order）最优的局限，使算法在实际应用中更具鲁棒性。

Abstract: The difference in gauge between two observers of the same physical system can be thought of as a group element acting on their common vector representations. Recovering that group element from a finite, noisy list of paired observations may be of use in both theory and experiment. The Kabsch and Horn algorithms efficiently align point clouds in $\mathbb R^3$, reconciling rotated frames of reference in Galilean relativity (i.e. $SO(3)$). In a previous work, we proposed an alternative Lie algebra method which extends to the Lorentz group $SO(3,1)_+$, and putatively to all Lie groups. In this work, we report the explicit formulae for applying the Lie algebra method to the classical matrix Lie groups (general linear $GL(n)$, special linear $SL(n)$, special orthogonal $SO(n)$, unitary $U(n)$, indefinite special orthogonal $SO(p,q)$, symplectic $Sp(n)$, spin $Spin(n)$, special Euclidean $SE(n)$) over both the real and complex fields. The four steps (pseudoinverse, matrix logarithm, projection onto the Lie algebra, matrix exponential) are exact in the noiseless case. The only group-dependent step is the projection, which we show produces the unique least squares-optimal element of the Lie algebra whenever its image lies in $\mathfrak g$ and its residual is orthogonal to $\mathfrak g$. Additionally, the Lie algebra method is optimal only to leading order for noisy data, so we refine it with a Newton-style correction. This correction matches the Lie algebra method in the noiseless case and direct least squares optimization in the noisy case, with performance between that of the Lie algebra method without correction and naive least squares optimization. The projections, their optimality, and the identity underlying the correction are formally proven in Lean~4.31.0 (with Mathlib 4.31.0), and numerical experiments are benchmarked in Julia.

</details>

### [70] [Dynamical Completion of Coupling-Charge Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30707)
*Kamal Hajian,Bayram Tekin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过引入标量-规范场对偶公式（scalar-gauge pair formulation）的局域动力学完备化，将引力耦合常数提升为守恒荷，允许标量场作为有质量自由度传播，同时保持热力学耦合为守恒积分常数，并完美保留原始黑洞解、第一定律和Smarr关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始的标量-规范场对偶公式将引力耦合常数（gravitational coupling constant）提升为守恒荷（conserved charge），有助于理解扩展黑洞热力学（extended black hole thermodynamics），但该公式将辅助标量场限制为刚性、非动力学构型，缺乏局域动力学自由度。

Method: 从拓扑形式场强（top-form field strength）与相应引力拉格朗日密度（gravitational Lagrangian density）之间的差——即缺陷（defect）——出发构造动力学动能项，使标量场作为有质量自由度（massive degree of freedom）传播，并确保该局域扇区作为荷守恒的有质量标量反作用（charge-preserving massive scalar backreaction），从而维持热力学耦合为守恒积分常数。

Result: 在常耦合构型下，辅助应力-能量贡献完全消失，原始黑洞解、热力学第一定律（first law）和Smarr关系（Smarr relation）被完美保留。该构造在宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）和高斯-博内耦合（Gauss-Bonnet coupling）上得到了验证。

Conclusion: 所提出的局域动力学完备化在赋予标量场传播能力的同时，成功避免了热力学耦合变为局域变化场，保持了其作为守恒积分常数的核心性质，从而为扩展黑洞热力学提供了一个自洽的动力学框架。

Abstract: The scalar-gauge pair formulation promotes gravitational coupling constants to conserved charges, clarifying their role in extended black hole thermodynamics. However, its original incarnation restricts these auxiliary scalar fields to rigid, non-dynamical configurations. In this paper, we introduce a local, dynamical completion of this framework. By constructing the kinetic sector from a defect, which is the difference between the top-form field strength and the associated gravitational Lagrangian density, we allow the scalar to propagate as a genuine massive degree of freedom. Crucially, this local sector acts as a charge-preserving massive scalar backreaction, ensuring the thermodynamic coupling remains a conserved integration constant rather than a locally varying field. When evaluated on constant-coupling configurations, the auxiliary stress-energy contributions vanish entirely, perfectly preserving the original black hole solutions, the first law, and the Smarr relation. We illustrate this construction using the cosmological constant and the Gauss-Bonnet coupling.

</details>


### [71] [Ray tracing ultracompact boson stars: visibility modulations and incomplete photon rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30729)
*Seppe J. Staelens,Ece Alkan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究通过射线追踪成像，分析了超紧凑玻色子星（ultracompact boson stars）产生的额外光子环（photon rings）在傅里叶空间（Fourier space）中的可见性调制特征，发现该调制仅发生于球对称情形和有限观测倾角范围，因此无法作为黑洞模拟体（black-hole mimickers）的普适可观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kerr黑洞的光子环结构已被充分理解，但修改黑洞和黑洞模拟体可能在射线追踪图像中产生额外光子环；未来事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope, EHT）版本如何约束非Kerr光子环的存在尚待研究。

Method: 生成了稳定与不稳定的超紧凑孤子型玻色子星（solitonic boson stars）在球对称和旋转两种情况下的射线追踪图像，并在傅里叶空间（即可见度振幅所在的数据空间）分析低频调制特征。

Result: 清晰的可见度振幅调制仅出现在球对称构型中，且限于有限观测倾角范围；对于旋转玻色子星，光子环是不完整的，可能需要不稳定的顺行光环（prograde light ring）来弥补这一缺失。

Conclusion: 额外光子环引起的可见度振幅调制不能作为超紧凑黑洞模拟体的普适预期可观测特征。

Abstract: Modified black holes and black hole mimickers can give rise to additional photon rings in ray-traced images. With the photon ring structure of Kerr well understood, the question arises how well future versions of the Event Horizon Telescope images would be able to constrain the presence of non-Kerr photon rings. In this work, we investigate how likely additional photon rings are to present themselves through low-frequency modulations of the visibility amplitude, i.e. in Fourier space where the data live. To this end, we generate ray-traced images of stable and unstable ultracompact, solitonic boson stars, both in spherical symmetry and with rotation. We find that clear modulations in the associated visibility amplitude are only present in spherical symmetry, for a restricted range of observer inclinations, hence suggesting that these modulations can not be a generic expectation of ultracompact black-hole mimickers. Additionally, we discuss how the photon rings are incomplete for the rotating boson stars considered, and how an unstable prograde light ring may be needed to remedy this.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 建立了一个涉及两种相互作用流体的宇宙学模型（a cosmological model involving two interacting fluids），以此描述黑洞种群与背景流体在收缩、反弹和膨胀各阶段的耦合演化。

Result: 研究发现，在固定几何（fixed geometry）的时空中，宇宙学流体会改变其性质；即黑洞的存在会反馈影响背景流体的行为。

Conclusion: 反弹宇宙学中黑洞与背景流体之间存在非平凡耦合，双流体模型为描述这种相互作用提供了有效框架。

Abstract: Bouncing cosmologies offer an alternative to the standard $Λ$CDM model by avoiding the problem of the initial cosmological singularity by construction. In these models, the universe undergoes a contraction phase that begins in a nearly flat and dilute state, followed by a bounce, after which the universe transitions into the expanding phase described by the $Λ$CDM model. During contraction, most large-scale structures are expected to be erased. Black holes, however, as shown by several previous investigations, may persist through the bounce.
  The goal of this work is to analyze the evolution of a black hole population throughout the contraction, bounce, and expansion phases. Additionally, we investigate how the presence of black holes influences the properties of the background cosmological fluid. To this end, we develop a cosmological model involving two interacting fluids. Our findings indicate that the cosmological fluid alters its properties in a spacetime with fixed geometry.

### [73] [Scalarization and descalarization in hyperbolic encounters of black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30865)
*Frederick C. L. Pardoe,Helvi Witek*

TL;DR: 本文通过数值相对论(numerical relativity)研究二次标量高斯-博内引力(quadratic scalar Gauss-Bonnet gravity)中黑洞双曲相遇所引发的标量场演化，发现双黑洞在相遇期间可发生动态标量化和自旋引起的永久标量化/去标量化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索二次标量高斯-博内引力中，单黑洞已知可通过标量化(scalarization)获得标量毛(scalar hair)，但双黑洞在双曲相遇(hyperbolic encounter)过程中的标量场动力学尚未被研究。

Method: 工作在退耦极限(decoupling limit)下，在背景度规上对标量场进行演化；为双黑洞系统播种初始标量场，通过数值相对论模拟分析其演化行为。

Result: 初始无法维持标量毛的构型在相遇期间会暂时标量化，即动态标量化(dynamical scalarization)，这在标量场与曲率之间正耦合和负耦合下均可实现；此外，双曲相遇中黑洞自旋大小的改变可导致永久性自旋诱导标量化或去标量化(spin-induced scalarization/descalarization)，称为自旋(去)标量化(spin-up (de)scalarization)。

Conclusion: 双黑洞双曲相遇能触发标量场的动态和永久性标量化效应，且这些效应依赖于耦合符号和黑洞初始自旋，为理解该引力理论中的非线性动力学提供了新见解。

Abstract: We use numerical relativity to study the scalar field evolution sourced by hyperbolic encounters of black holes in quadratic scalar Gauss-Bonnet gravity. In this theory, single black holes are known to acquire a scalar hair through scalarization for certain values of their mass and spin. We work in the decoupling limit and evolve the scalar field on top of a background metric. Seeding binary black holes with an initial scalar field, we find that configurations which initially cannot sustain a scalar hair temporarily scalarize during an encounter and thereby exhibit dynamical scalarization. This is possible for both positive and negative couplings between the scalar field and curvature in black hole binaries with zero and non-zero initial spins, respectively. Furthermore, we find that the change in the spin magnitude of black holes during certain hyperbolic encounters can lead to permanent spin-induced scalarization (or descalarization), which we refer to as spin-up (de)scalarization.

### [74] [A rotating black hole in a Hernquist dark matter halo: horizon geometry, thermodynamics, and quantum emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30962)
*A. A. Araújo Filho,Arun Kumar,N. Heidari,C. F. S. Pereira,Amilcar R. Queiroz,V. B. Bezerra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过Newman-Janis算法构建了嵌入Hernquist暗物质晕的旋转黑洞度规，系统分析了暗物质晕参数和旋转参数对黑洞几何、热力学及量子辐射性质的影响，发现暗物质晕会抑制温度、增加熵、延长蒸发时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究暗物质晕（dark matter halo）对旋转黑洞（rotating black hole）几何结构、热力学性质及量子辐射过程的影响，填补对嵌入暗物质分布的实际天体物理黑洞特性认识的不足。

Method: 利用Newman-Janis算法的非复化表述（noncomplexification formulation），从静态Hernquist暗物质晕背景下的黑洞时空构造其旋转对应解；通过径向函数Δ(r)的根确定视界结构，由g_{tt}=0条件求解静止极限面与能层（ergoregion）；采用Hamilton-Jacobi方法计算量子隧穿率（tunneling rate），并使用Stefan-Boltzmann近似估算霍金辐射（Hawking luminosity）、蒸发时间与谱发射率。

Result: Hernquist暗物质晕使外事件视界（outer event horizon）向更大半径移动，改变能层（ergoregion）大小，增加零角动量观测者（ZAMO）的角速度；暗物质晕抑制霍金温度（Hawking temperature），增加Bekenstein-Hawking熵，并通过Davies型临界点（Davies-type critical point）改变局部热稳定性；在弱晕慢转极限下，暗物质晕降低霍金辐射光度（Hawking luminosity）并延迟蒸发过程。

Conclusion: 嵌入Hernquist暗物质晕显著影响旋转黑洞的几何、热力学和量子辐射特性，所有结果在适当极限下退化为标准Kerr黑洞和Schwarzschild黑洞的情形。

Abstract: We investigate the geometrical, thermodynamic, and quantum emission properties of a rotating black hole immersed in a Hernquist dark matter halo. Starting from a static black hole spacetime surrounded by a Hernquist distribution, we construct its rotating counterpart through the noncomplexification formulation of the Newman-Janis algorithm and analyze the modifications induced by the halo parameter $ρ$ and the rotation parameter $a$. The horizon structure is determined from the roots of the radial function $Δ(r)$, while the stationary limit surfaces and the corresponding ergoregions are obtained from the condition $g_{tt}=0$. We show that the Hernquist contribution displaces the outer event horizon toward larger radii and modifies the size of the ergoregion, whereas rotation controls the oblateness of the horizon and the strength of frame dragging. The angular velocity of zero angular momentum observers is also increased by the surrounding matter distribution. We further derive the surface gravity, Hawking temperature, Bekenstein-Hawking entropy, and heat capacity, showing that the dark matter halo suppresses the temperature, increases the entropy, and changes the local thermal stability through a Davies-type critical point. The quantum tunneling rate is obtained from the Hamilton-Jacobi method, leading to the corresponding occupation number and particle creation density. Finally, we estimate the Hawking luminosity (radiation), evaporation time, and spectral emission rates within a Stefan-Boltzmann approximation. In the weak halo and slow rotation regime, the Hernquist distribution reduces the luminosity and delays the evaporation process. All standard Kerr and Schwarzschild results are recovered in the appropriate limiting cases.
