### [75] [Repetitive Penrose process for charged particles in Kerr-Newman black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30969)
*Mohammad Reza Alipour,Saeed Noori Gashti,Mohammad Ali S. Afshar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了极端Kerr-Newman黑洞中带电粒子的重复彭罗斯过程，构建了非线性迭代框架，通过三重转折点条件获得守恒方程的解析解，揭示了两个电磁耦合参数对提取过程的调控作用，并发现了四种电荷参数区域结构，表明Kerr-Newman黑洞可以越过中性态并反转电荷符号而不违反面积定理或宇宙审查假说。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重复彭罗斯过程（repetitive Penrose process）在极端Kerr-Newman黑洞中的行为尚未被系统研究，尤其是在粒子带有电荷且黑洞自身携带电荷与角动量的复杂情形下，需要建立自洽的非线性迭代框架来追踪黑洞参数演化。

Method: 构建非线性迭代框架，在每次提取事件后更新黑洞的质量、角动量、电荷和不可约质量；通过施加三重转折点条件（triple turning-point condition）获得守恒方程的解析解。

Result: 发现两个电磁耦合参数$\hat Q\hat q_0$和$\hat Q\hat q_1$分别控制重复过程的终止与负能态深度；吸引力耦合（$\hat Q\hat q_1<0$）显著增强能量回报率与利用效率；在临界电荷$\hat q_1\simeq-54.85405$附近，演化逼近可逆的Christodoulou-Ruffini极限；识别出捕获粒子电荷参数空间的四区域结构。

Conclusion: Kerr-Newman黑洞可以演化通过中性态并反转电荷符号，且不违反面积定理或宇宙审查假说（cosmic censorship），表明Reissner-Nordström情形中发现的放电屏障并非带电黑洞的普适性质。

Abstract: We investigate the repetitive Penrose process for charged particles in an initially extremal Kerr--Newman black hole and develop a nonlinear iterative framework in which the black-hole mass, angular momentum, electric charge, and irreducible mass are updated after every extraction event. By imposing the triple turning-point condition, we obtain an analytic solution of the conservation equations, allowing the entire extraction sequence to be followed self-consistently. The dynamics are governed by two electromagnetic couplings. The coupling $\hat Q\hat q_0$ determines whether the incident particle can continue to access the ergoregion and therefore controls the termination of the repetitive process, whereas $\hat Q\hat q_1$ governs the depth of the negative-energy states and the extraction efficiency. An attractive interaction ($\hat Q\hat q_1<0$) significantly enhances both the energy return on investment and the energy utilization efficiency and, above a critical charge, produces a transient increase of the dimensionless spin despite the continuous loss of angular momentum. We identify a four-region structure in the captured-particle charge parameter space. Near the critical charge $\hat q_1\simeq-54.85405$, the evolution approaches the reversible Christodoulou--Ruffini limit with the energy utilization efficiency approaching unity while the black hole remains sub-extremal. Beyond this point the irreducible mass decreases, indicating the breakdown of the test-particle approximation. Unlike the repetitive Penrose process in the extremal Reissner--Nordström spacetime, the Kerr--Newman black hole can evolve through the neutral state and reverse the sign of its electric charge without violating the area theorem or cosmic censorship, demonstrating that the discharge barrier found in the Reissner--Nordström case is not a generic property of charged black holes.

### [76] [Phase space quantization of anisotropic cosmologies: Taub and Kantowski-Sachs models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31049)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用完全对称的Weyl量子化映射（Weyl quantization map）和Moyal星积（Moyal star product）；通过对哈密顿约束（Hamiltonian constraint）进行正则分离（canonical separation），解决了星积通常伴随的形式收敛问题（formal convergence problems）。

Result: 成功构造了均匀但各向异性的Taub和Kantowski-Sachs宇宙学模型的非对角与对角Wigner分布（Wigner distributions）；从对角Wigner分布计算得到了标准波函数，在两种模型中均恢复了以修正贝塞尔函数（modified Bessel functions）表示的精确物理态（exact physical states）。

Conclusion: 所提出的相空间形变量子化方法可以有效规避传统正则量子化中的因子排序歧义，并能与常规量子宇宙学（quantum cosmology）建立严谨的联系，为各向异性宇宙学模型的量子化提供了可行的替代方案。

Abstract: We introduce an explicit construction of the non-diagonal and diagonal Wigner distributions for the homogeneous but anisotropic Taub and Kantowski-Sachs cosmological models within the framework of phase space deformation quantization. Conventional canonical quantization of these models via the Wheeler-DeWitt equation is inherently plagued by factor ordering ambiguities. To circumvent these issues, we employ the totally symmetric Weyl quantization map and the Moyal star product. By means of a canonical separation of the Hamiltonian constraint, we are able to resolve the formal convergence problems typically associated with the star product. Furthermore, to establish a rigorous connection with conventional quantum cosmology, we calculate the standard wave functions directly from the diagonal Wigner distributions, recovering the exact physical states in terms of modified Bessel functions in both cases.

### [77] [Geometric formulation for Palatini-Cartan gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31070)
*Jasel Berra-Montiel,Iván Cortes-Cruz,Alberto Molgado*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从多种几何-协变形式论（geometric-covariant formalisms）出发，系统分析了四维Palatini-Cartan引力模型在拉格朗日（Lagrangian）层、多辛（multisymplectic）框架、多辛（polysymplectic）框架以及瞬时Dirac-Hamilton形式论中的场方程、规范对称性、Noether流、Cauchy数据和约束结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功恢复了与无挠条件和爱因斯坦方程等价的正确场方程；构造了规范对称群的拉格朗日动量映射及其对应的Noether流；在多辛框架下恢复了系统的可容许Cauchy数据；通过引入基于广义Moore-Penrose逆的Dirac-Poisson括号获得了正确的场方程；通过空间+时间分解恢复了瞬时拉格朗日量、扩展哈密顿量以及在瞬时Dirac-Hamilton形式论中表征Palatini-Cartan模型的规范结构。

Conclusion: 多种几何-协变形式论能够一致且系统地表征Palatini-Cartan引力模型的核心结构，包括场方程、规范对称性、约束结构和Cauchy数据，为理解广义相对论的推广模型提供了统一的几何框架。

Abstract: Motivated by the increasing efforts to understand the covariant structure of physical models associated with General Relativity using different kinds of geometric frameworks, in this article we analyze the four-dimensional Palatini-Cartan model for gravity, which is a well-known generalization of General Relativity, from the perspective of various geometric-covariant formalisms for classical field theory. At the Lagrangian level, we do not only recover the correct field equations of the theory, which are equivalent to the torsion-free condition and the Einstein equations, but we also study the gauge symmetries of the model in order to construct the Lagrangian momentum map associated with the action of the gauge symmetry group on the configuration space of the system and, consequently, its corresponding Noether currents. Within the multisymplectic approach, we analyze the action of the gauge symmetry group on the multi-momenta phase space of the model, and we also introduce the induced momentum map that allows us to recover the admissible Cauchy data of the system. Further, we also apply the algorithm to treat singular systems within the polysymplectic framework, in which, in order to obtain the correct field equations of the model, we introduce a non-trivial Dirac-Poisson bracket characterized by the generalized Moore-Penrose inverse of the matrix induced by the second class constraints of the system. Finally, using the multisymplectic framework as a starting point, we perform the space plus time decomposition of the system to recover the instantaneous Lagrangian and the extended Hamiltonian of the theory, as well as the gauge structure that characterize the Palatini-Cartan model for gravity within the instantaneous Dirac-Hamiltonian formalism.

### [78] [Stability of the Minkowski spacetime in Newman-Unti gauge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31090)
*Jonathan Luk,Sung-Jin Oh,Claude Warnick*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明，在中心归一化出射零测地规范（centre-normalised outgoing null-geodesic gauge）下，闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）解在爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein's equations）中具有小数据全局稳定性。方法先利用Dafermos-Rodnianski的$r^p$估计控制满足解耦张量波动方程（decoupled tensorial wave equation）的Weyl张量（Weyl tensor）分量，再通过输运方程（transport equations）从规则中心轴初始条件控制其余几何量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究闵可夫斯基时空在广义相对论（general relativity）中的非线性稳定性问题，特别是针对初始数据仅弱衰减至平坦空间的情形，建立全局稳定性结果。

Method: 首先采用Dafermos-Rodnianski的$r^p$估计控制Weyl张量的某些分量，这些分量满足解耦的张量波动方程；在获得此控制后，其余几何量通过输运方程从规则中心轴的初始条件加以控制。

Result: 建立了对于弱衰减至平坦空间的初始数据的小数据全局稳定性；当数据具有更多结构时，还能建立额外的渐近控制（asymptotic control）。

Conclusion: 该方案有效证明了闵可夫斯基解在爱因斯坦方程中的全局稳定性，且对初始数据衰减性的要求较弱，同时允许在数据更结构化时获得更强的渐近性态控制。

Abstract: We prove small-data global stability of the Minkowski solution to Einstein's equations in a centre-normalised outgoing null-geodesic gauge. Our scheme involves first using the $r^p$-estimates of Dafermos-Rodnianski to control certain components of the Weyl tensor which satisfy a decoupled tensorial wave equation. Having established this control, all remaining geometric quantities are controlled by transport equations, taking initial conditions at a regular central axis. This method establishes global stability for initial data which decay only weakly to flat space and can establish additional asymptotic control when the data are assumed to have more structure.

### [79] [On the Kalb-Ramond modified Lorentz violating hairy black holes and Thorne's hoop conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31116)
*K. K. Nandi,R. N. Izmailov,R. Kh. Karimov,A. A. Potapov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Kalb-Ramond模型中放宽了能量条件，数值探索了一类扩大的洛伦兹破坏（Lorentz violating, LV）史瓦西黑洞的视界模式，发现了四种通用类型，其中包括类似膜世界（braneworld）黑洞的类型。研究表明，Thorne箍缩猜想（hoop conjecture）对其中三种类型成立，但对Schwarzschild-de Sitter型及其推广不成立。此外，膜世界潮汐荷黑洞对行星近日点进动的LV修正有不同于普通黑洞的定性影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作研究了Kalb-Ramond模型中满足能量条件（energy condition）的LV修正史瓦西黑洞，但存在大量不满足能量条件的黑洞尚未被探索。本文旨在放宽能量条件，系统研究更大类别的LV修正黑洞的视界结构及其物理性质。

Method: 采用数值方法探索放宽能量条件后扩大的LSMA黑洞的视界模式（horizon patterns），分析其与Thorne箍缩猜想（hoop conjecture）的关系，并计算行星近日点进动（perihelion advance）的LV修正。

Result: 发现了四种通用类型的LV修正黑洞，其中一类与膜世界黑洞（$ρ<0$）类似，赋予参数$Υ$"潮汐荷（tidal charge）"的新解释。Thorne箍缩猜想$\mathcal{H} \leq 1$对其中三种类型及其推广成立，但对Schwarzschild-de Sitter型及其推广不成立。膜世界潮汐荷黑洞增大LV修正对近日点进动的影响，与普通黑洞相反。

Conclusion: 放宽能量条件后LV修正黑洞的视界结构更加丰富；Thorne箍缩猜想的成立与否依赖于黑洞类型；膜世界潮汐荷黑洞与普通LV黑洞在近日点进动效应上存在定性区别，可为两类黑洞提供观测上的区分依据。

Abstract: Recently, a class of static spherically symmetric power law corrected Lorentz violating (LV) Schwarzschild black holes in the Kalb-Ramond model have been derived and studied in the specific range of LV parameters ($0<λ\leq 2,Υ\geq 0$) that correspond to energy condition preserving ($ρ>0$) source. On the other hand, there exist well known black holes that do not preserve the energy conditions. In this paper, we shall therefore relax energy conditions and numerically explore the horizon patterns of the enlarged class of LSMA black holes. Four generic types of LV corrected black holes emerge, which interestingly include the analogue of the \textit{braneworld} black hole ($ρ<0$) lending to $Υ$ a new interpretation of "tidal charge" known as an imprint from the $5d$ bulk in the Randall-Sundrum scenario. We shall then show that Thorne's hoop conjecture, $\mathcal{H} \leq 1$, where $\mathcal{H}$ is the Hod function, consistently holds for three types and their generalizations. However, intriguingly, it turns out that, for the remaining type (viz., Schwarzschild-de Sitter and its generalizations), the hoop conjecture does \textit{not} hold. It is also shown that braneworld tidal charge black holes increases the LV correction to planetary perihelion advance in contrast to the decrease due to ordinary black holes thereby providing a qualitative distinction between them.

### [80] [Galactic microlensing by backreacted massless wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31118)
*G. F. Akhtaryanova,R. Kh. Karimov,R. N. Izmailov,K. K. Nandi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了带电虫洞（charged wormholes）作为暗晕天体在银河系微引力透镜（microlensing）中的透镜效应，分析了光偏转角、透镜观测量和概率特征，并发现其光变曲线（Paczyński light curves）比史瓦西黑洞更暗且具有特征性凹槽（gutters），为通过重新分析历史微引力透镜数据探测带电虫洞提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Kim & Lee提出的带电虫洞作为暗晕天体（dark halo objects）在银河系微引力透镜中充当透镜的新应用，以期通过透镜效应区分虫洞与黑洞等传统致密天体。

Method: 基于Kim & Lee带电虫洞解，分别分析标量荷（α）与电荷（Q）对ADM质量的影响；对带电情形计算至4阶后牛顿近似（post-Newtonian, PPN）的光偏转角；进而分析透镜观测量（像位置、放大率、质心、时间延迟）；并基于虫洞透镜是否束缚于银河系的假设，分析光学深度（optical depth）与事件率（event rate）等概率特征。

Result: 标量荷与电荷虫洞均具有与背景Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞相同的零ADM质量；电荷Q引入了非平凡红移函数Φ并改变了喉半径r_th。带电虫洞的Paczyński光变曲线比史瓦西黑洞更暗，且在源星进入和离开爱因斯坦环时出现特征性凹槽；当Q趋近极端极限r_th/√2时，爱因斯坦半径R_E消失，凹槽逐渐合并。

Conclusion: 带电虫洞的微引力透镜信号具有独特的定性特征（光变曲线更暗且存在凹槽），通过重新分析已有的银河系微引力透镜历史数据，可能揭示带电虫洞的存在。

Abstract: We study here a novel application of Kim \& Lee charged wormholes assuming them to be dark halo objects playing the role of lenses in the Galactic microlensing with source stars belonging to the Galactic Bulge and the Large Magellanic Cloud. First, we observe that both the backreacted scalar ($α$) and electrically ($Q$) charged wormholes have the same zero ADM mass as has the background Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole having a special equation of state parameter $γ=-1$. In particular, we argue that, for $α\neq 0$, the solution formally resembles, but can at best be sourcewise different from, that of the background wormhole. The charge ($Q\neq 0$) thus provides an extra degree of freedom that introduces a non-trivial redshift function $Φ$ to the background, alters its throat radius to $r_{th}$, yet keeps the wormhole massless. Second, we focus on this electrically charged case and calculate the light deflection angle up to 4$^{th}$ PPN order, analyze the effect of $Q$ on the lensing observables such as the image positions, magnification, centroid and time delay of images of the source stars. Third, we analyze the probabilistic features such as optical depth and event rate estimated on the basis of the hypothesis that the wormhole lens could be bound or unbound to our Galaxy. Finally, we report an intriguing qualitative prediction that, compared to the Schwarzschild black hole, the Paczyński light curves of the electrically charged wormhole are much dimmer that also show characteristic gutters at the times the source enters and exits the Einstein ring. \textit{The gutters gradually come together as $Q$ approaches the extreme limit $r_{th}/\sqrt{2}$, at which the Einstein radius $R_{E}$ vanishes so that the source crosses it instantly.} It is speculated that re-analyzing past data on Galactic microlensing may betray the presence of charged wormholes.

### [81] [Quantum work extraction of an accelerated battery as an indicator of trajectory-modified vacuum fluctuations in Minkowski spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31120)
*Xiang Hao,Cheng-Tai Wu,Wei-Wei Zhang,Gao-Feng Gan,Tian-Xi Ren,Jia-Yin Shen,Yin-Zhong Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了沿匀加速直线运动和匀圆周运动两种轨迹运动的加速Unruh-DeWitt电池的物理模型，研究其最大量子功提取（ergotropy）作为真空涨落（vacuum fluctuations）的探针。结果表明：直线运动在低温下更优、圆周运动在高温下更优；边界附近ergotropy出现显著振荡与瞬时峰值，源于量子相干性（quantum coherence）的保护；远离边界时振荡被抑制并趋于稳态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索不同运动轨迹（匀加速直线与匀速圆周）下加速Unruh-DeWitt电池的量子功提取行为，利用ergotropy作为真空涨落受运动轨迹调制的见证（witness），并考察反射边界（reflecting boundary）对系统动力学的影响。

Method: 建立沿匀加速直线运动和匀速圆周运动两种轨迹运动的加速Unruh-DeWitt电池的物理模型，分别考虑有无反射边界的情形，通过ergotropy量化最大量子功提取量，分析其渐近行为与真空涨落、Unruh热效应（Unruh thermality）及Kubo-Martin-Schwinger条件的关系。

Result: 直线运动的ergotropy渐近行为可展示与边界无关的Unruh热性；低温下直线运动ergotropy更高，高温下圆周运动对Unruh效应估计更优；特定加速度下两种轨迹的量子功提取量相等；边界附近ergotropy出现显著振荡与瞬时峰值，远离边界时振荡被抑制并趋于稳态，圆周运动可延长振荡演化；随轨迹到边界距离增加，ergotropy渐近值逐渐上升至饱和。

Conclusion: 加速电池的ergotropy受运动轨迹与反射边界的共同调控，不同轨迹在温度区间内各具优势；边界附近的量子相干性保护是ergotropy振荡与峰值产生的关键机制，圆周运动具有延长振荡的作用；该研究为利用量子功提取探测量子真空涨落与Unruh效应提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We put forward a physical model of an accelerated Unruh-DeWitt battery moving along two distinct types of trajectories, namely a uniformly accelerated linear motion and a uniform circular motion. Each trajectory is considered without or with a reflecting boundary. The maximal amount of quantum work extraction, defined as the ergotropy, serves as a witness to vacuum fluctuations modified by motion trajectories. The asymptotic behavior of ergotropy in a linear motion can demonstrate the Unruh thermality with respect to the Kubo-Martin-Schwinger condition, which is independent of the presence of a boundary. Comparing two kinds of trajectories, we find that for a very low Unruh temperature, linear motion yields a high amount of ergotropy, while for a high temperature, circular motion becomes optimal for estimating the Unruh effect. For a certain acceleration, quantum work extraction is the same for two different trajectories. The observed ergotropy for the thermality is closely related to quantum coherence affected by trajectory-modified vacuum fluctuations. In the presence of a reflecting boundary plane, we study different ways for the dynamics of the ergotropy. When the battery moves near the boundary, the prominent oscillation of the ergotropy will happen and exhibit some large instantaneous peaks. The interesting phenomenon results from the protection of quantum coherence for the accelerated battery in the vicinity of the boundary. Far away from the boundary, the oscillation behavior can be suppressed and the ergotropy rapidly arrives at a steady value. By contrast, the circular motion contributes to prolonging the oscillation evolution. The asymptotic amount of the ergotropy can rise progressively up to a saturation value with increasing the distance from the circular trajectory to the boundary plane.

### [82] [Cosmological Stealth fields and Non-Equilibrium thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31180)
*Gilberto Aguilar-Pérez,Cuauhtemoc Campuzano,Víctor H. Cárdenas,Miguel Cruz,Joel Saavedra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了宇宙学隐形标量场（stealth scalar field）与非平衡热力学之间的联系。在平坦FLRW背景中，通过非最小耦合的标量场，发现隐形条件导出广义Riccati方程，其中耗散压（dissipative pressure）作为热力学驱动项。系统存在两个热力学分支——由熵产生（entropy production）选择的稳定吸引子（attractor）和不稳定排斥子（repeller）。在相空间结构中识别出临界区域（ζ=1/4），并构建了体粘滞（bulk viscous）实现，其中不可逆熵产生驱动宇宙渐近进入德西特（de Sitter）态。结果表明隐形场可视为非平衡宇宙演化的热力学追踪器（thermodynamic tracker）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索宇宙学隐形标量场与非平衡热力学之间的理论联系，理解隐形场在耗散宇宙学背景上的动力学行为及其热力学解释。

Method: 在空间平坦FLRW背景中引入非最小耦合标量场，其能动张量（energy-momentum tensor）恒为零，从而不产生引力反作用（gravitational backreaction）；通过隐形条件推导出广义Riccati方程；引入变量 y=φ̇/(Hφ) 进行相空间分析，并结合熵产生（entropy production）判据识别热力学分支。

Result: 隐形条件导出广义Riccati方程，耗散压作为热力学驱动项；系统存在由熵产生选择的稳定吸引子和不稳定排斥子两个热力学分支；在 (y, ω_eff) 相空间中识别出与 ζ=1/4 关联的近临界区域（near-critical regime）；构建了体粘滞实现，不可逆熵产生驱动宇宙渐近到达德西特态。

Conclusion: 隐形标量场可被解释为动态非平凡的热力学追踪器，跟踪非平衡宇宙学演化；该结果建立了隐形场与耗散热力学之间的形式对应关系。

Abstract: We investigate the connection between cosmological stealth scalar fields and non-equilibrium thermodynamics in a spatially flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) background. We consider a non-minimally coupled scalar field whose energy-momentum tensor vanishes identically, allowing the field to evolve on a dissipative cosmological background without producing gravitational backreaction. We show that the stealth condition leads to a generalized Riccati equation for the scalar-field kinematics, where the dissipative pressure acts as a thermodynamic driving term. In terms of the variable $y=\dotφ/(Hφ)$, the system admits two thermodynamic branches: a stable attractor selected by entropy production and an unstable repeller. We also construct the corresponding phase-space structure in the $(y,ω_{\rm eff})$ plane and identify a near-critical regime associated with $ζ=1/4$. Finally, we reconstruct the stealth potential and present a bulk viscous realization in which irreversible entropy production drives the universe toward an asymptotic de Sitter state while the stealth field tracks the dissipative background. Our results suggest that stealth fields can be interpreted as dynamically non-trivial thermodynamic trackers of non-equilibrium cosmological evolution.

### [83] [Semiclassical Backreaction of Massive Quantum Fields in the Spacetime of a Global Monopole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31255)
*Owen Pavel Fernández Piedra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在点状整体单极子（pointlike global monopole）时空中，研究了有质量标量场（massive scalar）、旋量场（spinor）和矢量场（vector）的领先半经典反作用（leading semiclassical backreaction）。基于Schwinger–DeWitt近似下的重整化应力-能量张量（renormalized stress-energy tensor），推导了由一般守恒对角源产生的一阶半经典几何，并具体分析了自旋0、1/2和1的场。量子源局域衰减为$r^{-6}$，诱导的度规修正为$r^{-4}$阶；标量场导致时间与径向度规函数分离，而旋量与矢量场产生单一函数几何。量子反作用仅引起单极子外部的局域变形，不影响其渐近立体角亏损（asymptotic solid-angle deficit）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解有质量量子场在整体单极子时空中的半经典反作用（semiclassical backreaction），分析不同自旋（spin）场的几何效应差异，并检验量子修正是否改变单极子的全局拓扑特征（如立体角亏损）。

Method: 采用Schwinger–DeWitt近似（Schwinger–DeWitt approximation）得到重整化应力-能量张量；从一般守恒对角源出发推导一阶半经典几何，再特化到自旋0、1/2与1的场；通过度规修正、曲率修正、静态观者加速度（acceleration of static observers）和测地运动（geodesic motion）分析解的适用范围。

Result: 量子源以$r^{-6}$衰减，度规修正为$r^{-4}$阶；标量场产生两个独立的度规函数（时间与径向），而旋量和矢量场仅产生一个度规函数。量子反作用导致单极子外部的局域变形，但渐近立体角亏损保持不变。

Conclusion: 不同自旋的量子场对整体单极子几何的半经典反作用具有不同的度规结构（标量场引起各向异性，旋量与矢量场保持各向同性），但均不改变其渐近拓扑性质。一阶解的有效性受到相应曲率修正和运动方程的约束。

Abstract: We study the leading semiclassical backreaction of massive scalar, spinor, and vector fields in the spacetime of a pointlike global monopole. Starting from the renormalized stress-energy tensors obtained in the Schwinger--DeWitt approximation, we derive the first-order semiclassical geometry generated by a general conserved diagonal source and then specialize it to fields of spin $0$, $1/2$, and $1$. The locally fixed quantum source falls as $r^{-6}$ and induces metric corrections of order $r^{-4}$. The scalar field generically produces distinct temporal and radial metric functions, whereas the spinor and vector fields lead to one-function geometries. We analyze the resulting curvature correction, the acceleration of static observers, geodesic motion, and the validity domain of the first-order solution. The quantum backreaction produces a local deformation of the monopole exterior but does not modify its asymptotic solid-angle deficit.

### [84] [Fragility of stealth solutions in mimetic gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31274)
*Alireza Allahyari,Clarisse Donio,Mohammad Ali Gorji,Zahra Gorji,Javad T. Firouzjaee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类受约束的广义相对论拟模（mimetic）扩展理论，其中约束项通过拉格朗日乘子（Lagrange multiplier）引入。在背景值\barλ=0的隐踪分支（stealth branch）上，约束扇区从背景动力学中解耦，该理论允许广义相对论的几何解作为隐踪解存在。然而，该分支与广义相对论在微扰层面简并，但\barλ→0的极限是非均匀的，导致屏蔽机制在微扰理论中存在病态问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一类包含拉格朗日乘子（λ）约束的拟模扩展引力理论的动力学行为与结构，特别是约束扇区在不同分支下的解耦机制和屏蔽极限（screening-like limit）的实现。

Method: 采用作用量形式（action formalism），引入标量泛函C[g,Ψ]和拉格朗日乘子λ构造约束项；选取标量场（scalar field）情形C=g^{μν}∂_μφ∂_νφ±1=0作为具体实现，利用汉密尔顿-雅可比方程（Hamilton-Jacobi equation）选取测地线族（geodesic congruences），并采用卡特可分离性（Carter separability）构造隐踪克尔解（stealth Kerr profile）。

Result: 在\barλ=0的隐踪分支上，约束扇区从背景动力学中完全退出，允许广义相对论的几何解作为隐踪解存在；标量场实现中成功构造了隐踪球对称解和隐踪克尔解。\barλ=0分支在微扰层次上与广义相对论简并，但约束扇区通过无限层级约束影响涨落（fluctuations），导致\barλ→0极限非均匀，屏蔽机制在微扰理论中病态。

Conclusion: 约束扇区在隐踪分支上虽从背景动力学家解耦，但在微扰层级仍对涨落施加无限层级约束，导致\barλ→0的屏蔽极限在微扰理论中不具备均匀性，表现出病态行为（pathological behavior）。

Abstract: We study a broad class of constrained mimetic-type extensions of general relativity with action $S=\int{\rm d}^4x\sqrt{-g}\,\bigl(R/2+λ\,C[g,Ψ]+{\cal L}_{\rm m}\bigr)$, where $R$ is the Ricci scalar, $λ$ is a Lagrange multiplier, $C[g,Ψ]$ is a scalar functional of the metric and generic field content $Ψ$ (possibly involving $Ψ$ and its covariant derivatives) and ${\cal L}_{\rm m}$ is the matter Lagrangian. The branch $\barλ\to 0$, with the bar denoting a background value, provides a simple screening-like limit in which the constrained sector decouples, as in cosmological realizations where $\barλ$ is typically nonzero on large scales while locally one expects $\barλ\simeq 0$. On the exactly stealth branch $\barλ=0$, the constrained sector drops out of the background dynamics, so, on domains where a background profile $\barΨ$ satisfying $\bar C=0$ exists, the theory admits the corresponding general relativity geometries as stealth solutions. As an explicit realization of this mechanism, we consider the scalar field case, where $C=g^{μν}\partial_μφ\partial_νφ\pm1=0$ becomes a Hamilton-Jacobi equation selecting geodesic congruences; in this setting, we study spherically symmetric solutions and construct a stealth Kerr profile using Carter separability. We then show, at the general level, that the $\barλ=0$ branch is perturbatively degenerate with general relativity: the constrained sector contributes to the dynamics only through terms weighted by $\barλ$, which vanish on the stealth branch, while still imposing an infinite hierarchy of constraints on the fluctuations. Consequently, the $\barλ\to0$ limit is generically non-uniform, making the would-be screening perturbatively pathological.

### [85] [Distance duality relation in symmetric teleparallel gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31299)
*Rocco D'Agostino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在对称遥平行理论（symmetric teleparallel theories）中研究了距离对偶关系（distance duality relation, DDR），证明在最小耦合下标准Etherington互易关系依然成立，但在非最小耦合的f(Q)理论中，光子数流不再守恒，导致DDR发生动力学破坏；并推导了广义DDR公式，建立了DDR偏差与有效精细结构常数变化之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对非黎曼几何（non-Riemannian geometry）中距离对偶关系（DDR）的有效性缺乏系统理解，尤其是当引力由非度量性（nonmetricity）介导时，标准Etherington互易关系是否仍成立尚不清楚。本文旨在统一框架下区分DDR破坏的几何起源与动力学起源，并为未来高精度观测检验非黎曼引力理论提供理论依据。

Method: 从一般度规-仿射（metric-affine）表述出发，采用几何光学近似；首先分析电磁场最小耦合情形，再扩展至电磁场与非度量性标量非最小耦合的f(Q)理论一族。在重合规范（coincident gauge）下的均匀各向同性时空背景中推导广义DDR公式，并讨论耦合函数的具体实例。

Result: 在最小耦合下，非度量性存在时标准Etherington互易关系仍成立；而非最小耦合会修改光子数流守恒，导致DDR发生动力学破坏。推导出直接联系观测距离测度与哈勃膨胀率（Hubble expansion rate）的广义DDR公式，并建立了DDR偏差与有效精细结构常数（fine-structure constant）变化之间的联系。示例表明，现象学上可行的模型仅预测与标准DDR的微小偏差。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个统一框架，用以区分DDR破坏的几何与动力学起源，为借助未来高精度天体物理和宇宙学观测检验非黎曼引力理论开辟了新途径。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the distance duality relation (DDR) in symmetric teleparallel theories, where gravity is mediated by nonmetricity. Starting from the general metric-affine formulation and adopting the geometrical optics approximation, we show that the standard Etherington reciprocity relation remains valid in the presence of nonmetricity when electromagnetism is minimally coupled and the photon number is conserved. We then extend the analysis to a class of $f(Q)$ theories with a nonminimal coupling between the electromagnetic field and the nonmetricity scalar. We demonstrate that such an interaction modifies the conservation of the photon number current, leading to a dynamical violation of the DDR. Focusing on a homogeneous and isotropic spacetime background in the coincident gauge, we derive a generalized DDR formula that directly relates observational distance measures to the Hubble expansion rate. Furthermore, we discuss the link between the deviations from Etherington's relation and variations of the effective fine-structure constant. Specific illustrative examples of the coupling function are also analyzed, showing that phenomenologically viable models predict only small deviations from the standard DDR. Our results provide a unified framework to distinguish between the geometric and dynamical origins of DDR violations, opening new avenues for testing non-Riemannian gravity with future high-precision astrophysical and cosmological observations.

</details>


### [86] [A parametric signal plus noise inference framework for short duration non-Gaussian noise transients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31304)
*Charlie Hoy,Ruxandra Bondarescu,Andrew Lundgren,Laura K. Nuttall*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出 bilby-antiglitch 方法，通过在非高斯噪声中联合分析天体物理信号与噪声瞬变（glitches），相比传统技术能够更准确地推断真实源参数，并避免对广义相对论的错误违背判定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地面引力波探测器中的噪声瞬变（glitches）常与天体物理信号重叠，破坏了传统引力波分析中噪声平稳且高斯的假设，导致推断结果出现偏差。

Method: 引入 bilby-antiglitch 框架，将准物理的短时非高斯噪声瞬变模型与信号模型一同纳入贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference），实现信号与噪声的联合分析。

Result: 在存在强噪声瞬变的模拟信号上，bilby-antiglitch 能够推断出真实的源参数，而传统方法产生偏差；该方法还防止了对广义相对论（General Relativity）的假阳性违背判定，并验证了引力波信号在含噪数据中的异常显著性。

Conclusion: bilby-antiglitch 为处理非高斯噪声下的引力波数据分析提供了一种有效方案，有望提升引力波天文学在真实观测中的推断可靠性。

Abstract: Gravitational waves are now routinely detected with ground-based observatories, and, through a process known as Bayesian inference, their source properties are inferred. However, terrestrial noise artifacts, often referred to as glitches, commonly overlap astrophysical signals. This invalidates a fundamental assumption of gravitational wave analyses: the noise is no longer stationary and Gaussian. As a result, traditional techniques can provide biased inferences in realistic data. One method for mitigating the effect of glitches is to jointly analyse both the signal and noise in a single framework. In this work, we introduce bilby-antiglitch to infer the astrophysical signal properties in non-Gaussian noise. By additionally including a quasi-physical glitch model to describe short duration non-Gaussian noise transients, we show that unlike traditional techniques, we infer the true source properties of simulated signals contaminated with loud glitches. We also show that bilby-antiglitch prevents false violation claims of General Relativity, and validates the exceptional nature of gravitational wave signals in spurious data.

</details>


### [87] [Compactness Inference in Gravitational-Wave Mergers with PhenomDECO: Catalog Benchmarks and Robustness Diagnostics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31350)
*Shrobana Ghosh,Charlie Hoy,Mark Hannam,Frank Ohme*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究利用一种基于有效紧致参数（effective compactness parameter）的现象学模型~\deco~，对GWTC-3中所有高显著性双黑洞并合事件进行检验，发现大部分事件与双黑洞预期一致，但低频噪声伪影可能引入虚假的偏离信号；其中GW231123信号需将分析起始频率提升至50Hz以上才能消除异常的低紧致性模态，表明低频数据处理是判别新奇物理信号的关键前提。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多项引力波（gravitational wave, GW）观测被识别为双黑洞（binary black hole, BBH）并合事件，但其中部分系统的成分质量挑战了典型形成模型，因而有必要系统性检验这些探测源是否确实与双黑洞解释一致，避免将噪声或伪影误判为新物理信号。

Method: 采用现有双黑洞模型的现象学扩展~\deco~，通过引入有效紧致参数（effective compactness parameter）刻画并合形态对双黑洞预期的偏离；对所有高显著性GWTC-3事件进行参数估计，并利用从应变数据中扣除最大似然BBH和~\deco~波形后的时-频残差（time–frequency residuals）评估数据是否更优地由紧致度变形描述。

Result: 识别出三类后验形态：60%事件呈现近高斯峰且紧致度$C\sim0.5$，符合双黑洞预期；部分事件出现高紧致度支撑（$C\ge0.8$）；约20%事件表现出主导的低紧致度模态（$C\sim0.15$），但该模态在从更高起始频率分析Livingston数据时消失，表明其源于低频噪声伪影。唯一例外是GW231123，需将两个探测器数据均从50Hz以上分析才能移除低紧致度模态。

Conclusion: 所有考虑的GWTC-3观测事件本质上均与双黑洞源一致；低频数据处理是区分真实物理偏离与噪声伪影的关键步骤，该项工作为当前及未来引力波探测中基于紧致度的并合形态测试提供了基准。

Abstract: Several gravitational wave (GW) observations have been identified as binary black hole (BBH) mergers, including systems with component masses that challenge typical formation scenarios. These observations motivate broader tests of whether the detected sources are consistent with this interpretation. We address this question using~\deco~, an existing phenomenological extension of a BBH model that uses an effective compactness parameter to characterize departures from the expected merger morphology. Applying this model to all high-significance BBH events from GWTC-3, we establish~\deco~as a robust test of the nature of compact binaries. In preliminary analyses we identify three recurring posterior morphologies: (i) near-Gaussian peaks consistent with the BBH expectation $C\sim0.5$, seen in 60\% of events; (ii) posteriors with additional high-compactness support $(C\ge0.8)$; and (iii) dominant low-compactness modes near $C\sim0.15$ in $\sim 20\%$ of cases. For the latter, the low-compactness modes disappear when the data, especially from Livingston, are analyzed from a higher starting frequency, indicating sensitivity to low-frequency noise artefacts. We further use time--frequency residuals, computed after subtracting maximum-likelihood BBH and~\deco~waveforms from the strain data, to assess if the data is better described by a compactness-based deformation. With this analysis, we conclude that all of the GWTC-3 observations that we have considered are indeed consistent with BBH sources. The exception is the high-mass GW231123 signal, for which data from \emph{both} detectors must be analyzed above 50Hz to remove a low-compactness mode. This study shows that low-frequency data treatment is crucial before attributing apparent deviations from BBH expectations to exotic physics, and provides a benchmark for compactness-based tests of merger morphology in current and future GW detections.

</details>


### [88] [Establishing Compactness as a Population Observable in Gravitational-Wave Astronomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31364)
*Shrobana Ghosh,Charlie Hoy,Mark Hannam,Frank Ohme*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过引入有效致密参数（effective compactness parameter），首次在引力波数据中对黑洞并合候选体的致密性进行直接测量，证实GWTC-3中所有高显著性信号均与黑洞假说一致，并将低致密奇异双星的并合率限制在较低水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典黑洞是最致密天体，在史瓦西极限（Schwarzschild limit）下致密度C=0.5；然而此前从未在引力波数据中直接测量并合天体的致密性以验证其黑洞本质。

Method: 本文通过有效致密参数（effective compactness parameter）直接探测双星并合过程中的最近距离（closest approach），从而对引力波数据中疑似黑洞并合事件的性质进行测量。

Result: 首次以高置信度表明GWTC-3中所有高显著性信号均与黑洞假说一致；层次化分析（hierarchical analysis）给出有效致密度C_eff=0.5^{+0.3}_{-0.1}，并将低致密奇异双星的并合率限制在<0.7 Gpc^{-3} yr^{-1}。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了致密度（compactness）作为引力波天文学（gravitational wave astronomy）中一项关键可观测量的地位。

Abstract: Classically, black holes (BHs) are the most compact objects predicted in nature with C=0.5 in the Schwarzschild limit; C is defined as the mass-to-radius ratio in geometric units. In this work we perform a novel measurement on the nature of putative BH mergers in the gravitational wave (GW) data by directly probing the binary's closest approach through an effective compactness parameter. We confidently show all such high-significance signals in GWTC-3 are consistent with the BH hypothesis for the first time. Our hierarchical analysis yields $C_{\rm eff} = 0.5^{+0.3}_{-0.1}$, and we further limit the merger rate of low-compactness exotic binaries to $< 0.7\,{\rm Gpc}^{-3}\,{\rm yr}^{-1}$. This work establishes compactness as a key observable in GW astronomy.

### [89] [The unavoidable de Sitter fate of a scale-invariant Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31472)
*Chiara Cecchini,Massimiliano Rinaldi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究证明，在广义的尺度不变标量-张量引力理论（scale-invariant scalar-tensor theory）中，除非标量场的四次自耦合严格为零，否则任何稳定的、非简并引力动力学配置都必须携带非零宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）。由于该条件无法抵御辐射修正（radiative corrections），残余宇宙学常数是该类理论的普适预测，暗示暗能量（dark energy）可能是早期宇宙尺度不变相（scale-invariant phase）的自然结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索尺度不变标量-张量引力理论中宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）存在的必然性，并解释暗能量（dark energy）是否可能源于早期宇宙的尺度不变相（scale-invariant phase）。

Method: 考虑一类非常广义的尺度不变标量-张量引力理论（scale-invariant scalar-tensor theory）及其平坦宇宙学解，通过分析稳定配置与引力动力学非简并性条件，推导宇宙学常数存在的必要条件。

Result: 任何具有非简并引力动力学的稳定配置都携带非零宇宙学常数，除非标量场的四次自耦合（quartic self-coupling）为零；而该零点条件不受辐射修正（radiative corrections）保护，因此残余宇宙学常数是此类理论的普适预测。

Conclusion: 暗能量（dark energy）可能是早期宇宙尺度不变相（scale-invariant phase）的自然结果，残余宇宙学常数（residual cosmological constant）作为尺度不变标量-张量引力理论的一个普适且稳健的预测出现。

Abstract: We consider a very general scale-invariant scalar-tensor theory of gravity and its flat cosmological solutions. We show that any stable configuration with non-degenerate gravitational dynamics carries a non-vanishing cosmological constant, unless the quartic self-coupling of the scalar field vanishes. Since this condition is not protected against radiative corrections, a residual cosmological constant is expected as a generic and robust prediction of this class of theories. This result suggests that dark energy may be a natural consequence of an early scale-invariant phase of the Universe.

### [90] [Probing globular clusters parameters through gravitational wave lensing with stellar-mass black hole binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31531)
*Sreekanth Harikumar,Abbas Askar,Michał Bejger,Marek Biesiada,Martin Hendry,Justin Janquart*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了球状星团（GCs）在波光学（wave-optics） regime 下对引力波（GWs）的引力透镜效应，并展示了如何利用这种效应来探测球状星团的内在特性（尤其是中心速度弥散）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将球状星团建模为奇异等温球（singular isothermal spheres），模拟类似GW150914的透镜引力波信号，并使用包含源参数和透镜参数的波形模板（waveform templates）进行贝叶斯参数估计（Bayesian parameter estimation）。

Result: 有效透镜质量（effective lensing mass）可以被恢复，结合引力波天球定位信息（sky localization information）和星团目录（GC catalogs），可估算星团的速度弥散。对于有利的源-透镜对准情况，注入值能够在置信区间内被良好恢复。

Conclusion: 透镜引力波可为球状星团动力学（GC dynamics）提供一种互补的探测手段，并激励在当前及未来的观测中搜寻此类透镜特征。

Abstract: Globular clusters (GCs) can act as gravitational lenses for gravitational waves(GWs) in the wave-optics regime, imprinting frequency-dependent signatures on the observed signal. We investigate whether such lensing effects can be used to probe intrinsic properties of GCs, in particular their central velocity dispersion. Modeling GCs as singular isothermal spheres, we simulate lensed GW150914-like signals and perform Bayesian parameter estimation using waveform templates that include both source and lens parameters. We show that the effective lensing mass can be recovered and, when combined with GW sky localization information and GC catalogs, allows for an estimate of the cluster velocity dispersion. For favorable source-lens alignments, the injected values are well recovered within credible intervals. Our results demonstrate that lensed GWs can provide a complementary probe of GC dynamics and motivate searches for such signatures in current and future observations.

### [91] [Eikonal Ringing, Shadows, Lensing, Grey-Body Factors, and Binding Energy of Asymptotically Flat Regular Black Holes in Phantom Dirac-Born-Infeld Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31710)
*Mardon Abdullaev,Gumisbek Allambergenov,Diyorbek Rashidov,Pakhlavon Jamolov,Javlon Rayimbaev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在幻影狄拉克-玻恩-因费尔德（phantom DBI）引力框架下，针对渐近平坦正则黑洞几何，建立了从类光测地线到类时测地线（包括eikonal准正则模态、阴影、强透镜、灰体因子及束缚能）的统一测地线光学描述，并证明这些可观测量均由一个关于核心尺寸参数的无量纲函数控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为渐近平坦正则黑洞几何提供一套完整的测地线光学（geodesic-optics）描述，涵盖eikonal准正则 ringing、黑洞阴影（shadow）、强透镜（strong lensing）、灰体因子（grey-body factors, GBFs）以及有质量粒子的束缚能（binding energy），并揭示这些可观测量之间的内在联系。

Method: 采用测地线光学方法分析类光与类时测地线结构；利用零轨道（null-orbit）结构的紧致解析处理，导出轨道频率（orbital frequency）和Lyapunov指数（Lyapunov exponent）的精确表达式；针对类时圆周运动（timelike circular motion），推导比能量（specific energy）与比角动量（specific angular momentum）的精确表达式，并以封闭隐式形式给出最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO）条件。

Result: 不稳定光子轨道（unstable photon orbit）在整个黑洞分支上保持施瓦西类（Schwarzschild-like）坐标半径不变，轨道频率与Lyapunov指数精确一致；eikonal准正则模态（quasinormal modes, QNMs）、阴影半径、灰体因子及强偏折可观测量均由一个关于核心尺寸参数的无量纲函数控制；随着正则核心增大，ISCO束缚效率（binding efficiency）降低。

Conclusion: 该构造在正则黑洞度规与其主要测地线可观测量之间提供了一个精确的单参数桥梁，为深入理解正则黑洞的观测特征提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We develop a geodesic-optics description of eikonal quasinormal ringing, blackhole shadows, strong lensing, grey-body factors (GBFs), and the binding energy of massive particles for the asymptotically flat regular black-hole geometry obtained in phantom Dirac-Born-Infeld (DBI) gravity. The null-orbit structure admits an especially compact analytic treatment. The unstable photon orbit remains at the Schwarzschild-like coordinate radius throughout the black-hole branch, while the orbital frequency and Lyapunov exponent coincide exactly. Consequently, eikonal quasinormal modes (QNMs), shadow radius, GBFs, and strong-deflection observables are all governed by a single dimensionless function of the core-size parameter. For timelike circular motion, we derive exact expressions for the specific energy and angular momentum, obtain the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) condition in closed implicit form, and show that the ISCO binding efficiency decreases as the regular core grows. We present illustrative plots for the exact geodesic invariants, the corresponding grey-body profiles, and the timelike binding-energy curves. The resulting construction provides an exact one-parameter bridge between the regular black-hole metric and its leading geodesic observables.

### [92] [Electromagnetic radiation from a point-like charge in a weak gravitational wave: a Shapiro-delay-motivated approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31999)
*Vladimir Epp,Konstantin Osetrin,Taya But*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了引力波中自由落体点电荷的电磁场。引力波作为闵可夫斯基度规的弱扰动，使得初始静态库仑场变得与时间相关并产生辐射。通过一阶微扰论求解麦克斯韦方程组，得到点电荷电磁势在整个空间的积分表达式，并借助Shapiro效应思想进行正则化。对于单色、任意偏振的引力波，显式计算出远区势及引力波诱导电磁辐射的角分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究引力波与电磁场的相互作用，具体分析一个自由落体点电荷在引力波背景下的电磁响应，探索引力波如何诱导电磁辐射。

Method: 将引力波视为闵可夫斯基度规（Minkowski metric）的弱扰动，在一阶微扰论（first order perturbation theory）框架下求解麦克斯韦方程组（Maxwell's equations），得到点电荷电磁四势（electromagnetic four-potential）在整个空间中的积分形式（quadratures）。利用受引力场中辐射时间延迟的Shapiro效应（Shapiro effect）启发的正则化方法处理势函数。对单色、任意偏振引力波情形，显式计算远区（far zone）的势函数。

Result: 获得了点电荷电磁势在整个空间中的积分表达式，并在正则化后显式给出远区势的解。推导出单色、任意偏振引力波诱导的电磁辐射的角分布（angular distribution）。

Conclusion: 初始静态的库仑场在引力波作用下变得与时间相关并产生电磁辐射。本文所采用的正则化方法和微扰计算为定量描述引力波-电磁相互作用提供了有效途径。

Abstract: We investigate the field of a point-like electric charge freely falling in a gravitational wave. In the presence of a gravitational wave, the initially static Coulomb field of the charge becomes time-dependent and generates corresponding radiation. The gravitational wave is treated as a weak perturbation of the Minkowski metric. The electromagnetic four-potential of the charge is sought as a solution to Maxwell's equations in the gravitational wave metric, to first order in perturbation theory. The potentials of the point charge are found in quadratures throughout the space. To regularize the potentials, an approach motivated by the Shapiro effect for the time delay of radiation in a gravitational field is used. The potentials of the charge in the far zone are calculated explicitly for a monochromatic, arbitrarily polarized gravitational wave. The angular distribution of the electromagnetic radiation induced by the gravitational wave is obtained.

</details>

### [93] [Critically Enhanced Magnon Transport in Low-dimensional Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30784)
*Ping Tang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个从体材料到二维极限的磁振子输运理论，发现具有长程偶极相互作用的（准）二维磁性薄膜中磁振子电导率呈对数发散，解释了超薄钇铁石榴石薄膜中观测到的异常高磁振子电导率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受超薄磁性薄膜和单层范德华磁体实验进展的推动，旨在理解空间维度从体材料到二维极限的跨越过程中磁振子输运性质的变化机制。

Method: 建立了一个涵盖从体材料到二维极限过渡区的磁性薄膜磁振子输运理论框架，重点分析了长程偶极相互作用在（准）二维体系中的效应。

Result: 发现磁振子电导率（magnon conductivity）在具有长程偶极相互作用的磁性软且稳定的（准）二维磁体中呈对数发散（logarithmically divergent），而这一临界增强在体材料体系中不存在。

Conclusion: 该结果揭示了低维体系中磁振子输运增强的内在机制，并表明原子级薄磁体可用于设计高效磁振子导体。

Abstract: Transport properties of (quasi)particles in condensed matter depend profoundly on the spatial dimension. Motivated by recent advances in growing ultrathin magnetic films and monolayer van der Waals magnets, we present a theory of magnon transport in magnetic films spanning the crossover from bulk to the two-dimensional (2D) limit. We find a magnon conductivity that diverges~\emph{logarithmically} in magnetically soft but stable (quasi)2D magnets with long-range dipolar interactions. This critical enhancement is absent in bulk systems and may explain the unusually large magnon conductivities recently observed in ultrathin yttrium iron garnet films. Our results reveal an intrinsic mechanism for enhanced magnon transport in low dimensions and highlight the potential for engineering high-efficiency magnon conductors in atomically thin magnets.

Method: 通过时间周期性Floquet调制（time-periodic Floquet modulation）在频率域耦合多模磁子共振（multimode magnon resonances），在单个YIG器件内实现电子可调的模间相互作用，从而构建可重构的模式空间晶格（mode-space lattice）。

Result: 实验证实了在不增加器件物理尺寸的情况下，可实现高维磁子动力学（high-dimensional magnonic dynamics），包括布洛赫振荡（Bloch oscillation）等功能的可重构模式空间晶格。

Conclusion: 合成维度方法为集成磁子技术（integrated magnonic technologies）提供了可扩展且可编程的路径，使磁子系统成为工程实现非平衡态涌现现象（emergent phenomena）的有力平台。

Abstract: Magnonic systems, which exploit spin-wave excitations in magnetic materials, offer a promising platform for coherent information processing due to their low dissipation, strong nonlinearities, and intrinsic nonreciprocity. However, scaling magnonic circuits remains challenging, particularly with low-loss insulators such as yttrium iron garnet (YIG), which are difficult to pattern. Here, we experimentally realize a synthetic dimension in a magnonic system by coupling multimode magnon resonances in the frequency domain using time-periodic Floquet modulation. This approach enables electronically tunable interactions between discrete modes within a single YIG device, forming a reconfigurable mode-space lattice that supports functionalities such as Bloch oscillation. Our results demonstrate that high-dimensional magnonic dynamics can be achieved without increasing device footprint, establishing synthetic dimensions as a scalable and programmable route for integrated magnonic technologies. This advancement positions magnonic systems as promising platforms for engineering emergent phenomena that are inaccessible at equilibrium.

### [95] [Carbon encapsulation of levitated Au nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30858)
*Joyce E. Coppock,Sunghyun Kim,B. E. Kane*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过测量四极离子阱中约200 nm直径金纳米颗粒的荷质比（Q/M），发现在高真空环境下经532 nm激光脉冲重复加热后，颗粒表面会形成一层阻碍蒸发的屏障层。实验表明，该屏障层很可能源于金表面石墨烯（graphene）的生长与氧化，但其形成速率不依赖于所添加含碳气体（CO、C₂H₄、CO₂）的压力，提示一种稀有表面态可能催化了碳引入反应，而重复激光脉冲加热对于碳的持续吸附和石墨烯层的生长是必需的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究纳米尺度金颗粒在高真空环境下经激光脉冲加热时，表面形成蒸发屏障层的机制及其影响因素。

Method: 采用四极离子阱（quadrupole ion trap）约束直径约200 nm的金纳米颗粒，通过精密测量荷质比（Q/M）随时间的变化，表征屏障层的形成过程，并系统考察脉冲间隔变化以及向真空腔中添加不同气体（CO、C₂H₄、CO₂、O₂）的影响。

Result: 发现颗粒质量在长时间真空暴露后缓慢增加，表明屏障层生长；预先暴露于CO形成屏障的颗粒，在后续暴露于O₂时质量迅速下降；屏障形成速率不依赖于CO、C₂H₄、CO₂等含碳气体的压力。

Conclusion: 实验结果与金表面石墨烯（graphene）层的生长及其后续氧化过程一致，该石墨烯层构成了蒸发屏障。屏障形成不依赖含碳气体压力，提示可能存在一种稀有表面态（rare surface state）催化碳引入反应；重复激光脉冲加热对于碳的扩散或表面态的再生、从而实现石墨烯层的持续生长是必要的。

Abstract: We investigate the formation of a barrier to evaporation that develops when levitated nanoscale Au nanoparticles are exposed to pulses of 532 nm laser radiation in a high vacuum (pressure $p=10^{-8}-10^{-7}$ Torr) environment. Our data are derived from precision measurements of the charge to mass ratio ($Q/M$) of $\sim$200 nm diameter Au particles confined in a quadrupole ion trap. We characterize the development of the barrier over time as the particle is repeatedly heated with laser pulses and determine the impact of variations of the interval between pulses and of exposure to several gases added to the vacuum chamber. We observe a slow increase in the mass of particles upon prolonged exposure to the vacuum, which we attribute to the growth of a barrier layer. For particles that have acquired a barrier during exposure to CO, we observe a rapid decrease in their mass upon subsequent exposure to O$_2$. These findings are consistent with the growth and subsequent oxidation of a graphene layer on the Au that forms the barrier to evaporation. However, we have not found that the rate of formation of the barrier depends on the pressure of carbon-containing gases (CO, C$_2$H$_4$, CO$_2$) we have added to the chamber. We hypothesize that a rare surface state on the solid Au particle catalyzes the reaction that introduces C to the particle. Repeated laser pulse heating is necessary--either to enable diffusion away from this state or to create fresh states that allow continued C uptake--to facilitate the growth of the surface graphene layer.

Abstract: Doping of transition metal oxides such as CaFe$_3$O$_5$ offers a controlled way to tune the interplay of charge, spin, and lattice degrees of freedom, yet local-probe studies remain difficult because strong correlations and dynamic charge-spin fluctuations obscure fine spectroscopic features in powder samples. Here, we employ quantum magnetometry based on nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in nanodiamonds impressed into an Mn-doped CaFe$_3$O$_5$ powder pellet to probe static and dynamic magnetic fields at the nanoscale across the weak ferromagnetic transition. The splitting and broadening of the optically detected magnetic resonance (ODMR) spectra exhibit an order-parameter-like increase by ~ 15 MHz upon cooling below the critical temperature, T$_{\rm c}$. Concomitantly, the spin-lattice relaxation rate, 1/T$_1$, exhibits a pronounced, divergence-like enhancement at T$_{\rm c}$, increasing by about one order of magnitude from its high-temperature value. Moreover, detailed lineshape fits of ODMR spectra together with the stretched-exponential NV magnetization recovery curves corroborate the proposed electronic phase segregation in charge-ordered and charge-averaged phases at the nanometric scales. The presented study demonstrates the viability of using nanodiamonds as a platform for nanoscale magnetic probing of strongly correlated matter, including phenomena such as electronic phase separation.

### [97] [Topological random alloy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30917)
*Subrata Pachhal,Aziz Hasan,Adhip Agarwala*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种拓扑随机二元合金（topological random binary alloy）的最小模型，发现掺杂可导致以掺杂剂为中心的拓扑手性电流环（dopant-centric chiral current loops），这些电流环能在平庸宿主中形成拓扑畴并引发拓扑相变，或在拓扑宿主中异常地稳定由畴间边缘模式（inter-domain edge modes）介导的金属态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑物相（topological phases of matter）通常存在于晶体材料中，为了将对其理解拓展到完美化学计量比（perfect stoichiometry）之外，本研究希望探索无序掺杂体系中拓扑相的实现机制。

Method: 引入了一个拓扑随机二元合金（topological random binary alloy）的最小模型，通过分析掺杂对近量子反常霍尔绝缘体（quantum anomalous Hall insulator）的影响，研究杂质能带工程（impurity-band engineering）的奇异物态。

Result: 与常规半导体中杂质钉扎Wannier电荷中心（Wannier charge centers）不同，掺杂近量子反常霍尔绝缘体会产生以掺杂剂为中心的手性电流环；即便在低掺杂浓度下，这些电流环也能在平庸宿主中形成拓扑畴并触发拓扑相变；当宿主的手性与掺杂剂相反时，掺杂反而会稳定由畴间边缘模式（inter-domain edge modes）介导体态输运的金属相。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了一种通过掺杂工程实现拓扑相变和非常规金属态的普适机制，拓展了对拓扑物相在非理想化学计量比条件下行为的理解。

Abstract: Topological phases of matter are often realized in crystalline materials. To extend their understanding beyond perfect stoichiometry, we introduce a minimal model of a topological random binary alloy and show that the system realizes an exotic form of impurity-band engineering. We reveal that, in contrast to Wannier charge centers pinned by impurities in conventional semiconductors, doping a proximate quantum anomalous Hall insulator results in dopant-centric chiral current loops. The nature of such current loops is intrinsically tied to the properties of both the host and the dopant. We demonstrate that, even at dilute dopant density, these current loops can form topological domains in an otherwise trivial host and trigger a topological phase transition. On the other hand, doping a topological host having chirality opposite to that of the dopants can unexpectedly stabilize a metallic phase in which bulk transport is mediated by inter-domain edge modes.

### [98] [Hodge Topology of Semiclassical Transport: A Coordinate-Free Geometric Framework for the Anomalous Hall Effect and Non-Linear Berry Dipole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31409)
*Zhi-Wei Wang,Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文建立了拓扑能带中反常输运的无坐标微分几何框架，利用布里渊区的Hodge-de Rham分解，从Berry曲率2-形式中分离出全局光滑的几何1-形式代理势$\mathcal{A}$，从而消除了传统方法中的数学奇异性（Dirac弦），并在线性和非线性输运、Maximally Localized Wannier Function（MLWF）规范映射以及数值稳定性方面展现出显著优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于量子Berry联络（Berry connection）的形式化在处理具有非零陈数（Chern number）的能带时面临数学奇异性（Dirac弦）的困扰；需要一种无奇点、全局光滑的几何框架来统一描述拓扑能带中的反常输运。

Method: 对Berry曲率2-形式施加Hodge-de Rham分解（Hodge-de Rham decomposition），从中分离出量子化的拓扑磁单极通量（topological monopole flux）和一个全局光滑的几何1-形式代理势$\mathcal{A}$；对线性输运采用余面积公式（co-area formula）进行精确几何推导；对非线性输运利用该光滑势统一几何描述；通过施加连续的Coulomb-Hodge规范（Coulomb-Hodge gauge, $δ\mathcal{A} = 0$）和消失的基本1-环上的调和和乐（harmonic holonomies）条件，将$\mathcal{A}$映射到平凡能带中的MLWF规范；通过求解Hodge Laplacian消除宏观布里渊区平均拓扑发散（uniform $\mathbf{R}=0$ zero-mode）。

Result: 线性横向输运响应被精确分解为连续的费米海拓扑背景项和局域的费米面几何线积分项；非线性输运描述统一且具有高数值稳定性；$\mathcal{A}$为拓扑受阻能带提供了非奇异的计算代理；所提出的协变形式化在离散$\mathbf{k}$-格点噪声下与标准方法具有相当的算法鲁棒性。

Conclusion: Hodge-de Rham分解方法提供了一种数学上一致、无奇异性的协变框架，可有效处理任意陈数的拓扑能带中的反常输运，在理论精确性和数值稳定性之间取得了良好平衡。

Abstract: We establish a coordinate-free differential geometric framework for anomalous transport in topological bands using the Hodge-de Rham decomposition of the Brillouin zone. Standard formulations face mathematical singularities (Dirac strings) when using the quantum Berry connection in bands with non-zero Chern numbers. Applying this decomposition to the Berry curvature 2-form isolates the quantized topological monopole flux from a globally smooth geometric 1-form proxy potential, $\mathcal{A}$. Substituting this regularized potential into semiclassical transport integrals yields distinct analytical advantages. For linear transverse transport, our cohomological decomposition enables an exact geometric derivation of Haldane's insight via the co-area formula, partitioning the response into a continuous Fermi sea topological background and a localized Fermi surface geometric line integral. For non-linear transport, this globally smooth proxy unifies the geometric description, reproducing the high numerical stability of scalar integration-by-parts techniques directly from its exact sector, accommodating arbitrary Chern numbers. By enforcing the continuous Coulomb-Hodge gauge ($δ\mathcal{A} = 0$) alongside vanishing harmonic holonomies over fundamental 1-cycles ($\oint_{γ_i} \mathcal{A} = 0$), we map the Hodge potential $\mathcal{A}$ to the Maximally Localized Wannier Function (MLWF) gauge in trivial bands, providing a non-singular computational proxy for topologically obstructed bands. Finally, we analytically demonstrate that solving the Hodge Laplacian for $\mathcal{A}$ zeroes the macroscopic Brillouin zone average (uniform $\mathbf{R}=0$ zero-mode) topological divergence, yielding a mathematically consistent covariant formulation that matches the algorithmic robustness of standard methods against discrete $\mathbf{k}$-grid noise.

</details>


### [99] [Tunable Extended Magnetic Non-Fermi Liquid in Graphene Moiré Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31028)

Conclusion: 本研究建立了一个超越传统理论框架的高度可调谐平台，用于研究以多种行为表现的非费米液体物理（non-Fermi liquid physics）的组织原理（organizing principles）。

Abstract: Exploring exotic quantum metallic states beyond Landau's Fermi liquid theory remains a central focus in condensed matter physics. Such non-Fermi liquid behavior is mostly observed near quantum criticality, yet growing attention is directed toward extended NFL phases with intrinsic quantum fluctuations rooted in the extended ground state. While these extended NFL states have been previously reported only in a limited set of d- and f-electron systems, realizing a single, highly tunable platform capable of exhibiting multiple resistance exponent values is essential for uncovering the connection between the resistance exponent and the dominant quantum fluctuations coupled to quasiparticles. However, corresponding experimental progress remains elusive. Here, we report the observation of tunable extended non-Fermi liquid behavior in twisted double bilayer graphene encapsulated by aligned hBN layers. This NFL phase spans a broad range of carrier densities and exhibiting a carrier density dependent resistance exponent. Combined with temperature dependent resistance, magnetotransport and differential resistance measurements, these findings support a scenario where strong quantum fluctuations emerge from the interplay between localized and itinerant carriers. Our work establishes a highly tunable platform beyond conventional frameworks to investigate the organizing principles of non-Fermi liquid physics manifested in diverse behaviors.

### [100] [Andreev reflection mediated by topological corner states in a two-dimensional honeycomb lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31079)
*Kai-Tong Wang,Yunjin Yu,Fuming Xu,Jian Wang*

Abstract: Topological corner states in two-dimensional second-order topological insulators (SOTIs) are localized in real space. We numerically demonstrate that such localized topological corner states can mediate Andreev reflection when coupled to a superconducting lead. We consider a transport setup based on a two-dimensional honeycomb lattice, consisting of a normal lead, a central SOTI region, and a superconducting lead. The central SOTI region is described by the modified Kane--Mele model with an in-plane Zeeman field and hosts topological corner states in a diamond-shaped flake. Although the central region is insulating, the local density of states shows that incident electrons can turn the localized corner state into an extended scattering state, which forms a resonant tunneling channel to the superconducting lead. This process leads to a perfect Andreev reflection peak near zero energy. Away from this resonance, antiresonance dips appear in the Andreev reflection spectrum, and their positions can be tuned by the Zeeman field strength. We show that the suppression of Andreev reflection is caused by quantum interference and the imbalance between electron and hole dwell times in the central region. These results demonstrate that topological corner states can provide a resonant tunneling path to the superconducting interface and mediate Andreev reflection in second-order topological systems.

</details>


### [101] [Observation of Intrinsic Anderson Localization in Few-Layer ReS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31233)
*Shreya Paul,Pritam Das,Devarshi Chakrabarty,Shamashis Sengupta,Sajal Dhara*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过全干法范德华组装（all-dry van der Waals assembly）和六方氮化硼（hBN）栅介质消除外部制备诱导的无序，在少层二硫化铼（ReS₂）中观测到本征安德森局域化（intrinsic Anderson localization），并通过温度依赖的输运测量定量表征了二维Mott变程跳跃（Mott VRH）及其局域化长度。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用全干法范德华组装（all-dry van der Waals assembly）消除外部制备诱导的无序，并使用六方氮化硼（hBN）栅介质抑制界面电荷捕获。通过温度依赖的输运测量分析电阻随温度的变化关系，识别跳跃传导机制的转变，并利用激活能对栅极电压的非单调依赖关系提取导带尾态密度（band-tail density of states）。

Result: 温度依赖的输运显示从最近邻跳跃（nearest-neighbor hopping）到二维（2D）Mott变程跳跃（variable-range hopping, VRH）的交叉。激活能对栅极电压呈现非单调依赖，直接揭示了ReS₂导带的能量分辨带尾态密度。二维Mott VRH给出的局域化长度（localization length）为（3.5 ± 0.1）nm，比无序主导的器件大一个数量级。

Conclusion: 通过消除外部无序，成功观测到少层ReS₂中的本征安德森局域化，并实现对其局域化长度的定量表征。该结果表明，外部无序在以往器件中显著掩盖了本征局域化行为，而优化制备工艺可以揭示二维材料中由降维驱动的电子局域化本质。

Abstract: Electron localization phenomena are expected to play an important role in the transport properties of two-dimensional materials. Rhenium disulfide (ReS$_2$), with its narrow conduction bandwidth, is uniquely susceptible to this effect. However, extrinsic disorder caused by fabrication methods obscures inherent localization behavior arising from reduced dimensionality and degrades transport properties. We report intrinsic Anderson localization in few-layer ReS$_2$ by eliminating extrinsic fabrication-induced disorder through all-dry van der Waals assembly and suppressing interface charge trapping through a hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) gate dielectric. Temperature-dependent transport reveals a crossover from nearest-neighbor hopping to two-dimensional (2D) Mott variable-range hopping (VRH). The non-monotonic gate-voltage dependence of activation energy provides direct access to the energy-resolved band-tail density of states of the ReS$_2$ conduction band. 2D Mott VRH yields a localization length of (3.5 $\pm$ 0.1) nm, an order of magnitude larger than disorder-dominated devices, providing a quantitative characterization of intrinsic Anderson localization in ReS$_2$.

### [102] [Thermal rectification due to phonon confinement in nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31263)
*Alexej D. Semenov,Mariia Sidorova,Alessio Zaccone,Marcel Di Vece*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明，仅通过声子几何限制（phonon confinement），在两个不同尺寸但材料相同的球形纳米颗粒接触点处即可产生热整流（thermal rectification）效应。作者基于卡西米尔区（Casimir regime）的声子限制与声子射线追踪建立了分析模型，推导了热流与整流效率关于颗粒尺寸和温度的表达式。模型预测在室温下半径几十纳米的颗粒可实现百分之零点几的整流效率，低温下效率更高。该机制无需材料非均匀性或强非线性，为颗粒纳米材料中的热整流提供了一条简洁可扩展的路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有热整流机制通常依赖材料异质性（material heterogeneity）或强非线性（strong nonlinearity），结构复杂且可扩展性有限。探索在完全均匀材料中仅通过几何尺寸效应实现方向依赖热传输的可能性，具有基础物理意义和器件应用价值。

Method: 基于声子限制（phonon confinement）和卡西米尔区（Casimir regime）的声子射线追踪（phonon ray-tracing）建立分析模型，推导了热流和整流效率作为颗粒半径和温度的解析表达式。

Result: 模型预测，对于半径几十纳米的球形纳米颗粒，室温下整流效率可达百分之零点几；低温下效率显著增大。整流源于尺寸依赖的声子态密度间隙（size-dependent gap in the phonon density of states）对不同方向长波声子的非对称抑制。

Conclusion: 所提出的几何限制机制为颗粒纳米材料（granular nanomaterials）中的热整流提供了一条简洁且可扩展的路径，无需材料异质性或强非线性即可实现方向依赖的热输运。

Abstract: We demonstrate that thermal rectification can arise at the contact between two spherical nanoparticles of identical material but different size due to the geometric confinement of phonons. This confinement suppresses long-wavelength phonons differently in differently sized particles and creates a size-dependent gap in the phonon density of states. This gives rise to direction-dependent heat transport even in perfectly homogeneous materials. We develop an analytical model based on phonon confinement and phonon ray-tracing in the Casimir regime and derive expressions for heat fluxes and rectification efficiency as functions of particle sizes and temperatures. The model predicts measurable rectification efficiencies for nanoparticles with radii of a few tens of nanometers, reaching fraction of percent at room temperature and much larger values at low temperatures. The proposed mechanism provides a straightforward and scalable route to thermal rectification in granular nanomaterials without requiring material heterogeneity or strong nonlinearities.

Abstract: Moire flat bands in graphene systems proximitized by transition-metal dichalcogenides (TMDCs) provide a setting where spin-orbit coupling (SOC) can reshape band topology. The crystallographic alignment angle twist angle between TMDC and graphene layers is predicted to tune the balance of Ising and Rashba SOC, but a combined theoretical and experimental understanding of how twist angle governs the topological character of correlated states has not been systematically established. Here we show that in chiral-stacked twisted double bilayer graphene in proximity to WSe2, twist angle between graphene and WSe2 determines the topological character of correlated Chern insulators. Continuum model calculations reveal that Ising spin-orbit coupling dominates at zero twist angle, giving rise to flat bands with finite valley Chern numbers, whereas Rashba coupling dominates at larger twist angle, resulting in topologically trivial bands. Transport measurements at quarter filling confirm this picture: twist angle = 0 deg devices exhibit C = +1 Chern insulators, consistent with spontaneous isospin polarization, whereas twist angle = 15 degree devices show C = 0 despite exhibiting similar correlated insulating behavior. The sharp contrast establishes crystallographic alignment as a new tuning knob, complementary to twist angle, displacement field, and carrier density, for engineering correlated topological states in van der Waals heterostructures.

### [104] [Floquet Majorana flat bands and emergent Cooper pair symmetries in $p-$wave magnet$-$superconductor heterostructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31550)
*Subhendu Kumar Patra,Gaurab Kumar Dash,Manisha Thakurathi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了p波磁体与s波超导体构成的二维异质结界面，发现了七种不同的节点拓扑相，并揭示了周期性驱动可以产生新型弗洛凯（Floquet）拓扑超导态，包括零能及π马约拉纳平带，且这些拓扑模式对强无序具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析节点能隙闭合（nodal gap closings）识别拓扑相；引入周期性驱动实现静态相到弗洛凯拓扑区（Floquet topological regimes）的转变；采用无序条件下的数值模拟验证拓扑模式的鲁棒性。

Result: 发现了七种不同的节点拓扑相（nodal topological phases），其特征为马约拉纳零能平带（Majorana zero-energy flat bands）和量子化零偏压电导峰（quantized zero-bias conductance peaks）。系统有效p波性质产生具有偶频奇宇称和奇频偶宇称的自旋三重态配对关联（spin-triplet pairing correlations）。轨道间跳跃产生奇异的轨道单态项（orbital-singlet term），具有奇宇称和奇频率。周期性驱动产生零能和π马约拉纳平带，并通过弗洛凯求和定则（Floquet sum rule）影响输运特征。驱动产生多个具有更高缠绕数（winding numbers）的节点点（nodal points）和多重马约拉纳平带；弗洛凯自由度使对称允许的库珀对关联（Cooper-pair correlations）数量翻倍，其中一类存在于偶弗洛凯扇区（even-Floquet sectors）且有静态对应，另一类局限于奇弗洛凯扇区（odd-Floquet sectors），是静态系统无法存在的非平衡配对通道。拓扑模式在强无序下保持鲁棒。

Conclusion: 周期性驱动不仅能改变拓扑超导体的相图，还能创造静态系统中不存在的全新配对通道；这些拓扑模式对强无序具有鲁棒性，表明其在稳定容错应用（fault-tolerant applications）中具有潜力。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of topological superconductivity at the two-dimensional heterostructure interface between a $p$-wave magnet (pWM) and an $s$-wave superconductor. By analyzing nodal gap closings, we identify seven distinct nodal topological phases, each characterized by the presence of Majorana zero-energy flat bands and quantized zero-bias conductance peaks. We demonstrate that the effective $p$-wave nature of the system gives rise to spin-triplet pairing correlations with even-frequency, odd-parity and odd-frequency, even-parity symmetries. Notably, the introduction of inter-orbital hopping induces an exotic orbital-singlet term characterized by simultaneous odd-parity and odd-frequency. Furthermore, we explore the transition from static phases to Floquet topological regimes through periodic driving. These driven phases host both zero and $π$ Majorana flat bands, with transport signatures governed by the Floquet sum rule. Most significantly, we show that periodic driving fundamentally reshapes the topological and superconducting landscape by generating multiple nodal points that support higher winding numbers and multiple Majorana flat bands, while the emergent Floquet degree of freedom doubles the number of symmetry-allowed Cooper-pair correlations. The first class of correlations is hosted by the even-Floquet sectors and has a direct counterpart in the static limit. In contrast, the second is a distinct Floquet-generated class that confines to the odd-Floquet sectors, representing a fundamentally nonequilibrium pairing channel that cannot exist in static systems. Finally, we demonstrate the robustness of these topological modes against strong disorder, confirming their potential for stable fault-tolerant applications.

### [105] [High-harmonic spin-current signatures of altermagnetic spin-group symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31573)
*Koki Mizuno*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过扩展动力学对称性（dynamical symmetry）以包含自旋点群（spin point group）操作，推导了电荷流与自旋流的高次谐波产生（high-harmonic generation, HHG）选择定则（selection rules），并证明自旋流谐波可作为区分交磁（altermagnetic）、铁磁（ferromagnetic）和反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）等自旋点群相的动力学期探针（dynamical probe）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋点群（spin point group）虽能分类弱自旋-轨道耦合（weak spin-orbit coupling, weak SOC）体系中的磁相并表征交磁相（altermagnetic phases）的静态性质，但其动力学后果（dynamical consequences）尚未被充分探索。

Method: 通过将动力学对称性（dynamical symmetry）扩展至包含自旋点群操作（spin point group operations），推导了电荷流与自旋流高次谐波产生（high-harmonic generation）的选择定则（selection rules）。

Result: 在最小交磁模型（minimal altermagnetic model）中：沿轴线性极化驱动（axis-aligned linearly polarized drive）无法区分铁磁相与交磁相，但反铁磁相可通过对应自旋流谐波的缺失来识别；对角线线性极化驱动（diagonal linearly polarized drive）可在弱SOC自旋群描述中区分三种自旋点群（SPG）相；单螺旋圆极化驱动（single-helicity circularly polarized drive）则提供更清晰的自旋流谐波判据以区分它们与磁点群（magnetic-point-group）模仿相。

Conclusion: 自旋流谐波（spin current harmonics）可作为自旋群对称性（spin group symmetry）的动力学期探针（dynamical probe），揭示电荷流谐波无法获取的磁信息。

Abstract: Spin point groups classify magnetic phases in the weak spin-orbit coupling regime and characterize the static properties of altermagnetic phases, but their dynamical consequences remain largely unexplored. Here, we derive selection rules for high-harmonic generation of charge and spin currents by extending dynamical symmetry to include spin point group operations. Since spin currents transform under both real and spin space operations, whereas charge currents transform only under real space operations, spin current selection rules can reveal magnetic information that is inaccessible to charge current harmonics. In a minimal altermagnetic model, an axis-aligned linearly polarized drive is non-diagnostic for distinguishing ferromagnetic and altermagnetic phases, although the antiferromagnetic phase is distinguished by the absence of the corresponding spin-current harmonics. A diagonal linearly polarized drive distinguishes the three SPG phases within the weak-SOC spin-group description, whereas a single-helicity circularly polarized drive provides a sharper spin-current-harmonic criterion for distinguishing them from magnetic-point-group mimics. These results establish spin current harmonics as a dynamical probe of spin group symmetry.

### [106] [Topological zero-reflection points in multi-terminal quantum wire junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31586)
*Abhiram Soori,Udit Khanna,Diptiman Sen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 论文研究了非相互作用的多终端量子线结中的散射现象，发现具有二面体对称性的结在终端数 N≥4 时可出现精确零反射点，并通过散射矩阵、拓扑绕数、时间反演对称破缺等机制揭示了这些反射点的性质、稳定性及实验可观测特征。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析散射矩阵（scattering matrix），在能量 E 与结跳跃振幅 t' 构成的参数空间中识别反射消失点；利用反射振幅相位对应的整数绕数（winding number）提供拓扑描述；引入磁通打破时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）以探索更多反射点；通过 Friedel 振荡（Friedel oscillations）讨论实验特征。

Result: 对于 N≥4 的终端，存在精确零反射点，这些点表现出对 N 的奇偶依赖性，并在大 N 极限下渐近收敛到同一极限值；反射消失点可由整数绕数刻画，表明其对弱无序具有拓扑稳定性；磁通可诱导额外反射消失点，包括 N=3 情形；四终端 π-通量结中存在反射振幅在整个能带内消失的独特参数区域。

Conclusion: 多终端量子线结的反射消失点具有拓扑起源和对称性依赖特征，对弱无序和弱相互作用具有一定稳定性，可通过 Friedel 振荡等实验手段观测。

Abstract: We study scattering in noninteracting multi-terminal quantum wire junctions and show that junctions with dihedral symmetry can exhibit exact zero-reflection points for $N \ge 4$ terminals. By analyzing the scattering matrix, we identify these reflectionless points in the $(E,t')$ parameter space, where $E$ is the incident particle energy and $t'$ is the junction hopping amplitude. These points exhibit an even-odd dependence on $N$ and converge asymptotically to a common limiting value in the large-$N$ limit. We show that the reflectionless points are characterized by an integer winding number associated with the phase of the reflection amplitude, providing a topological description for their stability against weak on-site disorder. We also consider junctions with broken time-reversal symmetry and find that a magnetic flux can induce additional reflectionless points, including for the $N = 3$ case. For a four-terminal junction threaded by a $π$-flux, we identify a unique parameter regime in which the reflection amplitude vanishes over the entire energy band. Finally, we discuss experimental signatures through the behavior of Friedel oscillations and examine the stability of these reflectionless points in the presence of weak interactions.

### [107] [Beating micromagnetic limits on skyrmion stability by long-range frustration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31633)
*Shiwei Zhu,Moritz A. Goerzen,Changsheng Song,Dongzhe Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明长程交换阻挫（long-range exchange frustration）能够在不增大斯格明子（skyrmion）尺寸或磁能量标度的情况下提升其塌缩能垒，突破了微磁学（micromagnetics）的传统标度关系，并提出交换优化框架预测该机制可在物理现实条件下使能垒翻倍，为高稳定性纳米斯格明子的设计提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统微磁学模型普遍认为斯格明子稳定性与斯格明子尺寸或交换刚度（exchange stiffness）成正比，但这一标度关系限制了在纳米尺度同时实现小尺寸与高稳定性。本文旨在探索打破该标度关系的物理机制。

Method: 将连续微磁模型映射到自旋晶格哈密顿量（spin-lattice Hamiltonian），通过比较具有相同微磁参数但不同原子级交换相互作用的斯格明子的能垒差异，识别鞍点织构（saddle point textures）的关键作用，并建立交换优化框架进行预测。

Result: 发现具有相同微磁参数的斯格明子可因底层原子交换相互作用的不同而表现出显著不同的能量势垒；长程交换阻挫可在物理现实条件下（如超薄膜或范德瓦尔斯磁体）使塌缩能垒翻倍，且该结果在不同晶格对称性下均成立。

Conclusion: 揭示了微磁学模型的内在局限性，提出长程交换阻挫工程（long-range frustration engineering）作为实现高度稳定的纳米斯格明子的有效途径。

Abstract: Skyrmion stability is commonly assumed to scale with skyrmion size or exchange stiffness within micromagnetic models. Here, we demonstrate that long-range exchange frustration can break this paradigm, enhancing the collapse energy barrier without increasing skyrmion size or magnetic energy scale. By mapping the continuum model onto a spin-lattice Hamiltonian, we find that skyrmions with identical micromagnetic parameters can exhibit significantly different energy barriers, depending on their underlying atomistic exchange interactions. We attribute this behavior to saddle point textures, whose pronounced noncollinearity captures long-range frustration beyond the micromagnetic approximation. We further develop an exchange optimization framework to predict that long-range frustration can double the energy barrier in physically realistic conditions, possibly valid for ultrathin films or van der Waals magnets. These results hold across different lattice symmetries, revealing an intrinsic limitation of micromagnetics and establishing long-range frustration engineering as a promising route toward highly stable nanoscale skyrmions.

</details>


### [108] [Strain-Tunable Harmonic Responses in Valley-Polarized Bilayer Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31684)
*Narjes Kheirabadi,Aliasghar Shokri*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用低能有效哈密顿量和量子动力学形式，理论研究了单轴应变下谷极化双层石墨烯的线性和二阶非线性光学响应，发现应变能显著调控二阶谐波产生（SHG）信号，并通过改变应变符号实现非线性光电流的方向切换，为应变工程调控谷依赖非线性光学现象提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索单轴应变如何调控谷极化双层石墨烯（valley-polarized bilayer graphene）的二阶非线性光学响应，特别是二阶谐波产生（second-harmonic generation, SHG），并寻找通过应变工程实现机械可控的非线性光电流切换机制。

Method: 采用包含三角翘曲（trigonal warping）和应变诱导各向异性的低能有效哈密顿量（low-energy effective Hamiltonian），在量子动力学框架（quantum kinetic formalism）内计算光学极化率（optical susceptibilities）。

Result: 谷平衡时SHG信号因谷间抵消而消失，而有限谷极化可打破该抵消产生净SHG信号；单轴应变通过扭曲电子结构和改变赝自旋织构（pseudospin texture）产生高度各向异性的SHG谱；在光子能量约等于费米能E_f和2E_f处出现显著共振增强；改变应变符号可反转诱导的二阶谐波电流方向。

Conclusion: 应变工程是调控双层石墨烯中谷依赖非线性光学现象的有效手段，为可调谐中红外光子学和谷光电子学（valley-optoelectronics）应用提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the linear and second-order nonlinear optical responses of valley-polarized bilayer graphene under uniaxial strain. Employing a low-energy effective Hamiltonian that incorporates trigonal warping and strain-induced anisotropy, we calculate the optical susceptibilities within the quantum kinetic formalism. We show that, while the second-order response vanishes in valley-balanced bilayer graphene owing to the cancellation of contributions from opposite valleys, a finite valley polarization lifts this cancellation and enables a net second-harmonic generation (SHG) signal. Uniaxial strain substantially modifies the nonlinear response by distorting the low-energy electronic structure and altering the pseudospin texture, producing a highly anisotropic SHG spectrum. Pronounced resonant enhancements occur at photon energies $\hbarω\approx E_f$ and $\hbarω\approx 2E_f$, associated with two-photon and one-photon interband resonances, respectively. Remarkably, changing the sign of the strain parameter reverses the direction of the induced second-harmonic current, providing a mechanically controlled switching mechanism for nonlinear optical transport. These results establish strain engineering as an effective route for manipulating valley-dependent nonlinear optical phenomena in bilayer graphene and suggest new opportunities for tunable mid-infrared photonic and valley-optoelectronic applications.

### [109] [Energy-time entanglement from a monolithically integrated quantum dot on silicon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31775)
*Marcel Hohn,Imad Limame,Peter Ludewig,Chirag C. Palekar,Aris Koulas-Simos,Kerstin Volz,Stephan Reitzenstein*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文在硅衬底上单片集成（monolithically integrated）InGaAs/GaAs量子点，通过相干双光子激发实现双激子-激子级联的相干控制，并在Franson干涉仪中观测到能量-时间纠缠（energy–time entanglement），展示了可与硅基架构兼容的确定性纠缠光子源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可扩展量子光子技术（scalable quantum photonic technologies）需要与成熟半导体制造平台兼容的确定性纠缠光子源。自组装III-V族半导体量子点（self-assembled III-V semiconductor quantum dots）虽是最有前景的按需纠缠产生方案之一，但其与硅基架构的集成仍是一个核心挑战。

Method: 在硅衬底上单片生长InGaAs/GaAs量子点；采用相干双光子激发（coherent two-photon excitation）实现双激子-激子级联（biexciton–exciton cascade）的相干控制，通过拉比振荡（Rabi oscillations）和缀饰态形成（dressed-state formation）加以验证；利用四通道Franson干涉仪（four-channel Franson interferometer）测量双光子干涉（two-photon interference）。

Result: 在80 ps积分窗口下，双光子干涉可见度（visibility）达到$(64.0 \pm 7.0)\%$，在1600 ps窗口下达到$(49.4 \pm 1.9)\%$，短时间尺度下接近贝尔不等式违背（Bell inequality violation）阈值。

Conclusion: 单片集成的III-V-on-silicon量子点可作为能量-时间纠缠光子源，为可扩展量子光子技术提供可行方案。

Abstract: Scalable quantum photonic technologies require deterministic sources of entangled photons that are compatible with established semiconductor manufacturing platforms. While self-assembled III--V semiconductor quantum dots are among the most promising sources of on-demand entanglement generation, their integration with silicon-based architectures remains a central challenge. Here, we demonstrate energy--time entanglement from a single InGaAs/GaAs quantum dot monolithically grown on a silicon substrate. Under coherent two-photon excitation, we achieve coherent control of the biexciton--exciton cascade, evidenced by Rabi oscillations and dressed-state formation. Using a four-channel Franson interferometer, we observe phase-dependent two-photon interference with visibilities up to $(64.0 \pm 7.0)\%$ for an 80 ps integration window (and $(49.4 \pm 1.9)\%$ for a 1600 ps window), approaching the threshold for Bell inequality violation at short time scales. These results establish monolithically integrated III--V-on-silicon quantum dots as promising sources of energy--time entangled photons for scalable quantum photonic technologies.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将传统用于可视化面内原子位移的暗场透射电子显微镜（dark field transmission electron microscopy, DF TEM）方法进行扩展，建立了局部堆叠（local stacking）与暗场图像强度之间的定量关系，从而从暗场图像中提取局部三维原子位移和层间距离（interlayer distance）。

Conclusion: 通过扩展暗场透射电子显微镜方法，实现了对扭曲二维材料重构原子系统的完整三维描述，为相关实验研究提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Reconstruction of the atomic crystal structure in twisted 2D materials has been demonstrated to be responsible for multiple exciting phenomena in van der Waals heterostructures, from the appearance of flat bands in twisted bilayer graphene to Wigner crystallization in transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs). However, there are still no experimental methods for accessing the 3D atomic distributions nor models that describe the exact atomic shifts in such reconstructed structures, which significantly impedes the development of the field. Dark field (DF) transmission electron microscopy (TEM) has been conventionally employed to visualize the local in-plane atomic displacements. Here we expand this method to obtain a full description of the reconstructed atomic systems and demonstrate the quantitative relations between the local stacking and the intensity in the DF image. We show how local 3D atomic displacements and the interlayer distance can be extracted from a DF image.

### [111] [Unconventional superconductivity in $A$V$_2X_2$O family of surface altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30766)
*M. Franz*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文分析了由V₂O平面构成的层状材料家族中的配对不稳定性，预测在这些材料（如KV₂Se₂O和Rb₁₋δV₂Te₂O）中，尽管体相可能是常规反铁磁体（仅表面呈现交变磁性），其主导配对不稳定性为奇异的等自旋三重态超导（equal-spin triplet superconductivity）。该三重态超导相具有非平凡拓扑性质，并能支持自旋极化持续电流，具有潜在技术应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受最近在层状氧硫族化合物Na₂₋ₓV₂Se₂O中发现16.3 K超导电性的启发，本文旨在研究更广泛的、由V₂O平面构成的层状材料家族中的配对不稳定性（pairing instabilities），这些材料的单层形式被认为具有交变磁性（altermagnetic order）。

Method: 作者基于这些材料独特的磁性和子晶格结构（sublattice structure）进行理论分析，指出其电子能带结构与常规自旋单态配对（spin-singlet pairing）不相容，从而推导出等自旋三重态超导为主导配对不稳定性。

Result: 分析预测，尽管体相材料KV₂Se₂O和Rb₁₋δV₂Te₂O可能是常规反铁磁体（仅在其表面表现出交变磁性），但这些材料中的主导配对不稳定性是奇异的等自旋三重态超导。预测的三重态超导相具有非平凡拓扑性质（topologically non-trivial），能够支持自旋极化持续电流（spin-polarized persistent currents）。

Conclusion: 这些预测的三重态超导相具有非平凡拓扑特性并能支持自旋极化持续电流，表明其在技术应用中具有潜在价值。

Abstract: Motivated by the recent discovery of superconductivity at 16.3 K in layered oxychalcogenide Na$_{2-x}$V$_2$Se$_2$O we investigate pairing instabilities in the broader family of layered materials composed of V$_2$O planes, believed to exhibit altermagnetic order in their monolayer form. Even though the bulk family members KV$_2$Se$_2$O and Rb$_{1-δ}$V$_{2}$Te$_{2}$O are likely conventional antiferromagnets that show only surface altermagnetism, our analysis predicts exotic equal-spin triplet superconductivity as the dominant pairing instability in these materials. This is a consequence of their unique magnetic and sublattice structure that renders electron bands incompatible with conventional spin-singlet pairing. The predicted triplet superconducting phases are topologically non-trivial and capable of supporting spin-polarized persistent currents, properties potentially useful in technological applications.
