### [112] [Magnetic Dipole in a Cuboidal Superconducting Trap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30808)
*Francis J. Headley*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文推导了封闭超导长方体陷阱中点偶极子的精确像-偶极子势，证明了像格子满足所有六面墙壁上的迈斯纳边界条件，并分析了偶极子的平衡取向与纵横比的关系。所有理论预测与有限元解的误差小于0.16%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将平行板几何中的像-偶极子势推广到约束所有平动自由度的封闭长方体超导陷阱中，并建立满足迈斯纳（Meissner）边界条件的像格子框架。

Method: 通过解析推导构造精确的像-偶极子势，利用埃普斯坦ζ型（Epstein-zeta-type）格子求和计算取向能的二次型系数，并结合有限元数值解进行验证。

Result: 中心偶极子的取向能退化为对角二次型，其系数由埃普斯坦ζ型格子求和给出；在无限和有限矩形陷阱中，偶极子在一定的纵横比范围内均沿较短的横截面轴取向；平衡取向的简并性通过相图（phase diagram）分类。

Conclusion: 所推导的像-偶极子理论精确描述了封闭超导长方体陷阱中的偶极子行为，理论预测与有限元数值解的误差低于0.16%，验证了方法的准确性。

Abstract: We derive the exact image-dipole potential of a point dipole inside a closed cuboidal superconducting trap. The construction generalises the parallel-plate result to a geometry that confines every translational degree of freedom, and we prove that the image lattice satisfies the Meissner boundary condition on all six walls. For a centred dipole the orientational energy reduces to a diagonal quadratic form whose three coefficients are Epstein-zeta-type lattice sums. We show that in both the infinite and finite rectangular traps the dipole orientation aligns with the \emph{short} cross-sectional axis over a finite range of aspect ratios. The equilibrium orientation in both cases is described by a phase diagram whose degeneracies we classify. Every prediction is verified against finite-element solutions of the same boundary-value problem, with agreement better than $0.16\%$.

### [113] [Thermal transport and low-temperature specific heat in 4Hb-TaS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30874)
*M. Gillig,I. Mangel,I. Feldman,V. Kocsis,A. Kanigel,D. V. Efremov,B. Büchner*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过超低温比热与热导率测量，研究了范德瓦尔斯异质结构超导体4Hb-TaS₂的低能激发谱。比热数据总体上支持无能隙节点的超导能隙，但存在残余低能态密度，其中低温upturn归因于核Schottky贡献。热导率在零场下电子线性项消失，表明残余态不形成可探测的传导通道；磁场下热传导迅速增长，面内场的增强行为比标准多带无节点超导图景更复杂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究范德瓦尔斯异质结构超导体4Hb-TaS₂的超导态低能激发谱，特别是其超导能隙结构（gap structure）与低能准粒子激发（low-energy quasiparticle excitation）的性质。

Method: 采用超低温比热（ultra-low-temperature specific heat）与热导率（thermal conductivity）测量，分别在磁场平行和垂直于晶格c轴（c axis）的方向上进行实验。

Result: （1）比热与无节点（nodeless）超导能隙一致，但存在有限的残余线性项，表明超导态中有残余低能态密度（residual low-energy density of states）；在约0.3K以下出现upturn，其弱磁场依赖及热导率中无对应特征支持该upturn源于核Schottky贡献（nuclear Schottky contribution）。（2）热导率在零场下电子线性项（electronic linear term）在实验不确定度内消失，说明残余态不形成可探测的巡游热传导通道（itinerant heat-conduction channel）。（3）外磁场下电子热导迅速增长；面外磁场响应与先前的多带无节点超导（multigap nodeless superconductivity）行为大致一致，而面内磁场的更陡峭增长表明准粒子响应比标准多带图像更复杂。

Conclusion: 4Hb-TaS₂的超导态具有无节点能隙，但存在局域化的残余低能态，这些态不贡献巡游热传导。磁场下的准粒子响应表现出超出标准多带无节点超导框架的复杂性，尤其是在面内磁场方向。

Abstract: We investigate the low-energy excitation spectrum of the van der Waals heterostructure superconductor 4Hb-TaS$_2$ using ultra-low-temperature specific-heat and thermal-conductivity measurements with magnetic fields applied parallel and perpendicular to the crystallographic $c$ axis. The specific heat is broadly consistent with a nodeless superconducting gap, but retains a finite residual linear contribution, indicating a small residual low-energy density of states in the superconducting state. In addition, a pronounced upturn appears below approximately 0.3K. Its weak magnetic-field dependence, together with the absence of a corresponding feature in thermal transport, supports an interpretation in terms of localized degrees of freedom, most likely a nuclear Schottky contribution. In contrast to the finite residual thermodynamic density of states, the thermal conductivity extrapolates to a vanishing zero-field electronic linear term within experimental uncertainty for both field orientations. Thus, the residual low-energy states do not form a detectable itinerant heat-conduction channel. In finite magnetic field, the electronic heat transport grows rapidly. For out-of-plane fields, this response is broadly consistent with previous thermal-conductivity measurements and with the behavior commonly associated with multigap nodeless superconductivity. The even steeper increase observed for in-plane fields suggests that the field-induced quasiparticle response of 4Hb-TaS$_2$ is more complicated than the standard multigap picture alone.

### [114] [Electronic theory for scanning tunneling microscopy spectra in bilayer nickelate thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31569)
*Marius Scholten,Steffen Bötzel,Frank Lechermann,Peayush Choubey,Ilya M. Eremin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用双轨道双层模型和连续格林函数形式论，理论分析了超导双层镍酸盐La2PrNi2O7薄膜的扫描隧道显微镜（STM）谱，揭示了轨道与能带选择的局域态密度特征，并提出了通过距离依赖测量识别γ能带起源及其相干峰带来源的实验路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近的扫描隧道显微镜（Scanning Tunneling Microscopy, STM）实验测量了环境压强和压缩应变下超导双层镍酸盐La2PrNi2O7薄膜的超导能隙特征，为研究该体系的库珀配对模型和能带选择性识别能隙特征铺平了道路。本工作旨在从理论上分析轨道与能带选择的局域态密度及相应的STM谱，以解释多轨道特性对谱特征的影响。

Method: 采用现实的双轨道双层模型（two-orbital bilayer model）和连续格林函数形式论（continuum Green's function formalism），理论分析轨道和能带选择的局域态密度（local density of states, LDOS）以及相应的STM谱。

Result: 研究发现，多轨道特性（multiorbital character）和Wannier函数的空间依赖性导致STM谱特征随探针位置而变化，从而能够实现超导相干峰（coherence peaks）和散射动量的能带分辨分析。此外，通过局域态密度的距离依赖测量及其杂质散射修正，可以识别存在争议的γ能带（gamma-band）的起始迹象以及相干峰的能带起源。

Conclusion: 本研究为实验测量提供了清晰的路径，不仅能够识别γ能带的起始迹象，还能通过距离依赖的局域态密度测量及其杂质散射修正，确定相干峰的能带起源。

Abstract: Recent Scanning Tunneling Microscopy (STM) experiments measuring the superconducting gap features in thin films of superconducting bilayer nickelates La2PrNi2O7 at ambient pressure and compressive strain paved the way to study the Cooper-pairing models and the band-selective identification of the gap features in these systems. Here, using the realistic two-orbital bilayer model and the continuum Green's function formalism, we theoretically analyze orbital and band-selective local density of states as well as the corresponding STM spectra. We find that the multiorbital character and the spatial dependence of the Wannier functions leads to the spectra developing characteristic features depending on the position of the scanning tunneling microscope's tip. This allows for a band-resolved analysis of the superconducting coherence peaks and scattering momenta. We identify a clear path for experimental measurements to not only identify the debated incipiency of the gamma-band, but also identification of the coherence peaks' band origins via distance dependent measurements of the local density of states and its corrections through impurity scattering.

</details>


### [115] [Universal Spectral Mirage Gaps in Superconductors with Time-Reversal-Symmetric Spin-Orbit Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31841)
*Xusheng Wang,Gaomin Tang,Shuai-Hua Ji*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文揭示了具有任意时间反演对称自旋轨道耦合（SOC）的超导体中，当外加磁场垂直于SOC纹理时，可在SOC能标附近产生幻影能隙（spectral mirage gaps）；平行分量则产生超导能隙附近的塞曼分裂特征。以Rashba和Rashba-Ising SOC为例验证了这一普适原理，表明超导光谱学可成为探测SOC纹理与强度的有力工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 幻影能隙此前被认为是有有限能量配对关联（finite-energy pairing correlations）的证据，但主要局限在伊辛SOC（Ising spin-orbit coupling）超导体中。本文旨在研究更一般的时间反演对称SOC超导体中幻影能隙的产生条件与行为。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，研究在任意时间反演对称SOC的超导体中施加磁场时，磁场分量相对于SOC纹理的方向对光谱特征的影响；并以Rashba SOC和Rashba-Ising SOC两种具体模型进行验证。

Result: 当外加磁场具有垂直于SOC纹理的分量时，可在SOC能标附近产生幻影能隙；而平行分量则在超导能隙附近产生塞曼分裂（Zeeman-split）光谱特征。该普适性规律在Rashba和Rashba-Ising SOC超导体中均得到验证。

Conclusion: 这些与磁场方向相关的普适光谱特征表明，超导光谱学（superconducting spectroscopy）是一种探测SOC纹理与强度的有效手段。

Abstract: Spectral mirage gaps, regarded as evidence of finite-energy pairing correlations, have so far been mainly studied in superconductors with Ising spin-orbit coupling (SOC). Here, we show that superconductors with any time-reversal-symmetric SOC can generate mirage gaps near the SOC energy scale when the applied magnetic field has a component perpendicular to the SOC texture, whereas the parallel component produces Zeeman-split spectral features near the superconducting gap. We demonstrate this general principle in superconductors with Rashba and Rashba-Ising SOC. These universal field-dependent signatures establish superconducting spectroscopy as a powerful probe of SOC textures and strengths.

</details>


### [116] [Anomalous Hall Effect Driven by Chiral Superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31851)
*Vladislav Poliakov,Alex Levchenko,Leonid Levitov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种零场霍尔拖动效应（zero-field Hall drag effect）作为手征超导电性（chiral superconductivity）的直接直流输运信号，该效应源于手征超导体与邻近时间反演对称性正常层之间的准粒子库仑拖动（Coulomb drag），并在超导层中引入包含准粒子正常流和凝聚超流的最小流体动力学理论（minimal hydrodynamic theory）进行描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非常规超导电性的直接直流特征信号稀缺，已有的探测手段（如相图异常、外场响应或光学测量）通常为间接方法。因此，需要寻找一种直接、可测量的直流输运信号来识别手征超导电性。

Method: 提出零场霍尔拖动效应作为直接探测手段；构建了最小流体动力学理论，该理论包含超导层中的准粒子正常流（quasiparticle normal current）和凝聚超流（condensate supercurrent）两个组分。在超导层处于开路条件下，凝聚产生的反向超流抵消净层电流，而有限的准粒子电流则负责传递横向拖动响应。

Result: 在温度降低至超导转变温度（$T_c$）以下时，异常霍尔电压信号会突然出现，其符号反映了超导序参量相位缠绕（order parameter phase winding）的符号。

Conclusion: 该效应为手征超导电性提供了一种直接且无外磁场的直流输运特征信号，有望弥补现有间接探测方法的不足。

Abstract: Direct dc-current signatures of unconventional superconductivity remain scarce. Existing probes of unconventional pairing are typically indirect, relying on phase-diagram anomalies, responses to external fields, or optical measurements. Here we propose a zero-field Hall drag effect as a direct transport signature of chiral superconductivity. The effect arises from Coulomb drag between quasiparticles in a chiral superconductor and those in an adjacent time-reversal-symmetric normal layer. We develop a minimal hydrodynamic theory that includes both quasiparticle normal current and condensate supercurrent in the superconducting layer. In an open-circuit superconducting layer, the condensate generates a counterflowing supercurrent that cancels the net layer current, while a finite quasiparticle current remains and mediates the transverse drag response. This results in anomalous Hall voltage signal appearing abruptly when $T$ is lowered below $T_c$, of the sign reflecting the sign of the superconducting order parameter phase winding.

</details>

### [117] [Rich Phenomenology from Simple Ingredients: A Review of Confining Dark Sectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30760)
*Pouya Asadi,Austin Batz,Graham D. Kribs*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了具有禁闭暗扇区（confining dark sectors）的理论模型，及其在暗物质、宇宙学、唯象学和标准模型未解难题中的应用，特别聚焦于可见物质与暗物质能量密度相似的丰度相似性谜题（abundance similarity puzzle），并呼吁进一步探索这类超越标准模型的理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用文献综述（literature review）方法，对禁闭暗扇区理论及其在暗物质候选体、丰度产生机制、对称性解释稳定性，以及直接探测、间接探测、天体物理观测量和对撞机等多通道发现途径等方面进行系统梳理和概念性概述，并强调不同实验之间的关联性。

Result: 识别出多种暗物质候选体，包括暗介子（dark mesons）、暗重子（dark baryons）和胶球（glueballs）等；总结了多种产生暗物质丰度的机制及其稳定性来源；指出存在直接探测、间接探测、天体物理观测量和对撞机等多种潜在发现通道及不同实验间的关联；特别突出了丰度相似性谜题这一关键应用方向。

Conclusion: 尽管禁闭暗扇区理论的理论图景非常广阔，但存在统一特征和适用于不同能区的计算技术。该理论在解释可见物质与暗物质能量密度相似性方面具有特殊潜力，值得进一步深入探索。

Abstract: We review theories with confining dark sectors and their implications for dark matter, cosmology, phenomenology, and unsolved Standard Model puzzles. Models with new strongly-coupled non-Abelian gauge interactions can lead to a variety of dark matter candidates (dark mesons, baryons, glueballs, etc.), as well as mechanisms to generate its abundance and symmetries that explain its stability. There are also many potential discovery channels, including direct detection, indirect detection, astrophysical observables, and colliders, as well as correlations between different experiments. We compile a broad conceptual overview of the literature on this topic, aimed at both theorists looking for which questions remain unanswered and experimentalists looking for novel search opportunities. While the theoretical landscape is vast, there are both unifying features and calculational techniques that apply to various regimes. We particularly highlight applications to explaining the similarity of visible and dark matter energy densities, i.e. the $abundance~similarity~puzzle$. We advocate further exploration of this class of theories in the effort to uncover physics beyond the Standard Model.

</details>


### [118] [Toponium effects on quantum steering and Bell nonlocality of top quarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30768)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文通过分析toponium贡献对自旋单态（spin-singlet）分量的增强效应，研究近阈值区域top夸克对产生中的量子关联。基于现有LHC实验数据，对量子操控和贝尔非局域性进行统计显著性（statistical significance）计算。

Result: toponium贡献显著增强了两个top夸克自旋之间的纠缠。量子操控的统计显著性约为10σ，贝尔非局域性的统计显著性在近阈值区域可达约9σ。

Conclusion: LHC近阈值区域的top夸克对产生为量子操控和贝尔非局域性的实验观测提供了可行途径，量子操控的观测可靠性较高，而贝尔非局域性的实现则依赖于对系统不确定性的有效控制。

Abstract: We investigate quantum steering and Bell nonlocality in top-quark pair production at the LHC near threshold. The toponium contribution strengthens the spin-singlet component and substantially enhances the entanglement between the two quark spins. With current LHC data, quantum steering appears observable with a statistical significance around $10σ$. For Bell nonlocality, the statistical significance can also be high close to threshold, reaching about $9σ$, although the feasibility of such a measurement will depend crucially on the control of systematic uncertainties.

### [119] [A Levitated-Magnet Vector Force Sensor for Spin-Dependent Exotic Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30781)
*Dorian W. P. Amaral,Lei Cong,Tim M. Fuchs,Hendrik Ulbricht,Dmitry Budker*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种磁悬浮铁磁矢量力传感器（magnetically levitated ferromagnetic vector force sensor），通过将沿不同轴的力映射到具有不同共振频率的平动模式上，实现对自旋依赖奇异相互作用（spin-dependent exotic interactions）方向特征的选择性探测，并以自旋-1 Z'玻色子为示例展示了其在毫米尺度下对超越标准模型（beyond Standard Model）相互作用的探测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋依赖奇异相互作用（spin-dependent exotic interactions）能够产生由相互作用体相对自旋构型（relative spin configuration）决定的方向性力信号，但现有探测手段难以有效分辨这些方向特征。因此需要一种能够选择性搜索这类相互作用的传感器平台。

Method: 采用磁悬浮铁磁体（magnetically levitated ferromagnet）作为矢量力传感器，将沿不同轴的力映射到具有不同共振频率（resonance frequencies）的平动模式（translational modes）上，从而在同一耦合类（coupling class）内分离不同的相互作用通道。以宇称破缺的轴矢-矢量（axial-vector--vector）相互作用为示例，结合匹配滤波似然分析（matched-filter likelihood analysis）评估探测能力。

Result: 基于已得到实验验证的方案，该传感器可在先前无法触及的力程范围（force range）λ ≲ 1 cm（对应中介玻色子质量 M_{Z'} ≳ 10^{-5} eV/c²）内探测纯电子-电子耦合 g_A^e g_V^e。

Conclusion: 磁悬浮铁磁体为毫米尺度（millimeter-scale）的自旋依赖第五种力（fifth forces）搜索，以及同一耦合类中多个有效势（effective potentials）的分辨提供了一种有前景的平台。

Abstract: We present a magnetically levitated ferromagnetic vector force sensor that enables selective searches for spin-dependent exotic interactions mediated by beyond-Standard-Model bosons. A defining feature of spin-dependent exotic interactions is that they can generate forces with distinct directional signatures set by the relative spin configuration of the interacting bodies. We show that our sensor resolves these signatures by mapping forces along different axes onto distinct translational modes with different resonance frequencies, thereby separating interaction channels within the same coupling class. As a representative example, we study parity-violating axial-vector--vector interactions mediated by a spin-1 $Z'$ boson between a sensing and a driving levitated ferromagnet. Using a matched-filter likelihood analysis, we show that a setup based on an already demonstrated experiment can probe the pure electron--electron coupling $g_A^e g_V^e$ in the previously inaccessible force range $λ\lesssim 1\,\mathrm{cm}$, corresponding to mediator masses $M_{Z'} \gtrsim 10^{-5}\,\mathrm{eV}/c^2$. Our results establish levitated ferromagnets as a promising platform for millimeter-scale searches for spin-dependent fifth forces and for resolving the multiple effective potentials associated with a given coupling class.

### [120] [Extraction of the nucleon axial form factor from Lattice QCD using NNLO chiral perturbation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30834)
*Fernando Alvarado,Luis Alvarez-Ruso*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在相对论性手征微扰论（relativistic chiral perturbation theory）框架下，计入Δ(1232)共振态，计算至次次领头阶（NNLO）的核子轴矢形状因子（nucleon axial form factor）。通过拟合近期晶格QCD（lattice-QCD）数据，确定了相关的低能常数（low-energy constants），并系统的描述了轴矢电荷与轴矢半径的π介子质量依赖关系及动量依赖关系。在物理点得到g_A=1.257±0.011和<r_A^2>=0.312±0.037 fm²。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在提供一种模型独立且可系统改进的参数化形式，以描述轴矢形状因子对π介子质量与动量转移的依赖关系，为晶格QCD结果外推到物理点（physical point）以及改进涉及核子的低能弱相互作用（low-energy weak interactions）预言提供理论基础。

Method: 采用相对论性手征微扰论（relativistic chiral perturbation theory），并显式包含Δ(1232)共振态作为自由粒子，计算至次次领头阶（next-to-next-to-leading order, NNLO）。通过拟合多个π介子质量下的晶格QCD（lattice-QCD）数据来确定相关低能常数（low-energy constants），同时考虑手征展开截断引入的不确定性（truncation uncertainty）。

Result: 在动量转移√Q²≲0.6 GeV以及π介子质量M_π≲400 MeV范围内，计算结果与晶格QCD数据吻合良好。显式包含Δ共振态是正确再现轴矢电荷（axial charge）与轴矢半径（axial radius）的π介子质量依赖以及形状因子动量依赖的必要条件。在物理点得到轴矢电荷g_A=1.257±0.011，轴矢均方半径⟨r_A²⟩=0.312±0.037 fm²。

Conclusion: 该分析提供了一个模型独立且可系统改进的轴矢形状因子参数化形式，适用于外推晶格QCD结果至物理点并改进涉及核子的低能弱相互作用预言。Δ共振态的显式引入是赝标量介子质量依赖性和形状因子动量依赖性的关键因素。

Abstract: We calculate the nucleon axial form factor in relativistic chiral perturbation theory with $Δ(1232)$ up to next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO). Relevant low-energy constants are determined by fitting to recent lattice-QCD results at several pion masses, while accounting for the uncertainty associated with the truncation of the chiral expansion. We obtain a good description of the lattice data for momentum transfers up to $\sqrt{Q^2}\simeq0.6$ GeV and pion masses up to $M_π\simeq400$ MeV. We find that the explicit inclusion of the $Δ$ resonance is required to reproduce the lattice-QCD pion-mass dependence of the axial charge and axial radius, as well as the momentum dependence of the form factor. At the physical point we obtain $g_A=1.257\pm 0.011$ and $\langle r_A^2\rangle=0.312\pm0.037~\mathrm{fm}^2$. Our analysis provides a model-independent and systematically improvable parametrization of the pion-mass and momentum dependence of the axial form factor, offering a framework for extrapolating lattice-QCD results to the physical point and for improving predictions of low-energy weak interactions involving nucleons.

</details>


### [121] [Quantum Information as a New Lens for Precision Neutrino Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31996)
*Khushboo Dixit,Ritam Kundu,Papia Panda,Soebur Razzaque,Ramita Sarkar*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用量子信息理论，通过全 concurrence（total concurrence）量化中微子味态（flavor states）中的量子关联，发现纠缠度（entanglement）局部极小值对应风味态最接近可分离态（separability）的能量区域，可优化中微子振荡参数的提取。通过将 NOνA 和 T2K 实验的基准振荡区域对准最小纠缠区域，提升了联合参数约束精度，并利用 GLoBES 模拟和真实数据评估了量子关联对 CP 破坏敏感性、θ₂₃八重简并分辨及质量顺序确定等关键物理量的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长基线中微子振荡实验（如 NOνA 和 T2K）因能量区间差异导致参数测量存在张力（tension），需探索新视角优化参数提取精度。量子信息理论中的纠缠度量有望为理解味态振荡行为提供互补工具，从而提升对振荡参数的精确测定能力。

Method: 将中微子三味振荡中的味态映射为类量子比特（qubit-like）表示，利用全 concurrence 量化量子关联；通过定位 concurrence 局部极小值确定风味态最接近可分离态的能量区域；将 NOνA 和 T2K 实验的基准振荡区域对准这些最小纠缠区域，并结合 GLoBES 模拟与真实数据进行联合分析。

Result: 在正常顺序（normal ordering）下，在 (sin²θ₂₃, δ_CP) 平面得到 (0.581^{+0.0136}_{-0.0150}, 195^{+38}_{-32}°)，在 (sin²θ₂₃, Δm²₃₁) 平面得到 (0.580^{+0.0140}_{-0.0153}, 2.515^{+0.0344}_{-0.0344}×10⁻³ eV²)，联合约束显著改善。分析表明最小化纠缠可显著影响 CP 破坏敏感性、θ₂₃八重简并（octant degeneracy）分辨及质量顺序确定能力。

Conclusion: 量子信息度量可成为中微子味振荡的互补探测工具，揭示了量子关联（quantum correlations）在精密中微子物理中的重要作用，为降低实验间张力和提升参数测量精度提供了新思路。

Abstract: We present a quantum-information-theoretic study of three-flavor neutrino oscillations in long-baseline experiments by mapping flavor states to qubit-like representations and quantifying quantum correlations through total concurrence. The local minima of this entanglement measure identify energy regions where the flavor state is closest to separability, enabling cleaner extraction of oscillation parameters. We explain how these local minima offer opportunities for precision measurements and provide insight into the accurate determination of neutrino oscillation parameters. We then propose a strategy to improve parameter extraction by aligning the benchmark oscillation regions of NO$ν$A and T2K with the minimum entanglement achievable in each experiment. This shifts the concurrence minima toward higher-event-count energy regions, leading to tighter constraints and reducing the tension arising from their different energy regimes. For normal ordering, we obtain $(0.581^{+0.0136}_{-0.0150},,195^{+38}_{-32},^\circ)$ in the $(\sin^2θ_{23},δ_{\rm CP})$ plane and $(0.580^{+0.0140}_{-0.0153},,2.515^{+0.0344}_{-0.0344}\times10^{-3},\mathrm{eV}^2)$ in the $(\sin^2θ_{23},Δm^2_{31})$ plane, yielding improved joint constraints. Using GLoBES simulations together with real data, we assess how local minima of quantum correlations influence leptonic CP-violation sensitivity, $θ_{23}$ octant-degeneracy resolution, and mass-ordering determination. Our results show that minimizing entanglement can significantly affect these key sensitivities, highlighting quantum information measures as complementary probes of neutrino flavor oscillations and offering new insight into the role of quantum correlations in precision neutrino physics.

</details>


### [122] [Regularized Compton double scattering via unitarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30825)
*Shanmuka Shivashankara,Isra Gashi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究初始纠缠光子在经历双重康普顿散射（Compton double scattering）后产生的电子关联效应。在保持树级幺正性（unitarity）的前提下，得到了与近期文献不同的结果。通过Vieta公式（Vieta's formulas）将面积发散（area divergences）正则化，并将双重散射类比为杨氏双缝衍射实验（Young's diffraction experiment）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨两个初始纠缠光子各自发生康普顿散射（Compton scattering）后，散射电子之间是否产生关联，以及幺正性（unitarity）如何处理散射过程中出现的发散问题。

Method: 将初始四粒子系统（两个纠缠光子及其对应的两个靶电子）写为两个态叠加的形式，引入相对相位（relative phase）。在树级（tree level）保持幺正性，对最终的约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrix）中出现的两个面积发散（area divergences）进行正则化处理——通过求解代表无散射概率的多项式的根。利用Vieta公式（Vieta's formulas）将这些发散与有限散射截面（finite cross-sections）联系起来。

Result: 得到了初始纯态下的最终密度矩阵（final density matrix）和最终电子极化（electronic polarizations）关联的解析表达式。发现该关联与杨氏双缝衍射实验（Young's diffraction experiment）具有类比性：两个初始叠加态相当于圆形孔径（circular apertures），费曼振幅（Feynman amplitudes）相当于发生干涉的复光场（complex light fields）。

Conclusion: 双重康普顿散射中电子关联可类比为杨氏双缝衍射；正则化程序暗示了一种散射截面（scattering cross-section）的新定义方式；幺正性在树级有效保留时，可得到与现有文献不同的结果。

Abstract: When two initially entangled photons each undergo Compton scattering, the scattered electrons become correlated. However, the final reduced density matrix of one scattered pair is not influenced by the other scattered pair due to unitarity. Herein, we keep unitarity up to tree level for Compton double scattering and obtain different results than recent literature. The initial four particles, where the initial photons are entangled, are written as a superposition of two states with a relative phase. The final density matrix has two area divergences that are regularized with unitarity. The regularization procedure, i.e. solving for the roots of a polynomial that represents the probability for no scattering, suggests a novel definition of the scattering cross-section. Vieta's formulas relate these divergences to finite cross-sections. For an initial pure state, the formulas for the final density matrix and the correlation of final electronic polarizations are given. The correlation implies double scattering is analogous to Young's diffraction experiment. The two initial superposed states are the circular apertures while the Feynman amplitudes are the interfering complex light fields.

</details>


### [123] [LinApart3: efficient algorithm for multivariate partial fraction decomposition with linear denominators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30708)
*L. Fekésházy,A. Kardos*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种针对线性分母有理函数的高效多元部分分式分解算法LinApart3，利用线性代数和留数提取替代多项式理想计算，避免了中间表达式膨胀问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于Gröbner基或Leinartas方法的多元部分分式分解虽能处理任意多项式分母，但面临中间表达式膨胀（intermediate expression swell）问题，影响计算效率。

Method: LinApart3利用分母定义的超平面排列（hyperplane arrangement）的几何结构，将多项式理想计算替换为线性代数（linear algebra）和留数提取（residue extraction），从而规避中间表达式膨胀。

Result: 该算法保证每项包含至多与部分分式变量数量相等的原始集合中互异分母，不引入假奇点（spurious singularities），不依赖变量排序（variable ordering），且对旁观变量（spectator variables）不敏感。此外，各基贡献独立，具备天然的可并行化（naturally parallelizable）特性。

Conclusion: LinApart3在Wolfram Mathematica和FORM中均有实现，展示了其在多元部分分式分解中的实用性和高效性。

Abstract: We present LinApart3, an efficient multivariate partial fraction decomposition algorithm for rational functions with linear denominators. Our decomposition algorithm guarantees that each term contains at most as many distinct denominators from the original set as partial fraction variables, introduces no spurious singularities, is independent of variable ordering, and is insensitive to the presence of spectator variables. While general multivariate approaches based on Gröbner bases or Leinartas' method handle arbitrary polynomial denominators, they suffer from intermediate expression swell. LinApart3 replaces polynomial-ideal computations with linear algebra and residue extraction by exploiting the geometry of the hyperplane arrangement defined by the denominators, circumventing this issue just as LinApart did in the univariate case. Because the individual basis contributions are independent, the algorithm is moreover naturally parallelizable. To showcase the utility of our algorithm we implemented the algorithm both in Wolfram Mathematica and FORM.

</details>


### [124] [Particle Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31812)
*Venus Keus*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该文概述了粒子宇宙学（particle cosmology）作为一门融合粒子物理学与宇宙学的交叉学科，旨在通过粒子物理原理理解宇宙的起源与演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期宇宙可作为天然高能实验室，能够探索在地面加速器上无法实现的物理现象，从而推动对自然界基本规律的理解。

Method: 结合极小尺度（基本粒子与力）与极大尺度（宇宙结构与演化）的物理学原理，同时利用宇宙学观测（如宇宙微波背景辐射、星系分布、宇宙加速膨胀）与粒子物理理论发展（如暴胀、重子生成、暗物质）进行交叉研究。

Result: 宇宙学观测为理解自然界基本规律提供了窗口；粒子物理的理论进展则提出了暴胀（inflation）、重子生成（baryogenesis）和暗物质（Dark Matter）等理论，有助于解释宇宙的关键特征。

Conclusion: 粒子宇宙学通过整合极小与极大尺度物理学，为理解宇宙的诞生与演化提供了统一框架，并揭示了理论与观测之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: Particle cosmology is the branch of science that seeks to understand the birth and evolution of the Universe by applying the principles of particle physics. It brings together the physics of the very small (fundamental particles and forces) with the physics of the very large (the structure and evolution of the cosmos). In many ways, the early Universe acts as a natural laboratory - one far more energetic than any collider we can build - offering unique insights into phenomena that may never be accessible on Earth. Cosmological observations such as the Cosmic Microwave Background, the distribution of galaxies, and the accelerating expansion of the Universe serve as windows into the fundamental laws of nature. At the same time, theoretical developments in particle physics have led to theories, such as inflation, baryogenesis, and Dark Matter, that help explain key features of the cosmos.

### [125] [PBHs and GWs from Scaling Monopoles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31937)
*Daiki Aburatani,Wakutaka Nakano,Wen Yin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过经典格点模拟发现，弱耦合或来自全局对称性的磁单极子（monopole）在早期宇宙中形成的标度网络（scaling network），在希格斯期望值 v≳0.1M_pl 条件下可产生具有宽质量谱的原初黑洞（PBH），同时产生与原初黑洞谱相关、未来可探测的引力波（GW）信号；若规范玻色子质量终止标度演化，部分原初黑洞可携带磁荷，其磁库仑力与引力相当，构成该场景的明确信号特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索弱耦合磁单极子或来自全局对称性的磁单极子在早期宇宙形成标度网络的过程中，能否产生原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）及引力波（gravitational waves, GWs），并检验这些信号的可观测性及与暗物质（dark matter）可能的关联。

Method: 采用经典格点模拟（classical lattice simulations）估计哈勃视界（Hubble patch）内磁单极子数的随机涨落导致的过密度（overdensities），从而计算原初黑洞的形成及其质量谱。

Result: 当希格斯期望值 v≳0.1M_pl 时，标度网络演化可产生具有宽质量谱的原初黑洞；同步产生的引力波与原初黑洞谱相关且幅度未来可测；若标度演化被规范玻色子质量终止，部分原初黑洞可携带磁荷（magnetic charge），其磁库仑力与引力相当。

Conclusion: 该场景提供了原初黑洞、引力波及磁荷黑洞的联合信号特征（smoking-gun signature），并指出类似的标度宇宙弦（scaling cosmic strings）场景也可能使原初黑洞构成主导暗物质（dominant dark matter）。

Abstract: Monopoles with sufficiently weak gauge couplings, or from global symmetries, can form scaling networks in the early Universe whose average energy density tracks the cosmological background. In this work, we find, by performing classical lattice simulations to estimate the overdensities, that primordial black holes (PBHs) with a broad mass spectrum can be produced during this evolution if the Higgs expectation value $v$ satisfies $v\gtrsim 0.1 M_{\rm pl}$. The formation is driven by the stochastic realization of the monopole number in Hubble patches causing the overdensities. We also show that gravitational waves (GWs) generated by the scaling dynamics are produced at the same epoch, with spectra correlated with the PBH spectra and with amplitudes testable in future observations. Interestingly, if the scaling regime is terminated by the gauge boson mass for the gauged monopole, a non-negligible fraction of the PBHs can carry magnetic charge, and the resulting magnetic Coulomb force between such charged PBHs is predicted to be comparable to the gravitational force. Together with the PBH and GW signals, this provides a smoking-gun signature of the scenario. We also point out simple cosmological scenarios, which may also apply to PBH formation from scaling cosmic strings, that allow PBHs to constitute dominant dark matter.

### [126] [Hadronic exceptional points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31697)
*Ahmad Jafar Arifi,Kei Suzuki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出虚磁场可作为强子系统中非厄米动力学（non-Hermitian dynamics）的简单实现，通过手征有效拉格朗日量和组分夸克模型分析中性介子质量谱，发现了奇异点（exceptional points）并揭示了从实能谱吸引到退禁闭相变的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异点（exceptional points）作为非厄米系统（non-Hermitian systems）的核心特征已在光子学、原子物理和凝聚态系统中得到广泛研究，但在量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics, QCD）中却鲜有关注。本文旨在填补这一空白，探索非厄米动力学在强子系统中的实现与效应。

Method: 采用两种理论方法：一是强子有效拉格朗日量（hadronic effective Lagrangian），二是组分夸克模型（constituent quark model）。通过引入虚磁场（imaginary magnetic field）实现非厄米动力学，计算中性介子的质量谱。

Result: 发现奇异点将实能谱区域与复本征值区域分隔开。在弱场下，实能谱呈现强子态之间的能级吸引（level attraction）；在强场下，强子退禁闭（deconfined），表现为场致反转势（field-induced inverted potential）的特征。

Conclusion: 本工作为在非厄米环境中研究QCD动力学开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Exceptional points, where eigenvalues and eigenvectors coalesce, are a defining feature of non-Hermitian systems and have been extensively observed in photonic, atomic, and condensed matter systems. However, they have received little attention in quantum chromodynamics (QCD), which is the fundamental theory of quarks, gluons, and hadrons. We propose that imaginary magnetic fields provide a simple realization of non-Hermitian dynamics in hadronic systems. Based on two theoretical approaches, a hadronic effective Lagrangian and a constituent quark model, we compute mass spectra of neutral mesons and find exceptional points separating the real-spectrum and complex-eigenvalue regimes. In small fields, the real spectrum exhibits level attraction between hadronic states, whereas in larger fields, hadrons are deconfined, which is a signature of a field-induced inverted potential. Our findings open a new avenue for studying QCD dynamics in non-Hermitian environments.

### [127] [Reheating in No-Scale Models of Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31975)
*Ignatios Antoniadis,John Ellis,Dimitri V. Nanopoulos,Keith A. Olive,Sarunas Verner*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了广义无标度暴胀（no-scale inflation）模型中暴胀子（inflaton）衰变到标准模型（Standard Model）粒子的抑制问题及其规避机制，分析了场空间曲率、非最小规范动能项和反常诱导耦合对重加热温度（reheating temperature）及（n_s, r）平面预测的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始Starobinsky R+R²模型和最小无标度暴胀模型中，暴胀子衰变到共形耦合（conformally coupled）标量场和标准模型（Standard Model）场的过程受到抑制，这限制了重加热（reheating）过程的效率；因此需要研究如何在广义无标度暴胀模型中规避这种抑制。

Method: 通过引入场空间曲率参数α（即R = 2/(3α)）的广义化模型（包括弦理论（string theory）导出模型），以及包含非最小规范动能项（non-minimal gauge kinetic terms）和反常诱导耦合（anomaly-induced couplings）的模型，分析暴胀子与规范玻色子（gauge bosons）和规范微子（gauginos）之间的直接与反常诱导耦合，并验证Kähler标架不变性（Kähler-frame invariance）下的物理规范耦合（physical gauge coupling）。

Result: 确定了不同广义模型下对应的重加热温度（reheating temperature）及其在（n_s, r）平面上的预测；同时发现R³形变（R^3 deformation）虽然改变了暴胀子与稳定子（stabilizer）扇区，但本身并不产生新的树图级（tree-level）暴胀子与可见物质场的耦合。

Conclusion: 广义无标度暴胀模型通过调节场空间曲率参数α、引入非最小规范动能项或反常诱导耦合，可以有效规避暴胀子衰变到标准模型场的抑制；R³形变则需结合其他机制才能产生新的耦合。

Abstract: Analogously to the suppression of inflaton decays into conformally-coupled scalar fields in the original Starobinsky $R + R^2$ model of inflation, inflaton decays to Standard Model fields are also suppressed in minimal no-scale models of inflation with field space curvature $\mathcal{R} = 2/3$. We study how this suppression can be avoided in generalized no-scale inflationary models. These include models in which the field space curvature $\mathcal{R} = 2/(3α)$ with $α\ne 1$ as exemplified by models derived from string theory, as well as models with non-minimal gauge kinetic terms and anomaly-induced couplings. We analyze direct and anomaly-induced inflaton couplings to gauge bosons and gauginos and demonstrate the Kähler-frame invariance of the physical gauge coupling. We determine the resulting reheating temperatures and the corresponding predictions in the $(n_s,r)$ plane. Finally, we consider an $R^3$ deformation of Starobinsky supergravity, which modifies the inflaton and stabilizer sectors but does not, by itself, generate new tree-level inflaton couplings to visible matter fields.

### [128] [Navigating committor landscape of biomolecules with a general pairwise interaction model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31832)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 受AlphaFold 3范式的启发，本文提出一种新颖的通量函数学习框架。该框架将轻量级、可微的原子级嵌入（differentiable atom-level embedding）与简化的Pairformer架构相结合，无需专门的先验知识即可捕捉多种生物体系的复杂动力学特征（dynamical features）。

Result: 该框架在多个原子尺度过程中展现出优越的表达能力和准确性。在chignolin小蛋白折叠任务中，模型揭示了其过渡态系综（transition state ensemble, TSE）的更精细结构以及一个详细的分叉反应机制（bifurcated reaction mechanism）。在杯芳烃（calixarene）主-客体系统中，模型建立了统一的通量函数，阐明了配体取代基（ligand substituents）如何调控不同结合路径（binding pathways）的比例。

Conclusion: 该工作为基于结构的药物设计（structure-based drug design）提供了新的视角，证明了将蛋白质结构预测中的先进架构迁移至稀有事件采样领域的可行性与有效性。

Abstract: Sampling rare conformation transitions between metastable states is a central challenge in atomistic simulations. While the committor function serve as an ideal reaction coordinate for driving enhanced sampling, their high-dimensional inputs and complex functional forms limit the efficacy of standard feedforward neural networks in modeling them. Inspired by recent breakthroughs in biomolecular structure prediction, we propose a novel committor learning framework grounded in the AlphaFold 3 paradigm. By integrating a lightweight, differentiable atom-level embedding with a simplified Pairformer architecture, our method inherently captures intricate dynamical features of diverse biosystems without requiring specialized prior knowledge. We demonstrate the superior expressiveness and accuracy of the proposed framework across multiple atomistic processes. For the folding of the chignolin mini-protein, our model reveals the finer-grained structure of its transition state ensemble (TSE) and a detailed bifurcated reaction mechanism. Furthermore, for calixarene host-guest systems, we develop a unified committor model that elucidates how ligand substituents regulate the ratio between distinct binding pathways, offering new perspectives for structure-based drug design.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在定向折一侧，对膜态（brane states）进行扫描，类似于类型I弦理论中D0-膜（D0-brane）的情形，识别出限制规范群的旋量态（spinorial states）；在杂化弦与玻色弦一侧，规范群由内禀动量格点（internal momentum lattices）给出。通过比较两边的群结构来检验对偶性。

Conclusion: 验证了Blum–Dienes和Bergman–Gaberdiel两种对偶提案的有效性，并指出后者存在一个额外的投影条件。

Abstract: We test two dualities of non-supersymmetric type 0 orientifolds with heterotic and bosonic string theories, the Blum--Dienes and the Bergman--Gaberdiel proposals, by comparing the global forms of the gauge groups on both sides. On the orientifold side, we perform a scan of brane states, similar to the case of the D0-brane in type I string theory, and identify spinorial states that constrain the gauge group; on the heterotic and bosonic side, the gauge groups are provided by the internal momentum lattices. In both cases, we find agreement between the group structure of the orientifolds and the proposed duals, up to a subtle projection for the Bergman--Gaberdiel duality.

### [130] [CFTs on Squashed Spheres and the Thermal Effective Action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30716)
*Klaas Parmentier,Nikolay Bobev*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文通过两种互补极限——球面小形变和Seifert流形小纤维大压扁极限——研究三维共形场论（CFT）。在球面附近，利用共形微扰理论将自由能响应表达为应力张量关联函数，证明球形自由能是度量形变空间中的局部最大值，并将这一结果推广至守恒自旋-s流。在小纤维极限（高温区），配分函数由二维热有效作用量控制，该作用量将不同背景（包括压扁透镜空间）上的CFT自由能联系起来，并针对自由场、大N临界O(N)模型和全息CFT确定了Wilson系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解三维共形场论（CFT）在紧致欧几里得流形上的自由能行为，特别是度量形变如何影响自由能，以及高温极限下有效理论的构建。

Method: 采用两种互补极限：一是对小形变球面运用共形微扰理论（conformal perturbation theory），通过谐波空间公式导出自由能的二次响应；二是针对Seifert流形的小纤维大压扁极限，构建二维热有效作用量（thermal effective action），包含Weyl重标度基度量和Kaluza–Klein场强。

Result: 证明了球形自由能是度量形变空间中的局部最大值，该二次响应与应力张量两点函数系数c_T成正比；守恒自旋-s流的二次响应呈现交替符号。在小纤维极限下，导出了热有效作用量的Wilson系数，涉及压扁透镜空间上的自由能关系。

Conclusion: 对于幺正CFT，球面自由能在度量形变下为局部最大值；高温极限下的二维热有效作用量统一描述了不同背景上的CFT自由能行为。研究涵盖了自由场、大N临界O(N)模型和全息CFT等具体实例。

Abstract: We study three-dimensional CFTs on compact Euclidean manifolds in two complementary limits: small deformations of the round $S^3$ and the small-fiber, large-squashing limit of Seifert manifolds. Near the round sphere, conformal perturbation theory expresses the free-energy response through integrated stress-tensor correlators. We derive a harmonic-space formula for the universal quadratic response to arbitrary metric squashing and show that it is proportional to the $c_T$ coefficient of the stress-tensor two-point function. For unitary CFTs this establishes that the sphere free energy is a local maximum in the space of metric deformations. This result extends to conserved spin-$s$ currents, whose quadratic response alternates in sign. For the specific case of squashing the Hopf fiber, we find an explicit form for the cubic response, and in addition obtain the leading correction to the two-point function of scalar operators. In the small-fiber limit, corresponding to the large temperature regime of the CFT, the partition function is governed by a two-dimensional thermal effective action constructed out of the Weyl-rescaled base metric and a Kaluza--Klein field strength. The thermal effective action relates CFT free energies on different backgrounds, including squashed Lens spaces, which we discuss in detail. We also explicitly determine the Wilson coefficients of this effective action, to various orders in the high-temperature expansion, for free fields, the large-$N$ critical O($N$) model, and holographic CFTs.

</details>


### [131] [The auxiliary-deformed Breitenlhoner-Maison model: duality frames and higher-dimensional origin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30717)
*Daniele Bielli,Mattia Cesàro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文扩展了二维Breitenlohner-Maison模型的可积形变理论，推导了μ-frame辅助场视角，并基于对偶不变拉格朗日形式构造了两种描述到四维的提升，得到的四维形变模型为高阶导数理论且缺乏显式的微分同胚不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维Breitenlohner-Maison (BM) 模型是D=4广义相对论中具有两个对易Killing等度规（commuting Killing isometries）的经典可积子扇区，通过Kaluza-Klein约化至D=2得到。近期已有研究通过ν-frame辅助场构造了该模型的可积形变。本文旨在从互补的μ-frame辅助场视角扩展这一观点，并进一步将两种描述显式提升至四维。

Method: 首先推导与ν-frame互补的μ-frame辅助场视角；然后基于对偶不变拉格朗日形式（duality-invariant Lagrangian formulation）的启发式假设（ansatz），将两种描述分别提升（uplift）到四维。

Result: 得到的四维形变模型是一个高阶导数理论（higher-derivative theory），且在ν-frame和μ-frame两种框架下均缺乏显式的微分同胚不变性（manifest diffeomorphism invariance）。

Conclusion: 本文对四维模型中缺乏显式微分同胚不变性这一令人困惑的特征的可能解决方案进行了评述，并讨论了该模型在四维中的物理诠释。

Abstract: The two-dimensional Breitenlohner-Maison (BM) model is a classically integrable subsector of $D=4$ general relativity endowed with two commuting Killing isometries, obtained via Kaluza-Klein reduction to $D=2$. Integrable deformations of such a theory have recently been constructed via auxiliary fields in the so-called $ν$-frame. In this work we first extend this point of view by deriving the complementary auxiliary field perspective known as $μ$-frame, and then explicitly construct the uplift to $D=4$ of both descriptions, relying on an ansatz inspired by duality-invariant Lagrangian formulations of Einstein theory. The resulting four-dimensional deformed model thus obtained is a higher-derivative theory which lacks manifest diffeomorphism invariance in both frames. We comment on possible resolutions of this puzzling feature and on the physical interpretation of the model in $D=4$.

</details>


### [132] [Complex Conformal Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30720)
*Yuma Furuta,Wataru Harada,Yuya Kusuki,Yin Tang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出通过将精确边际耦合（exactly marginal couplings）解析延拓到复平面来系统构造复数共形场论（complex CFTs），利用紧致自由玻色子、伊辛模型缺陷及AdS/BCFT对偶等可解体系，揭示了复数共形流形的全局结构，并严格证明复数有理共形场论（rational CFTs）不存在，为理解非厄米临界性、弱一级相变及行走重整化群流提供了可控的理论桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复数共形场论（complex CFTs）在非厄米临界性（non-Hermitian criticality）、弱一级相变（weakly first-order phase transitions）和行走重整化群流（walking renormalization group flows）等前沿问题中扮演关键角色，但其一般结构尚未清楚。本文旨在为这类理论建立系统化的构造方案。

Method: 本文采用的主要方法是将精确边际耦合解析延拓（analytic continuation）到复平面，以构造复数共形场论。该程序统一适用于体（bulk）、边界（boundary）和缺陷（defect）形变，并保持共形对称性。通过紧致自由玻色子（compact free boson）作为可解实验室，研究复数高斯（Gaussian）共形流形的全局结构；在伊辛CFT缺陷情形中，使用解析延拓导出缺陷谱、能量传输系数和有效中心荷（effective central charge）的精确表达式；并借助AdS/BCFT对偶研究复数边界重整化群流。

Result: 研究发现复数有理共形场论（rational CFTs）不存在——有理点严格限制在实参数区域，提供了实数与复数理论之间的清晰分界。在伊辛CFT缺陷情形中，通过解析延拓得到了缺陷谱、能量传输系数和有效中心荷的精确表达式，并在非厄米临界伊辛链和自由费米子链中通过体-缺陷关联函数（bulk-defect correlators）、纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）和复数能量输运得到了精确验证。

Conclusion: 复数共形流形（complex conformal manifolds）可以作为可解格点模型、复数共形场论和全息对偶（holography）之间的可控桥梁，同时为非幺正共形自举（nonunitary conformal bootstrap）提供严格的解析基准。

Abstract: Complex conformal field theories (CFTs) have recently emerged as essential frameworks for understanding non-Hermitian criticality, weakly first-order phase transitions, and walking renormalization group flows, while their general structures remain largely unknown. In this work, we propose a systematic construction of complex CFTs by analytically continuing exactly marginal couplings into the complex plane. This procedure applies uniformly to bulk, boundary, and defect deformations, preserving conformal symmetry while generically complexifying operator spectra and other universal data. Using the compact free boson as a solvable laboratory, we uncover the global structure of the complexified Gaussian conformal manifold. More generally, we demonstrate that genuinely complex rational CFTs do not exist: rational points remain confined to the real regime, providing a sharp distinction between real and complex theories. In the defect case, we investigate the one-parameter family of conformal defects in the Ising CFT and derive exact expressions for the defect spectrum, energy transmission coefficient, and effective central charge from analytic continuation. The theoretical predictions are precisely verified in non-Hermitian critical Ising and free fermion chains using bulk-defect correlators, entanglement entropy, and complex energy transport, providing concrete evidence for the complex defect conformal manifold. Finally, we study complex boundary renormalization-group flows through the AdS/BCFT correspondence. Our results establish complex conformal manifolds as a controlled bridge between solvable lattice models, complex CFTs, and holography, while providing stringent analytic benchmarks for the nonunitary conformal bootstrap.

</details>


### [133] [Ryu-Takayanagi area from Virasoro modular data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30723)
*Jennifer Lin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文展示了在全息二维共形场论中，纠缠熵可以同时具有微观解释并与Ryu-Takayanagi公式的大c主导项匹配，这种表示通过将交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）应用于副本流形（replica manifolds）获得，并揭示了RT面积项源自对缠绕切割上粗粒化Virasoro交织子（coarse-grained Virasoro intertwiners）的统计求和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索全息二维共形场论（holographic 2d CFTs）中纠缠熵的微观起源，并建立其与Ryu-Takayanagi公式在大中心荷（large central charge, large-c）极限下的一致性联系。

Method: 通过将交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）应用于副本流形（replica manifolds），对纠缠熵进行重写；利用Virasoro代数（Virasoro algebra）的代数纠缠熵（algebraic entanglement entropy）表示，并将边界共形场论（BCFT）中粗粒化的重初级场（heavy primaries）按刘维尔动量（Liouville momenta）分箱（bin）作为中心标记（center labels）。

Result: 重写后的纠缠熵在大c极限下由鞍点（saddle point）主导；熵的O(c)部分源自主导箱中重初级场的Cardy密度（Cardy density），并等价于Ryu-Takayanagi面积项（Ryu-Takayanagi area）。

Conclusion: RT面积项的物理统计起源可理解为来自纠缠切割（entangling cut）上粗粒化的Virasoro交织子；研究还给出了维持该物理解释所需的粗粒化程度的定量判据。

Abstract: We show that in holographic 2d CFTs, the entanglement entropies across several choices of global state and subregion can be written in a way that at once has a microscopic interpretation and matches the leading large$-c$ organization of the Ryu-Takayanagi formula. This representation is obtained by applying crossing symmetry to the replica manifolds. From the boundary point of view, each rewritten entropy looks like an algebraic entanglement entropy for the Virasoro algebra restricted to the region, with center labels obtained by coarse-graining heavy primaries of the BCFT on the regulated region into bins labeled by Liouville momenta. At large $c$, a resulting sum over bins is dominated by a saddle, and the $O(c)$ part of the entropy comes from the Cardy density of heavy primaries in the dominant bin. We identify this $O(c)$ part of the entropy with the Ryu-Takayanagi area. Physically, this suggests a concrete statistical origin for the Ryu-Takayanagi area as coming from coarse-grained Virasoro intertwiners across the entangling cut. The result also provides quantitative criteria for the amount of coarse-graining allowed for the consistency of the interpretation.

</details>


### [134] [Constrained particle on a group: from propagators to correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30725)
*Guanda Lin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种“群上粒子”（particle-on-a-group）形式体系来描述超-JT引力（super-JT gravity），通过将理论映射为在等距群（isometry group）上运动且受边界条件约束的粒子，推导出超-Schwarzian作用量、量子化后的超粒子以及超对称区间传播子（interval propagator），并构建了计算关联函数（correlator）的算法，获得了N=2和N=4超-JT引力的三点核函数与零能三点函数，以及零能四点无序时间序（OTOC）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在发展一种计算超-JT引力中超对称关联函数（supersymmetric correlator）的新形式体系，以克服传统方法在处理超对称约束和费米子自由度时的困难。

Method: 将超-JT引力描述为在等距群上运动且受边界条件约束的粒子，其中N=2和N=4理论分别对应SU(1,1|1)和PSU(1,1|2)上的约束粒子；通过求解约束得到超-Schwarzian作用量，并对约化后的超粒子（superparticle）进行量子化，谨慎处理费米子约束（fermionic constraint）；从变换保持约束的要求导出物理世界线超荷（supercharge），构造超对称区间传播子和边界锚定威尔逊线算符（Wilson-line operator），最后构建关联函数算法。

Result: 获得了N=2和N=4超-JT引力的三点组合核（three-point composition kernel）和零能标量三点函数；对于四点函数，该方法复现了标准玻色JT无序时间序（OTOC），并给出了N=2和N=4超-JT引力中明确的零能OTOC，这潜在可用于研究贝里曲率（Berry curvature）和BPS混沌（BPS chaos）。

Conclusion: 所提出的群上粒子形式体系为超-JT引力的关联函数计算提供了一套系统化算法，并成功获得了N=2和N=4超对称情况下的新结果，包括零能OTOC，为研究超对称引力中的混沌和量子信息提供了工具。

Abstract: We develop a particle-on-a-group formulation of super-JT gravity aimed at computing supersymmetric correlators. We show that the (super)JT gravity can be described by a particle moving on the isometry group satisfying constraints from boundary conditions of (super)JT gravity. In this language the $\mathcal N=2$ and $\mathcal N=4$ theories are described by constrained particles on $SU(1,1|1)$ and $PSU(1,1|2)$. Solving the constraints gives the super-Schwarzian actions. We also quantize the reduced superparticle, with careful treatment of the fermionic constraints. We then derive the physical worldline supercharges from the requirement that the transformations preserve the constraints. These charges allow us to construct supersymmetric interval propagators in invariant variables and to formulate boundary-anchored Wilson-line operators for both superconformal primary and descendant insertions. Finally, we use these ingredients to build an algorithm for correlators. We obtain the $\mathcal N=2$ and $\mathcal N=4$ three-point composition kernels and zero-energy scalar three-point functions. For four-point functions, the same method reproduces the standard bosonic JT OTOC, gives an explicit zero-energy OTOC in $\mathcal N=2$ and $\mathcal N=4$ SJT, which is potentially useful for studying Berry curvature and BPS chaos.

</details>


### [135] [Radial Solutions of Multi-Field de Sitter Galileons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30728)
*Alice Garoffolo,Mary Gerhardinger,Kurt Hinterbichler,Mark Trodden*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了so(N)不变的多场de Sitter Galileon理论中静态球对称屏蔽解，发现宇宙视界和强耦合半径共同影响解的可行性，曲率可在一定程度上缓解超光速问题，但代价是有效理论的有限有效区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弯曲时空（尤其是de Sitter时空）背景下研究Galileon理论中的非线性屏蔽（screening）机制，分析宇宙视界（cosmological horizon）和强耦合（strong-coupling）效应对屏蔽解的影响，并比较de Sitter与Anti-de Sitter情形的差异。

Method: 基于so(N)不变的多场de Sitter Galileon理论，引入保持内部对称性的物质耦合，求解静态球对称径向方程，分析近源处四次相互作用（quartic interaction）主导的非线性屏蔽分支与远处二次项（quadratic terms）主导的de Sitter Vainshtein半径（Vainshtein radius）的交叉行为，并研究扰动稳定性与亚光速条件。

Result: 屏蔽解只有在Vainshtein半径交叉发生在强耦合半径之前才可行；存在有限径向区域内扰动稳定且亚光速的分支；曲率可以缓解Galileon理论中的超光速问题，但代价是有效理论（effective theory）的适用范围有限。

Conclusion: 曲率效应对Galileon理论的屏蔽机制有显著影响，既可能改善超光速问题，也限制了有效理论的有效区域；de Sitter与Anti-de Sitter情形存在来自宇宙视界和曲率的不同效应。

Abstract: We study static, spherically symmetric screening solutions in the $\mathfrak{so}(N)$-invariant multi-field de Sitter Galileon theory, with matter couplings preserving the internal symmetry. Unlike in flat space, the de Sitter radial problem is affected both by the cosmological horizon and by the possible appearance of a finite strong-coupling radius, where the radial equation becomes singular and the effective description breaks down. Near the source, the quartic interaction governs the nonlinear screened branch, while farther away the quadratic terms dominate, defining a de Sitter analog of the Vainshtein radius at their crossover. A screened solution is viable only if this crossover occurs before the strong-coupling radius is reached. We study perturbations around the radial background and identify branches for which perturbations are stable and subluminal, within a restricted radial domain set by the strong-coupling point. Finally, we compare the de Sitter and Anti-de Sitter cases, isolating effects due to curvature from those specific to the cosmological horizon. Our results indicate that curvature can alleviate the superluminality issues that arise in Galileon theories for appropriate choices of matter couplings, though this comes at the price of a finite region of validity for the effective theory.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过大质量形变（massive deformation）从 $T[SU(N)]$ 理论（四维 $\mathcal{N}=4$ $SU(N)$ SYM 的 S-对偶界面）构造出三维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFT，并将其识别为所需的重整化群墙界面（RG-wall interface）和半 BPS 边界条件（half-BPS boundary condition）的低能描述。

Result: 识别出了实现四维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ $SU(N)$ SYM 重整化群墙界面（RG-wall interface）的三维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFT，并通过半指标（half-indices）匹配以及界面碰撞（interface collision）的非平凡自洽性条件验证了该识别。

Conclusion: 该三维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFT 是连接四维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ $SU(N)$ SYM 紫外和红外描述的重整化群墙界面（RG-wall interface）的三维实现，同时也在低能下描述了该理论的半 BPS Dirichlet 边界条件（half-BPS Dirichlet boundary condition）。

Abstract: We identify the 3d theory that realizes the RG-wall interface of 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ $SU(N)$ Super-Yang-Mills, interpolating between the UV Lagrangian and the IR Seiberg-Witten effective description. The same theory also describes the low-energy boundary condition that corresponds to giving half-BPS Dirichlet boundary condition in the Lagrangian description of 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ $SU(N)$ SYM. The theory is a 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFT that can be obtained as a massive deformation of the $T[SU(N)]$ theory, which is the S-duality interface of 4d $\mathcal{N}=4$ $SU(N)$ SYM. As the main validating tests, we match half-indices and discuss non-trivial consistency conditions when colliding such interfaces.

### [138] [On Black Holes Surrounded by Radiation: I. Classical Considerations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30794)
*Marcos Riojas,Matthew J. Strassler*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究爱因斯坦方程中一种球对称静态解：由零径向压力的无质量粒子构成的厚壳包裹的史瓦西黑洞，称为“hillingar黑洞”。该类解将光子球层扩展为任意深度的区域，在经典层面上与普通黑洞光学不可区分，并对其是否存在及观测可能性进行了推测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 考虑球对称静态爱因斯坦方程解，其中黑洞被具有零径向压力的无质量粒子构成的厚壳包围。将轨道气体视为稳定爱因斯坦星团（Einstein cluster）的边际稳定极限，从而将光子球（photon sphere）扩展为任意深度区域。

Result: 得到了一类称为“hillingar黑洞”的解析解。该解在经典层面上具有多项特殊性质，尤其对无穷远观测者而言，其光学表现与普通黑洞不可区分。

Conclusion: 这类天体可能存在于自然界中，但外观与普通黑洞极其相似，使得观测区分面临挑战。其热力学和稳定性将在后续论文中研究。

Abstract: We consider spherically symmetric static solutions to Einstein's equations describing a Schwarzschild black hole enveloped by a thick shell of orbiting massless particles with zero radial pressure. The orbiting gas is ultra-compact and ultra-relativistic, and can be viewed as the marginally stable limit of a stable Einstein cluster. These solutions, which we refer to as "hillingar black holes", extend the photon sphere into a region of arbitrary depth. We compare these objects to black holes surrounded by other gases and note they have numerous special properties at the classical level; in particular, they appear optically indistinguishable from ordinary black holes to observers at infinity.
  We speculate concerning the possibility that these objects (or others much like them) might exist in nature, and whether they might be observable despite their similar outward appearance to ordinary black holes. We examine their thermodynamics and stability in companion papers.

### [139] [On Black Holes Surrounded by Radiation II: Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30797)
*Marcos Riojas,Matthew J. Strassler*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文论证了“希林加黑洞”（hillingar black hole, HBH）在热力学上完全模拟了同等质量普通黑洞的行为，即在假设热平衡成立的前提下，该系统具有与质量 $M$ 的普通黑洞相同的温度和熵。作者通过多种方法验证了这一结论，并指出在 AdS 空间中该模拟不成立，结构更为丰富。此外，若热平衡能够建立并维持，处于半径 $\geq 3M$ 空腔中的 HBH 可以蒸发，可能在有限小体积内引发信息悖论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在前期工作中，作者已发现由质量 $m$ 的史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）被厚“粒子海洋”包裹的“希林加黑洞”在光学上模拟了同 ADM 质量 $M$ 的普通黑洞。本文旨在进一步检验该体系在热力学层面是否同样具有模拟能力。

Method: 采用多重方法（multiple methods）对热平衡假设下的系统进行热力学分析，包括同行另一论文中给出的另一方法及亚稳定性（metastability）指示。在 AdS 空间中进行对比分析。

Result: 在热平衡假设下，希林加黑洞的温度和熵与质量为 $M$ 的普通黑洞完全相同。但在 AdS 空间中该模拟不成立，解结构更为丰富。处于半径 $\geq 3M$ 空腔中的 HBH 若维持热平衡，可以蒸发。

Conclusion: HBH 在热力学上成功模拟普通黑洞，且其蒸发过程可能在有限小体积内重现信息悖论（information puzzle），这为黑洞演化研究提供了潜在联系，但作者也谨慎指出这些系统是否可作为更现实模型尚不明确。

Abstract: In a companion paper we considered a Schwarzschild black hole of mass $m$ enveloped by a thick "ocean'' of massless particles that extends the black hole's photon sphere into a region of finite depth. There we showed that this "hillingar black hole'', of ADM mass $M$, optically mimics an ordinary black hole of the same mass. Here we find it also mimics the black hole thermodynamically: the formal assumption of thermal equilibrium implies the system has the same temperature and entropy as an ordinary black hole of mass $M$. We check this result carefully using multiple methods; a further method and indications of metastability are given by one of us in a companion paper. In AdS space, the mimicry does not hold, and the solutions have a richer structure. While it is far from clear that these systems are models for more realistic ones, we note possible connections with black hole evolution. In particular, assuming thermal equilibrium can be established and maintained, an HBH in a cavity of radius $\geq 3M$ can evaporate, potentially posing the information puzzle in a small finite volume.

</details>


### [140] [As Cold as a Black Hole: Extended Photon Spheres](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30798)
*Marcos Riojas*

Abstract: It is widely believed that self-gravitating radiation cannot reach thermal equilibrium with a black hole in asymptotically flat spacetime. The following observation is used to describe an exception to this rule. The photon sphere controls central aspects of the Israel junction conditions (IJCs), the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equation, and finite-radius black hole thermodynamics. Through these results, we will describe how to compute coarse-grained entropies without using the Euclidean path integral. For instance, we find the IJCs and TOV equation are precisely equivalent at zero radial pressure. At fixed mass, adding shells in regions of positive specific heat lowers the asymptotic Hawking temperature, and the inverse specific heat at the photon sphere is proportional to $-Λ$.

Strassler, where we found that a "hillingar black hole" (HBH) mimics an ordinary Schwarzschild black hole of mass $M$, sharing its Hawking temperature, photon ring, and, in equilibrium, its coarse-grained entropy $S = 4 πM^2$. Here, we show these features are not tuned; they follow uniquely from joint mechanical and thermodynamic constraints. A necessary and sufficient condition for thermodynamic mimicry is found that is satisfied by a one parameter family of self-similar systems, all of which, excepting the HBH, require massless walls at the edges of their extended photon spheres. ### [144] [Spin-Induced Fractal Time-Crystal-Like Dynamics and Non-Markovian Memory in the Bateman Dual Oscillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30890)

Method: 采用由自旋（spin）诱导的空间形变所生成的(2+1)维相空间非对易框架（phase-space noncommutative framework），构建量子Bateman振子，并利用时间无关的厄米哈密顿量（Hermitian Hamiltonian）描述系统，以及约化动力学（reduced dynamics）和记忆核（memory kernel）分析其非马尔可夫性。

Result: 该封闭量子系统展现出精确的离散标度协方差（discrete scaling covariance），产生无须外部驱动的自相似时间演化；约化动力学呈现固有的是非马尔可夫性，受历史依赖的记忆核支配；标度结构可几何表示为与放大和阻尼支路对应的对数螺旋轨迹（logarithmic-spiral trajectories）。

Conclusion: 自旋是Bateman放大与阻尼动力学、自相似标度周期性、对数螺旋结构和非马尔可夫记忆的共同物理来源；该机制依赖于非平衡约化动力学而非平衡态局域可观测量，因此不受平衡时间晶体不可行定理的限制；该机制可自然推广至相对论性任意子系统（relativistic anyonic systems）。

Abstract: Can a closed quantum system generate time-crystal-like nonequilibrium behavior, self-similar scaling structures, and non-Markovian memory without external driving or coupling to a macroscopic environment? The resulting doubled quantum dynamics is governed by a time-independent Hermitian Hamiltonian and exhibits an underlying SU(1, 1) structure with amplified and damped collective modes. We show that these modes satisfy an exact discrete scaling covariance, leading to self-similar temporal evolution without external driving. Upon tracing over one oscillator sector, the reduced dynamics becomes intrinsically non-Markovian and is governed by a history-dependent memory kernel. The same scaling structure admits a geometric representation in terms of logarithmic-spiral trajectories associated with the amplified and damped branches of the Bateman system. Because the mechanism relies on nonequilibrium reduced dynamics rather than equilibrium expectation values of local observables, it lies outside the assumptions underlying conventional no-go theorems for equilibrium time crystals. Our results identify spin as the common physical origin of the amplified and damped Bateman dynamics, self-similar scaling periodicity, logarithmic-spiral structures, and non-Markovian memory, also suggesting a natural extension of the mechanism to relativistic anyonic systems.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 厄米矩阵模型中矩积分的计算在耦合常数为复数时面临挑战，现有方法可能失效或收敛缓慢，需要一种高效且普适的计算工具。

Method: 提出渐近自举方法，处理形如 $a_n=\int^{\infty}_{-\infty} x^n \exp(-V(x)) dx$ 的归一化积分，其中势函数 $V(x)$ 为多项式，允许系数为复数；收敛性由首个次领头耦合（subleading coupling）$g_{2\ell-2}$ 决定，要求其实部为正且幅角绝对值小于 $\pi/{\ell}$。

Result: 该方法在由 $g_{2\ell-2}$ 确定的锥形区域内具有渐近指数级收敛速度；通过构造与这些测度相关的正交多项式（orthogonal polynomials），可用于研究厄米矩阵模型的相结构（phase structure）。

Conclusion: 渐近自举方法为复数耦合常数下的矩积分提供了高效可靠的渐近方案，并拓展了正交多项式方法在矩阵模型相结构研究中的应用。

Abstract: We propose an asymptotic bootstrap method to evaluate moment integrals that arise in problems related to hermitian matrix models. These are normalized integrals of the form $a_n=\int^{\infty}_{-\infty} x^n \exp(-V(x)) dx$ where $V(x)$ is a polynomial of $x$. The method is applicable even when the coupling constants in $V(x)= x^{2\ell}/(2\ell) + g_{2\ell-2} x^{2\ell-2}/(2\ell-2) + \dots$ are complex. We prove that the method converges asymptotically exponentially fast on a cone region determined by the first subleading coupling $g_{2\ell-2}$, which must have a positive real part and an absolute value of the argument less than $π/{\ell}$. We use our method to study the phase structure of Hermitian matrix models by constructing the orthogonal polynomials associated to these measures.

### [147] [Phase Transition and Censorship Principle for Holographic Casimir Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31001)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了平行球面缺陷的全息卡西米尔效应（holographic Casimir effect），发现其在小宽度下由含连接EOW膜的AdS孤子（AdS soliton）描述，随宽度增大转变为含断开EOW膜的AdS空间，导致一级相变（first-order phase transition）且效应在断开相中消失。宇宙监督（cosmic censorship）为卡西米尔力的吸引性提供了全息解释，而拓扑监督（topological censorship）则解释了平行缺陷真空与AdS孤子对偶的起源。

Method: 利用全息对偶（holographic duality），以AdS孤子和含EOW膜（end-of-world branes）的AdS空间作为引力对偶，通过比较小宽度与大连度下的构型，研究平行球面缺陷卡西米尔效应的相变行为及力的性质。

Result: 平行球面缺陷的全息卡西米尔效应存在一级相变：小宽度时由连接EOW膜的AdS孤子主导，效应非零；宽度增大后转变为断开EOW膜的AdS空间，效应消失。自由理论在该构型下符合全息卡西米尔界。卡西米尔力在相同边界条件下的吸引性可由宇宙监督解释；排斥力对应裸奇点（naked singularity），通常被视为不允许的。

Conclusion: 平行球面缺陷的全息卡西米尔效应展现出与自由理论及其他缺陷构型不同的相变行为。宇宙监督和拓扑监督为卡西米尔力的吸引性及真空对偶结构提供了全息层面的物理解释。

Abstract: This paper explores the holographic Casimir effect associated with parallel spherical defects. The gravity dual is dominated by the AdS soliton with connected EOW branes at small widths, transitioning to AdS space with disconnected EOW branes as the width increases. Consequently, the holographic Casimir effect undergoes a first-order phase transition and vanishes in the disconnected phase. This new behavior highlights a significant difference from free theories, holographic parallel plane defects, and hyperbolic defects. Additionally, we confirm that the free theories adhere to the holographic bound for the Casimir effect in the case of parallel spherical defects.
  Interestingly, we observe that cosmic censorship provides a holographic interpretation of the attractive nature of the Casimir force when identical boundary conditions are imposed on both parallel surfaces. The repulsive Casimir force is associated with the bulk spacetime containing a naked singularity, which is generally considered forbidden. Additionally, we argue that topological censorship offers a natural explanation for why the vacuum of parallel defects is dual to the AdS soliton.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点仅将杂化紧致化视为由模参数（moduli）标定的一族解，但这一视角忽略了在模空间上纤维化所引入的额外几何结构。本文旨在阐明该额外结构的组织形式，并展示其如何自然地包含 α'² 阶的超对称修正。

Method: 采用数学上的纤维化（fibration）观点，将紧致化数据（compactification data）视为在模空间（moduli space）上的纤维丛，从而将原本独立的形变（deformations）重新解释为通用曲率（universal curvatures）的分量。通过该几何框架，将 α'² 阶超对称修正纳入描述。

Result: 揭示了杂化紧致化族在模空间上纤维化后，形变自然地成为通用曲率的分量；该框架能够自洽地包含 α'² 阶的超对称修正。

Conclusion: 杂化紧致化在模空间上的纤维化结构提供了比单纯解空间更丰富的组织方式，且这一结构可以容纳高阶（α'² 阶）超对称修正。

Abstract: A family of heterotic compactifications carries more structure than a collection of solutions parametrised by moduli. Once the compactification data are fibred over moduli space, deformations become components of universal curvatures. This note reviews that organisation and explains how it incorporates the $α'^2$ supersymmetry corrections.

</details>


### [149] [Two-scalar-field $f(R)$ Thick Branes, Gravitational Resonances and Quasinormal Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31330)
*Xin-Yi Pan,Heng Guo,Jing-Xin Gong,Hong-Tao Jiang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在f(R)引力框架下研究双标量场支撑的厚膜世界，通过分析Bloch型内部结构能否在无鬼影分支中产生长寿命张量共振，发现实轴诊断无窄共振峰，而准正则模谱显示所有张量激发均为宽且短寿命的耗散模式。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用双标量场提供可调能量密度分裂的解析翘曲背景；通过f_R>0约束分离无鬼影分支与奇异分支；使用渐近迭代法（Asymptotic Iteration Method）和含超对称伙伴势（supersymmetric partner potential）的时域演化作为零模过滤工具提取准正规频率。

Result: 在无鬼影分支中，相对概率谱和相移透射谱均未显示窄实轴共振峰；尖锐准局域化峰仅出现在奇异分支，由有效耦合消失导致的张量势发散引起；无鬼影分支的准正规模式具有负虚部，品质因子Q≈0.9-1.9，表明是宽且短寿命的耗散模式。

Conclusion: 厚膜内部结构本身无法在无鬼影区域产生长寿命张量共振；准正则模谱提供了对Kaluza-Klein动力学恰当且完整的复频率描述。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate thick brane worlds in $f(R)$ gravity supported by two-scalar-field. The two-scalar sector provides an analytical warped background with tunable energy-density splitting, allowing us to test whether a Bloch-type internal structure can generate long-lived tensor perturbations resonances in the physically admissible region. We impose the positivity of \(f_R\equiv df/dR\), the derivative of the gravitational Lagrangian with respect to the Ricci scalar, which plays the role of an effective gravitational coupling in \(f(R)\) gravity. This separates the smooth ghost-free branch from a singular branch where this effective coupling vanishes. In the ghost-free branch, neither the relative-probability spectrum nor the phase-shift transmission spectrum shows narrow real-axis resonant peaks. These real-axis diagnostics indicate that the internal brane structure alone does not produce long-lived tensor resonances in the ghost-free region. Sharp quasi-localization peaks appear only in the singular branch, where the vanishing effective coupling induces divergent structures in the tensor potential; these peaks should therefore be interpreted as singular-boundary signals rather than ghost-free resonances of the smooth brane background. We then characterize the ghost-free massive Kaluza-Klein modes in the complex-frequency plane. Using the Asymptotic Iteration Method where applicable and time-domain evolutions with a supersymmetric partner potential as a zero-mode filtering tool, we extract the fundamental quasinormal frequencies. The modes have negative imaginary parts and quality factors \(Q\simeq0.9-1.9\), showing that the ghost-free massive tensor excitations are broad, short-lived dissipative modes. Thus the QNM spectrum provides the appropriate complex-frequency description of the Kaluza-Klein dynamics when no narrow real-axis resonances are resolved.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 尖点附近的线状奇点对粒子具有普遍俘获效应；零质量轨道的显式解析解及随机行为缺失表明该问题可能具有可积性。

Abstract: We study the critical behavior of the Lin-Lunin-Maldacena (LLM) geometry in the case when a droplet in the LLM base space develops a cusp. This cusp is a generic feature of the density of complex eigenvalues in the dual complex matrix model (CMM) computing the correlation functions of huge 1/2-BPS operators in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM theory. It is also related to the criticality in CMM describing the pure $2D$ quantum gravity behavior. The supergravity dual -- LLM metric in the vicinity of the tip of the cusp -- acquires a universal $ISO(1,3)\times SO(5)$ symmetric form, with a naked singularity along a half-infinite line. Both massless and massive particles get trapped by this line singularity for almost any impact parameter. Generic trajectories ending on the singular line reach it in finite affine time, while the corresponding observer time diverges. An explicit analytic solution for a large class of massless trajectories together with the absence of stochastic behavior in the vicinity of the cusp hint on a certain integrability of the problem.

Abstract: We investigate the dynamical role of internal vibrational modes in the Abelian Higgs model, focusing on how Derrick-type excitations modify vortex dynamics and scattering processes. We study the scattering of excited vortices and show that the interplay between spectral flow and mode excitation generates effective forces and enables resonant energy transfer between translational and internal degrees of freedom. As a result, vortex dynamics become strongly non-adiabatic, exhibiting super-elastic collisions, oscillatory dependence of the final state on initial conditions, and the emergence of fractal structures in scattering diagrams. Our results demonstrate that internal vibrational modes play a fundamental role in vortex interactions, going beyond the standard moduli space approximation and revealing a rich phenomenology driven by mode dynamics.

### [152] [Kaluza-Klein Gravitons in a Higher Curvature Warped Geometry : A New Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31561)
*Abhirup Karmakar,Isika Mandal,Soumitra SenGupta*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在含5维f(R)=R+αR²引力和宇宙学常数的双膜翘曲几何中，通过欧几里得路径积分方法求解类薛定谔方程，得到了高曲率修正对KK引力子（Kaluza-Klein graviton）能谱、与标准模型耦合及衰变宽度的影响，并发现其可在未来对撞机实验中探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: KK引力子是高维体物理在四维宇宙中的直接对撞信号，而翘曲时空虽能优雅地解决规范层级问题（gauge-hierarchy problem），但底层的AdS₅体具有普朗克尺度的曲率，自然要求引入高曲率修正（higher-curvature corrections）以更完整地描述物理。

Method: 在5维f(R)=R+αR²引力框架下，对小幅高曲率参数α进行微扰求解修正后的引力场方程，得到主导阶的背反应翘曲因子（back-reacted warp factors）；随后在翘曲膜世界（braneworld）背景中，利用欧几里得路径积分形式（Euclidean path integral formalism）求解描述引力子涨落的类薛定谔方程，通过量子力学传播子直接获得KK引力子能谱和归一化波函数，并以此为基础解析计算高曲率修正。

Result: KK引力子质量出现显著上移，而引力子与标准模型物质场的耦合仅有轻微改变；涉及虚引力子过程的净截面被压低，而引力子衰变到双轻子（dilepton）和双光子（diphoton）的衰变宽度因高曲率修正而显著增强。

Conclusion: 这些效应将导致大质量KK引力子的产生和衰变信号发生可观测的修改，有望在未来的高精度对撞机实验中得到检验。

Abstract: Kaluza-Klein (KK) Gravitons are the direct collider imprints of the higher dimensional bulk physics in our four dimensional universe, arising from the compactification of an extra spatial dimension. In this work, we consider a two-brane warped geometry with a 5D $f(\mathcal R) = \mathcal R + α\mathcal R^2$ gravity along with cosmological constant $Λ$. The warped spacetime provides an elegant resolution of the gauge-hierarchy problem without introducing any intermediate scale, while the Planck-scale curvature of the underlying $AdS_5$ bulk naturally motivates the inclusion of higher-curvature corrections. For small values of higher-curvature parameter ($α$), we obtain the leading-order back-reacted warp factors perturbatively from the modified gravitational field equations. In the backdrop of a warped braneworld model, we have solved the Schrödinger-like equation governing the graviton fluctuations using a Euclidean path integral formalism, yielding the KK graviton spectrum and normalized wavefunctions directly from the corresponding quantum-mechanical propagator. Treating these results as the unperturbed background, we analytically determine the higher curvature corrections to KK graviton spectrum and their couplings to Standard Model (SM) matter fields. We find that there is an appreciable upward shift in the KK graviton masses while leaving the graviton-SM couplings only mildly modified as compared to a model with only Einstein gravity in the bulk. However the net cross-section of processes involving virtual gravitons appears to be suppressed whereas the dilepton and diphoton decay widths of the gravitons are significantly enhanced because of the higher curvature corrections. Overall, these effects lead to observable modifications to both the production and decay signatures of massive KK gravitons and may be probed in some future precision collider experiments.

Conclusion: 该工作将dS全息重新诠释为幺正AdS/CFT希尔伯特空间中的态制备过程，为非幺正边界条件与幺正体态理论之间的兼容性提供了具体范例，并为dS量子引力在AdS/CFT框架下的理解开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We propose that AdS$_3$ gravity coupled to dS$_2$ end-of-the-world branes is dual to a unitary holographic CFT$_2$ with non-unitary conformal boundary conditions. These boundary conditions have complex $g$-functions and appear in conjugate pairs. The associated gravitational path integral admits no real saddles, but does admit complex saddles. We show that an AdS$_3$ black hole microstate with a dS$_2$ brane behind the horizon corresponds to the unitary time evolution of a pure CFT state prepared by a Euclidean path integral on a cylinder with such boundary conditions. The construction predicts a boundary-condition-changing primary with $h=-c/8$, which resides in the boundary sector rather than the bulk spectrum and is therefore compatible with unitarity of the underlying CFT. This realizes dS holography as state preparation in a unitary AdS/CFT Hilbert space.

In a special limiting case, the complexity exhibits oscillatory behavior with a logarithmic envelope, signaling a transition to a qualitatively distinct regime. ### [156] [Fate of "Space-like singularities" in $c=1$ Matrix Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31925)
*Sumit R. Das,Shaun D. Hampton,Sinong Liu,Gautam Mandal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究二维弦论（two-dimensional String Theory）中依赖于时间的背景，这些背景在世界面上产生超光速Liouville壁（superluminal Liouville walls）。通过在矩阵模型（matrix model）中引入量子淬火（quantum quench）并保留非线性项，作者发现早期行为与双标度理论（double scaled theory）一致，但在时间尺度~log N时红外壁（IR wall）效应显著，随后费米面折叠（folds on the fermi surface）增殖，最终相空间密度松弛到与初始状态无关的平衡值。这表明时空类奇点（space-like singularity）的出现是严格双标度极限（double scaling limit）的人为产物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维弦论中一类时间依赖背景会诱导超光速Liouville壁，对应的矩阵模型中出现类奇点行为。作者希望理解这些背景的真实动力学，并检验类奇点是否作为双标度极限的人为产物出现。

Method: 在双标度c=1矩阵模型中引入量子淬火，保留矩阵势中的非线性项以偏离双标度极限。采用费米子图像（fermion picture）和Thomas-Fermi近似分析相空间密度（phase space density）的演化；使用作用-角变量（action-angle variables）研究晚期动力学行为，并对角度空间进行粗粒化处理（coarse-grained density）。

Result: 早期相空间密度行为与双标度理论一致；在时间尺度~log N时红外壁效应变得显著；在更晚的特征卷曲时间~ (log N)^2时，费米面折叠增殖并稠密覆盖允许相空间区域。晚期相空间密度在时间无关且角度无关的值附近快速振荡，粗粒化后的角度密度以幂律（power law）松弛到平衡值，该幂律指数是普适的（universal），与初始状态细节基本无关。

Conclusion: 时空类奇点的出现是严格双标度极限的人为产物；真实的矩阵模型动力学中，非线性效应导致系统最终松弛到平衡态。文中还评论了该末态在弦论中的解释。

Abstract: A class of time dependent backgrounds in two dimensional String Theory leads to superluminal Liouville walls on the worldsheet. In the dual double scaled $c=1$ matrix model these backgrounds involve eigenvalues leaking out to infinity, and the collective field fluctuations become strongly coupled along space-like regions, resembling singularities. We realize these backgrounds as results of quantum quenches in the matrix model, retaining non-linear terms in the matrix potential, thus departing from a double scaling limit. Working in the fermion picture in a Thomas-Fermi approximation, we show that while the early time behavior of the phase space density near the maximum of the potential agrees with that obtained in the double scaled theory, at times of the order $(\log N)$ the effect of the IR wall becomes significant. At later times, with a characteristic winding time of order $(\log N)^2$, folds on the fermi surface proliferate and eventually cover the allowed region in phase space densely. Using action-angle variables, we show that the phase space density oscillates around a time independent and angle independent value rapidly at late times. A coarse-grained density in the angle space relaxes to a time independent equilibrium value as a power law with a universal exponent largely independent of the details of the initial state. Thus, the appearance of a space-like singularity is an artifact of the strict double scaling limit. We comment on the interpretation of the final state in String Theory.

</details>


### [157] [Convergence of Nekrasov instanton sum for unitary quivers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31953)
*Bruno Le Floch*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，在参数开稠子集中，4维$\mathcal{N}=2$幺正规范群箭图规范理论的Nekrasov配分函数的收敛半径为正，并通过AGT对偶推出Virasoro与W-代数共形块具有正收敛半径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Nekrasov配分函数（Nekrasov partition function）作为瞬子计数参数（instanton counting parameters）的级数展开，其收敛性问题长期未获严格证明。作者旨在为一大类四维超对称规范理论建立该级数的正收敛半径。

Method: 将配分函数表达为分拆元组（tuples of partitions）之和，利用组合不等式对（共）钩长（(co)hook lengths）的乘积进行控制，从而证明级数的绝对收敛性（absolute convergence）。

Result: 对$U(N)$ SQCD，当等变参数（equivariant parameters）之比$b^2=ε_1/ε_2\in\mathbb{C}\setminus[0,+\infty)$且库仑参数（Coulomb parameters）或质量远离某个超平面格点时，收敛半径为正。对一般箭图仅在$b^2\in\mathbb{C}\setminus\mathbb{R}$时成立。渐近自由规范多重态时半径为无穷大；质量形变的共形情形下半径有仅依赖于$b^2$的正下界。

Conclusion: 通过AGT对应（AGT correspondence），该结果意味着球面或环面上的大量Virasoro与W-代数共形块（conformal blocks）在一般维数和复中心荷下具有正收敛半径。

Abstract: The convergence radius of Nekrasov partition functions (as a function of instanton counting parameters) is shown to be positive for 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ quiver gauge theories with unitary gauge groups in an open dense subset of parameters. For $U(N)$ SQCD this is established if the ratio of equivariant parameters $b^2=ε_1/ε_2$ belongs to $\mathbb{C}\setminus[0,+\infty)$ and Coulomb parameters or masses are away from a lattice of hyperplanes. For general quivers it is only established for $b^2\in\mathbb{C}\setminus\mathbb{R}$. When gauge multiplets are asymptotically free, the radius is infinite, whereas in the (mass-deformed) conformal case the radius admits a positive lower bound that only depends on $b^2$. The proof relies on the expression of the partition function as a sum over tuples of partitions, and a proof of absolute convergence based on combinatorial inequalities on products of (co)hook lengths. Through the AGT correspondence this implies that large classes of Virasoro and W-algebra conformal blocks on the sphere or torus have positive convergence radius, for generic dimensions and complex central charges.

</details>


### [158] [BMPV black hole at first order in $α'$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31987)
*Alejandro Ruipérez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文推导了描述三个不等荷超对称极值BMPV黑洞一阶α'修正的解析解，并通过推广的Wald公式计算了修正后的黑洞熵，结果与基于超对称指标的文献结论一致。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弦论（string theory）框架下研究黑洞的量子引力修正，具体针对杂优弦（heterotic string）的低能有效作用量，探究α'修正对超对称极值BMPV黑洞（具有三个不等电荷）的几何与熵的影响。

Method: 从杂优弦的低能有效作用量出发，解析求解描述一阶α'修正的超对称极值BMPV黑洞解，该解在渐近平坦区域（asymptotically-flat region）与近地平线几何（near-horizon geometry）之间插值；利用文献中推广的Wald公式（Wald formula）计算修正后的黑洞熵，该公式能够正确处理Lorentz Chern-Simons项。

Conclusion: 本文获得的解析解及其熵修正与已有文献结果吻合，验证了推广Wald公式在处理包含Lorentz Chern-Simons项的弦论有效作用量时的正确性与有效性。

Abstract: We consider the low-energy effective action of the heterotic string and derive an analytic solution describing the first-order $α'$ corrections to the supersymmetric and extremal BMPV black hole with three unequal charges. The solution interpolates between an asymptotically-flat region and the near-horizon geometry. We compute the corrected black hole entropy using a generalization of Wald formula available in the literature, which correctly accounts for the Lorentz Chern-Simons term. The resulting expression agrees with recent results in the literature, which are based on the evaluation of an appropriate supersymmetric index.

### [159] [The geometric bookkeeping guide for $\varepsilon$-factorised differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31994)
*Antonela Matijašić*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种系统化的算法框架，用于构建任意费曼积分（Feynman integrals）族的ε-因子化微分方程（ε-factorised differential equations），不依赖于底层几何结构，基于扭曲上同调（twisted cohomology）和Baikov表示（Baikov representation），通过两步流程实现：先按几何性质排序Laporta算法（Laporta algorithm）获得Laurent多项式形式，再构造变换矩阵实现ε-因子化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能实验的精确预言（precision predictions）依赖于在多圈多尺度费曼积分中准确评估维数正规化（dimensional regularisation）下的结果。微分方程法（method of differential equations）是标准工具，但其全部威力仅在系统能转化为ε-因子化形式时才能实现。现有方法缺乏通用的几何无关框架，因此需要一种系统化的算法来构建这种形式。

Method: 方法基于扭曲上同调框架，研究Baikov表示下与费曼积分族相关联的微分形式空间。第一步，对Laporta算法引入一种特定排序（ordering），根据费曼积分的几何性质对其在扇区（sector）内排序，该排序得到的基（basis）具有关于维数正规化参数ε的Laurent多项式（Laurent polynomial）形式的微分方程。第二步，系统构造变换矩阵（transformation matrices），将Laurent多项式系统转换为ε-因子化形式。

Result: 该方法对于任意费曼积分族——无论其底层几何结构如何——均能系统性地构造出ε-因子化的微分方程系统。第一步得到的基对应的微分方程具有Laurent多项式形式，第二步通过变换矩阵最终实现ε-因子化。

Conclusion: 该算法框架为费曼积分的精确计算提供了一种几何无关的系统化途径，有望进一步提升多圈多尺度积分计算的自动化水平，从而支持高能实验的更精确理论预言。

Abstract: Precision predictions for high-energy experiments rely on accurately evaluating multi-loop, multi-scale Feynman integrals in dimensional regularisation. The method of differential equations is by now the standard tool for this task, but its full power is only realised when the system can be brought into an $\varepsilon$-factorised form. In this talk, we present an algorithmic framework that systematically constructs $\varepsilon$-factorised differential equations for arbitrary integral families, independent of their underlying geometry. We work in the setting of twisted cohomology and study the space of differential forms associated with a given family of Feynman integrals in the Baikov representation. Our approach consists of two steps. First, we introduce a particular ordering for the Laporta algorithm that orders Feynman integrals within a sector according to their geometric properties. We observe that this order relation yields a basis whose differential equation is in a Laurent polynomial form in the dimensional regulator $\varepsilon$. In the second step, we systematically construct transformation matrices such that the resulting system is in the $\varepsilon$-factorised form.

</details>
