### [160] [An Interaction Language Model: Mechanism Discovery from Statistical Patterns of Physical Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30922)
*Triparna Ganguly,Hanqi Jiang,Xinliang Li,Yi Pan,Junhao Chen,Miyuki Karunathilaka,Tianming Liu,Yohannes Abate*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出交互语言模型（Interaction Language Model, ILM），将物理、化学和生物系统中的构件间交互视为一种可学习的结构化语言。ILM通过学习组件间的统计依赖和顺序，推断交互路径、识别缺失步骤并预测下一步交互。通过PhenoLink（有向图，存储从文献中提取的交互证据与转移概率）和PhenoSeq（序列模型，补全端点约束下的缺失机制步骤）两个互补组件，形成生成-验证流水线。在分子扩散领域的172个查询测试中，ILM匹配了零样本Claude Opus 4.7的分布内准确率，但能够对无证据查询做出确定性拒绝（最高拒绝93.5%的转移），并提供可审计的逐步骤支持，弥补了零样本生成在证据缺失时的虚构缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理、化学和生物系统中的构件间交互遵循结构化模式，可视为一种可学习的语言。现有零样本生成方法在面对无证据查询时倾向于虚构（fabrication）回答，且缺乏可审计的逐步骤支持，因此需要一种能够基于语料库证据进行确定性推理和拒绝的框架。

Method: 提出交互语言模型（Interaction Language Model, ILM），包含两个互补组件：PhenoLink（从文献中提取的有向交互图，每条边聚合段落级证据并携带转移概率，该概率被解释为信息成本）和PhenoSeq（序列模型，在端点约束下提出缺失的机制步骤）。两者构成生成-验证流水线（generate-then-verify pipeline），返回每个带有可复现、逐步骤、基于语料库的审计轨迹（audit trail）的解释。

Result: 在172个查询的四个保留测试集（held-out suites）上，ILM流水线在分布内准确率（in-distribution accuracy）上匹配了零样本Claude Opus 4.7基线；但与基线不同（基线对每个不可能查询都虚构链条），ILM通过构造性方式拒绝了多达93.5%的语料证据缺失的转移。

Conclusion: ILM实现了零样本生成在结构上无法实现的两个功能：对缺乏证据的查询进行确定性拒绝（deterministic refusal），以及提供可审计的逐步骤支持。该框架可扩展到分子、细胞、设备或其他构件之间通过序列和条件交互产生功能的自然与工程系统。

Abstract: Interactions among building blocks in physical, chemical, and biological systems follow structured patterns interpretable as a learnable language: just as language models learn which words tend to follow others, one can learn which physical phenomena follow others and under what conditions. We introduce an Interaction Language Model (ILM): a framework that treats interaction as a statistically structured, learnable language for design-to-function reasoning across fields. By learning statistical dependencies and ordering among components, ILMs infer interaction pathways, identify missing steps, and predict the next likely interaction. We demonstrate it through two complementary components, PhenoLink and PhenoSeq, applied to molecular diffusion, a ubiquitous mechanism for energy and particle transport. PhenoLink is a directed graph of interactions among diffusion-based events extracted from publications, where each edge aggregates paragraph-level evidence and carries a transition probability interpreted as an information cost. PhenoSeq complements this with a sequence model that proposes missing mechanistic steps under endpoint constraints. Together they form a generate-then-verify pipeline returning every explanation with a reproducible, per-step, corpus-grounded audit trail. Across four held-out suites of 172 queries, the pipeline matches a zero-shot Claude Opus 4.7 baseline on in-distribution accuracy, yet unlike the baseline, which fabricates a chain for every impossible query, it refuses up to 93.5% of transitions in corpus evidence by construction. ILM thus delivers what zero-shot generation structurally cannot: deterministic refusal of evidence-absent queries and auditable, per-step support. The framework extends to natural and engineered systems where function emerges from sequential and conditional interactions among molecules, cells, devices, or other components.

</details>

### [161] [Large CISS Polarization from the Hierarchy Between Transport and Geometrical Spin Currents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30670)
*Zeev Vager*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出，手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）中观察到的大自旋极化现象，可能源于电子在弯曲路径（如双链DNA）中运动时固有的几何自旋电流（geometrical spin current），而非仅由弱自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit interaction）引起；实验测量电流可被视为该几何自旋电流的弱泄漏，从而解释了极化的量级矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）实验中观察到的大自旋极化（large spin polarization）难以用有机材料中微弱的微观自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit interaction）定量解释，已有理论与实验结果之间存在量级矛盾。

Method: 作者重新审视了此前针对受限于弯曲路径（curved paths）的电子所引入的几何自旋电流（geometrical spin current）概念，并提出一个适用于双链DNA（dsDNA）输运的尺度论证（scale argument）。

Result: 使用代表性dsDNA参数估算的几何自旋电流本征尺度（intrinsic geometrical spin-current scale）远大于许多CISS实验中测得的实际输运电流。

Conclusion: 该量级层级关系（hierarchy）表明，实际输运可理解为对底层弯曲自旋电流态（curved spin-current states）的弱泄漏（weak leakage）；在此图像下，大CISS极化源于输运过程对预先存在的自旋电流分支（pre-existing spin-current branches）的选择。

Abstract: Large spin polarization observed in chiral-induced spin selectivity (CISS) remains difficult to explain quantitatively. Experimental polarizations measured in chiral molecular systems are often substantially larger than expected from weak microscopic spin-orbit interaction in organic materials. We revisit the geometrical spin current introduced previously for electrons constrained to curved paths and propose a scale argument relevant to transport through double-stranded DNA (dsDNA). Estimation of the intrinsic geometrical spin-current scale using representative dsDNA parameters yields current magnitudes substantially larger than measured transport currents in many CISS experiments. We suggest that this hierarchy allows transport to be interpreted as weak leakage from underlying curved spin-current states. Within this picture, large CISS polarization emerges as transport selection of pre-existing spin-current branches.

### [162] [Unsupervised Thermodynamics of Molecular Diffusion Models: Action-Operator Semantics and Auditable Free-Energy Readout](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30687)
*Wenjie Xi*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个与扩散模型（diffusion models）原生兼容的“动作-算子框架”（action-operator framework），将扩散模型从黑箱坐标采样器转化为可审计的热力学估计器，能够在无重叠构象系综间通过自洽的噪声算子桥（noisy operator bridge）直接读取自由能差（ΔF），并在丙氨酸二肽和配体-口袋微扰体系中验证了其精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型在分子结构与构象系综建模中应用日益广泛，但其学习到的表示（representations）和分数（scores）的热力学含义尚不明确，阻碍了模型从纯坐标采样器向可解释热力学工具的转化。

Method: 作者构建了一个数学自洽的动作-算子框架：将固定分子环境定义为基动作（base action）S₀(x)，将炼金微扰（alchemical perturbation）定义为算子（operator）O(x)；标准扩散加噪（diffusion noising）过程产生有效含噪动作和算子，其梯度和炼金导数由模型学习到的场直接表示。这种自洽性催生了“噪声算子桥”（noisy operator bridge），可从端点系综（endpoint ensembles）和逐帧评估中读出自由能差。

Result: 在丙氨酸二肽（alanine dipeptide）受控实验中，引入物理归纳偏置可部分恢复基动作与微扰算子。在C6-H到C6-F配体-口袋非键微扰（185L/IND）这一相空间重叠极小的挑战性任务中，监督桥方法估计的炼金ΔF与19态MBAR参考的偏差约在1 k_BT以内。仅用端点坐标与二值标签即可部分恢复算子形状与中心化自由能标度，无需任何力或动作监督。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一条将生成式分子扩散模型从黑箱坐标采样器转化为可审计热力学估计器的严格路径，在无重叠构象系综下实现了高精度的自由能差预测。

Abstract: Diffusion models are increasingly utilized for modeling molecular structures and conformational ensembles, yet the thermodynamic meaning of their learned representations and scores remains elusive. To resolve this ambiguity, we introduce a mathematically consistent action-operator framework natively compatible with diffusion models. By defining a fixed molecular environment as a base action $S_0(x)$ and an alchemical perturbation as an operator $O(x)$, standard diffusion noising induces effective noised actions and operators whose gradients and alchemical derivatives are directly represented by the model's learned fields. This rigorous self-consistency enables a ``noisy operator bridge'' capable of reading out free-energy differences ($ΔF$) from endpoint ensembles and per-frame evaluations. In controlled experiments on alanine dipeptide systems, we show that incorporating physical inductive biases enables partial recovery of the base action and perturbation operator. When applied to a challenging C6-H to C6-F ligand-pocket nonbonded perturbation (185L/IND) with negligible phase-space overlap, our supervised bridge estimates the alchemical $ΔF$ within approximately $1\ k_\mathrm{B}T$ of a stable 19-state MBAR reference. Finally, we demonstrate that endpoint coordinates and binary labels alone are sufficient to partially recover the operator shape and a centered free-energy scale without any force or action supervision. This work provides a rigorous path toward transforming generative molecular diffusion models from black-box coordinate samplers into auditable thermodynamic estimators.

</details>


### [163] [Extension of openCOSMO-RS Into a Full Open-Source Equation of State: Implementation, Parameterization, and Benchmarking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30892)
*Jan Markgraf,D. G. Lisboa Girardi,Irina Smirnova,Simon Müller*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该工作将COSMO-SAC-Phi模型（一种将活度系数框架扩展为完整状态方程的方法）在openCOSMO-RS平台上实现，构建了openCOSMO-RS-Phi模型；通过约1800种纯组分的大规模参数集和二元混合物的基准测试，验证了其与原始模型相当的精度，并向学术界提供完全开源的实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在COSMO-SAC活度系数框架基础上，Soares等人提出的COSMO-SAC-Phi模型通过显式考虑压力效应并将其扩展为完整的状态方程（equation of state, EoS），但该模型尚缺乏一个开源、可广泛获取的实现版本。本工作旨在将该扩展在openCOSMO-RS框架中实现，并提供完全开源的参数集与代码，以促进学术界的可重复研究与后续发展。

Method: 将COSMO-SAC-Phi模型实现在openCOSMO-RS框架中；纯物质与混合物被表示为伪混合物（pseudo-mixture），包含实际摩尔数和描述自由体积（free volume）或空穴（holes）的额外伪组分。四个纯组分参数通过拟合每种物质的蒸气压（vapor pressure）和液态摩尔体积（liquid-molar volume）数据确定。在评估中未引入任何二元交互作用参数（binary interaction parameters）。

Result: 构建了包含约1800个纯组分条目的开源参数集（open-source parameter set）。模型性能在两个基准状态方程数据库（纯化合物与二元混合物）上进行了评估。openCOSMO-RS-Phi模型达到了与原始COSMO-SAC-Phi formulation相当的精度。

Conclusion: openCOSMO-RS-Phi模型再现了原始COSMO-SAC-Phi公式的准确性，同时为科学社区提供了一个完全开源且可访问的实现。该工作还为未来预测性电解质溶液（electrolyte solutions）状态方程的发展奠定了基础。

Abstract: The COSMO-SAC-Phi model developed by Soares et al. extends the COSMO-SAC activity-coefficient framework into a full equation of state by explicitly accounting for pressure effects. In this approach, pure substances and mixtures are represented as pseudo-mixtures consisting of the actual number of moles and an additional pseudo-component that describes free volume, or holes. In this work, we implement this extension within the openCOSMO-RS framework and evaluate it using a large and diverse set of molecules and binary systems. The resulting equation of state includes an extensive open-source parameter set with around 1800 pure-component entries, made freely available to the academic community. The four pure-component parameters were fitted to vapor-pressure and liquid-molar volume data for each substance. Model performance was assessed against two benchmark equation-of-state databases, one for pure compounds and one for binary mixtures, without introducing any binary interaction parameters. The resulting openCOSMO-RS-Phi model reproduces the accuracy of the original COSMO-SAC-Phi formulation while providing a fully open-source and accessible implementation for the scientific community. Beyond its immediate utility, it also establishes a foundation for future development of predictive EoS for electrolyte solutions.

</details>


### [164] [Contrastive Regularization of Machine Learning Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31660)
*Dimitrios Tzivrailis,Georgios Sotiropoulos,Alberto Rosso,Eiji Kawasaki*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出，基于均方误差（MSE）训练的机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials）尽管在点预测上达到化学精度，但作为采样器（sampler）会在分子动力学模拟中产生错误的低能漂移和失真的热力学可观测量。作者提出对比正则化MSE（Contrastive Regularized MSE, CRMSE），在MSE损失中融入基于KL散度（Kullback-Leibler divergence）的对比项，利用持久化朗之万链（persistent Langevin chains）自洽修正势能面的分布偏差，无需新增ab initio数据。在MD17数据集的乙醇和阿司匹林分子上，CRMSE恢复了能量分布、原子间距离分布和二面角自由能廓线，与密度泛函理论（DFT）接近定量吻合，同时保持力精度和化学精度范围内的能量误差；该方法训练集缩减时仍有效。结论表明：可靠采样依赖的是分布级训练（distribution-level training），而非单纯增加回归数据量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习原子间势虽被训练用于预测能量和力，但其实际用途是驱动分子模拟（molecular simulations），可观测量需对势能定义的平衡分布（equilibrium distribution）求平均。这是一个更广泛的AI问题：作为生成器（generator）部署的回归器（learned regressor），点级精度（pointwise accuracy）无法保证正确的分布。标准MSE训练在MD17这类广泛使用的基准上，即使达到化学精度（chemical accuracy），仍会在采样时失败，产生虚假低能态和失真的热力学量。

Method: 提出对比正则化MSE（Contrastive Regularized MSE, CRMSE），作为一种后训练（post-training）步骤：在标准MSE损失中加入基于Kullback-Leibler散度的对比项，该项衡量势能隐式玻尔兹曼分布（implicit Boltzmann distribution）与目标分布之间的差异。网络作为其自身的能量模型（energy-based model），通过持久化朗之万链（persistent Langevin chains）暴露模型容易漂入的错误构型并提升其能量，整个过程不引入新的ab initio数据。

Result: 在MD17数据集的乙醇（ethanol）和aspirin分子上，CRMSE将采样器限制在物理构型空间内，恢复了能量分布、原子间距离分布和二面角自由能廓线（dihedral free-energy profiles），与DFT接近定量一致；同时保留了力精度（force accuracy），能量误差保持在化学精度范围内。即使训练集大幅缩减，CRMSE仍然有效。相比之下，标准MSE训练在相同基准上失败。

Conclusion: 标准MSE训练在MD17这一广泛使用的基准上失败，而一个最小化的对比性修正即可修复该问题，这说明可靠采样（reliable sampling）更多地依赖于针对模型自身生成分布的训练，而非单纯增加数据量。分布级训练（distribution-level training）不是回归精度的细化改进，而是一个独立的要求（distinct requirement）。

Abstract: Machine learning interatomic potentials are trained to predict energies and forces but built to be sampled: their purpose is to drive molecular simulations whose observables average over the equilibrium distribution the potential defines. They exemplify a broader AI problem -- learned regressors deployed as generators -- where pointwise accuracy does not guarantee a correct distribution. We show that potentials trained by standard Mean Squared Error (MSE) minimization on Density Functional Theory (DFT) data can reach chemical accuracy on held-out data, yet still fail as samplers: their trajectories drift into spurious low-energy minima and return thermodynamic observables that depart sharply from the reference. To correct this, we introduce Contrastive Regularized MSE (CRMSE), a post-training step that augments the MSE with a contrastive term derived from the Kullback--Leibler divergence between the potential's implicit Boltzmann distribution and the target. The network serves as its own energy-based model: persistent Langevin chains expose the configurations it drifts into and raise their energy, adding no new ab initio data. On the ethanol and aspirin molecules of the MD17 dataset, CRMSE confines the sampler to the physical basin and recovers the energy distribution, interatomic-distance distributions, and dihedral free-energy profiles to near-quantitative agreement with DFT, while preserving force accuracy and keeping energy errors within chemical accuracy; it remains effective when the training set is sharply reduced. That MSE training fails this way on MD17 -- one of the most widely used benchmarks -- while a minimal contrastive correction repairs it suggests that reliable sampling depends less on data volume than on training the model against the distribution it produces: distribution-level training is not a refinement of regression accuracy, but a distinct requirement.

</details>

### [165] [Minkowskian open/closed conformal field theory possibly without vacuum: the Cardy case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30928)
*Bin Gui*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 对于任意共形网（conformal net），无论是否有理，该论文在代数量子场论框架下构造了闭弦和开弦的Cardy型共形场论，并证明了多双锥（multi-double-cones）和边界区间（boundary intervals）的哈格对偶（Haag duality）的三种形式，分别对应模不变性（modular invariance）、Cardy一致性条件（Cardy consistency condition）和边界场代数的莫里塔等价（Morita equivalence）的闵可夫斯基版本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往Cardy型共形场论（conformal field theory）的构造多局限于有理共形网（rational conformal net），对于一般（非有理）共形网缺乏系统的代数构造方法。该工作旨在填补这一空白，将构造推广至任意共形网。

Method: 采用代数量子场论（algebraic quantum field theory）框架，在闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）上分别针对闭弦和开弦构造共形场论。对于闭弦，时空为$(\mathbb R/2π\mathbb Z)\times\mathbb R$；对于开弦，时空为$[0,π]\times\mathbb R$。

Result: 成功构造了对应于任意共形网（无论是否有理）的Cardy型共形场论，并验证了其若干基本性质。进一步证明了多双锥和边界区间的哈格对偶的三种形式，这些形式分别被解释为模不变性、Cardy一致性条件和边界场代数莫里塔等价的闵可夫斯基版本。

Conclusion: 该工作将Cardy型共形场论的代数构造从有理共形网推广至一般情形，并在代数量子场论的语言下建立了共形场论中几个关键概念（模不变性、Cardy一致性、Morita等价）与哈格对偶之间的对应关系。

Abstract: For any conformal net, not necessarily rational, we construct the associated Cardy-type conformal field theory on the Minkowski spacetimes $(\mathbb R/2π\mathbb Z)\times\mathbb R$ for closed strings and $[0,π]\times\mathbb R$ for open strings within the framework of algebraic quantum field theory. In addition to verifying some of their basic properties, we prove three forms of Haag duality for multi-double-cones and boundary intervals, interpreted respectively as the Minkowskian versions of modular invariance, the Cardy consistency condition, and the Morita equivalence of boundary field algebras.

Result: 成功构造了源自重整化群流和非无穷小规范固定变化的量子主作用新同伦，并基于这些同伦对应的场重定义构建了具有同构有效作用的量子主作用跨。

Abstract: We review the notion of homotopy of quantum master actions in geometric Batalin-Vilkovisky formalism. ### [167] [Boundaries in the Instantaneous Formulation of Field Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31265)
*Silvester G. A. Borsboom*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了经典场论中边界条件对瞬时状态空间（instantaneous state space）的结构性影响，发现不同边界条件会导致切丛（tangent bundle）结构或扇区结构（sector structure），并探讨了由此产生的规范变换（gauge transformation）的哈密顿性（Hamiltonian property）以及边界对称群（boundary symmetry group）的定义与性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典场论中边界条件（boundary conditions）对状态空间（state space）和规范对称性（gauge symmetry）的影响尚未被系统厘清，特别是在瞬时形式（instantaneous formulation）下，不同边界条件会如何改变状态空间的几何结构以及规范变换的哈密顿性质（Hamiltonian nature），进而影响物理边界对称群（physical boundary symmetry group）的定义。

Method: 基于GiMmsy的协变形式（covariant formulation）和瞬时形式（instantaneous formulation）对经典场论的边界条件进行分析。分别考察了恒定狄利克雷边界条件（constant Dirichlet boundary condition）和仅速度在边界为零的边界条件，通过勒让德变换（Legendre transform）从扇区化状态空间导出扇区化相空间（sectored phase space），并利用叶状规范泊松结构（leafwise canonical Poisson structures）进行分析。

Result: 恒定狄利克雷边界条件导致瞬时状态空间是满足该条件的场位形空间（configuration space）的切丛（tangent bundle）。仅速度在边界为零时，状态空间出现扇区结构（sector structure），每个扇区是一个由边界位形标记的切丛。扇区移动规范变换（sector-moving gauge transformations）因缺少边界动量（boundary momentum）而非哈密顿（non-Hamiltonian），由此提出将边界保持哈密顿变换（boundary-preserving Hamiltonian transformations）商去平凡变换（trivial ones）作为渐近或边界对称群（asymptotic/boundary symmetry group）的新定义。电磁学的物理边界对称群在所有扇区同时考虑时等同于全局规范群（global gauge group）的一个副本。

Conclusion: 边界条件决定经典场论瞬时状态空间的几何结构：恒定狄利克雷条件对应单一切丛，仅速度为零条件导致切丛扇区化。扇区移动变换的非哈密顿性要求重新定义边界对称群，电磁学中该群在所有扇区下退化为全局规范群。讨论了非阿贝尔杨-米尔斯理论（non-Abelian Yang-Mills theory）在何种条件下也能得到相同结论。

Abstract: We study boundary conditions in GiMmsy's covariant and instantaneous formulations of classical field theories and show that the instantaneous state space in the presence of a constant Dirichlet boundary condition is a tangent bundle to the configuration space of fields satisfying said condition. We then study the instantaneous state space when only the velocity of the field is required to vanish at the boundary and show that this results in a sector structure, where each sector is a tangent bundle labeled by the configuration at the boundary. Taking the Legendre transform of this sectored state space yields a sectored phase space with leafwise canonical Poisson structures. We apply this to Yang-Mills theory with spatial boundary conditions and relate our results to flux superselection sectors. The sector-moving gauge transformations are not Hamiltonian because of the lack of a boundary momentum, prompting us to propose a novel definition of the asymptotic or boundary symmetry group as the quotient of the boundary-preserving Hamiltonian transformations by the trivial ones. The physical boundary symmetry group of electromagnetism is then shown to be a copy of the global gauge group even when all sectors are considered simultaneously. Conditions are discussed under which the same holds for non-Abelian Yang-Mills theory.

</details>

Result: 在多个示例中成功应用该算法，分析了拓扑算子（topological operator）的作用，并在本原单位根（primitive roots of unity）处计算了不可约TL特征（irreducible TL characters）的模变换（modular transformation）。

Conclusion: 该算法为分析融合范畴驱动的晶格模型中的对称性与表示结构提供了系统框架，并揭示了拓扑算子在态空间分解中的角色。

Abstract: We consider classical 2d lattice models with face interactions defined in terms of a fusion category. The symmetries of such models typically include an algebra of topological operators sitting on a closed path in the lattice. In the case when the face interactions obey the Temperley-Lieb (TL) relations, we present a generic algorithm to determine the decomposition of the transfer-matrix space of states as a direct sum of simple TL modules. We apply this approach to several examples, and analyse the action of topological operators. As an application, we compute the modular transformation of the irreducible TL characters at primitive roots of unity.

### [171] [Kinetic derivation of thermal viscous models for nematic liquid crystal dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31784)
*P. E. Farrell,J. Málek,O. Souček,U. Zerbinati*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文从基于BGK型碰撞算子的动力学理论出发，建立了向列相液晶（nematic liquid crystals）的宏观热力学理论，通过Chapman-Enskog展开和Rajagopal-Srinivasa约束最大化方法，推导了包括粘性、热和自旋扩散效应的本构方程，推广了近期无粘动力学理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有向列相液晶的动力学理论主要局限于无粘情况，缺乏对粘性、热传导和自旋扩散等耗散效应的系统处理。本文旨在从微观动力学描述出发，建立包含这些效应的自洽宏观热力学理论。

Method: 采用含BGK型碰撞算子的动力学理论（kinetic theory），其中取向有序通过Vlasov平均场势（Vlasov potential）描述，并假设取向弛豫时间尺度远快于平动动量弛豫。利用零阶和一阶Chapman-Enskog展开（Chapman-Enskog expansions）推导Helmholtz自由能的本构方程及熵产生率的结构形式，再结合动力学信息确定熵产生率的本构关系，最后应用Rajagopal-Srinivasa约束最大化程序（constrained maximisation procedure）得到Cauchy应力张量、偶应力张量（couple-stress tensor）以及能量和熵通量的本构方程。

Result: 得到了包含质量、线动量、角动量、能量和熵的平衡方程；推导了Helmholtz自由能的本构方程；识别了熵产生率的结构形式并确定了其本构关系；最终获得了Cauchy应力张量、偶应力张量以及能量和熵通量的本构方程，从而将无粘理论推广到包含粘性、热和自旋扩散效应的情形。该理论同时给出了可压缩和不可压缩两种形式。

Conclusion: 通过动力学理论与约束最大化方法的结合，成功建立了一个能够描述向列相液晶粘性、热和自旋扩散效应的宏观热力学理论，推广了Farrell、Russo和Zerbinati的无粘动力学理论。该理论采用了最简单的BGK型碰撞算子近似。

Abstract: We develop a macroscopic thermodynamic theory of nematic liquid crystals starting from a kinetic theory of ordered fluids with a collision operator of Bhatnagar-Gross-Krook (BGK) type. The kinetic description incorporates mean-field alignment interactions through a Vlasov potential and relies on a separation of time scales, with orientational relaxation occurring on a faster time scale than translational momentum relaxation. At the continuum level, we establish the balance equations for mass, linear and angular momentum, energy, and entropy. Using the zeroth and first order Chapman-Enskog expansions, we derive a constitutive equation for the Helmholtz free energy and identify the associated structural form of the entropy production rate. We then exploit additional information from the kinetic description to determine a constitutive relation for the entropy production rate itself. Finally, by applying the constrained maximisation procedure of Rajagopal and Srinivasa, we obtain constitutive equations for the Cauchy stress and couple-stress tensors, as well as for the energy and entropy fluxes. In this way we generalise the recent inviscid kinetic theory of Farrell, Russo, and Zerbinati to account for viscous, thermal, and spin-diffusive effects, using the simplest BGK-type approximation of the collision operator. Both compressible and incompressible variants of the theory are presented.

### [172] [Quantum Stokes matrices and quantum Riemann-Hilbert-Birkhoff maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31809)
*Xiaomeng Xu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文为非交换形式的有理线性常微分方程组（ordinary differential equations, ODEs）引入了量子斯托克斯矩阵（quantum Stokes matrices），证明了其满足量子交换关系（quantum exchange relations），并将这些矩阵解释为黎曼-希尔伯特-伯克霍夫映射（Riemann-Hilbert-Birkhoff map）的形变量子化（deformation quantization）下的结合代数同态（associative algebra homomorphism）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典斯托克斯现象（Stokes phenomenon）在可积系统与代数几何中具有核心地位，但将其推广到非交换（noncommutative）或量子化（quantized）框架下的严格数学结构尚不充分。作者旨在为具有$p+1$阶极点的非交换亚纯线性系统的量子斯托克斯矩阵建立严格的代数基础。

Method: 作者构造了非交换版本的量子斯托克斯矩阵，并证明它们满足自然的量子交换关系。基于这些关系，进一步将量子斯托克斯矩阵阐释为结合代数同态，从而在代数层面上刻画其结构。

Result: 证明了量子斯托克斯矩阵满足量子交换关系；揭示了该矩阵可视为黎曼-希尔伯特-伯克霍夫映射（在泊松映射（Poisson map）意义下）的形变量子化所对应的结合代数同态。

Conclusion: 量子斯托克斯矩阵提供了一种将经典斯托克斯几何推广到非交换/量子框架的代数途径，建立了量子交换关系与黎曼-希尔伯特-伯克霍夫映射形变量子化之间的形式关联。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce quantum Stokes matrices for a noncommutative version of meromorphic linear systems of ordinary differential equations with a pole of order $p+1$. We prove that these quantum Stokes matrices satisfy natural quantum exchange relations. These relations allow us to interpret the quantum Stokes matrices as an associative algebra homomorphism, which may be viewed as a deformation quantization of the Riemann-Hilbert-Birkhoff map, regarded as a Poisson map, for meromorphic connections with a pole of order $p+1$.

</details>

### [173] [Density Wave Ordering with Disordered Ultracold Fermions in Optical Cavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30769)
*Óscar Rios Alves,Filippo Ferrari,Lorenzo Fioroni,Alberto Mercurio,Vincenzo Savona*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究超冷费米子气体中腔诱导密度波有序与可控无序之间的相互作用，发现无序通过重正化有效光-物质耦合降低了超辐射阈值，并使密度波晶格发生畸变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索光学腔中超冷费米子气体中腔诱导密度波有序与可控无序之间的相互影响机制，揭示无序如何改变系统的超辐射相变行为。

Method: 采用线性响应理论（linear response theory）推导超辐射阈值，并利用数值平均场方法（numerical mean-field treatment）分析腔内光子数和实空间费米子密度。

Result: 无序相互作用重正化（renormalize）有效光-物质耦合，平均而言降低了临界泵浦强度，且阈值在短散斑相关长度下呈现自平均（self-averaging）行为；无序使密度波晶体发生畸变，激发了超出纯净腔几何所选择傅里叶分量的模式。

Conclusion: 发射的腔光与原位密度图像均可作为探测与光学腔耦合的费米子物质中工程化无序的探针。

Abstract: We investigate the interplay between cavity-induced density-wave ordering and controllable disorder in a trapped two-dimensional gas of ultracold fermions. The atoms are dispersively coupled to an optical cavity and transversely driven by a pump beam, while an additional speckle beam spatially modulates the atom-light coupling through an AC-Stark shift of the atomic transition. In momentum space, this disorder converts the usual coupling between the cavity mode and a discrete set of density-wave Fourier components into a coupling to a continuum of fermionic density modes, weighted by the spectrum of the speckle pattern. Using linear response theory, we derive the superradiant threshold and show that the disordered interaction renormalizes the effective light-matter coupling, lowering the critical pump strength on average, with the threshold becoming self-averaging for short speckle correlation lengths. We complement this analysis with a numerical mean-field treatment that gives access to the intracavity photon number and to the real-space fermion density across the transition. These results confirm that the disorder shifts the photonic phase boundary and, above threshold, distorts the density-wave crystal by populating Fourier components beyond those selected by the clean cavity geometry. Our findings identify both the emitted cavity light and in situ density images as probes of engineered disorder in fermionic matter coupled to optical cavities.

### [174] [Deviations beyond the Kibble-Zurek mechanism in a Spin-Orbit-Coupled Bose-Einstein Condensate with phenomenological damping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31406)
*Jun-Hang Ren,Sheng Liu,Yong-Sheng Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维自旋-轨道耦合玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（SOC-BEC）从平面波相（PW）到条纹相（ST）的淬火动力学，发现无耗散时会出现状态停滞现象；引入唯象耗散后，弱耗散下Kibble-Zurek机制（KZM）的普适标度律仍然成立，而强耗散或长淬火时间则导致显著偏离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究一维自旋-轨道耦合玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体在PW–ST相变淬火过程中的非平衡动力学行为，特别是状态停滞现象的成因，以及耗散存在时Kibble-Zurek机制（KZM）标度律的适用性。

Method: 采用含唯象耗散项的Gross-Pitaevskii方程（dissipative Gross-Pitaevskii equation）进行数值模拟，对比无耗散与有耗散情形下淬火动力学行为，并分析冻结时间（freeze-out time）和缺陷密度（defect density）的标度关系。

Result: 无耗散时，慢淬火导致系统因临界慢化（critical slowing down）引起的能隙而停滞于PW相；弱耗散下KZM的幂律标度（power-law scaling）仍保持，而强耗散或长淬火时间下出现显著偏离。

Conclusion: Kibble-Zurek机制在适当条件下仍适用于耗散量子系统，为理解开放量子系统中的非平衡动力学提供了重要启示。

Abstract: We investigate the quench dynamics in a one-dimensional spin-orbit-coupled Bose-Einstein condensate (SOC-BEC) across the phase transition from plane-wave (PW) to stripe (ST), incorporating phenomenological damping. In the dissipation-free case, a state stagnation phenomenon emerges during the PW-ST quench: for slow quenches, the system remains trapped in the PW phase due to the energy gap induced by critical slowing down, which prevents spontaneous relaxation to the stripe ground state. To explore this phenomenon and examine the universal scaling predicted by the Kibble-Zurek mechanism (KZM) in open systems, we introduce a dissipative Gross-Pitaevskii equation with a phenomenological damping term. Numerical simulations reveal that weak dissipation preserves the expected KZM power-law scaling for the freeze-out time and defect density, whereas strong dissipation or long quench times lead to significant deviations. Our results demonstrate that the KZM remains applicable in dissipative quantum systems under appropriate conditions, providing insights into nonequilibrium dynamics in open quantum systems.

### [175] [Universal scaling of many-body effects in quantum tunneling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31659)
*Hongmian Shui,Chi-Kin Lai,Chengyang Wu,Lorenzo Pizzino,Chi Zhang,Guohao Shen,Thierry Giamarchi,Hepeng Yao,Xiaoji Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用六角-三角量子模拟器，通过独立调控势垒、温度与相互作用，实验观测到多体效应在量子隧穿过程中的普适标度行为。在弱相互作用区，临界隧穿系数与温度呈抛物线标度，区别于单粒子隧穿的线性标度；当相互作用超出平均场区域时，标度指数下降，与量子场论预言一致。该工作回答了多体效应如何重整化量子隧穿这一基本问题，对关联量子物质与器件有直接启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然冷原子实验已在多粒子系综中成功模拟隧穿过程，但量子隧穿中的多体本质（many-body nature）仍很大程度上未被探索。本工作旨在实验上研究与揭示多体效应对量子隧穿（quantum tunneling）过程的重整化作用。

Method: 使用一个六角-三角量子模拟器（hexagonal-triangular quantum simulator），实现对势垒（barrier）、温度（temperature）和相互作用（interaction）的独立调控，从而研究多体隧穿的标度行为。

Result: 在弱相互作用（weak-interaction）区域，临界隧穿系数（critical tunneling coefficient）随温度呈抛物线标度（parabolic scaling），而非单粒子隧穿的线性标度（linear scaling）。当相互作用增强并超出平均场（mean-field）区域时，标度指数（scaling exponent）降低，与量子场论（quantum field theory）预言一致。

Conclusion: 该实验观察到多体效应在量子隧穿中的普适标度行为，解决了多体效应如何重整化量子隧穿这一基本问题，对关联量子物质（correlated quantum matter）及相关器件具有直接意义。

Abstract: Quantum tunneling is fundamental to diverse phenomena and underpins a wide range of modern technologies. In the study of superconducting quantum computation and high-temperature superconducting materials, tunneling on multi-particle scale is central. Recently, several cold atom experiments successfully simulated the tunneling process in a many-particle ensemble. However, the many-body nature remains largely unexplored. Here, we observe the universal scaling of many-body effects in quantum tunneling process, using a hexagonal-triangular quantum simulator with independent control of barrier, temperature and interaction. In the weak-interaction regime, the critical tunneling coefficient scales parabolically with temperature under various conditions, in contrast to the linear scaling of single-particle tunneling. By further increasing the interactions beyond the mean-field regime, the scaling exponent decreases, consistent with quantum field theory predictions. Our results address the fundamental question of how many-body effects renormalize quantum tunneling, with direct implications for correlated quantum matter and devices.

</details>


### [176] [Suppressing Parametric Instabilities in Driven Bosonic Lattices through Multi-tone Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31667)
*Robbie Cruickshank,Samuel Lellouch,Marin Bukov,Eugene Demler,Nathan Goldman,Elmar Haller*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和理论证明，在多频驱动（multi-tone driving）方案下，可以有效抑制周期性驱动量子系统中的加热和动力学不稳定性，从而稳定驱动多体系统，提升Floquet工程（Floquet engineering）的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 周期性驱动量子系统虽然能灵活调控有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）和合成能带结构（synthetic band structure），但伴随的加热和动力学不稳定性限制了多体态的相干性和寿命。本文旨在探索抑制这些不稳定性的方法。

Method: 采用两种多频驱动方案：由奇次谐波构成的脉冲驱动和具有可调振幅与相对相位的双音驱动。实验上利用光学晶格中的铯原子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）进行验证，并结合基于Bogoliubov-de Gennes方程的数值模拟与理论建模。

Result: 两种方案均可独立控制有效隧穿振幅（effective tunneling amplitude）和Peierls相位因子（Peierls phase factor），同时显著抑制声子激发（phonon excitation）及由此导致的凝聚体快速衰变。优化驱动条件下的数值模拟和理论分析确认了不稳定模式的抑制。

Conclusion: 多频驱动是稳定驱动多体系统的有效工具，为实现具有相互作用的鲁棒Floquet工程（robust Floquet engineering）奠定了基础。

Abstract: Periodically driven quantum systems offer remarkable flexibility in tailoring effective Hamiltonians and synthetic band structures. However, such driving also induces heating and dynamical instabilities that limit the coherence and lifetime of many-body states. Here, we demonstrate that these instabilities can be suppressed by employing multi-tone driving schemes. Using a Bose-Einstein condensate of cesium atoms in an optical lattice, we experimentally explore two approaches: pulsed driving composed of odd harmonics and two-tone driving with tunable amplitude and relative phase. We show that both methods allow independent control of the effective tunneling amplitude and Peierls phase factor, while significantly reducing phonon excitation and the resulting rapid decay of the condensate. Numerical simulations and theoretical modeling based on Bogoliubov-de Gennes equations confirm the suppression of unstable modes under optimized driving conditions. Our results establish multifrequency drives as powerful tools for stabilizing driven many-body systems and pave the way toward robust Floquet engineering with interactions.

</details>

### [177] [The Invariant Measure of Multiscale Markov Chains via Fast Arborescence Factorization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31596)
*Diego Alberici,Davide Gabrielli,Giulia Pallotta*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文针对具有多时间尺度跃迁的连续时间马尔可夫链（continuous-time Markov chains）族，在转移速率依赖参数 $N$ 且 $N$ 很大时出现不同时间尺度的条件下，给出了极限不变测度（invariant measure）的递归刻画。该递归由一种森林结构编码，其证明基于马尔可夫链树定理（Markov chain tree theorem）的组合表示，并利用迹过程（trace process）约化、有效动力学（effective dynamics）引入以及快速树状结构（fast arborescences）的分解等步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有多时间尺度转移行为的有限强连通马尔可夫链族，目的是在转移速率呈现不同时间尺度时，刻画其极限不变测度的结构。

Method: 基于马尔可夫链树定理给出的不变测度组合表示，通过迹过程约化链结构、引入有效动力学，并对展开式中相关树状结构进行精细分析，特别是利用快速树状结构的分解，最终建立递归刻画。

Result: 给出极限不变测度的递归表征，该递归由一种森林结构编码，该结构与近期亚稳态（metastability）动力学分析中发展的结构等价。作为副产品，还获得了加权有向图（weighted digraphs）的广义星-三角约化（generalized star-delta reduction）中树状结构的性质。

Conclusion: 本文为多时间尺度马尔可夫链的极限不变测度提供了一种递归且组合化的刻画方法，其证明框架可进一步服务于亚稳态动力学分析中的相关研究。

Abstract: We consider a family of continuous-time Markov chains with finite strongly connected transition graph and rates $\left(r_N\right)_{N>0}$ depending on a parameter $N$, so that, when $N$ is large, transitions may happen on different time scales. Under suitable general assumptions on the asymptotic behavior of the rates, we give a recursive characterization of the limiting invariant measure. The recursion is encoded in a forest structure equivalent to the one recently developed in the analysis of dynamical aspects of metastability \cite{BL,LX}.
  Our proof is based on a combinatorial representation of the invariant measure, given by the Markov chain tree theorem. Basic steps are the reduction of the chain by a trace process, the introduction of an effective dynamics, and a careful analysis of the set of relevant arborescences in the expansion. In particular we use a factorization of fast arborescences. As a byproduct we obtain properties of the arborescences of generalized star-delta reductions of weighted digraphs.

### [178] [An Enhanced RPA-LDA Model for Ion Stopping Power from Cold Matter to High-Energy Density Plasmas: A Unified, Open-Source Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30978)
*Thomas A. Mehlhorn,Ming Feng Gu,Igor Golovkin*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种增强型随机相位近似-局域密度近似（e-RPA-LDA）模型，通过引入强碰撞校正、静态局域场校正、电子束缚校正以及高阶Barkas-Bloch项，实现了从冷固体到高温稠密等离子体宽条件下离子阻止本领的准确描述，并提供了公开的代码与数据资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RPA-LDA模型在离子阻止本领的计算中尚存在不足，尤其是在大动量转移、电子关联、电子束缚效应以及高能等离子体状态下的精度有限；同时，半经验模型（如SRIM）缺乏物理基础，难以推广到极端条件。因此需要发展一种物理驱动、计算高效且适用于宽范围条件的阻止本领模型。

Method: 在平均原子（average-atom）框架下，利用柔性原子代码（Flexible Atomic Code）在 muffin-tin 势中计算电子密度，结合RPA介电响应与局域密度近似（LDA）计算电子阻止；并对 Wang 等人的早期 RPA-LDA 模型引入四项校正：强碰撞校正、静态局域场校正、电子束缚校正以及 Barkas 和 Bloch 高阶项。此外，在电子阻止基础上加入核阻止和离子弹性阻止，构成完整的阻止本领描述。

Result: 质子阻止本领与 NIST PSTAR 和 IAEA 数据库在全周期表和化合物中吻合；复现了有限的公开等离子体实验数据，包括带电粒子输运工作坊基准、含时密度泛函理论（time-dependent DFT）计算结果以及等离子体中轻离子增强阻止的首次测量。模型进一步扩展至质子和 α 粒子的完整总阻止本领。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了一种基于物理原理的替代方案，可替代 SRIM 等半经验程序，且由于平均原子方法包含所有电子贡献、计算高效、适用于任意温度与简并度下的低Z和高Z靶材，特别适合惯性聚变与高能量密度科学（high-energy-density science）研究。代码与数据已在 GitHub 上公开。

Abstract: We present an enhanced random-phase-approximation--local-density-approximation (e-RPA-LDA) model for the stopping power of ions that is valid over a wide range of conditions, from cold solids through warm dense matter to high-energy-density plasmas. The electronic stopping is computed from the RPA dielectric response in the local-density approximation over an average-atom electron density obtained in a muffin-tin potential with the Flexible Atomic Code, augmented by four corrections to the earlier RPA-LDA model of Wang et al.: a strong-collision correction for large-momentum-transfer events, a static local-field correction for electron correlations, an electron-binding correction, and the higher-order Barkas and Bloch terms. The resulting proton stopping powers agree with the NIST PSTAR and IAEA databases across the periodic table and for compounds -- providing a physics-based alternative to semi-empirical codes such as SRIM -- and reproduce the limited published plasma data, including charged-particle transport-workshop benchmarks, time-dependent DFT calculations, and the first measurements of enhanced light-ion stopping in plasmas. We further extend the model to a complete total stopping power for protons and alpha particles by adding nuclear and ionic (elastic ion-ion) stopping to the electronic term, yielding a continuous, self-consistent description of energy deposition from cold matter to hot dense plasmas. Because the average-atom treatment includes contributions from all electrons -- unlike Kohn-Sham DFT -- while remaining computationally efficient and applicable to low- and high-Z targets at arbitrary temperature and degeneracy, the model is well suited to inertial fusion and high-energy-density science. The computational framework is available on GitHub (https://github.com/dedx-erpa/dedx), with tabulated stopping powers and ranges in the data/ subdirectory.

</details>

# math.SP [[Back]](#toc)

### [179] [Capacity and measure approximations for Schrödinger operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31051)
*Burak Hatinoğlu,Svetlana Jitomirskaya*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文证明了在零李雅普诺夫指数区间下，拟周期薛定谔算子的相并谱（phase-union spectra）的对数容量（logarithmic capacity）收敛性具有鲁棒性，仅需势函数连续即可成立。同时将结果推广到多频率薛定谔算子和一般遍历薛定谔算子框架，并给出了在极限频率为有理数时的反例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究拟周期薛定谔算子在零李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）区间下，相并谱的对数容量收敛性是否具有鲁棒性，并探索该收敛性成立所需的最小条件。

Method: 通过仅要求势函数（potential）连续来证明对数容量收敛；利用有理频率下的相并谱 $S^+(p/q)$ 逼近无理频率下的谱 $Σ(α)$，并分析其对数容量与调和测度（harmonic measure）的极限行为；将结果推广至多频率薛定谔算子和一般遍历薛定谔算子（ergodic Schrödinger operator）框架，其中几乎必然谱（almost sure spectrum）在豪斯多夫度量（Hausdorff metric）下被周期算子的并谱逼近。

Result: 证明了若在无理频率 $\alpha$ 下李雅普诺夫指数在谱上为零，则对任意 $p_n/q_n\to\alpha$，对数容量 $Cap(S^+(p_n/q_n))\to Cap(Σ(\alpha))$，且相应的调和测度收敛。平衡测度（equilibrium measure）在弱星拓扑（weak$^*$ topology）下收敛到密度依赖于状态测度（density of states measure）。该结果可推广至多频率及一般遍历薛定谔算子，并给出了极限频率为有理数时不成立的反例。

Conclusion: 对数容量收敛在零李雅普诺夫指数区间下具有鲁棒性，势函数连续是充分条件；该结论在更广泛的遍历薛定谔算子框架下仍成立，但有理频率极限情况下会出现反例，表明无理频率条件不可或缺。

Abstract: We prove that logarithmic capacity convergence for phase-union spectra of quasi-periodic Schrödinger operators in the zero Lyapunov exponent regime is robust, requiring only continuity of the potential. Let $S^+(p/q)$ denote the union, over the phase, of the spectra at rational frequency $p/q$. We show that if the Lyapunov exponent vanishes on the spectrum $Σ(α)$ at an irrational frequency $α$, then for every sequence $p_n/q_n\toα$, the logarithmic capacities $Cap(S^+(p_n/q_n))\longrightarrow Cap(Σ(α)).$ We also prove convergence of the corresponding harmonic measures.
  As a consequence, the equilibrium measures of $S^+(p_n/q_n)$ converge in the weak$^*$ topology to the density of states measure of the quasi-periodic Schrödinger operator. We extend these results to multi-frequency Schrödinger operators and prove analogous convergence theorems, for logarithmic capacity, harmonic measure, and equilibrium measure, for ergodic Schrödinger operators in a general setting where the almost sure spectrum is approximated in the Hausdorff metric by union spectra of periodic operators. This abstract formulation applies, in particular, to uniformly almost periodic potentials along sequences of almost periods. We also provide counterexamples when the limiting frequency is rational.

</details>

### [180] [Fully compensated ferrimagnetic triferroics and multistate transport in hidden-phase wurtzite MnSe monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31419)
*Zhuang Ma,Hongfei Liang,Po Ma,Guangqian Ding,Xuehao Wu,Sikander Azam,Guoying Gao,Long Zhang*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过从纤锌矿(001)面提取的隐藏相MnSe单层，发现了一种本征的全补偿铁磁体(fFIM)单层，该材料同时具有单极磁半导体(UMS)特性和铁电性、铁弹性，构成三铁性体系，并在隧道结中展现出巨大的隧穿磁电阻、电电阻和弹电阻效应，为超高密度低功耗存储器件提供了平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知的全补偿铁磁体(fFIM)大多局限于复杂的三维(3D)体系，或需要在二维(2D)异质结构中施加外场，本征的fFIM单层尚未得到探索。因此，寻找并研究本征二维fFIM材料具有重要的基础与应用意义。

Method: 从纤锌矿(wurtzite)的(001)面提取出一种隐藏相(hidden-phase)的MnSe单层，通过第一性原理计算分析其电子结构、磁性与铁性序的共存特性，并构建In2Se3/MnSe异质结和隧道结(tunnel junction)进行电学调控与输运性能研究。

Conclusion: 该自发形成的二维fFIM与三铁性序共存，为超高密度、低功耗和小型化存储器件提供了有前景的材料平台。

Abstract: Fully compensated ferrimagnets (fFIMs) have attracted interest due to their compensated moments and nonrelativistic spin splitting across the Brillouin zone. Known fFIMs, however, are mostly restricted to complex three-dimensional (3D) systems or require external fields in two-dimensional (2D) heterostructures, leaving intrinsic fFIM monolayers unexplored. We identify a hidden-phase MnSe monolayer, derived from the (001) planes of wurtzite, as an intrinsic fFIM featuring inequivalent sublattices not linked by any symmetry. It is a unipolar magnetic semiconductor (UMS) with perpendicular magnetic anisotropy (528.60 * 10^-3 eV per unit cell) and simultaneously exhibits ferroelectricity (polarization 4.63 * 10^-10 C/m) and ferroelasticity (signal 61%), with barriers of 7.6 * 10^-3 and 0.10 eV/f.u., respectively, establishing a single-phase triferroic system. The ground fFIM UMS characteristics are robust against strain up to 3%. The In2Se3/MnSe heterostructure enables nonvolatile electrical control between semiconducting and metallic states. Constructed tunnel junctions exhibit giant tunneling magnetoresistance (2.98 * 10^5%), electroresistance (6.97 * 10^14%), elastoresistance (7.95 * 10^4%), and near-perfect spin filtering (~100%). Collectively, this spontaneous 2D fFIM with coexisting triferroic orders provides a promising platform for ultrahigh-density, low-power, and miniaturized memory devices.

### [181] [Log Conifold Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31072)
*Rodolfo Aguilar*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究指数为二的Fano三维流形对（Fano threefold pairs）的对数锥形过渡（log conifold transitions），利用相对Clemens猜想的近期成果构造法丛为$\OO(-1)\oplus\OO(-1)$的有理曲线，并证明节点局部光滑可提升为全局一阶形变且形变理论无条件无阻碍，从而构造出新的非Kähler三维流形并分析其有效几何与Hodge理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在指数为二的Fano三维流形对上定义并研究对数锥形过渡（log conifold transitions），这是对经典Calabi-Yau情形中锥形过渡的推广，旨在利用Fano几何特有的无阻碍性（unobstructedness）构造新的非Kähler三维流形（non-Kähler threefolds）。

Method: 在边界除子上爆破锚定点（anchored points）构造法丛为$\OO(-1)\oplus\OO(-1)$的有理曲线，将其收缩得到具有通常二重点（ordinary double points）的奇异空间；证明节点局部光滑可提升为全局一阶形变，并利用边界del Pezzo曲面的几何保证形变理论无条件无阻碍；利用Fano几何迫使全局拓扑平衡条件（global topological balancing conditions）消失，使得节点局部一阶光滑可独立提升。

Result: 建立了指数为二的Fano三维流形对的对数锥形过渡的形变理论，构造了新的非Kähler三维流形，确定了其Picard群（Picard groups），证明了自由曲线（free curves）的持续性，并研究了这些非Kähler三维流形的Hodge理论（Hodge theory）。

Conclusion: Fano几何的边界del Pezzo曲面结构保证了形变理论的无条件无阻碍性，且与Calabi-Yau情形不同，拓扑平衡条件的消失允许节点光滑独立提升，为构造和研究非Kähler三维流形提供了新途径。

Abstract: We define log conifold transitions for Fano threefold pairs of index two and study their deformation theory. Relying on the recent solution to the relative Clemens conjectures in this setting, we construct rational curves with normal bundle $\OO(-1)\oplus \OO(-1)$ by blowing up anchored points on the boundary divisor. Contracting these curves yields a singular space with ordinary double points. We prove that local smoothings of the nodes can be lifted to global first-order deformations, and that the global deformation theory of both the log resolution space and the singular log pair is unconditionally unobstructed. Crucially, the geometry of the boundary del Pezzo surface guarantees this unobstructedness. Furthermore, unlike the classical Calabi-Yau case, the underlying Fano geometry forces the vanishing of global topological balancing conditions, allowing local first-order smoothings of the nodes to be lifted independently.
  As applications, we construct new non-Kähler threefolds via smoothings, we analyze the effective geometry of the smoothed threefolds by determining their Picard groups and proving the persistence of free curves. Finally, we study the Hodge theory of these non-Kähler threefolds.

### [182] [A Coherence Law for Trainability in Noisy Equivariant Quantum Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30688)
*Hassan Ugail,Newton Howard*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了等变量子电路中梯度在噪声下存活的决定性物理量——读出可见的扇区相干性（readout-visible sector coherence），并推导出一个紧凑的训练定律来预测梯度衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称性（symmetry）虽然能为量子神经网络提供结构，但一旦存在噪声，它本身无法保证网络的可训练性（trainability）。因此需要明确何种物理量决定等变电路（equivariant circuit）的梯度能否在退相干（decoherence）下幸存。

Method: 研究对象为U(1)-等变的砖墙电路（brickwork circuits），该电路守恒一个电荷。通过因果性（causality）将梯度限制在读出算符的向后光锥（backward light cone）内，并通过相干性（coherence）描述梯度沿离对角扇区模式（off-diagonal sector modes）的衰减。定义读出可见对齐相干速率（readout-visible aligned coherence rate）作为噪声生成元沿梯度承载模式的瑞利商（Rayleigh quotient），并通过微扰开系统分析（perturbative open-system analysis）将其转化为低阶训练定律。最后用密度矩阵模拟（density-matrix simulations）验证。

Result: 证明了无噪声梯度被限制在扇区约束光锥内，且下界与总量子比特数无关；噪声下的梯度退化服从由噪声深度和相干收缩构建的单一累积变量，决定系数达0.979。针对相关退极化信道（correlated-dephasing channel），该定律预测无梯度损失，模拟结果证实了此预测。

Conclusion: 扇区相干性（sector coherence）优于所有标准的信道诊断指标；读出可见的扇区相干性是连接等变架构（equivariant architecture）、开系统动力学（open-system dynamics）和噪声可训练性（noisy trainability）的关键量。

Abstract: Symmetry provides a quantum neural network structure, but on its own it does not keep the network trainable once noise is present. We ask which physical quantity decides whether the gradients of an equivariant circuit survive decoherence, and we answer with a compact training law. Working with U(1)-equivariant brickwork circuits that conserve a charge, we find that two distinct effects govern a trainable gradient. Causality fixes where the gradient can live, confining it to the backward light cone of the readout inside the active charge sector. Coherence then determines how fast it decays through the contraction of the off-diagonal sector modes that the projected readout can actually observe. We prove a light-cone reduction that pins the noiseless gradient to the sector-restricted cone with a lower bound independent of the total qubit number, and we define a readout-visible aligned coherence rate as a Rayleigh quotient of the noise generator along the gradient-carrying mode. A perturbative open-system analysis turns this rate into a leading-order training law. Density-matrix simulations then confirm that the finite-noise degradation follows a single accumulated variable built from noise depth and coherence contraction, with a coefficient of determination of 0.979. The sharpest test comes from a correlated-dephasing channel that has a large worst-case rate but a near-zero aligned rate. The law predicts no gradient loss for this channel, and none is seen. Sector coherence outperforms every standard channel diagnostic we compare it against, and the analysis identifies readout-visible sector coherence as the quantity that links equivariant architecture, open-system dynamics and noisy trainability.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文推导了纯量子态子系统的冯·诺依曼熵（von Neumann entropy）所有幂矩（power moments）的简洁封闭表达式，采用舒尔-外尔对偶（Schur-Weyl duality）与对称群 $S_N$ 的示性理论（character theory）方法，而非传统的随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）与拉盖尔多项式（Laguerre polynomials）路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在均匀分布的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）中随机抽取纯态，计算其子系统的冯·诺依曼熵（即纠缠熵，entanglement entropy）的统计性质，是量子信息与多体物理中的基础问题。现有方法多依赖随机矩阵理论与拉盖尔多项式，本文旨在提供一种不同的、自洽的推导方案。

Method: 利用舒尔-外尔对偶（Schur-Weyl duality）以及对称群 $S_N$ 的示性理论（character theory）导出熵的所有幂矩（power moments）的封闭表达式；通过简单微分即可从幂矩获得熵的各阶矩（moments of the entropy）。论文提供了完整的数学背景，力求自成体系。

Result: 得到了子系统冯·诺依曼熵所有幂矩的简洁封闭表达式，并表明熵的各阶矩可通过微分从这些幂矩中直接计算。

Conclusion: 本文为随机纯量子态子系统的纠缠熵统计提供了不同于随机矩阵理论的新解析途径，且数学上自洽完整。

Abstract: We revisit the calculation of the von Neumann (or "entanglement") entropy of a subsystem of a pure quantum state, under the assumption that the latter is drawn at random from a uniform distribution on the full Hilbert space. We derive simple and closed expressions for all power moments, from which the moments of the entropy can be computed by simple differentiation. Our approach (different from the usual one based on random matrix theory and Laguerre polynomials) makes use of Schur-Weyl duality and the character theory of the symmetric group $S_N$ . The paper is self-contained, providing all the necessary mathematical background.

### [184] [Cumulant-based quantum relative Rényi functional](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31205)
*Atirat Meunson,Tanapat Deesuwan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于累积量生成函数（CGF）的量子相对Rényi泛函，作为候选的量子Rényi散度，并将其与经典统计累积量之间的联系推广到量子领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子Rényi散度（如Petz散度和夹层量子Rényi散度）主要基于算子代数或操作原理构建，缺乏统计结构层面的动机。该工作旨在引入一种具有统计基础的新构造。

Method: 从量子相对惊奇算子的累积量生成函数（CGF）出发，通过Lie-Trotter乘积展开得到路径积分形式的表示，并在支撑条件$\operatorname{supp}(ρ)\subseteq\operatorname{supp}(σ)$下定义其自然非正则化域（$α>1$）及正则化版本。

Result: 在非正则化域上证明了正性、约化到经典情形、可加性、幺正不变性、连续性和关于Rényi参数$α$的单调性。正则化版本在$α=0$时定义了相对量子性（relative quantumness）量，该量为零当且仅当两态对易。数值模拟支持对易保持信道（CoP）下的QDPI型单调性猜想。

Conclusion: 所提泛函为量子Rényi散度提供了新的统计构造途径，并给出了非对易性的充要刻画；但一般CPTP映射下的量子数据处理不等式（QDPI）是否成立仍为开放问题。

Abstract: We introduce a new cumulant-based quantum relative Rényi functional as a candidate quantum Rényi divergence, derived from the cumulant-generating function (CGF) of the quantum relative surprisal operator and extending the classical connection between Rényi divergence and statistical cumulants to the quantum setting. Unlike the Petz and sandwiched quantum Rényi divergences, the proposed construction is motivated by statistical structure rather than operator-algebraic or operational principles. The functional naturally admits a path-integral-like representation through the Lie-Trotter product expansion, providing a trajectory-based interpretation of quantum divergence in Hilbert space. On its natural non-regularized domain for $α>1$ under the support condition $\operatorname{supp}(ρ)\subseteq\operatorname{supp}(σ)$, we establish several fundamental properties, including positivity, reduction to the classical case, additivity, unitary invariance, continuity, and monotonicity with respect to the Renyi parameter $α$. Whether the functional satisfies the quantum data-processing inequality (QDPI) under arbitrary CPTP maps remains open. To extend the analysis beyond the studied regime, we introduce a regularized version of the functional and study its behavior at $α=0$. We show that the resulting relative quantumness quantity vanishes if and only if the underlying states commute, yielding a necessary and sufficient characterization of non-commutativity. For commutativity-preserving (CoP) channels, we further conjecture a QDPI-type monotonicity relation for this quantity. Extensive numerical simulations provide strong evidence in support of this conjecture, with no violations observed for the CoP channels considered in this work.

</details>


### [185] [Projection Operator Stochastic Equations for Non-Markovian Quantum Systems Under Continuous Measurement-Based Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31321)
*H. I. Nurdin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将投影算符方法（projection operator approach）推广至包含随机反馈（stochastic feedback）的连续测量非马尔可夫量子系统（continuously measured non-Markovian quantum systems），导出了投影态随机微分方程（stochastic differential equations, SDEs），并证明其形式与无反馈情形一致，但确定性项变为依赖于测量记录的随机项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子马尔可夫假设（quantum Markov assumption）在一般量子系统中不成立，而现有投影算符方法虽能处理非马尔可夫效应（non-Markovian effects），但仅限于无反馈的开环控制（open-loop control）场景。本文旨在将该方法推广至包含测量反馈（measurement-based feedback）的情形，以拓展其适用范围。

Method: 在连续测量的非马尔可夫量子系统中，引入基于连续测量记录的随机反馈（stochastic feedback），将投影算符方法推广至反馈控制场景，推导出投影态所满足的随机微分方程（SDEs）。该推导覆盖了一类广义测量类型，包括连续（可自适应）零差测量（homodyne measurement）和光子计数测量（photon counting measurement）。

Result: 推导出的随机微分方程与无反馈情形具有相同的形式，但原本确定性的项变为依赖于测量记录的随机项，符合物理直觉。该结果对于包含连续（可自适应）零差测量和光子计数测量的广义测量类均成立。

Conclusion: 本文成功将投影算符方法从非马尔可夫量子系统的无反馈开环控制扩展至含随机反馈的闭环控制场景，为建模更一般的非马尔可夫量子反馈控制系统提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Quantum Markov models have been successfully used to accurately model various physical quantum systems in fields such as quantum optics, optomechanics and superconducting circuits and they provide the basis for (measurement-based) quantum feedback control. However, the quantum Markov assumption is a strong one and it is not expected to hold for general quantum systems of interest. The projection operator approach is one approach that has been developed to model non-Markovian quantum systems by considering its embedding in a larger Markovian quantum system, but mainly in the context of quantum master equations for the dynamics of the unmonitored reduced quantum state of a quantum system. This approach was recently adapted for continuously measured non-Markovian quantum systems, which enables open-loop control but did not yet consider the presence of feedback of the stochastic measurement record, deriving non-Markovian SDEs for the evolution of the projected state of the Markovian embedding. This paper generalizes these stochastic equations to the setting of stochastic feedback based on the continuous-measurement record and shows that the equations take the same form but that previously deterministic terms become stochastic ones which depend on the measurement record, as would be intuitively expected. The stochastic equations are obtained for a generalized class of measurements that includes continuous (possibly adaptive) homodyne and photon counting measurements.

</details>


### [186] [Wave-particle duality as an uncertainty relation for the average confidence width](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31443)
*Shengjun Wu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入平均置信宽度（average confidence width）Δ_a x 作为位置不确定性的新度量，证明了 Δ_a x Δ_a p ≥ c ħ 的不确定性关系，并指出该不等式同时刻画了波粒二象性（wave-particle duality）的上界。通过平均熵论证与傅里叶不变算子 |x|+|p| 的基态分析，给出了最优常数 c* 的严格界限 π/e ≤ c* ≤ E_0² < 4/π，表明最优态为亚高斯态（sub-Gaussian），而非传统的高斯态（Gaussian）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有不确定性原理（uncertainty principle）的表述（如海森堡关系和熵关系）以高斯态（Gaussian）为最优，但其是否在波粒二象性（wave-particle duality）的统一框架下同样最优尚不清楚。本文旨在引入一种新的位置-动量联合度量，以统一描述不确定性与波粒二象性，并寻找真正的最优量子态。

Method: 定义平均置信宽度 Δ_a x 为置信宽度（confidence width）Δ_c x(θ_x) 在置信水平 θ_x 上的积分，并证明其等价于 |ψ|² 的递减重排（decreasing rearrangement）的一阶矩，即 L¹ 平均绝对偏差（mean-absolute-deviation）。利用该量的膨胀不变性（dilation invariance）推导 Δ_a x Δ_a p ≥ c ħ。采用基于 Bialynicki-Birula-Mycielski 关系的平均熵（mean-entropy）论证得到 c ≥ π/e，并通过傅里叶不变算子（Fourier-invariant operator）|x|+|p| 的基态（ground state）数值计算给出可达常数 c* ≤ E_0²。

Result: 建立了新的不确定性不等式 Δ_a x Δ_a p ≥ c ħ，其下界同时对应波粒二象性的上界：1/Δ_a x 作为粒子性（particle character）度量，1/Δ_a p 作为波动性（wave character）度量。最优常数 c* 满足 π/e ≤ c* ≤ E_0² ≈ 1.217，且 E_0² < 4/π，表明最优态为亚高斯态（sub-Gaussian），而非海森堡关系和熵关系中的最优高斯态。

Conclusion: 不确定性与波粒二象性（uncertainty and wave-particle duality）是同一不等式的两个面。在平均置信宽度的框架下，最优量子态是亚高斯态（sub-Gaussian），而非高斯态（Gaussian），后者并非波粒二象性意义上的最优态。

Abstract: We introduce the average confidence width $Δ_a x=\int_0^1 Δ_c x (θ_x) d θ_x$: the confidence width $Δ_c x(θ_x)$ -- the smallest position interval carrying a fraction $θ_x$ of the probability -- averaged over all levels. It is the first moment of the decreasing rearrangement of $|ψ|^2$, an $L^1$ mean-absolute-deviation measure of localization, so the product $Δ_{a} x\,Δ_{a} p$ is dilation invariant and obeys $Δ_{a} x\,Δ_{a} p\ge c\,\hbar$. Reading $1/Δ_{a} x$ as a particle character and $1/Δ_{a} p$ as a wave character, this lower bound on combined spread is identically an upper bound on combined particle-and-wave character: uncertainty and wave-particle duality are two faces of one inequality. A mean-entropy argument with the Bialynicki-Birula-Mycielski relation gives the rigorous $c\geπ/e$, while the achievable constant $c^\ast$ is set by the ground state of the Fourier-invariant operator $|x|+|p|$, $c^\ast\le E_0^2\approx 1.217$. Hence $π/e\le c^\ast\le E_0^2<4/π$: the optimal state is sub-Gaussian, so the Gaussian -- optimal for the Heisenberg and entropic relations -- is not the duality optimum.

</details>


### [187] [The contact temperature of arbitrary quantum states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31969)
*Alain Joye,Marco Merkli*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通用量子温度计模型，通过分析系统与温度计耦合时的热流行为，为任意量子态定义唯一的接触温度（contact temperature）β_op，该温度来源于热流消失的唯一逆温度参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为量子系统的任意状态赋予一个直觉性的温度定义，即通过观察与温度计耦合时的热流方向来确定温度。

Method: 引入一种通用温度计模型，该温度计事先制备在吉布斯平衡态（Gibbs equilibrium state），逆温度为β；将其与任意态的系统进行热接触，通过求解热流为零的条件得到唯一的逆温度β_op，定义为系统的接触温度（contact temperature）。

Result: 该通用温度计对于任意有限维量子系统的任意状态，均能给出唯一的接触温度β_op ∈ ℝ。

Conclusion: 该通用温度计模型为任意量子态提供了基于热流机制的唯一定温方案，有望用于非平衡量子系统的温度定义与测量。

Abstract: An intuitive scheme to assign a temperature to an arbitrary state of a quantum system is to investigate the heat flow resulting from the coupling to a thermometer. We introduce a simple model of a universal thermometer with the following property. When it is prepared in a Gibbs equilibrium state at inverse temperature $β\in\mathbb R$ and brought into thermal contact with a system in any state, the heat flow between the system and thermometer vanishes for a unique value of $β$. We call this value the contact temperature $β_{\rm op}\in\mathbb R$ of the system state. The thermometer is universal in that it yields a unique contact temperature for arbitrary states of finite dimensional quantum systems.

</details>


### [188] [Relativistic Gravity-Induced Entanglement via Frame Dragging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31678)
*Eyuri Wakakuwa,Luciano Petruzziello,Trinidad B. Lantaño,Susana F. Huelga,Martin B. Plenio*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了由参考系拖曳效应（frame dragging）产生的引力诱导纠缠（gravity-induced entanglement），在干涉仪设置中通过两种互补方法计算纠缠相位，并指出该纠缠在标准局域性/媒介子假设下可作为引力相互作用非经典性的见证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于引力诱导纠缠检验引力非经典性的方案大多局限于牛顿极限（Newtonian limit），而涉及真正后牛顿（post-Newtonian）特征的参考系拖曳效应尚未被充分探索。

Method: 在干涉仪设置中，通过两种互补方式计算纠缠相位：(i) 在大角动量极限下，用量化的Lense-Thirring哈密顿量（quantized Lense-Thirring Hamiltonian）进行薛定谔演化；(ii) 在稳相近似（stationary phase approximation）下，通过线性化量子引力（linearized quantum gravity）的在壳作用量（on-shell action）进行路径积分推导。

Result: 两种方法得到了相同的纠缠相位，该相位与干涉仪两臂之间的固有时差（proper time difference）一致。路径积分推导进一步揭示了引力推迟效应（gravitational retardation）如何修正纠缠相位，使得局域的、相对论因果的线性化引力描述得以显式化。

Conclusion: 在现有论证中使用的标准局域性/媒介子假设下，由参考系拖曳产生的纠缠将见证引力相互作用的非经典性（non-classicality），为桌面实验检验引力的后牛顿非经典特征提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: Gravity-induced entanglement has been proposed as a method for testing the non-classical nature of gravity via tabletop experiments. While most existing proposals are restricted to the Newtonian limit, the frame dragging effect offers access to genuinely post-Newtonian features of the gravitational interaction and remains comparatively less explored. Here, we study gravity-induced entanglement generated by frame dragging in an interferometric setting and compute the entanglement phase between the rotational degrees of freedom of a source mass and the paths of a particle in two complementary ways: (i) via Schrödinger evolution with a quantized Lense-Thirring Hamiltonian in the large angular momentum limit, and (ii) via the on-shell action of linearized quantum gravity within the stationary phase approximation. Both approaches yield the same entanglement phase, consistent with the proper time difference between the interferometer arms. The path integral derivation further reveals how gravitational retardation modifies the entanglement phase, thereby making the local, relativistically causal linearized-gravity description explicit. Under the standard locality/mediator assumptions used in existing arguments, the resulting entanglement would witness non-classicality of the gravitational interaction.

</details>


### [189] [Controlling the non-Markovianity of quantum Brownian motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30730)
*Guglielmo Pellitteri,Vittorio Giovannetti,Vasco Cavina*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子布朗运动（quantum Brownian motion）是研究开放量子系统（open quantum systems）动力学的重要模型。理解并量化其非马尔可夫性，并探究如何通过调节系统-环境相互作用通道来实现对非马尔可夫性的控制，对于量子信息处理和量子热力学等领域具有关键意义。

Method: 采用高斯主方程（Gaussian master equation）方法分析模型的精确动力学；利用Gorini--Kossakowski--Sudarshan--Lindblad（GKSL）定理以及基于信息回流（information backflow）的定量度量来形式化刻画非马尔可夫性（non-Markovianity）。

Result: 通过调制特定相互作用通道的相对权重，可以实现对系统非马尔可夫性的精准控制，并诱导系统从非马尔可夫动力学到马尔可夫（Markovian）动力学的过渡。

Conclusion: 本研究阐明了广义量子布朗运动模型现象背后的物理机制，并由此为通过策略性调谐耗散通道（dissipation channels）来进行环境工程（environment engineering）提供了一个系统化的理论平台。

Abstract: We analyze the exact dynamics of a generalized quantum Brownian motion model, employing Gaussian master equation methods. We demonstrate that, by modulating the relative weights of specific interaction channels, we can control the degree of non-Markovianity of the system, and induce a transition from non-Markovian to Markovian regimes. The non-Markovianity of the evolution is formally characterized by leveraging the Gorini--Kossakowski--Sudarshan--Lindblad theorem and by employing quantitative measures of information backflow. Finally, we clarify the physical mechanism behind the phenomenology of this model, thereby providing a systematic platform for environment engineering through the strategic tuning of dissipation channels.

</details>


### [190] [Disorder-Induced Enhancement of Fermionic Superradiance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30735)
*David Pascual Solis,Andrea Legramandi,Soumik Bandyopadhyay,Philipp Hauke*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究费米子-光腔耦合系统中无序（disorder）对超辐射（superradiance）相变的影响，发现无序可以促进而非抑制集体光-物质行为，并产生一种由多个灰色费米子态参与的集体相干新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在传统的集体光-物质现象（如Dicke超辐射）中，通常假设自旋与玻色模（bosonic mode）均匀耦合，形成单一的亮模（bright mode）。然而在费米子系统中，泡利不相容原理（Pauli exclusion）和费米面结构会显著改变这一图像；同时，原子-光耦合中的随机性提出了一个关键问题：无序（disorder）是促进还是抑制集体行为？本文旨在系统研究这一机制。

Method: 作者构建了一个费米子-光腔模型，其中费米子通过一个可调均值和方差的随机全对全（all-to-all）相互作用矩阵与光子模耦合。采用了数值平均场方法（mean-field methods）、解析稳定性分析（stability analysis）和随机矩阵理论（random-matrix theory）预测，并辅以精确对角化（exact diagonalization）进行基准验证。

Result: 平均耦合与无序方差在超辐射相变起始点上的贡献相同，但在凝聚相（condensed phase）内部的行为截然不同：均匀耦合支持单个亮费米子模，呈现Dicke型标度行为（scaling）；而无序则产生一种新的集体机制，多个灰色费米子态（grey fermionic states）相干参与，导致凝聚体的标度随系统尺寸呈参数性增强（parametrically enhanced scaling）。

Conclusion: 无序可以出乎意料地促进集体光-物质现象，揭示了一种反直觉的机制：在费米子-光腔系统中，随机性通过激发多个灰色费米子态参与相干过程，增强了超辐射凝聚体的集体行为。

Abstract: Collective light-matter phenomena such as Dicke superradiance are often described as a collection of effective spins coupled homogeneously to a bosonic mode, giving rise to a collective bright mode with enhanced light-matter coupling. In fermionic systems, Pauli exclusion and Fermi-surface structure can significantly modify this picture, while randomness in the atom-light couplings raises the question of whether disorder promotes or suppresses collective behavior. Here, we study a cavity model in which fermionic particles couple to a photonic mode through a random all-to-all interaction matrix with tunable mean and variance. Combining numerical mean-field methods, analytic stability analysis and random-matrix predictions, and benchmarks against exact diagonalization, we characterize both the onset and structure of the superradiant phase. While mean coupling and disorder variance contribute in the same way to the onset, they lead to drastically different behavior within the condensed phase. Uniform coupling supports a single bright collective fermionic mode with conventional Dicke-like scaling of the cavity field. Disorder, instead, gives rise to a qualitatively different collective regime in which many grey fermionic states participate coherently, producing a parametrically enhanced scaling of the condensate with system size. Our results reveal a mechanism through which disorder can, perhaps counterintuitively, promote collective light-matter phenomena.

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种利用扩散模型（diffusion model）对具有连续对称性的自旋系统进行可扩展采样的新技术。将该方法应用于XY模型，证明温度条件化的扩散模型在较小晶格上训练后，能够为更大晶格生成准确的样本。结合少量马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）步骤，可将热化时间（thermalization time）降低一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法在面对不同系统大小时难以泛化，且热化过程耗时较长。文章旨在利用生成模型解决连续自旋系统在大尺度下的高效采样问题。

Method: 训练一个温度条件化的扩散模型（temperature-conditioned diffusion model），在小尺寸XY模型晶格上进行训练，随后将其用于生成更大晶格的样本。采样后仅需少量MCMC步骤即可达到平衡。

Result: 实验表明，扩散采样结合少量MCMC步骤，相比随机初始化的标准MCMC，可将热化时间降低一个数量级。生成的样本在自旋关联（spin correlations）等关键物理可观测量上保持准确性。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了生成模型（尤其是扩散模型）在可扩展采样连续态凝聚态系统（continuous-state condensed matter systems）中的潜力，为大规模系统的高效蒙特卡洛模拟提供了新思路。

Abstract: We introduce a novel technique for scalable sampling of spin-system states with continuous symmetries using diffusion models. By applying our approach to the XY model, a fundamental continuous-spin model in condensed matter physics, we show that our technique addresses the shortfalls of the Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) in generalization to varying system sizes. More specifically, we show that training a temperature-conditioned diffusion model on smaller-size XY model lattices enables the generation of accurate samples in larger lattice sizes. By tracking physically important observables of the model, such as spin correlations, our experiments demonstrate that diffusion sampling followed by a few MCMC steps reduces the thermalization time by an order of magnitude relative to the standard MCMC with random initialization. Our study provides valuable insight as to how generative models can be used to study continuous-state condensed matter systems at scale.

</details>


### [192] [Overcoming Configuration Bottleneck: Modular Pathways to Stable Semiconductor Spin-Qubit Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30883)
*Justyna P. Zwolak,Anthony Sigillito*

TL;DR: 本文从自动化视角将半导体自旋量子比特（semiconductor spin qubit）操作重构为模块化工作流，涵盖从初始启动到漂移感知维护的五个模块，并论证规模化运行需依赖标准化接口、中间数据产品及工作流级指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过去十年半导体自旋量子比特已从少数量子比特演示发展到大规模器件制备，核心挑战已从在精心调谐的器件中实现高保真度操作，转向在多种相互依赖的控制参数、器件几何结构和材料平台上可靠地发现、验证并维持稳定工作条件。

Method: 将自旋量子比特操作视为模块化自动化问题，将其工作流分解为五个模块：基于最小先验信息的启动（bootstrapping）、配置调谐（configuration tuning）、物理门虚拟化为有效控制轴（virtualization）、量子比特级调谐（qubit-level tuning），以及包含漂移感知维护的操作层（operation layer）。

Result: 基于自身和更广泛社区的研究，指出规模化将依赖于模块间的显式接口、标准化中间数据产品，以及工作流级指标，包括吞吐量（throughput）、成功概率（success probability）、稳定时间（stability time）、恢复时间（recovery time）和鲁棒性（robustness）。

Conclusion: 未来需要超越孤立的调谐演示，转向持续运行的基础设施建设，具体包括：量子比特性能感知反馈、可复用软件与基准测试任务，以及实验、理论与软件团队之间的紧密协作。

Abstract: Over the past decade, semiconductor spin qubits have progressed from few-qubit demonstrations towards larger-scale devices fabricated in increasingly reproducible academic and industrial processes. This progress marks an inflection point: the central challenge is no longer to demonstrate high-fidelity operation in carefully tuned devices, but to discover, verify, and maintain stable operating conditions reliably across many interdependent controls, varied device geometries, and disparate material platforms. In this Perspective, we frame spin-qubit operation as a modular automation problem. We decompose the workflow into five modules: bootstrapping from minimal prior information, configuration tuning, virtualization of physical gates into effective control axes, qubit-level tuning, and an operation layer with drift-aware maintenance. Using recent demonstrations from our work and the broader community, we argue that scalability will depend on explicit interfaces between modules, standardized intermediate data products, and workflow-level metrics such as throughput, success probability, stability time, recovery time, and robustness. We close by outlining the infrastructure needed to move beyond isolated tuning demonstrations toward sustained operation: qubit-performance-aware feedback, reusable software and benchmark tasks, and tight collaboration among experimental, theoretical, and software efforts.

### [193] [Atom diffraction in the strong-coupling regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31183)
*Carina Kanitz,Jakob Bühler,François Aguillon,Vladimír Zobač,Jaime Glerum,Toma Susi,Maxime Debiossac,Philippe Roncin,Christian Brand*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和模拟表明，在千电子伏特能量下氦原子通过单层石墨烯衍射时，传统基于微扰理论的Debye-Waller因子不再适用，进入了一种新的强耦合（strong coupling）区域；而氢原子衍射仍保持弱耦合（weak coupling）区域，并提出了与耦合强度无关的描述方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于物质波衍射的解析方法是凝聚态研究的基石，传统上认为衍射图案主要由平衡态晶格决定，而振动引起的畸变可通过微扰（perturbative）处理。本文旨在检验该微扰方法在千电子伏特能量下氦原子通过单层石墨烯衍射时的适用性。

Method: 实验上测量了氦原子和氢原子在千电子伏特能量下通过独立单层石墨烯的衍射图案；同时进行数值模拟，并结合实验结果与模拟，建立了一个与耦合强度无关（regime-independent）的描述框架。

Result: 发现氦原子衍射进入强耦合区域，射弹同时与多个晶格原子的电子密度强相互作用，导致相移（phase shift）达数个弧度，晶格畸变带来的相位散布无法用Debye-Waller因子描述。氢原子衍射则仍保留弱耦合区域特征。

Conclusion: 传统的微扰Debye-Waller处理在高能原子-石墨烯衍射中失效，存在一个强耦合新区域；通过模拟提出了一个与耦合强度无关的方法，可普遍描述声子对原子衍射现象的影响。

Abstract: Analytic methods based on matter-wave diffraction are a cornerstone in condensed-matter research, providing access to static and dynamic materials properties down to the atomic level. In these experiments, the shape of the diffraction pattern is largely determined by the lattice at equilibrium whereas vibrationally-induced distortions are treated perturbatively. Here, we show that the perturbative approach does not hold for helium diffracted at kiloelectronvolt energy through freestanding single-layer graphene. In this case, we enter a new regime of strong coupling where the projectile strongly interacts with the electron density of several lattice atoms simultaneously, leading to phase shifts of several radians. In consequence, lattice distortions introduce a significant phase spread that cannot be described by the typically employed Debye-Waller factor. We show that the weak-coupling regime is retained for atomic hydrogen diffraction. The experimental results are supported by simulations, providing a regime-independent approach to describe the influence of phonons on atom diffraction phenomena.

### [194] [Cone Minimax Principles for Non-Selfadjoint Operator Pencils](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31129)
*Yavdat Il'yasov,Nur Valeev*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 提出一种基于扩展双变量瑞利商（extended two-variable Rayleigh quotient）的变分方法，用于非自伴算子束（non-selfadjoint operator pencils）的主谱值（principal spectral values）分析，在有序锥（ordered cone）框架下建立了瑞利型极小极大公式（Rayleigh-type minimax formulas），并证明了有限维近似的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准自伴变分理论（standard selfadjoint variational theory）不适用于非自伴算子束，且基于正性（positivity）的方法可能无法直接应用。因此需要发展一种新的变分框架，以获得选定实谱级的极小极大刻画。

Method: 构造定义在可允许锥对（admissible cone pairs）上的扩展双变量瑞利商（extended two-variable Rayleigh quotient）ℛ(u,v)=⟨ℒu,v⟩/(𝒢u,v)_H，由此导出对偶的上确界-下确界（sup-inf）与下确界-上确界（inf-sup）主谱级、锥拟特征值（cone quasi-eigenvalues）以及相应的捕获原理（trapping principle）和鞍点原理（saddle-point principle）。

Result: 所得极小极大公式刻画了非自伴算子束的选定实锥谱级（real cone levels）；当存在正左右特征对（positive right-left eigenpairs）时，这些公式与主谱值一致，且适用于非可逆算子和奇异权函数情形。该公式在有限维近似下稳定，并提供了后验谱证书（a posteriori spectral certificates）、单边扰动界（one-sided perturbation bounds）和近似估计。

Conclusion: 经典有限维变分逼近谱数据的思想在有序锥背景下获得了非自伴算子束的类比物。椭圆型示例验证了方法的适用范围和估计的尖锐性。

Abstract: We propose a variational approach to principal spectral values of non-selfadjoint operator pencils $\mathcal L u=λ\mathcal G u$, where the weight operator $\mathcal G$ may be singular. The aim is to obtain Rayleigh-type minimax formulas for selected real spectral levels in settings where the standard selfadjoint variational theory is unavailable and positivity-based methods may not apply directly. The construction is based on the extended two-variable Rayleigh quotient \[ \mathcal R(u,v) = \frac{\langle \mathcal L u,v\rangle} {(\mathcal G u,v)_H},\] defined on admissible cone pairs. It leads to dual sup-inf and inf-sup principal levels, cone quasi-eigenvalues, and corresponding trapping and saddle-point principles. The resulting minimax formulas characterize selected real cone levels of non-selfadjoint operator pencils and identify them with principal spectral values whenever positive right-left eigenpairs exist, including cases with non-invertible operators and singular weights.
  We prove that these formulas are stable under finite-dimensional approximation. Thus the classical idea of approximating spectral data by finite-dimensional variational problems acquires an analogue for non-selfadjoint operator pencils in an ordered cone setting. The method also yields a posteriori spectral certificates, one-sided perturbation bounds, and approximation estimates. Elliptic examples illustrate both the scope of the method and the sharpness of the estimates.

</details>


### [195] [Generalization of Hallaire-Luikov Moisture Transfer Equation: Direct Problem with the $ψ$-Prabhakar Operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31403)
*Erkinjon Karimov,Shokhzodbek Khasanov*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对包含ψ-Prabhakar分数阶积分-微分算子的Hallaire-Luikov水分迁移方程，建立了初边值（直接）问题的解的存在性、唯一性和稳定性，并通过分离变量法和逐次逼近法给出了解的显式表达，解由一种新的四变量Mittag-Leffler型函数表示，同时建立了问题的先验估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究带有ψ-Prabhakar分数阶积分-微分算子的Hallaire-Luikov水分迁移方程的初边值问题，以推广经典水分迁移模型，并为其数学分析提供严格的理论基础。

Method: 采用分离变量法（separation of variables）和逐次逼近法（method of successive approximations，即迭代法）构造显式解，并引入一种新的四变量Mittag-Leffler型函数（quadrivariate Mittag-Leffler-type function）表达解的形式。

Result: 证明了所提初边值问题解的存在性、唯一性和稳定性，并建立了问题的先验估计（a priori estimate）；解以显式形式给出，并表示为一种新型四变量Mittag-Leffler函数。

Conclusion: 本文为带有ψ-Prabhakar算子的分数阶Hallaire-Luikov水分迁移方程提供了完整的数学分析框架，包括解的存在唯一性、稳定性及显式构造，拓展了经典Mittag-Leffler函数在分数阶扩散方程中的应用。

Abstract: This paper focuses on the analysis of an initial-boundary value (direct) problem for the Hallaire-Luikov moisture transfer equation involving the $ψ$-Prabhakar integral-differential operator of fractional order. We establish the existence, uniqueness, and stability of the solution to the formulated problem. To construct the solution, we employ the method of separation of variables and the method of successive approximations (iteration method), and obtain the solution to the considered problem in an explicit form. Furthermore, the solution is expressed in terms of a novel quadrivariate Mittag-Leffler-type function. An a priori estimate for the problem is also established.

</details>

# physics.flu-dyn [[Back]](#toc)

### [196] [Lagrangian velocity statistics of homogeneous isotropic turbulence in dilute polymer solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31283)
*Yusuke Koide,Susumu Goto*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本研究通过对稀聚合物溶液中均匀各向同性湍流（homogeneous isotropic turbulence）进行直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulation），探究了聚合物对拉格朗日速度统计量（Lagrangian velocity statistics）的调节作用，并基于尺度分解分析揭示了该调节源于聚合物从小尺度到大尺度依次抑制涡旋的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解稀聚合物溶液中湍流的拉格朗日速度统计特性，以及聚合物如何通过改变涡旋结构来影响这些统计量。

Method: 采用直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulation）方法，对稀聚合物溶液中的均匀各向同性湍流进行模拟；通过改变雷诺数（Reynolds number）、强迫方式（forcing method）和聚合物松弛时间（polymer relaxation time），分析拉格朗日速度的功率谱密度（power spectral density）和拉格朗日积分时间尺度（Lagrangian integral timescale）。为阐明机制，进一步将拉格朗日速度分解为不同长度尺度涡旋的贡献，进行尺度分解分析（scale-decomposition analysis）。

Result: 随着聚合物松弛时间增加，拉格朗日速度功率谱密度的衰减从高频逐渐延伸至低频，拉格朗日积分时间尺度增大。尺度分解分析表明，拉格朗日速度统计量的调节源于聚合物对涡旋的抑制，该抑制过程从小尺度逐步扩展至大尺度。

Conclusion: 聚合物通过从小尺度到大尺度依次抑制涡旋，从而调节拉格朗日速度统计量；这一机制解释了功率谱密度衰减范围随松弛时间增大而扩展的现象。

Abstract: We conduct direct numerical simulations of homogeneous isotropic turbulence in dilute polymer solutions to investigate the Lagrangian velocity statistics. We show how polymers modulate the power spectral density of the Lagrangian velocity and the Lagrangian integral timescale by varying the Reynolds number, forcing method, and polymer relaxation time. As the polymer relaxation time increases, the attenuation of the power spectral density extends successively from high to low frequencies, and the Lagrangian integral timescale increases. To clarify the mechanism underlying the modulation of the Lagrangian velocity statistics, we decompose the Lagrangian velocity into the contributions from vortices at different length scales. Using this scale-decomposition analysis, we demonstrate that the observed modulation of the Lagrangian velocity statistics results from polymer-induced suppression of vortices that proceeds from smaller to larger scales.

</details>

### [197] [Relativistic magnetohydrodynamics from kinetic theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31327)
*Khwahish Kushwah*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本论文基于相对论性玻尔兹曼-弗拉索夫方程（relativistic Boltzmann-Vlasov equation）和14矩近似（14-moment approximation），发展了强电磁场下相对论耗散磁流体力学（relativistic dissipative magnetohydrodynamics）的动理学理论框架，依次构建了无阻双组分等离子体、有阻双组分等离子体的因果二阶流体力学方程，揭示了电磁场驱动的各向异性输运、电流-剪切反馈及耗散振荡等效应，为重离子碰撞中的强磁夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）及天体物理系统提供了微观基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重离子碰撞中产生的夸克-胶子等离子体处于强电磁场环境下，而传统相对论耗散流体力学在描述此类磁化等离子体时存在因果性和稳定性不足的问题。为此，需要从动理学理论出发，系统构建能够同时处理耗散、强电磁场及因果性约束的磁流体力学框架。

Method: 以相对论玻尔兹曼-弗拉索夫方程为起点，采用矩方法（method of moments）并在14矩近似截断下，逐步推导二阶流体力学方程。首先回顾Israel-Stewart型瞬态理论以保证因果性与稳定性；然后逐层引入电磁场微观作用、无阻双组分情形和有阻双组分情形，分析洛伦兹力（Lorentz force）对矩层级（moment hierarchy）的修正及耦合效应。

Result: 对无阻双组分等离子体，磁场耦合两种组分的耗散扇区，产生相对耗散电流和耦合剪切动力学，在Bjorken膨胀下横向剪切扇区出现与回旋运动（cyclotron motion）相关的阻尼振荡。对有阻双组分等离子体，电场动态演化并与电荷扩散及剪切应力耦合，揭示出电流-剪切反馈、瞬态电磁生成的动量各向异性以及欠阻尼耗散振荡。在均匀和Bjorken膨胀等离子体中的应用表明，阻性和电磁效应显著改变了超越标准流体力学的演化行为。

Conclusion: 本论文将相对论耗散流体力学拓展至磁化及阻性等离子体系统，为强磁夸克-胶子等离子体及天体物理系统的后续研究提供了从动理学出发的微观理论基础。

Abstract: This thesis develops a kinetic-theory framework for relativistic dissipative magnetohydrodynamics under strong electromagnetic fields, motivated by quark-gluon plasma in heavy-ion collisions. Starting from the relativistic Boltzmann-Vlasov equation and using the method of moments within the 14-moment approximation, it derives causal second-order hydrodynamic equations for relativistic plasmas with increasing generality. The work first review relativistic dissipative hydrodynamics and its kinetic foundations, emphasizing the need for Israel-Stewart-type transient theories to preserve causality and stability. Electromagnetic fields are then introduced at the microscopic level, where the Lorentz force modifies the moment hierarchy and produces anisotropic transport effects absent in field-free fluids. Next, it develops relativistic dissipative magnetohydrodynamics for a non-resistive two-component plasma of oppositely charged particles. Here, the magnetic field couples the dissipative sectors of the two species, generating relative dissipative currents and coupled shear dynamics. For Bjorken expansion, the theory predicts damped oscillations in the transverse shear sector associated with cyclotron motion. Finally, the thesis treats the resistive two-component case, where the electric field evolves dynamically and couples to charge diffusion and shear stress. The resulting theory reveals current-shear feedback, transient electromagnetic generation of momentum anisotropy, and underdamped dissipative oscillations. Applications to homogeneous and Bjorken-expanding plasmas show how resistive and electromagnetic effects modify evolution beyond standard hydrodynamics. Overall, the thesis extends relativistic dissipative hydrodynamics to magnetized and resistive plasmas, providing a microscopic foundation for future studies of strongly magnetized quark-gluon plasma and astrophysical systems.

</details>
