### [198] [Rheological and Photoelastic Response of Hydrated Soft Granular Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30913)
*Brandon Hayes,Krishnaroop Chaudhuri,Rylan Hodgson,Benjamin McMillan,Ruby Gans,Hale Burke,Stephanie McNamara,Thomas Chalklen,Nathalie M. Vriend*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文总结了浸没式光弹颗粒（photoelastic particles）在流体介质中用于二维颗粒体系水动力学相互作用研究的现状，介绍了水合光弹颗粒流变与光学特性的表征方法，并提出了相关实验考量与标准框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光弹颗粒已被广泛应用于干颗粒体系中的应力可视化，但在浸没式（immersed）颗粒悬浮液中几乎未见研究，尽管其在工业与自然界中具有重要应用。流体相的引入会改变颗粒的流变与光弹行为，亟需系统性的表征与框架指导。

Method: 本文采用文献综述与实验表征相结合的方法。首先总结当前浸没式光弹颗粒材料中应力解析的最新技术水平；其次引入表征技术以探测水合光弹颗粒在流变（rheological）与光学性质上的变化；最后报告在浸没实验中使用光弹颗粒的注意事项。

Result: 提供了水合光弹颗粒的流变与光学特性变化表征方法，识别了在浸没式实验中引入流体相所带来的额外考量因素，并建立了一套适用于二维浸没光弹颗粒体系水动力学相互作用研究的标准框架。

Conclusion: 该工作旨在为在流体介质中浸没式光弹颗粒的二维系统研究提供领先框架，推动对水动力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions）的理解，并填补光弹悬浮液研究领域的空白。

Abstract: Photoelasticity is a qualitative and quantitative optical technique to image internal stress distributions in transparent materials. In the past few decades, discrete photoelastic particles have been used as a proxy for dry granular materials in both static, quasistatic, and dynamic analogue experiments. The technique allows the visualization of force chains, determination of the location and magnitude of contact forces, and outputs a stress tensor for each particle with shear and normal stress components. To date, little to no work has investigated photoelastic suspensions, where photoelastic granular particles are immersed in a fluid medium, despite its relevance in industrial and natural applications. The introduction of a fluid phase yields additional considerations in the rheological and photoelastic behavior of our proxy particles. In this manuscript, we summarize the state-of-the-art in resolving forces in immersed photoelastic granular materials. We introduce characterization techniques to probe changes in rheological and optical properties of hydrated photoelastic particles, and we report considerations for use of photoelastic particles in immersion-based experiments. We intend for this work to provide the leading framework to study the hydrodynamic interactions in 2D systems of photoelastic particles immersed in a fluid medium.

### [199] [Deep Indentation of Hyperelastic Materials Reveals Tip Independent Parabolic Force Depth Response via Strain Energy Delocalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30971)
*Mohammad Shojaeifard,Zhenwei Ma,Jimmy Hsia,Norman Fleck,Mattia Bacca*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文发现在深压痕（D >> R）条件下，平头和球形压头均遵循相同的抛物线力-深度定律 F = β E D²，系数β独立于压头半径和尖端形状，仅受界面摩擦的轻微影响，并由超弹性应变硬化响应控制。该标度行为源于应变能离域化，激活体积正比于D³，从而解释了压头形状独立性，并建立了β与Ogden应变硬化参数α的联系，使得从深压痕数据中提取超弹性参数成为可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统压痕法通常局限于浅压痕（indentation depth D << indenter radius R）区间，此时响应由局部接触几何控制，主要识别小应变杨氏模量（Young's modulus）E。然而，当标准测试困难、具有破坏性或无法原位进行时，需要探索深压痕这一替代路径，但其机理性理解尚不充分。

Method: 采用有限元模拟（finite-element simulations）分析深压痕（D >> R）条件下平头和球形压头的力学响应；通过应变能密度（strain-energy density, SED）的分布分析识别激活体积的标度行为；并将结果与Boussinesq远场解进行对比。

Result: 深压痕下，平头和球形压头的力-深度关系收敛到同一抛物线定律 F = β E D²；系数β与压头半径和尖端形状无关，仅受界面摩擦轻微影响。应变能离域化导致激活区域呈椭球状，其尺寸正比于D³，储弹能U ~ E D³，从而导出F ~ E D²。归一化距离a = √(F/E)后，应变能密度场坍塌到Boussinesq远场解，且a在深压痕区间正比于D。

Conclusion: 该发现为压头形状独立性提供了机理性基础，建立了β与Ogden应变硬化参数（strain-stiffening parameter）α的定量联系，从而使得从深压痕数据中提取超弹性参数成为可能，拓展了压痕法在软材料表征中的适用范围。

Abstract: Indentation is a practical route for probing soft materials when standard tests are difficult, destructive, or cannot be performed in situ. Conventional indentation is usually interpreted in the shallow-depth regime, where the indentation depth D is small compared with the indenter radius R. In this limit, the response is controlled by local contact geometry and primarily identifies the small-strain Young's modulus E. Here, we show that at deep indentation, D >> R, flat and spherical indenters converge to the same parabolic force-depth law, F = beta E D^2. The coefficient beta is independent of indenter radius and tip shape, only mildly affected by interfacial friction, and controlled by the hyperelastic strain-stiffening response. Finite-element simulations show that this scaling arises from strain-energy delocalization: the region where SED/mu > 0.01 expands into a spheroidal domain whose size scales with D. The activated volume therefore scales as D^3, giving stored elastic energy U ~ E D^3 and force F = dU/dD ~ E D^2. Far from contact, the strain-energy-density fields collapse toward the Boussinesq far-field solution when distances are normalized by a = sqrt(F/E), which scales as D in the deep-indentation regime. These results provide a mechanistic basis for tip-shape independence and link beta to the Ogden strain-stiffening parameter alpha, enabling hyperelastic parameter extraction from deep-indentation data.

</details>


### [200] [Self-consistent field theory of semiflexible nematics: Density-nematic coupling, anisotropic elasticity, and defect core sizes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31009)
*Longyu Qing,Jorge Viñals*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过自洽场理论（self-consistent field theory）研究了蠕虫链（wormlike chains）在向列相（nematic phase）中的线性响应，揭示了密度-向列序耦合对向列态稳定性的影响，以及链柔性对弗兰克弹性常数（Frank elastic constants）和关联长度（correlation lengths）的调控机制，并与+1/2向错核的结构特征进行了对比验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在定量理解半刚性高分子在向列相中的线性响应行为，特别是密度与向列有序度之间的耦合如何影响向列态的稳定性，以及链柔性对弹性常数和关联长度的作用机制，为解释向错核等缺陷结构提供理论依据。

Method: 采用自洽场理论（self-consistent field theory）构建模型哈密顿量，包含Maier–Saupe取向相互作用和各向同性排除体积相互作用（模拟隐式溶剂介导的链间相互作用，适用于溶致向列相（lyotropic nematic））。通过构建均匀向列态的有效自由能描述，统一处理密度-有序度耦合、各向同性-向列相共存及向列相稳定性极限。基于自由能进行线性响应分析，导出弗兰克弹性常数和关联长度。

Result: 强密度-向列序耦合可导致向列态失稳，失稳位置取决于排除体积与向列相互作用之比 $u_0/u_2$。向列畸变与密度、向列序变化仅在更高阶耦合，在线性响应范围内几乎解耦。增加柔性显著抑制弯曲（bend）和扭曲（twist）弹性，但对展曲（splay）弹性影响较弱，导致弹性主导从弯曲型向展曲型转变。关联长度和弗兰克弹性各向异性可很好地解释+1/2向错核的指向矢轮廓及核尺寸，核尺寸与平衡关联长度成正比，符合Landau–de Gennes标度律。

Conclusion: 自洽场理论能够统一描述半刚性向列高分子的密度-序参量耦合及其对稳定性的影响；线性响应分析给出的关联长度和弹性各向异性与向错结构观测一致，验证了Landau–de Gennes标度关系。

Abstract: The linear response of wormlike chains in the nematic phase is studied by self-consistent field theory. The model Hamiltonian incorporates Maier--Saupe orientational interactions together with an isotropic excluded volume interaction. The latter models implicitly solvent mediated chain interactions, as appropriate for a lyotropic nematic. An effective free energy description for uniform nematic states is constructed in terms of the chain segment density and uniaxial nematic order parameter, providing a unified framework for density--degree of order coupling, isotropic-nematic coexistence, and the limit of stability of the nematic phase. Our results show that strong density--nematic degree of order coupling can destabilize the nematic state. The location of the instability depends on the ratio of excluded volume and nematic interaction, $u_0/u_2$. In contrast, director distortions couple to density and nematic order variations only at higher order, remaining effectively decoupled in the linear response regime. The Frank elastic constants and the correlation lengths are obtained from a linear response analysis based on the self-consistent field theory free energy. Increasing flexibility strongly suppresses twist and bend elasticity while affecting splay elasticity comparatively weakly, leading to a crossover from bend-dominated to splay-dominated elasticity. The correlation lengths and Frank elastic anisotropy obtained from the linear response analysis explain well director profiles around a +1/2 disclination core, including the core size. The latter is proportional to the equilibrium correlation length, in agreement with Landau--de Gennes scaling.

</details>


### [201] [Beyond binary scission: a generalized three-species cascade breakage model for wormlike micellar solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31059)
*Rongxin Lu,Jiwei Jia,Young Ju Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文针对蠕虫状胶束流体（wormlike micellar fluids）的复杂流变行为，提出了一种三物种级联断裂模型（three-species cascade breakage model），引入中间胶束状态（intermediate micellar state）以改进现有双物种模型无法解析中间结构态和宽弛豫谱的局限。该模型能描述三模黏弹性响应、非单调本构曲线、剪切带（shear banding）形成以及瞬态流变特征，为宏观流动局域化与微观结构演化之间建立联系提供了物理解释框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有双物种模型（two-species models）仅提供胶束群体的粗粒化二元表示，无法解析中间结构状态（intermediate structural states）和宽弛豫谱（broad relaxation spectra），限制了其对蠕虫状胶束流体复杂流变行为的描述能力。

Method: 构建了一个三物种级联断裂模型，包含凝胶网络（gel-network）、长链（long chains）和短链（short chains）三类物种，通过引入中间胶束状态，在统一的动力学框架（kinetic framework）中连接短片段的快速弛豫与凝胶网络的缓慢恢复。

Result: 该模型产生了三模式黏弹性响应（three-mode viscoelastic response），改善了动态模量（dynamic moduli）的高频描述，呈现出非单调本构曲线（non-monotone constitutive curve），该曲线在库埃特流动（Couette flow）中演变为存在共存剪切带（coexisting shear bands）的应力平台。此外，模型成功捕捉了应力过冲（stress overshoot）、滞后（hysteresis）以及剪切停止后的多步弛豫（multistep relaxation）等瞬态响应特征。

Conclusion: 提出的三物种模型为蠕虫状胶束剪切带现象提供了一个物理可解释的框架，能够捕捉级联微观结构演化、宽弛豫动力学与宏观流动局域化之间的关联。

Abstract: Wormlike micellar fluids exhibit complex rheological behavior driven by the continuous breakage and recombination of self-assembled micellar networks. Existing two-species models provide a coarse binary representation of the micellar population, limiting their ability to resolve intermediate structural states and broad relaxation spectra. To address this limitation, we develop a three-species cascade breakage model consisting of gel-network, long chains, and short chains. By introducing an intermediate micellar state, the model links the rapid relaxation of short fragments to the slow recovery of the gel-network within a unified kinetic framework. This additional structural pathway gives rise to a three-mode viscoelastic response, improves the high-frequency description of the dynamic moduli, and produces a non-monotone constitutive curve that evolves into a stress plateau with coexisting shear bands in Couette flow. This cascade mechanism also governs the transient response, including stress overshoot, hysteresis, and multistep relaxation after shear cessation. Overall, the proposed three-species model provides a physically interpretable framework for worm-like micellar shear banding, capturing the connection between cascade microstructural evolution, broad relaxation dynamics, and macroscopic flow localization.

</details>


### [202] [Designing bistable nanostructures for target behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31620)
*Andreas Ehrmann,Marija Krstić,Sahar Samadzadeh,Carl P. Goodrich*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种模块化逆向设计（inverse-design）框架，用于构建具有受控能量分布（energy profile）的双稳态纳米结构（bistable nanostructures）。通过铰链-臂（hinge-arm）范式，研究发现能量势垒和亚稳态结合位点间距易于编程，而过渡态位置和能量分布全形状则需要更多设计自由度。可微设计框架表明，部分数值上不精确的解仍能实现目标功能，强调了基于功能评估标准的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多生物机器通过受控构象转变（conformational transitions）发挥作用，但设计具有预定动力学行为的人工纳米结构仍是一项重大挑战。本文旨在解决这一设计难题。

Method: 受蛋白质中由柔性铰链连接的刚性结构域启发，提出了铰链-臂（hinge-arm）范式：小尺寸双稳态铰链控制构象转变的能量分布，刚性臂将该转变映射到外部结合位点（binding sites）之间的分离距离上。采用可微设计（differentiable design）框架，在不同设计约束下探索目标能量分布的可编程性。

Result: 能量势垒（energy barriers）和两个亚稳态状态下的结合位点分离距离易于设计；控制过渡态（transition state）位置或能量分布的完整形状则需要额外的设计自由度。部分优化解在数值上不精确，但仍表现出目标能量分布所对应的功能性行为。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了双稳态纳米结构可设计性（designability）的实用层级结构，为连接构象转变与目标行为（target behavior）的合成纳米机器（synthetic nanomachines）提供了实现路径。

Abstract: Many biological machines function through controlled conformational transitions, yet designing synthetic nanostructures with prescribed dynamical behavior remains a major challenge. Here, we develop a modular inverse-design framework for bistable nanostructures whose function is controlled by an energy profile along a geometric reaction coordinate. Inspired by proteins with rigid domains connected by flexible hinges, we introduce a hinge-arm paradigm in which a small bistable hinge controls the energetics of a conformational transition, while rigid arms map this transition onto the separation between external binding sites. Specifically, we ask which features of a target energy profile can be programmed under different design constraints. We find that the energy barriers and the binding-site separations in the two metastable states can be readily designed, while controlling the location of the transition state or the full shape of the energy profile requires additional design freedom. Using a differentiable design framework, we find that some optimized solutions are numerically inexact but still display the functional behavior for which the target profile was selected, emphasizing the importance of function-based evaluation criteria. These results establish a practical hierarchy of designability for bistable nanostructures and provide a route toward synthetic nanomachines that couple conformational transitions to target behavior.

</details>


### [203] [Mesoscopic simulations of linear and ring polymer solutions with explicit hydrodynamics under good and poor solvent conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31656)
*Ashish Kumar Singh,Angelo Rosa*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 采用大规模耗散粒子动力学（Dissipative Particle Dynamics, DPD）模拟，研究了线形和环形聚合物在稀溶液中的结构及动力学，发现溶剂质量（solvent quality）主导其组织与输运行为，而拓扑效应（topological effects）在该参数范围内相对较弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 考察溶剂质量、流体动力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions）、链拓扑结构（chain architecture）及分子间缔合（intermolecular association）之间的耦合关系，明确稀溶液下聚合物构象与输运行为的主要决定因素。

Method: 采用大规模耗散粒子动力学（DPD）模拟，在显式溶剂（explicit solvent）条件下分别模拟线形聚合物（linear polymers）和无结非连锁环形聚合物（unknotted, non-concatenated ring polymers）的稀溶液，并系统改变溶剂质量。

Result: 良溶剂条件下，两类聚合物均保持膨胀（expanded）和良好分散（well dispersed），质心动力学（center-of-mass dynamics）符合正常扩散（normal diffusion）；不良溶剂中，聚合物间吸引导致形成不规则聚集体（irregular aggregates），并呈现部分链塌缩（partial chain collapse）、显著互穿（substantial interpenetration）及动力学减慢。两种拓扑结构在结构响应和动力学响应上高度相似。

Conclusion: 在所考察的稀溶液参数范围内，溶剂质量是决定聚合物组织与输运性质的主导因素，而拓扑效应的影响相对较弱。

Abstract: We employ large-scale Dissipative Particle Dynamics simulations to investigate dilute solutions of linear polymers and unknotted, non-concatenated ring polymers in explicit solvent. By systematically varying solvent quality, we examine the interplay between hydrodynamic interactions, chain architecture, and intermolecular association. Under good solvent conditions, both linear and ring polymers remain expanded and well dispersed, displaying center-of-mass dynamics consistent with normal diffusion. In poor solvents, attractive polymer-polymer interactions drive the formation of irregular aggregates characterized by partial chain collapse, substantial interpenetration, and slower dynamics. Despite their different topologies, the two polymer architectures exhibit remarkably similar structural and dynamical responses across the solvent conditions considered. These results indicate that solvent quality largely determines the organization and transport properties of dilute polymer solutions, whereas topological effects remain comparatively weak in the investigated regime.

*Avraham Moriel,Howard A. Stone*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过耦合Flory-Huggins热力学与双流体黏弹性理论，研究源驱动聚合物液滴的扩散行为，识别出扩散前沿存在普适的结构压缩边缘，并通过标度律、数值模拟和实验数据验证该框架能够捕捉核仁（nucleolus）的结构与动力学特征，揭示了聚合物扩散在非平衡生物输运中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多亚细胞凝聚体（subcellular condensates）持续产生生物聚合物，其非平衡输运机制尚不清晰。本文旨在探究源驱动聚合物液滴的扩散行为，并揭示其在核仁等生物凝聚体中的适用性。

Method: 将Flory-Huggins热力学（Flory-Huggins thermodynamics）与双流体黏弹性理论（two-fluid viscoelasticity）耦合，结合解析标度律（analytical scaling laws）、数值模拟和实验数据进行分析。

Result: 识别出源驱动聚合物液滴的扩散前沿存在一个普适的结构压缩边缘（universal structural compressive rim）；该框架能够有效捕捉核仁的关键结构与动力学特征。

Conclusion: 聚合物扩散在非平衡生物输运（non-equilibrium biological transport）中发挥重要作用，该耦合框架为理解亚细胞凝聚体的动态行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Many subcellular condensates continuously produce biopolymers. Coupling Flory-Huggins thermodynamics to two-fluid viscoelasticity, we probe the diffusion of such source-driven polymeric droplets, and identify a universal structural compressive rim at their diffusion front. Integrating analytical scaling laws, numerical simulations, and experimental data, we show that this framework captures key structural and dynamic characteristics of the nucleolus, demonstrating the role of polymer diffusion in non-equilibrium biological transport.

### [205] [Optimal interactions for addressable self-assembly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31838)
*Tighe McAsey,Sushrut Tadwalkar,Ali Fele-Paranj,Miranda Holmes-Cerfon*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了可寻址自组装（addressable self-assembly）中的单体耗竭（monomer depletion）问题，通过反应方程和数值优化发现最优相互作用满足：强键形成目标结构的生成树（spanning tree），其余键很弱。生成树结构可避免单体耗竭和动力学陷阱，形成一种鲁棒的设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可寻址自组装要求每个构建块（building block）精确到达目标结构的特定位置，但单体耗竭导致产率低下——更多目标结构开始成核，却没有足够的构件完成生长，形成无法完成的碎片。本文旨在探索如何设计构建块之间的相互作用，以在给定时间内实现最高产率。

Method: 采用描述所有中间组装步骤的反应方程（reaction equations）结合数值优化（numerical optimization）方法，分析最优相互作用模式；随后通过图论证明生成树结构的性质，并在更大结构上进行数值模拟验证。

Result: 最优相互作用满足两个条件：(i) 所有键要么非常强要么非常弱，(ii) 强键形成目标结构的生成树。生成树结构确保组装总能沿能量下坡方向进行，不存在动力学陷阱（kinetic traps），从而避免单体耗竭。这一性质是底层相互作用图（interaction graph）的组合性质，不依赖于具体的动力学模型。更紧凑的生成树通常具有更高的产率。

Conclusion: 研究提出了一种鲁棒的设计原则：构建一个无环的强相互作用网络，并使其他相互作用大大弱化。该框架可用于理解DNA纳米技术（DNA nanotechnology）中的自组装，并为某些多蛋白复合物（multiprotein complexes）的组装路径提供洞察。

Abstract: Addressable self-assembly asks that each building block assemble into a particular location in a target structure. Although particles may all be distinct, achieving high yield is a challenge because of monomer depletion: more target structures can nucleate than there are building blocks for, so they form partial fragments which cannot complete growth. We ask how to design the interactions between building blocks to achieve the highest yield in a given time. Using reaction equations describing all the intermediate steps of assembly, combined with numerical optimization, we show that the optimal interactions are such that (i) all bonds are either very strong or very weak, and (ii) the strong bonds form a spanning tree of the target structure. We then prove that when interactions form a spanning tree, monomer depletion cannot occur: assembly can always proceed downhill in energy space, with no kinetic traps. This result is a combinatorial property of the underlying interaction graph, and does not depend on the particular model for the kinetics. It suggests a robust design principle: create a network of strong interactions that has no loops, and make all other interactions much weaker. We validate this principle in numerical simulations of larger structures, and we further show that spanning trees that are more compact have typically better yield. Our results suggest a new framework for understanding monomer depletion and addressable self-assembly, which may be applied to DNA nanotechnology and which may give insight into the assembly pathways of certain multiprotein complexes.

</details>


### [206] [Designing topological edge currents in chiral active matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31840)
*Yuta Kuroda,Ellen Meyberg,Gaurav Gardi,Thomas Speck,Saeed Osat*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过引入手性切换（chirality switching）的二维手性主动游泳者粒子模型，展示了该模型在任意约束几何和缺陷存在下均能产生鲁棒的边缘流（edge currents）；进一步发现手性切换可引发与运动性诱导相分离（motility-induced phase separation）不同的相分离，并伴随界面边缘流；通过线性化流体力学方程的拓扑性质分析，证明边缘流是真实的拓扑边缘模（topological edge modes），为设计主动物质系统中的鲁棒边缘流提供了指导方针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有研究在手性主动物质（chiral active matter）中观察到边缘流，但使其对约束几何和缺陷保持鲁棒的微观规则尚不清楚。本文旨在揭示这一微观机制并建立理论解释。

Method: 构建二维手性主动游泳者的简单粒子模型，引入手性切换机制；通过自底向上的粗粒化（bottom-up coarse-graining）导出有效流体力学理论；对线性化流体力学方程进行拓扑性质分析。

Result: 单粒子约束下，无论约束几何或缺陷存在与否，边缘流均会出现。相互作用粒子在体相中表现出由手性切换诱导的相分离，该相分离不同于运动性诱导相分离，并伴随界面边缘流。线性化流体力学方程的分析表明，边缘流属于真实的拓扑边缘模。

Conclusion: 手性切换诱导的相分离可视为两个拓扑不同域（topologically distinct domains）的共存；研究结果为在主动物质系统中设计鲁棒边缘流提供了指导原则。

Abstract: Achieving robust functionality in active matter driven away from thermal equilibrium is a current theoretical and experimental challenge. Several recent studies have reported edge currents--persistent transport along walls and density inhomogeneities--in chiral active matter. Yet, the microscopic rules that render these edge currents robust with respect to the confinement geometry and defects remain elusive. Here, we introduce a simple particle model of two-dimensional chiral active swimmers that undergo chirality switching and demonstrate that the model exhibits robust edge currents, i.e., when a single particle is confined, edge currents arise regardless of the confinement geometry or the presence of defects. We also investigate the collective behavior of interacting particles in bulk and find that chirality switching induces phase separation accompanied by edge currents along interfaces. This phase separation is distinct from motility-induced phase separation and is qualitatively explained by an effective hydrodynamic theory derived via bottom-up coarse-graining. Furthermore, by analyzing the topological properties of the linearized hydrodynamic equations, we show that the edge currents in our system are genuine topological edge modes. Notably, phase separation induced by chirality switching can be regarded as the coexistence of two topologically distinct domains. Our results provide guidelines for designing robust edge currents in active matter systems.

</details>


### [207] [Self-Generated Electric Fields in Polyelectrolyte Gradients Increase Microparticle Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31902)
*Max Huisman,Ali Azadbakht,Patrick B. Warren,Daniela J. Kraft*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文理论预测并实验验证了在聚电解质（polyelectrolyte）梯度中带电微粒因电荷分离动力学自生宏观电场，该电场能显著增强微粒的趋电推进（phoretic propulsion）速度；高分子量聚电解质下推进行为变为梯度无关，符合非对称电解质的扩散电泳（diffusiophoresis）理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然界和工业中广泛存在带电微粒暴露于带电聚合物（charged polymers）梯度的场景（如DNA/RNA梯度中的酶、呼吸道液滴中的病毒颗粒、分层涂料层中的胶体颗粒），但聚电解质梯度中微粒的趋电推进机制尚不明确，尤其自生电场（self-generated electric field）的作用未被充分研究。

Method: 理论层面，从聚电解质梯度中连续扩散驱动力下的电荷分离动力学出发，推导出自生宏观电场的存在。实验层面，测量带电微粒在聚电解质梯度中的推进速度，验证电场存在及其效应。此外，对比不同分子量聚电解质下的推进行为。

Result: 实验证实了自生电场的存在，并表明该电场显著提升了带电微粒的趋电推进速度。对于高分子量聚电解质，推进速度变得梯度无关，与不对称电解质的扩散电泳预测一致。

Conclusion: 聚电解质梯度中的自生电场可增强微粒输运，该机制适用于任何不同迁移率（mobility）的带电物种被持续驱动远离平衡态的场景。

Abstract: There are many situations in nature and industry where small particles are exposed to gradients of charged polymers, such as enzymes in biological gradients of DNA or RNA, virus particles in respiratory droplets, and colloidal particles in stratifying paint layers. Here, we study the phoretic propulsion of charged microparticles in a polyelectrolyte gradient. We theoretically predict the emergence of a macroscopic electric field from charge-separation dynamics in a polyelectrolyte gradient under a continuous diffusive driving force. We confirm the presence of this self-generated electric field experimentally and show that it significantly increases the phoretic velocity of the microparticles. Finally, for high molecular weight polyelectrolytes we observe that propulsion becomes gradient-independent, consistent with diffusiophoretic predictions for asymmetric electrolytes. Our results show that self-generated electric fields in polyelectrolyte gradients can enhance microparticle transport, with potential applicability wherever charged species of different mobility are continuously driven out of equilibrium.

### [208] [Drift-diffusion interplay in active Brownian particles under orienting field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31914)
*Andrey A. Kuznetsov,Vittoria Sposini,Sofia S. Kantorovich,Aleksei V. Chechkin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文建立了均匀磁场中三维活性布朗运动（active Brownian motion）的理论框架，解析了耦合的平动-转动动力学，揭示了长期行为中增强扩散与永久漂移的共存，以及中间时间尺度上的非高斯位移统计，首次通过时间特性展示了磁场对活性物质搜索与靶向传输的调控潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性活性粒子（magnetic active particles）结合自驱动与外场可调取向，为实现外部可控的微尺度输运提供了多功能途径，但在均匀磁场中三维活性布朗运动的完整理论描述尚缺乏。

Method: 发展了一个理论框架来描述均匀磁场中的三维活性布朗运动，纳入耦合的平转动力学（coupled translational and rotational dynamics），并给出了低阶位移矩的解析近似。

Result: 长期动力学简化为增强扩散（enhanced diffusion）与永久漂移（permanent drift）的组合，而常规活性布朗粒子缺乏后者；中间时间尺度上，转动噪声、自推进与磁取向的相互作用导致显著的非高斯位移统计（non-Gaussian displacement statistics）；首次通过性质（first-passage properties）表现出强磁场敏感性。

Conclusion: 磁场充当外部控制器，将活性导向两种运动模式之一；理论预测与数值模拟一致，突出了磁导引在优化搜索过程与活性物质靶向递送中的应用潜力。

Abstract: Magnetic active particles offer a versatile route to externally controlled microscale transport by combining self-propulsion with field-tunable orientation, as realized in both synthetic and living magnetic microswimmers. Here, we develop a theoretical framework for three-dimensional active Brownian motion in a uniform magnetic field, incorporating coupled translational and rotational dynamics and providing analytical approximations for low-order displacement moments. At long times, the system dynamics reduces to a combination of enhanced diffusion and permanent drift absent in regular active Brownian particles. The field acts as an external controller, channeling activity toward one of these two types of motion. At intermediate time scales, the interplay between rotational noise, self-propulsion, and magnetic alignment results in pronounced non-Gaussian displacement statistics. First-passage properties exhibit strong field sensitivity, highlighting the potential of magnetic guidance to optimize search processes and targeted delivery in active matter systems. Theoretical predictions are validated by numerical simulations.

</details>
